IMeya yeTheku ingenelela enkingeni yombhikisho
IMEYA yeTheku ithembise ukuyisukumela ngokushesha inkinga yomphakathi waseReservoir Hills onqume ukuvala imigwaqo izolo ekuseni, ubhikishela ukunganakwa kwezindlu ohlala kuzo ezacekelwa phansi wumlilo.
Phakathi kwezinkinga ezikhungethe lo mphakathi kubalwa ukungafakwa kwamapayipi endle nokungalungiswa kukagesi okubikwa ukuthi uqale ukuhlupha ngemva komlilo owashisa izindlu.
UMnuz Mxolisi Kaunda, ohambele lo mphakathi unxenxe uphiko lukagesi ukuthi luyilungise inkinga ekhungethe le ndawo.
"Sivumelane ngomhlangano ozoba ngeSonto, esizolalela kuwo ezinye izimfuno zomphakathi.
Amalungu omphakathi analo ilungelo lokuzwakalisa izikhalazo zawo kodwa siyawanxusa ukuthi aqikelele ukuthi awayilimazi impahla yomkhandlu," kusho uKaunda.
Eqhuba, uqinisekisile emalungwini omphakathi ukuthi umasipala uzozibophezela ekuphuthumiseni izidingo zawo.
Uphinde wawatusa ukuthi asebenzise imigudu efanele uma efuna ukuzwakalisa izikhalo zawo.
"Siwguhulumeni olalelayo futhi neminyango yethu ivulekile kulabo abafuna ukuxhumana nathi ngezimfuno zomphakathi," kubeka imeya.
Amajaji azomemezela usuku lwesinqumo kwelakaShembe
INKANTOLO yoMthethosisekelo kulindeleke ukuba ikhiphe usuku ezothula ngalo isinqumo ngombango wobuholi ebandleni lamaNazaretha njengoba izolo icala lingazange libe khona.
Leli cala liphakathi kwabaseThembezinhle nabaseBuhleni.
EBuhleni baholwa yiNkosi Mduduzi "Nyazilwezulu" Shembe, eThembezinhle baholwa iNkosi Phinda Shembe, emuva kokuba kukhothame iNkosi Vela "Misebeyelanga" Shembe.
Isolezwe likhuluma nommeli waseThembezinhle uMnuz Trevor Nkosi, uthe bebenolwazi lokuthi icala lizoba khona izolo njengoba kwakubhalwe kanjalo kwi-website yoMthethosisekelo kodwa kwangenzeka lokho ngenxa yokuba matasa kwamajaji namanye amacala.
"Icala belingekho ohlwini lwamacala namhlanje, kwakufakwe ukuthi lizoba khona namhlanje kwi-website yenkantolo kodwa kwabuye kwasuswa lokho.
Silindele unobhala wasenkantolo ukuba asazise ukuthi amajaji alungele nini ukuba athule isinqumo.
Amajaji besazi ukuthi bese ekulungele ukuletha isinqumo.
Sesizozwa ngawo, ngoba ngisho nomabhalane wenkantolo uthe uzolindela wona amajaji ukuba akhiphe usuku," kusho uNkosi.
Besibhekwe ngabomvu lesi sinqumo njengoba kuzoba isona sokugcina kuleli cala eselidonse kusukela ngo-2011.
Umbango wasuka emuva kokukhothama kweNkosi uVimbeni Shembe uThingolwenkosazana.
Okwasusa umsindo kwaba ukuthi iNkosi Mqoqi Ngcobo yamemezela uNyazilwezulu njengomholi ekubeni kuthiwa yayingagunyaziwe.
Ummeli uMnuz Zwelabantu Buthelezi waba nobufakazi obuqinile bokuthi umholi ofanele yiMisebeyelanga ngoba wasebenzisa incwadi eyasayinwa wuThingolwenkosazana.
Icala lasuka Nkantolo eNkulu eThekwini, laya kweNkulu yaseMgungundlovu, ladlulswa layiswa eNkantolo yokuDluliswa kwamaCala eBloemfontein.
UNkosi uthe yize engenalwazi lokuthi isinqumo sizokhishwa nini kodwa kungaba noma yinini.
Uma nje amajaji esekulungele ukusikhipha.
I-SACP yeseka uKhongolose empini yokulwa nenkohlakalo
ISOUTH African Communist Party (SACP) yamukele isinqumo se-ANC sokumisa ezikhundleni amalungu ayo anamacala enkohlakalo nabucayi ezinkantolo.
NgoMsombuluko, i-ANC iphothule umhlangano wesigungu esiphezulu odonse izinsuku ezintathu.
Kuvele ukuthi kukhona abaholi abazishenxele ngokwabo kwathi labo abahlulekile babhalelwa izincwadi ezibamisayo.
I-SACP ithi nayo izoqhubeka nohlelo lwayo lokuqondisa ubugwegwe amalungu ayo anamacala enkohlakalo nabucayi ezinkantolo.
Esitatimendeni esithumele ngemva komhlangano we-ANC, i-SACP income isinqumo sikaKhongolose sokumisa abagoloze ukushenxa ezikhundleni yathi yisinyathelo esihle ekulweni nenkohlakalo.
Ithe kuzoba yisifundo nakwabanye abebesacabanga ukuzimbandakanya nezenzo zenkohlakalo.
Omunye wabaholi ababhalelwe incwadi emumisa enhlanganweni uNobhala jikelele uMnuz Ace Magashule.
Lo mholi akahlangabezananga nomnqamulajuqu wezinsuku ezingu-30 ayebekelwe wona nabanye abanamacala ezinkantoloLeli qembu liveze nokuthi liyayeseka iKhomishana kaZondo, ephenya ngezinsolo zokulawulwa koMbuso yidlanzana.
Ithe iyaweseka uKhongolose empini yawo elwa nenkohlakalo yanxenxa amalungu amadlela ndawonye nomphakathi wonkana ukuba benze okufanayo.
I-SACP iyalweseka uhlelo lokuhlelwa kabusha kwenhlangano yomakadebona bezempi uMkhonto Wesizwe nokuqinisekiswa kobulungu bamalungu ayo.
Le nhlangano ithi iyasamukela isinqumo se-ANC sokulwa nodlame lwangokobulili yathi izosebenzisana nayo ekulweni lempi.
AmaKhomanisi anombono ofanayo nowe-ANC efuna kuqiniswe ubudlelwano namaxhama ezokuxhumana nezwe iCuba.
Ziyanda izinkinga nezikweleti  kwabeNFP
WILLEM PHUNGULAZIYAQONGA izinkinga ezihambisana nezikweleti kwiNFP, okubukeka zingase ziphazamise leli qembu ezinhlelweni zokungenela ukhetho.
Izinhlangothi osekunesikhathi eside zingabhekani kuleli qembu likaNkk Zanele KaMagwaza-Msibi, zilokhu ziqhubeke nokugijimisana ezinkantolo, okudalela iqembu izikweleti ezingapheli.
Muva nje uhlangothi oluholwa yilungu lePhalemende, uMnuz Emmam Mansoor noMnuz Vikizitha Mlotshwa onguSihlalo waKwaZulu-Natal, selufake amaphepha eNkantolo eNkulu eMgungundlovu lufuna inkantolo ihlawulise futhi ishushise abaholi beqembu abaqhubeka nomsebenzi phezu kokuba kunesinqumo sesikhashana, esithi ingasebenzi indaba yengqungquthela yango-2019 eyakhetha ubuholi bukazwelonke.
Laba baholi ngoMnuz Canaan Mdletshe onguNobhala Jikelele, nguMnu Bhekithemba Dlamini onguSihlalo noMnuz Obed Ngcamu onguMgcinimafa.
Ngaphandle kokudelela isinqumo senkantolo, uhlangothi lukaMansoor lufuna la madoda ahlawule uR100 000 iyinye ngokudukisa amalungu eqembu ngokuzibiza ngabaholi kungafanele.
UMnuz Teddy Thwala, okhulumela uhlangothi lukaMansoor ukuqinisekisile ukuthi bafake amaphepha enkantolo.
Uthe babone kufanele baphindele enkantolo ngoba laba baholi abathathu badelele umyalelo wenkantolo wangoSepthemba nyakenye, othi ingqungquthela eyabakhetha ngo-2019 indaba yayo mayingasebenzi okwesikhashana.
Uthe lokhu kwakusho ukuthi nobuholi obakhethwa kuyo buzoke bume ukusebenza kuze kuphume isinqumo njengoba sagodlwa ngoMashi.
"Sifuna inkantolo ibajezise ngokudelela umthetho wezwe.
Le nto yokushaya indiva umyalelo wenkantolo iyingozi enkulu ezweni ngoba uma izwe lingasenamthetho lifana nelingekho," kusho uThwala.
Uthe bafuna inkantolo ibagwebe bese ivuma nesicelo sabo sokuthi bahlawulise uR100 000 emunye.
Ethintwa uNobhala weNFP, uMnuz Canaan Mdletshe, ongomunye wababekwa icala, uthe bona bayaqhubeka nomsebenzi wabo, okusezinkantolo bakushiyela kubameli babo.
Uthe bamatasa nezinhlelo zokulungisela ukhetho ukuze kungenzeki okwenzeka ngo-2016 lapho iqembu laphuthwa yithuba lokungenela ukhetho.
Ngokwamaphepha abonwe yileli phephandaba, ayalela ukuba abamangalelwa bafake amaphepha aphikisayo mhla ka-14 May bese zombili izinhlangothi zifike enkantolo ngomhla ka-26 kuyo ephezulu, kuzoqulwa.
Leli phephandaba lihoshe ukuthi kuseza esinye isikweleti sikaR400 000 ebuholini bukazwelonke beqembu, esidalwe wukwehlulwa ecaleni elabeka eceleni ingqungquthela nesidalwe wukwehlulwa emzamweni yokukhipha uMansoor ePhalamende ngo-2019.
Loku kuphonsana ezinkantolo sekushiya imibuzo ukuthi ngabe leli qembu lizokwazi kanjani ukulungiselela ukhetho ubuholi bungekho.
URamaphosa nenselelo entsheni
UMENGAMELI Cyril Ramaphosa usephonsele inselelo intsha yakuleli ukuba ivuke izakhele amathuba, ingalindeli ukukhangezwa wuhulumeni.
Ekhuluma emcimbini wokugubha uSuku lweNtsha obuseMgungundlovu izolo, uRamaphosa utshele intsha yakuleli ukuba ilandele ezinyathelweni zentsha yango-1976, ilwele ikusasa layo.
URamaphosa ukhumbuze intsha yakuleli ukuthi yona ayifani nentsha yango-1976 eyabhikishela ukufundiswa ngesiBhunu, ebalula ukuthi intsha yanamhlanje ikhulela ezweni elikhululekile.
"Esikhundleni sokuthi nibuze uhulumeni ukuthi uzonenzelani, kufanele nizibuze ukuthi nina yini enizoyenza ukushintsha isimo enikuso.
Nginiphonsela inselelo ukuba niqhamuke namaqhinga okuthuthukisa izwe.
"Nginiphonsela inselelo ukuba nikhombise ukuba nomdlandla ekuthuthukiseni leli lizwe nekusasa lenu.
Uma sibambisene singawenza umehluko.
"URamaphosa unxuse intsha ukuba ingazihlanganisi nabenza ubugebengu.
"Noma ngabe bangabangani benu, ziqhelelaniseni nabo.
Kufanele sisebenze ngokubambisana ukulwa nezinkinga ezibhekene nezwe, ezifana nokuhlukunyezwa kwabesifazane, izimpi zemigulukudu nokusetshenziswa kwezidakamizwa.
"Kufanele silwisane nodlame olubhekiswe kwabathandana nabobulili obufanayo kanjalo nolubhekiswe kwabokufika kuleli.
""URamaphosa ukuvumile ukuthi intsha yanamhlanje ibhekene nezinselelo eziningi.
"Cishe u-64% wabantu abasha bakuleli abasebenzi.
Lesi yisimo esingamukelekile.
Abantu abasha yibona abayikusasa lezwe.
"URamaphosa ubuye wasebenzisa le nkulumo ukumemezela izinhlelo ezahlukene zokuthuthukisa intsha.
Umemezele uhlelo olusha okuhloswe ngalo ukulekelela intsha ukuba ithole amathuba ezomnotho, iSA Youth.
"Lolu hlelo luzohlanganisa iminyango kahulumeni eyisishagalombili.
"Njengentsha yango-1976, intsha yanamhlanje inamaqhinga futhi inomdlandla.
Iyona engakwazi ukushintsha isimo.
Yibona abahlale besikhumbuza ukuthi abafuni ukukhangezwa.
Bahlale bethi ayikho into ethinta bona ezokwenzeka ngaphandle kwabo," kusho uZikalala.
Uzochitha impelasonto ejele 'ohubhuze amanga' ezweni
OWESIFAZANE okhathaze abantu abaningi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ethi kudunwe imoto yakhe wavalelwa ebhuthini uzohlala ejele impelasonto yonke kulandela ukuboshwa ngokuqamaba amanga emaphoyiseni.
Lo wesifazane ubhekene necala lokuqamba amanga, elokukhwabanisa, nelokuphazamisa ukusebenza kwengalo yomthetho ngokuvula icala elingekho lokudunwa imoto esiteshini samaphoyisa ePretoria Glen, eSoweto.
Bekumele avele enkantolo yeMantshi ePitoli namhlanje, kodwa kuthiwa amaphoyisa athe udaba lwakhe seluyiswe enkantolo yeMantshi eRandfontein.
Kulindeleke ukuthi avele khona ngoMsombuluko.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa eGoli uCaptain Mavela Masondo uveze ukuthi lowesifazane uzivumele yena ukuthi ubehubhuza amanga ekhasini lakhe kuFacebook ngesikhathi ebhala ngokuthunjwa kudunwa imoto yakhe.
Uvume lokhu ngemuva kophenyo lwamaphoyisa asheshe athola ukuthi kuningi okungahlangani ngabatshela khona.
Abantu abaningi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana bakujabulele ukuboshwa kwakhe ngoba bethi udlala ngezinto ekungadlalwa ngazo.
Abanye bathe utshengisa ukungabi nalo uzwelo kubantu abahlukumezekile ezigamekweni ezifana nalezi phambilini.
Wasting state resources like that & not to mention, toying with peoples' emotions.
Her actions have honestly trivalised the traumatic, lived experiences of others.
Umsindo kumenyezelwa uMntwana uMisuzulu njengeSilo esisha
INCWADI ebhalwe yiBambabukhosi elisanda kukhothama iNdlovukazi uMantfombi Shiyiwe Mantfombi Dlamini Zulu isicacisile ngokuqokwa kukaMntwana uMisuzulu Zulu njengeSilo esizolandela.
Lokhu kumenyezelwe ngu-Advocate Madoda Griffiths Madonsela efunda incwadi yamafa eshiywe yiNdlovukazi namhlanje kusihlwa.
UMisuzulu (46) uyindodana yokuqala yeMbube uGoodwill Zwelithini neNdlovukazi.
Kuvele ukuthi yiSilo esaqoka iNdlovukazi uMantfombi encwadini yefa eyalotshwa ngo-2016 ukuthi athathe ubukhosi uma sesikhothama.
INdlovukazi ibe isiziqokela uMntwana uMisuzulu ngoMashi nonyaka ukuthi kube nguye ozoba yiSilo esilandelayo.
"Uma engaphumeleli uMntwana uMisuzulu, ngibeka noma iyiphi enye indodana yami ukuthi ithathe isihlalo sobukhosi.
Amadodana ami azokhetha ngokuvota phakathi kwawo ukuthi ngubani ofanele ukuba sesihlalweni," kuso incwadi yamafa.
Ngemuva kwalesi simemezelo nokufundwa kwefa kusuke umsindo kulo mhlangano buhanjelwe abantwana bonke kanye namanye amalungu omndeni kubangwa yona indaba yefa kwakhishwa abezindaba Kwakhangelamakengana.
Umsindo ususwe wuMntwana uThokozani ophakame kusanda kuphothulwa ukwethulwa kwencwadi yefa esola iBambabukhosi ngokuhluleka ukwenza umsebenzi abewubekelwe... Udaba oluphelele kwiSolezwe NgoMgqibelo.
UDuduzane Zuma wothe iSilo uMisuzulu
INDODANA yowayengumengameli wezwe uMnuz Jacob Zuma, uMnuz Duduzane Zuma, yothe iSilo, uMisuzulu kaZwelithini izolo.
UZuma uhambele esigodlweni KwaKhangelamankengane lapho ehlangane khona neSilo.
UZuma, ongusomabhizinisi, ufike esigodlweni nesipho sezinkomo eziyishumi.
Uvaleleke emhlanganweni neSilo isikhathi eside.
Umhlangano wabo wubuhanjelwe nangundunankulu kaZulu, uMntwana Mangosuthu Buthelezi.
Akukuningi akushilo emuva kwalo mhlangano uZuma.
"Uyinkosi yami.
Njengendoda yomZulu ngibone kubalulekile ukuthi ngizokotha iSilo," kushaya uZuma ngamafishane emuva komhlangano.
Ebuzwa ngokuxoxwe kulo mhlangano, uZuma unqabile ukuphumela obala.
Izolo bekungolunye usuku olumatasa eSilweni njengoba izivakashi ezahlukene beziphuma zingena esigodlweni.
Selokhu iSilo sibuyile eSwatini lapho besiyoqoqa khona izimpahla zaso njengoba bese sihlala khona, kusukela kwakhothama iSilo uGoodwill Zwelithini, baningi abantu abahlukene abafikayo esigodlweni.
Iningi labo lisuke lizozwakalisa ukweseka iSilo njengoba sisanda kuqokelwa esikhundlenni esikuso.
Udaba lokuqokwa kweSilo seluhlukanise phakathi indlunkulu njengoba kukhona abangeneme ngokuqokwa kweSilo.
Yize kunemizamo yokuthola isivimbelo senkantolo esivimba ukugcotshwa ngokusemthethweni kweSilo, indlunkulu iyaqhubeka namalungiselo.
Alukaziwa usuku okuzogcotshwa ngalo ngokusemthethweni iSilo njengoba kusalindelwe izimpendulo ezibuya kuhulumeni wesifundazwe nokazwelonke.
Zimkhalele  emngcwabeni ’wesigebengu’ owemoto eyebiwe
ZIMKHALELE esemngcwabeni wosolwa ngokuba isigebengu, owesilisa otholwe ehamba ngemoto entshontshiwe e-Springville, eHighflats.
Umsolwa oneminyaka engu-35 uzithele phezu kwamaphoyisa abeqaphe isimo ngeSonto njengoba bekungcwatshwa uMnuz Lucas Mazibuko, ongomunye wabayisikhombisa abadutshulwe ngamaphoyisa eScottsville, eMgungundlovu, ngeledlule.
Isolezwe lithole ukuthi amaphoyisa abetshaliwe ezindaweni ezehlukene kule mpelasonto lapho bekungcwatshwa khona abasolwa ngokwahlukana.
Abanye bafihlwe ngoMgqibelo, abanye bafihlwa ngeSonto.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uColonel Thembeka Mbele, uthe kuzobhekwa ukuthi umsolwa akathinteki yini kwamanye amacala obugebengu.
"Umsolwa uboshwe kade amaphoyisa eqaphe isimo emngcwabeni kaMazibuko.
UMazibuko obeyingxenye yeqembu lezigebengu owabulawa kade bedubulana namaphoyisa eMgungundlovu.
Umsolwa uboshwe ngeSonto ngabo-12.
45 etholwa nemoto entshontshiwe.
Ngokombiko wamaphoyisa, le moto kwabikwa ukuthi yebiwa ngo-Septhemba 13, 2020, emgwaqweni u-Percy Osborne, eMorningside.
"Umsolwa uboshelwe icala lokutholwa nemoto eyebiwe, kuzobhekwa ukuthi akazange yini athinteke kwamanye amacala enziwa eHighflats nasesifundazweni.
Umsolwa bekulindeleke ukuba avele enkantolo yasePhungashe namhlanje (izolo)," kusho uCol Mbele.
Umphumela wecala ubungakatholakali njengoba idokodo lisagcinwe enkantolo.
Khonamanjalo; izolo bekuvele nabasolwa abane ababoshiwe eMgungundlovu, ebekusolwa ukuthi nabo bayingxenye yabayisikhombisa ababulewe.
Idokodo lokuvelwa kwabo enkantolo yaseMgungundlovu lisagcinwe enkantolo.
Laba batholwe kwenye indawo eqashisayo behlome ngezibhamu.
Kuxoshwe isikhulu kuMasipala weTheku
IBHANTSHI ligcwale umoya eNhlokweni yophiko lwezamaPaki, ezokuNgcebeleka namaSiko kuMasipala weTheku, uMnuz Thembinkosi Ngcobo.
Izolo umasipala ukuqinisekisile ukuthi uNgcobo uxoshiwe njengoba etholwe necala lokungenzi kahle emsebenzini ngenxa yokuhluleka ukubika icala elenziwa wumsebenzi owakhokhela usomabhizinisi imali engu-R140 000 kungafanele.
Okhulumela umasipala, uMnuz Musawakhe Mayisela, ukuqinisekisile ukuxoshwa kwalesi sikhulu, wathi akekho osafakwe esikhaleni sakhe okwamanje.
"Singakuqinisekisa ukuthi lowo msebenzi okhuluma ngaye uxoshiwe.
Lokhu kwenzeke emuva kokuba kuphume isinqumo esigungwini esiqula amacala abasebenzi bakahulumeni.
Umqashi udaba waluyisa kulesi sigungu emuva kokuba kade kunecala elalifakwe kumasipala.
Isigungu sibe seseseka isinqumo sikamasipala.
Akekho osabekwe ukuba angene esikhundleni salo msebenzi oxoshiwe," kusho uMayisela.
Incwadi yalesi sigungu, esayinwe mhlaka 12 Juni nonyaka, engamakhasi angu-52, iveze ukuthi isinqumo ngaleli cala ukuthi uNgcobo ulahlwa icala, ukuxoshwa yisona sodwa isigwebo esimfanele ngakho-ke bayamxosha kuMasipala waseThekwini.
Ngokwecala alithwesiwe, kuthiwa uNgcobo wabikelwa wusomabhizinisi ukuthi wakhokhelwa u-R140 000 ngokungafanele ngomsebenzi abebethi wawenza wokuhlinzeka nge-sound system netende eliwubukhazikhazi nathe yinto angakaze ayenze.
UNgcobo kuthiwa lolu daba walunyathela ngezinyawo, wangalubika emaphoyiseni noma kwabaphenyayo kumasipala.
"Ngo-2015 wabikelwa umangalelwa (usomabhizinisi), ukuthi wakhokhelwa u-R140 000 kungafanele okwenziwa ngomunye wabasebenzi (igama lakhe), owayesebenza emnyangweni wakho.
Kwakumele lokhu ukubike emaphoyiseni nakulabo abalwisana nenkohlakalo.
Ukuhluleka kwakho ukwenza lokho waphula umthetho wesigaba 1,2,3 ngokuqondisa izigwegwe umsebenzi othi: kumele umsebenzi enze umsebenzi wakhe ngokuthembeka, ngokuzimisela nangawo wonke amandla akhe," kusho isinqumo sesigungu.
UNgcobo selokhu waqhoqhobala lesi sikhundla kusukela ngo-1999.
Icala beliqulwa ngo-Ephreli noMeyi.
Umcimbi weBeach Festival wawungo-Okthoba 2015.
Ummangali wathi akazange enze lutho kulo mcimbi kodwa wafonelwa kuthiwa akafake isicelo sokukhokhelwa ngezindleko zakhe.
Uthe ngempela wakwenza lokho wabe esekhokhelwa kungafanele.
Umsebenzi owayethe lo somabhizinisi akafake isicelo wabe esesula emsebenzini ngawo u-2015.
NgoMashi 2017 wabe eseqashwa futhi kumasipala kodwa komunye umnyango, waphinde wesula ngoFebhuwari 2018.
Omunye umsebenzi naye owayethinteka wasula, kwathi owesithathu umsebenzi, owayesolwa naye kuleli cala, washona.
UNgcobo ngokwakhe uthe wayengazi ukuthi ngo-2015 khona imali eyakhokhwa kungafanele.
Ngokwakhe, uthi wazi ngo-2018 sekuphenywa, waze waba nemininingwane egcwele ngo-2020 esebekwa icala.
Isolezwe lifonele uNgcobo izolo ngokuxoshwa kwakhe, ucingo lubanjwe ngowesifazane ongazange azidalule wathi umatasa.
"Uzobuyela kuwena, akakwazi ukukhuluma nocingo okwamanje, kukhona amatasa ngakho," kusho owesifazane.
UZikalala akaneme ngophenyo lwamacala abucayi
KAYIGCULISI indlela okulandelwa ngayo amacala abucayi, aphenywa ngamaphoyisa asiteshini saseHammarsdale eMpumalanga.
Lawa ngamazwi kaNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Sihle Zikalala, ofike kungazelele muntu izolo eyohlola ukusebenza kwalesi siteshi ngaphansi komkhankaso, i-Operation Siyahlola.
Ubephelezelwa nguNgqongqoshe wezokuThutha, ukuPhepha nokuXhumana koMphakathi, uNkk Peggy Nkonyeni noKhomishana wamaPhoyisa esifundazweni uLieutenant General Nhlanhla Mkhwanazi.
UZikalala uthe isiteshi saseHammarsdale singesinye abakhathazekile ngaso KwaZulu-Natal, kuhlanganisa esaseNanda, eMlaza, ePlessislaer nezinye.
"Kule ndawo yaseHammarsdale namaphethelo izinga lobugebengu liphezulu, ukubulawa kwabantu kuphezulu, ukudlwengula nokuhlaselwa kwabantu kuphezulu.
Indlela okulandelwa ngayo la macala kayenelisi neze," kusho uZikalala.
Uthe bavumelene ngemuva kwalokhu kuhlola ukuthi uNkk Nkonyeni nomnyango babuke wonke amadodoko, ikakhulukazi lawo athinta awokubulala, ukudlwengula nokushaya ukuthi ahamba kanjani.
"Sifuna ukutholaukuthi yingani liphansi izinga lokuboshwa kwabantu.
Yingani ekugcineni kungekho abantu okutholakala ukuthi bayagwetshwa," kusho uZikalala.
Uthe useke waya eMgugundlovu wayohlola izinhlelo zokwakhiwa kwezindlu eMsunduzi nasesiteshini samaphoyisa KwaHlabisa nasemtholampilo wakhona.
Uthe izolo bebeseMpumalanga, beyohlola indlela okusebenza ngayo isiteshi namaphoyisa aso.
Nakuba enelisekile ngesibalo samaphoyisa akhona kulesi siteshi, kodwa ukhala ngokuntuleka kwezinsiza ezidingekayo ukuze kwenziwe umsebenzi ngempumelelo, kubalwa nokushoda kwezimoto.
Kushubile ubabezala ejola nomakoti
NKOSIKHONA CELEIDIDEKILE futhi ithi idunyelwa yikhanda indodana ethole ukuthi uyise oyizalayo uthandana nomakoti wayo isinyelela.
UMnuz Sifiso Khumalo (36) waseNquthu uthi uzizwa sengathi ulele uyaphupha, mhlawumbe usazophaphama.
Uma echaza, uthi ushade noNksz Zinhle Sibisi (32) eminyakeni emibili eyedlule.
Uthi uyise omzalayo, uMnuz Themba Khumalo (58), wayejabule kuhle okwengane ibona amaswidi ngesikhathi ziwushaya phakathi kwakhe nomakoti wakhe.
Emshadweni uthi uyise wayegiya aze amhashe ngezibongelo zakhe, aphinde adanse.
Uthi uyise wamxhasa ngesamba esikhulu semali ngesikhathi eyolobola umkakhe.
Uthi useyabona manje ukuthi uyise wayezilobolela yena futhi nangesikhathi egiya wayejatshuliswa ukuthi ""usenentombi.
""Utshele iSolezwe NgoMgqibelo ukuthi uyise nomakoti wakhe bangamathe nolimi.
Uthi ubengakaze acabanga ukuthi uyise angagila le migilingwane athi ihlasimulisa umzimba.
Uthi umngani wakhe wamtshela ukuthi makavule amehlo, kukhona okudla amantshontsho emsamo.
"Ngikhuluma nawe nje kasisazwani nhlobo nomngani wami.
Sibanga ukuthi wangitshela ngokujola kukababa nomkami, ethi mangivule amehlo kukhona okushaya amanzi," echaza.
Uthi indlela abaxabana ngayo nomngani wakhe, isandla sakhe saze saphunyuka wamgingqa phansi ngequpha.
Uthi umngani wakhe akazange aphindisele kodwa kunalokho wamshiya namazwi ayethi: " Kulungile mngani wami kodwa ngelinye ilanga uyongikhumbula.
"Uthi ukuze athole ukuthi uyise uthandana nomkakhe, uhletshelwe ngomunye wasendaweni.
Uthi wamshayela ucingo ethi akazobona uyise eqabulana nomkakhe endaweni ebuqamama nakubo.
Uthi ekubeni yena ubazi ukuthi uZinhle uye edolobheni.
Uthi akazange apholise maseko, ushaye imoto yalibangisa kuleyo ndawo.
Uthi kuthe uma efika wazibonela ngawakhe uyise enkonkoshelene umakoti wakhe emotweni.
"Ngibabuzile ukuthi yini lena abayenzayo.
Akekho phakathi kwabo ongiphendulile.
Kunalokho umakoti wami uvele wakhihla isililo, wacela uxolo.
Ubaba yena uvele wangigqolozela nje kwaba sengathi uhanjelwa yingqondo, " echaza.
ISolezwe NgoMgqibelo likhulume naye uZinhle ovele wakhihla isililo wacela uxolo entathelini.
"Ngiyaxolisa bandla bhuti nami angazi ukuthi lento yenzeke kanjani.
Ngiyazisola kakhulu.
Ngiyacela bandla ungalubhali lolu daba, " usho kanje.
Ngemuva kwesikhathi esingangehora intatheli ikhulumile noZinhle, ibe seyithinta uMnuz Khumalo okhwele wadilika entathelini eyibuza ukuthi igunyazwe ngubani ukuthi ibhale ngomndeni wayo ephepheni.
Usabise ngokuthi uma intatheli ike yabhala nje ngalolu daba izowukhomba onotshwala. "
Mfana wami, senajwayela labo okuthiwa bayazesaba izintatheli, mina angikwesabi futhi angikwenqeni.
Qhubeka-ke nalo doti womsangano owuqalayo, uzongibona kahle.
Angiyona mina into yokudlala wena.
Kuhle ngoba ngiyalizwa nephimbo lakho ukuthi uyibhobhodleyana nje lomfana, angeke umelane nami, " usho kanje egaklaza phansi ucingo.
ISolezwe NgoMgqibelo litholile ukuthi uMnuz Khumalo ugila le mikhuba nje ngo-2017 kwashona umkakhe, uNkk Nomaswazi Khumalo (umaGumede) exinwe yisifo sikashukela.
Kuyavela nokuthi uMnuz Khumalo wayekade esembonini yamatekisi kodwa ngemuva kokushona komkakhe wathatha isinqumo sokushenxa.
ISolezwe NgoMgqibelo litholile ukuthi uZinhle usekhona kwaKhumalo.
UMnuz Khumalo kuthiwa uke wazama ukuxolisa endodaneni yakhe ngesamba semali engu-R50 000 kodwa indodana yenqaba.
Inkantolo izofuna izizathu zokuhoxa kwabakaZuma
ABAMELI bowayengumengameli wakuleli kumele bachazele inkantolo enkulu yaseMgungundlovu namuhla ukuthi kungani bethathe isinqumo sokuthi bahoxe ekumeleni uMnuz Jacob Zuma ecaleni lenkohlakalo abhekene nalo.
Ummeli uMnuz Mpumelelo Zikalala ekhuluma neNewzroom Afrika izolo, uthe inkantolo izodinga ukwazi izizathu zokuthi kungani abameli benqume ukuhoxa.
Uma kuyizizathu ezithinta imali, inkantolo izofuna ukwazi ukuthi ngabe lokhu kwenzeke ngaphambi kokuthi beze enkantolo lapho kwavunyelwana khona ukuthi konke sekumi ngomumo ngecala noma emuva kwalokho.
Uthe uma kuwukuthi lesi sinqumo sithathwe emuva kokuthi abameli nenkantolo bavumelana ngokuthi konke sekumi ngomumo inkantolo ingakuphikisa ukuhoxa kwabameli ngenxa yokuthi umthetho iLegal Practitioners Act nemigomo yokuziphatha kwabameli ayikuvumeli ukuthi kube khona okuzophazamisa ukushesha kokuqulwa kwecala, inkantolo ingabanxusa abameli ukuthi baqhubeke uma isizathu kungesemali kuphela.
Uthe kodwa uma kuwukuthi kukhona esinye isizathu okungaba esokuthi ababoni ngaso linye nabamumele okungenza ukuthi bangabe besakwazi ukumumela ngendlela efanele inkantolo izobe isibuza uZuma ukuthi unabo yini abanye abameli abangamumela.
UZikalala uthe kubalulekile ukuthi inkantolo ithole izizathu zokuhoxa kwabameli isebenzisa uhlelo lokuthola izizathu kummeli ngaphansi kukaSection 342A weCriminal Procedure Act, ngoba ibisibeke isikhathi eside ukuze kuqale ukuqulwa kwaleli cala.
Inkantolo ifuna ukwazi ukuthi izizathu ziyabambeka yini ngoba ibinganika ijaji elizokwengamela icala elinye icala ukuthi ilenze ngalesi sikhathi noma inike abameli esinye isikhathi sokuthi ixazulule inkinga ekhona phakathi kwabo nabamumele.
Uthisha umiselwe 'ukufafaza' amanga
UMISIWE emsebenzini wuMnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal uthisha owahlaba ikhwelo ngokudla athi kubolile, okuthiwa kuphekelwa abafundi esikoleni samabanga aphakeme, iZiphembeleni, eNanda.
UMnuz Sicelo Bhengu, obuye abe wumengameli wenyunyana yothisha i- Educators Union of South Africa (EUSA), ngenyanga edlule ufake ekhasini lakhe leTwitter i-video ngokudla okubolile okuthiwa kunikezwa abafundi kulesi sikole.
Kwi-video unamathelisa igama likaNgqonggqoshe wezeMfundo esifundazweni, uMnuz Kwazi Mshengu.
Lokhu kuphoqe umnyango ukuthi uqale uphenyo.
Esitatimendeni esikhishwe wumnyango ngoMsombuluko, sigxeka uBhengu ngokufafaza amanga ngalolu daba.
Siveza ukuthi uphenyo olwenziwe luthole ukuthi lolu daba lungamampunge.
Lokhu kuholele ekutheni izolo, umnyango umnike incwadi yokumiswa kwakhe emsebenzini.
Okhulumela umnyango, uMnuz Muzi Mahlambi ukuqinisekisile ukumiswa kwakhe.
Ngesikhathi Isolezwe lithinta uBhengu, uthe usamile ekutheni ukudla okuphekelwa izingane esikoleni afundisa kuso kubolile.
"Ukubhala ekhasini lami leTwitter ngibhale njengomengameli wenyunyana yothisha, kangibhalanga njengothisha.
Uma umnyango ubuzimisele ukuthola iqiniso ngalolu daba, kungani ungajubanga ithimba labaphenyi abazimele esikhundleni sokuthi uthumele izikhulu zomnyango?"
kubuza uBhengu.Usole ithimba ebelithunywe esikoleni ngokuchema nothishomkhulu, athe naye uwumngani omkhulu womuntu ophakela ukudla khona esikoleni.
Uthe izingane ezalandwa ukuyofakaza ngokudla okudliwa esikoleni, zazilandwa nguthishomkhulu.
Uthe maningi amathuba okuthi wazisabisa.
Uthe unayo i-video lapho ezinye izingane zifakaza ngalolu daba ukuthi luyiqiniso (ayithumele Isolezwe).
Encwadini yokumiswa kwakhe, Isolezwe elinayo ikhophi yayo, kuvela ukuthi umiselwe ukufafaza ulwazi olungesilo iqiniso, olufaka umnyango ehlazweni.
Kubuye kuvele ukuthi usoleka ngokusabisa abafundi ababehlonywa ngemibuzo ngesikhathi kuqhubeka uphenyo, ukungalandeli imiyalelo kathishomkhulu nokumsabisa yena namalungu esigungu esilawula isikole.
Umiswe izinyanga ezintathu zilandelana ehola, noma kuze kuphothulwa ukulalelwa kwecala abekwe lona.
UMahlambi uveze ukuthi uBhengu usolwa ngokufunza abafundi ipolitiki, kodwa uBhengu ukuphikile lokhu.
Esitatimendeni somnyango kuvela ukuthi ubeseke wamiswa phambilini, kodwa uBhengu uveze ukuthi ukumiswa kwakhe phambilini kwakumayelana nokuthi waqhumbusa ithumba ngemali enguR170 000 okwakusolwa uthishomkhulu walesi sikole waphambilini, okuthe ngokuqhubeka kwesikhathi kwatholakala ukuthi akuveza kuyiqiniso, uthishomkhulu waxoshwa yena, uBhengu wabuyiselwa emsebenzini.
I-ANC igxeke abahlukanisa inhlangano
IKOMITI elibhekele ukusebenza kwansuku zonke le-ANC, ligxeke izinkulumo zabaholi ababeyoseka owayengumengameli we-ANC nezwe uMnuz Jacob Zuma, ngesikhathi evela enkantolo yaseMgungundlovu ngamacala enkohlakalo ngeledlule.
UNksz Jessie Duarte, iPhini likaNobhala Jikelele le-ANC, ligxeke uNobhala Jikelele wale nhlangano osamisiwe, uMnuz Ace Magashule, ilungu lesigungu esiphezulu uMnuz Tony Yengeni noMnuz Carl Niehaus womakadebona be-ANC, ngezinkulumo zabo athe zihlukanisa inhlangano.
"Ikomiti iNational Working Commitee (NWC) ligxeke izinkulumo zalaba baholi ezinenhlese yokuhlukanisa inhlangano ngesikhathi kuvela uZuma enkantolo.
Siyalele iNational Presenter kwi-ANC ukuthi ibheke lokhu kuphulwa kwemigomo kwalaba baholi, bese iphenya ukuthi yimaphi amacala abangabekwa wona kulandelwa umthethosisekelo we-ANC," kusho uNksz Duarte.
Laba baholi bathi kabayi ndawo futhi ngeke basatshiswe ngokuthi baseka uMagashule, bazoqhubeka bameseke.
Kwenzeka lokhu nje uZuma ubuyele enkantolo namhlanje njengoba kulalelwa isicelo esifakwe ngabameli bakhe, sokuthi kuhoxe uMshushisi u-Advocate Billy Downer SC.
Uthe ukhulumile noMagashule, wathi ukuhoxisile ukuthi bazoza neningi uma sebeseka uZuma namhlanje.
UMagashule wathi uzofika nabo bonke abantu baseFree State uma uZuma esevela enkantolo.
UNksz Duarte uthe iNWC yeseke isicelo senkantolo sokuthi kuphikiswe isicelo sikaMagashule, sokuthi kubekwe eceleni ukumiswa kwakhe kwi-ANC.
UNksz Duarte umemezele ukuthi anikwe kuze kube wuJuni 15, amagatsha e-ANC ukuthi abe nemihlangano.
Uyalele ukuthi kuqokwe amalungu amane kule mihlangano, azophakanyiselwa ekutheni abe ngamakhansela njengoba kubhekwe okhethweni lohulumeni basekhaya.
Uthe la malungu kumele kube ngabesilisa ababili nabesifazane ababili.
Uqhube wathi kumele kube nokulingana uma kuqokwa amalungu, umuntu ozothola amavoti amaningi nguyena ozodla umhlanganiso.
"Sizogxila entsheni, isipiliyoni naso sibalulekile yingakho sithi kasifuni ukuthi abantu abadala nabo banganikwa indawo yabo."
Uthe ngenxa yemigomo elawula izwe njengoba kuneCovid-19, cishe bazoba ngu-250 abantu abazohambela imihlangano yamagatsha.
Kuminze iphoyisa lidoba olwandle
KUMINZE iphoyisa likaMasipala weTheku ngesikhathi beyodoba olwandle iWestbrook ngasoThongathi izolo ekuseni.
Kuthiwa u-Inspector Anthony Pattison (54) ubengekho emsebenzini ezikhiphele olwandle nomngani wakhe beyodoba ngesikhathi kwenzeka lesi sehlo.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa alomkhandlu, uSenior Superintendent Parboo Sewpersad uthe isehlakalo senzeke ngemva kuka-7 ekuseni.
Ulandise wathi umufi ubesophikweni lwebhendi kamasipala eviliyela uma kunemicimbi nemingcwabo obekuthi uma engekho emsebenzini enze izinto eziningi zokuzijabulisa okubalwa nakho ukudoba.
"Uye nomngani wakhe olwandle kanti uzobona isikhuphashe (crayfish) edoba wasigxumela.
Uhlangabezane nobunzima ngenkathi etshuza, wayesephela emehlweni," kusho uSewpersad.
Uqhube wathi umngani kaPattison uzamile ukumfuna emanzini wangamthola waphuma wahlaba umkhosi.
Kuthiwa ubuyelile esehamba nabatakuli namaphoyisa atshuzayo.
"Bamtholile bamkhiphela ngaphandle kwamanzi.
Amaphoyisa nabosizo lokuqala bazame konke okusemandleni abo ukuhlenga impilo yakhe kwanhlanga zimuka nomoya.
Uhlonzwe njengoshonele endaweni yesehlo," kusho uSewpersad.
USewpersad udlulise amazwi enduduzo emndenini, kubangani nasembuthweni wamaphoyisa kamasipala wathi ibuhlungu into ebehlele.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal uColonel Thembeka Mbele, uthe kuvulwe idokodo ngokufa komuntu eliphenywayo mayelana nalesi sehlakalo.
Kwesinye isehlakalo, kulimale kabi iphoyisa lomgwaqo elishayiswe yimoto emgwaqweni onguthelawayeka uN2 ngaseProspecton eThekwini izolo ekuseni.
Abezimo eziphuthumayo kwaNetcare 911 babizelwe kule ndawo ebudebuduze nesikhumulo sezindiza esidala bafica iphoyisa lilele phansi.
Kuphazamiseke ukuhamba kwezimoto njengoba kudingeke ukuba ivalwe isikhashana imizila kuhlengwa iphoyisa.
Okhulumela abakwaNetcare 911, uShawn Herbst uthe lilimale kabi iphoyisa.
Uqhube ngokuthi kudingeke ukuthi babize indiza enophephela emhlane ephuthumise iphoyisa esibhedlela.
Uveze nokuthi umshayeli wemoto eshayise iphoyisa akabalekanga kodwa uthathwe amaphoyisa.
Kushiswe iveni yamaphoyisa kubhikishwa
KUNGQONGQISWE iveni yamaphoyisa kaMasipala weTheku neveni yophiko lwezamanzi ngesikhathi umphakathi obuwotha ubomvu ubhikishela ukungabi bikhona kwamanzi eMvini KwaXimba, ngeSonto ebusuku.
Kujikijelwe amaphoyisa ngamatshe kwajikiswa nogandaganda obubizwe ikhansela lendawo ukuba uzomba kulungiswe inkinga yamanzi lomphakathi okhala ngawo.
Nayizolo besimazonzo isimo kule ndawo, abafundi nabasebenzi behleli emakhaya, kuvalwe izintuba ezingenayo neziphuma, kusetshenziswa amatshe, imfucuza kadoti namathayi avuthayo.
Bathi isibami emphinjeni indaba yokuntula amanzi, osekunezinyanga eziyisithupha kwenzeka.
Bakhale nangokuthi balethelwa amanzi ngamaloli afika ngesikhathi besemsebenzini noma ebusuku sebelele.
Laba bantu bathi kwawona amanzi abalethelwa wona kawekho esimweni esigculisayo.
Bakhala ngokuthi kukhona abaguliswa yila manzi.
"Yimeya kuphela noma yisikhulu ophikweni lwamanzi esizobalalela uma bekhuluma manje.
Sizame sahluleka ukuxoxa nekhansela ngale nkinga kodwa kasisizakalanga," kusho ilungu lomphakathi elingathandanga ukudalulwa.
Ikhansela lale ndawo eku-ward 1 kuMasipala weTheku, uMnuz Bongumusa Mkhize, lithe inkinga yamanzi kakuyona eyaseMvini kuphela.
Uthe eMvini amanzi ayaba khona abuye anqamuke, okuyinto esiyenzeke izinyanga ezintathu.
UMkhize uthe bahlele ukuba nomhlangano womphakathi kusasa ngo-2 emini.
"Akuyona indlela yokulungisa izinto lena abayenzile, beshisa izimoto.
Inkinga yamanzi ikhungethe iTheku lonke ngoba abantu bayanda emiphakathini, ingqalasizinda isindala idinga ukulungiswa futhi kayanele imali yokubhekana nenkinga yamanzi," kusho uMkhize.
Uthe uhlezi exhumana nomphakathi nezinhlaka ezehlukene eziwumele ngakho uyamangala ngoba umbhikisho uqale esanda kuxoxa ehhovisi lakhe nabantu abanolwazi ngezinhlelo zamanzi kule ndwo.
"Yisimo esingasazi, esingajwayelekile futhi esingamukelekile le nto eyenzeka eMvini.
Laba bantu bashise izimoto, balimaza umgwaqo.
Kuvinjwa abasebenzi bophiko lwamanzi uma bezosebenza, bayathukwa basatshiswe emafonini.
Akudedelwe abantu benze umsebenzi wokulungisa inkinga yamanzi," kusho uMkhize.
IMeya yeTheku uMnuz Mxolisi Kaunda ikugxekile ukuthungelwa ngomlilo kwezimoto zomkhandlu.
Unxenxe amaphoyisa ukuba aphenyisise khona kuzoboshwa abantu abathinteka kulesi sehlakalo athe kasinangqondo.
Uthe isehlakalo senzeke ngesikhathi abophiko lwezamanzi nokuthuthwa kwendle bekule ndawo, bezama ukulungisa inkinga yamanzi.
"NgoMashi kwadingeka ukuthi amaphoyisa ayokhulula abasebenzi bakamasipala ababevinjezelwe wumphakathi.
Sicela amalungu omphakathi ukuthi ahlukane nokuzimbandakanya nodlame uma enenkinga ngokulethelwa izidingo zawo," kusho uKaunda.
Uthe akukhona okokuqala kwenzeka isigameko esifuze lesi futhi bakhathazekile.
Ubuze ukuthi kuzosizangani ukuthungela ngomlilo imoto kamasipala?Ucele umphakathi ukuthi ubabekezelele njengoba besebenza ngokuzikhandla belungisa inkinga yamanzi ekhungethe umphakathi.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala uthe kuvulwe icala lokususa udlame emphakathini, eliphenywa ngamaphoyisa asesiteshini uMsunduzi.
Uthe iqulu labantu abangu-300 ebelingalawuleki livale imigwaqo ngamathayi avuthayo, kwashiswa nezimoto ezimbili.
Uthe bajikijele amaphoyisa ngamatshe.
"Akukho muntu olimalile futhi amaphoyisa akhona asiqaphe ngeso lokhozi isimo kule ndawo," kusho uCapt Gwala.Ngesikhatho sokuloba udaba imigwaqo yakule ndawo ibisavaliwe izolo emini
Udide odokotela                   ezala-10 wezingane
UQOPHE umlando owesifazane ebeletha izingane ezingamawele ezingu-10 esibhedlela esiseTshwane, eGauteng, ngoMsombuluko ebusuku.
UNksz Gosiame Thamara Sithole (37), wase-Tembisa, Ekurhuleni, ubelethe izingane zabafana eziyisikhombisa namantombazane amathathu.
Lo wesifazane ohlinzwe kungakafiki isikhathi sokubeletha, kuthiwa uphule irekhodi le-Guinness World Record, ebeliphethwe ngu-Nkk Malian Halima Cissé waseMorocco, yena obelethe izingane eziyisishiyagalolunye ngenyanga edlule.
Isolezwe lithinta udokotela wabesifazane, uDkt.
Dumisani Zungu, uthe into engajwayelekile lena eyenzekile.
"Into eyivela kancane kakhulu lena evelile.
Kuba yisimo esinzima ukubhekana naso kowesifazane osuke ezithwele.
Kuphela ngisho nendawo esiswini njengoba izingane ziningi kangaka.
Into enkulu, isibeletho sisheshe sikhathale, singalindi izinyanga eziyisishiyagalolunye.
Ingane ibe isiba nesimo esinzima uma iphuma kungakashayi isikhathi.
Kuzodinga izinto ezisezingeni eliphezulu ukugcina izingane ziphilile.
Nangendlela yokugcina izingane kuzoba nezinselelo.
"Akuwona umthwalo omncane, kuzoba nezinkinga eziningi njengoba izingane ziphume kungakashayi isikhathi," kusho uDkt Zungu.
Uthe uma izingane ziphezu kwezimbili noma ezintathu kusuke sekumele owesifazane abelethe ngokuhlinzwa.
Uthe ukwanda kwenzingane kuyenziwa uhlelo lokukhulelwa kusetshinziswa ubucwepheshe i-In vitro fertilization (IVF).
"Kungaba i-In vitro fertilization (IVF) engenza izingane zibe ningi kangaka, ayikho indlela yokuchatha nokugeqa engenza ukuba izingane zibe ningi kangaka.
Ngaphandle kwalokhu, kuba yimvelo nje," kusho uDkt Zungu.
Ephetha uthe: "Isibusiso ukuthola izingane ngalolu hlobo.
Sidinga idolo (ukuthandaza), ukuba ahambe ibanga elingaka izingane zize ziphume.
Bese ziyaphila.
"Odokotela babetshele lo wesifazane ukuthi uzithwele izingane ziyisithupha, kwabuye kwatholakala ukuthi ziyisishiyagalombili, njengoba bekukhona ezimbili ezazigaxele endaweni engafanele.
Esebeletha kube isimanga esethola ukuthi zingu-10 izingane.
Umyeni walo wesifazane, uMnuz Teboho Tsotetsi, uveze ukuthi bajabule kakhulu ngokubavelele.
UNksz Sithole kuvele ukuthi unamawele aneminyaka eyisithupha, awathola ngaphambilini.
Ekhuluma nephepha elinguzakwabo weSolezwe i-Pretoria News, ngoMsombuluko ebusuku uTsotetsi, uthe uThamara ubelethe enamasonto angu-29 ezithwele.
"Abafana abayisikhombisa namantombazane amathathu.
Ubenezinyanga eziyisikhombisa ezithwele, nezinsuku eziyisikhombisa.
Angikwazi nokukhuluma nje, ubuye ungithinte," kusho uTsotetsi.
Lezi zithandani kuke kwakhulunywa nazo ngenyanga edlule kodwa zacela ukuba udaba lungashicilelwa ngenxa yosiko nokusabela izingane.
Ngazizwa sengathi uNkulunkulu ungikhethile.
Kuyisibusiso ukuba nginikwe izingane ezingaka, abantu abaningi bayazifisa izingane.
Kuyisimangaliso, engisijabulelayo.
Ngaze ngaya kosesha ukuthi ngempela umuntu uyakwazi yini ukubeletha izingane ezingaka ezingaka.
Bekuyinto entsha.
Bengazi ngamawele, amathathu, ngisho namane kodwa hhayi lokhu.
Kuthe sengithola ukuthi into eyenzekayo sengibona nemibiko kadokotela, ngajabula kakhulu.
Sengijahe ukubagona," kusho uTsotetsi.
Ezinkundleni zokuxhumana abantu bebejabulela lezi zithandani ngesimanga esingaka.
Abanye bebethi bona bangaphisana ngazo, abanye bethi bangazigcina zonke.
Abanye belibeka ngembaba ukuthi bangakhihla isililo nje uma into efana nalena ibavelela.
Kwizinkundla zokuxhumana bebesho ukuthi bekumele kube ne- National baby shower, benikezwe izipho.
Lokhu kuvele ukuthi kuphakanyiswe owayengumholi kwi-DA uNksz Lindiwe Mazibuko.
Lokhu kube sekugcwala izinkundla zokuxhumana kuswekwa abanye abantu.
Abanye bephakamisa ukuba kusizwe lomndeni, ngokondla lezi zingane.
Bebodwa abazibophezele ukuba beseke lezi zithandani ngamanabukeni nezinye izinto ezizodingwa izingane.
Indida kunyamalala ingoduso ngosuku lomembeso
USEPHENDUKE ihlaya owesilisa waseMagabheni, ngemva kokubhuntsha kwezinhlelo zokuthi ayocela, ambese futhi kumule ingoduso yakhe enyamalale yaze yabuya ngoMgqibelo ebusuku, abantu sebehlanze ngedela.
UMnuz Thanduxolo "Maqa" Mjodi, ongumnikazi weMaqa's Place, okuyindawo yobumnandi eseMagabheni, ukhala uyazithulisa ngemali yakhe echithekile elungisela umicimbi egcine ingenzekanga ngempelasonto edlule.
Elandisa Isolezwe ngeSonto, uthe kwaphoqeleka ukuthi kudliwe Ingasenzekanga imicimbi ebihleliwe emuva kokunyamalala kwengoduso ngoLwesihlanu, yaze yabuya sekuhlwile ngakusasa.
"Ucingo lokuqala ngaluthola ngoLwesihlanu ngifonelwa ngabantu engingabazi bethi kumele ngikhiphe uR100 000 ukuze bangibuyisele umakoti wami.
Kwaqala lapho ukuphithana ikhanda ngoba ngangingasazi ukuthi ngizokwenzenjani," kuchaza uMaqa.
Uthe waqhubeka wayolanda inkomo, iziklabhu nembuzi ngoba wayesanethemba lokuthi uzoqhubeka umcimbi.
Uveze ukuthi ithawula uze waliphonsa ngemuva kokukhuluma nesithandwa sakhe ocingweni, lapho esimtshela khona ukuthi sithunjwe ngabantu abathathu futhi sebesiphuzise notshwala.
Uthe besimnxenxa ukuthi ayihlanganise imali ngokushesha.
"Kwaze kwasa engabuyile, lacishe lashona ilanga sekucaca ukuthi kuzohlwa abantu bengadlile ngoba kwase kusobala ukuthi kawusekho umcimbi.
Sathatha isinqumo sokuthi sizihlabe iziklabhu ukuze kudliwe nami ngazigqokela isudi yami engangizohloba ngayo," usho kanje.
UMaqa nesithandwa sakhe abese benonyaka bethandana naso basaqhubeka nokuxhumana ngocingo njengoba leli phephandaba liyibonile imiyalezo abebethumelana yona.
Inkomo nembuzi obekuzohlatshelwa emcimbini bekusekhona ngesikhathi ithimba lezintatheli lihambele khona.
Ngisho ikhekhe lomcimbi belingakasikwa.
Unina kaMaqa, uNkk Sibongile Mjodi, uthe abasazi bona lesi simanga abasenzelwe ngumakoti enyamalala ngomzuzu wokugcina.
"Ngiphelelwe ngamandla, ngagula uma sengizwa ukuthi umakoti usenyamalele ekubeni kwase kufike zonke izihlobo, ngisho ezisuka eKapa zizomzimazisa.
Selokhu ngazalwa bengingakaze ngiyizwe into efana nale, eyehlele indodana yami," kubalisa uNkk Mjodi.
Ebuzwa ngesigameko uNksz Lungile Cele (ingoduso) ongowakhona endaweni, uthe ulivulile icala kodwa bebengakamthumeleli inamba yecala.
"Ngisathuthumela ngokungehlele.
Angikakabi sesimweni sokukhuluma.
Kuthe uma exinwe ngeminye imibuzo, wathi: "Ngangingeke ngisho kodwa kusenesikhathi uma ngingafuni ukuthi angicele.
Ibihlungu le nto yokuthi angikholakali ekubeni la madoda ayengithumbile ayelokhu ebuza ngezingane zami.
"Ubebonakala ebusweni uMaqa ukuthi inhliziyo igaya izibozi njengoba ebelokhu ekhale njalo ngemali yakhe emlahlekele.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe uthe akukho akutholayo mayelana nalolu daba.
Kuphenywa ngokubulawa kwephoyisa
OKLEBE baphenya icala lokubulawa kwephoyisa lesifazane elineminyaka engu-25, okuthiwa lidutshulwe ngumlisa ongaziwa ngoLwesihlanu, kwa- E, eMlaza.
Kuthiwa iphoyisa elinguConstable Portia Mhlanga, belisebenzela esiteshini esikuleli lokishi.
Beliselivini ngenkathi lihlaselwa.
Kubikwa ukuthi kuqhamuke umsolwa obhekise isibhamu ngakulo, lisalinde isoka lalo emotweni.
Umsolwa kubikwa ukuthi udubule amahlandla amahlanu, maqede wanyamalala emehlweni.
UCaptain Simphiwe Mhlongo, okhulumela oKlebe, uthe ithimba lophiko lobugebengu obuhleliwe eThekwini, limatasa nophenyo lokubulawa kwephoyisa.
"Imbangela yokubulawa kwalo ayikaziwa.
Akukaboshwa muntu," kubeka uCapt Mhlongo.
Umufi ubelinde isoka lakhe ebelisangene endaweni yokudla ekuleli lokishi, Ebenvilla ngenkathi kugasela umsolwa okuthiwa umdubule kwesingenhla emzimbeni.
Amaphoyisa kubikwa ukuthi athole izinhlamvu ezine endaweni yesigameko.
Kuthiwa umufi, ushone esesibhedlela, iPrince Mshiyeni Memorial.
I-NSFAS ichithe izitshudeni ezingu-96 000 ezifeyilile
ZINGAPHEZU kuka-140 000 izitshudeni ezichithwe yisikhwama esixhasa ngezimali zokufunda, iNational Student Financial Aid Scheme (NSFAS), ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme kulo nyaka wezimali.
Lokhu kuvezwe nguMnuz Ishmael Mnisi, okhulumela uMnyango weMfundo ePhakeme, othi ezingu-93 532 bezizofunda emakolishi amakhono, amaTechnical Vocational Education and Training (TVET).
Uthe u-52 992 ubufunda emanyuvesi.
"Izitshudeni ezingu-5 376 zasemaTVET azixhaswanga ngoba iziqu ebezizenza azikho ohlwini lwezixhaswayo.
Ezingu-22 014 zasemanyuvesi azixhaswanga ngoba vele sezinazo iziqu zokuqala," usho kanje.
Uthe ezinye izitshudeni ezingu-88 016 zasemaTVET nezingu-8 326 zasemanyuvesi azixhaswanga ngoba zifeyile unyaka odlule.
"Izitshudeni ezingu-13 zasemanyuvesi asizixhasanga ngoba zixhaswe ngeminye imifundaze.
I-NSFAS ixhasa abadinga usizo ngoba beqhamuka emindenini entulayo futhi abenza kahle ezifundweni zabo," kusho uMnisi.
Uthe baxhasa izitshudeni ukuthi zithole iziqu zokuqala ezikhungweni zemfundo.
Lesi sikhwama sixhaswe ngo-R35.
457 billion kulo nyaka wezimali.
Babalelwa ku-779 017 abafaka izicelo zoxhaso kulo nyaka, u-67% wabafake izicelo abathola isondlo sabantwana.
Lesi sikhwama sihlose ukuxhasa izitshudeni ezibalelwa esigidini emanyuvesi nesigidi emakolishi.
UMnisi uthe uNgqongqoshe walo mnyango, uDkt Blade Nzimande, unxuse izitshudeni ukuthi ziyifunde imigomo ethinta uxhaso ukuze zingazitholi sezichithwa ekutheni zithole uxhaso.
"UNzimande unxuse iNSFAS nezikhungo ukuthi ziqhubeke zixoxe nezinhlangano ezifana neSouth African National Student Union kanjalo nayo yonke imikhandlu yezitshudeni ukuze singandi isibalo sezitshudeni ezingaxhasiwe," kusho uMnisi.
Uthe umnyango uzoqhubeka nokusiza labo abafuna ukufunda ezikhungweni zemfundo ngohlelo lweKhetha ukuze bakhethe iziqu abazozenza.
I-ANC inqumele uMagashule ugwayi katiki
UNOBHALA Jikelele we-ANC osamisiwe emsebenzini, uMnuz Ace Magashule, usenqunyelwe ugwayi katiki ukuba axolise ngokubhala incwadi yokumisa uMengameli wale nhlangano, uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa.
Umhlangano wesigungu esiphezulu osongwe izolo, unikeze uMagashule isikhathi esingadalulwanga ukuba axolise ngokubhala leyo ncwadi noma abhekana nokuqondiswa ubugwegwe.
Lokhu kuvezwe nguRamaphosa obethula inkulumo yokuvala umhlangano wezinsuku ezintathu wesigungu esiphezulu, izolo.
URamaphosa uthe uMagashule wayengenalo igunya lokubhala incwadi.
"Umhlangano wesigungu esiphezulu uvumelene ngokuthi indlela aziphathe ngayo uNobhala Jikelele (osamisiwe), kayamukelekile futhi ingukuphula imithetho ye-ANC.
Uma ehluleka ukuxolisa kulesi sikhathi asibekelwe, i-ANC izomthathela izinyathelo zokumqondisa ubugwegwe ngokulandela umthethosisekelo wenhlangano.
"UMagashule wayibhala le ncwadi emuva kokuba kuputshuke incwadi emmisa emsebenzini we-ANC.
UMagashule wamiswa emsebenzini emuva kokuba kuphele umnqamulajuqu wezinsuku ezingu-30, ayezinikeziwe nabanye abaholi be-ANC, ababhekene namacala, ukuba bashenxe ezikhundleni abakuzo .
UMagashule ubhekene necala lenkohlakalo, elithinta ithenda kaR230 million yokushintshwa kophahla lwezindlu ezifulelwe ngetsheboya eFree State.
Ithenda yakhishwa ngesikhathi esengundunankulu kulesiya sifundazwe.
URamaphosa uthe njengoba uMagashule esamisiwe emsebenzini, akanalo ilungelo lokwenza umsebenzi wenhlangano noma ukumela i-ANC, ukukhuluma izindaba ezithinta iqembu noma ukukhuluma emihlanganweni yabalandeli beqembu.
URamaphosa uthe njengoba uMagashule esamisiwe emsebenzini, iPhini likaNobhala Jikelele, uNksz Jessie Duarte, yilona elizobamba esikhundleni sikaMagashule.
Ukugxekile ukuhlaselwa kukaNksz Duarte nabanye abasebenza kule nhlangano, abanikwe umsebenzi wokuba benze isiqinisekiso sokuthi bonke ababhekene namacala bayashenxa ezikhundleni.
"Bahlaselwe ngokuthi basabiswe, bathukwe nokuthi kusabalaliswe amampunge ngabo.
Kuyasikhathaza ukuthola ukuthi umgqugquzeli wesigungu esiphezulu, uMnuz Andries Nel, yena usabiswe ngokuthi uzobulawa.
Sesimyalele ukuba abike lolu daba emaphoyiseni.
"URamaphosa uthe baningi abaholi be-ANC asebeshenxile ezikhundleni, abanye bathunyelwa izincwadi zokubamisa emsebenzini emuva kokuthi behlulekile ukushenxa ungakapheli umnqamulajuqu ababewunikiwe.
Phakathi kwabamisiwe kubalwa nelungu lesigungu esiphezulu, uMnuz Bongani Bongo, naye obhekene necala lokukhwabanisa.
URamaphosa uthe bonke laba baholi abamisiwe nabashenxile ezikhundleni bazoqhubeka nokuhola ngoba imithetho elawula ezokuphathwa kwabasebenzi kayikuvumi ukuthi kumiswe imiholo yabo.
Ubuye waveza ukuthi iyaqhubeka imihlangano yamagatsha yokulungisela izingqungquthela zokukhetha ubuholi bezifunda.
URamaphosa uthe amagatsha angaphezu kuka-2000 asebe nayo imihlangano yawo yokulungiselela izingqungquthela.
Indlala iwumthelela wemibhikisho ezweni
INDLALA inomthelela ekutheni kube nemibhikisho ehlale ithe chithi saka ezweni lethu, ngokumbono kaNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal.
UNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Sihle Zikalala usho kanje ngesikhathi kuvulwa ngokomthetho ikhishi lenhlangano engenzinzuzo ephakela abaswele ukudla iFood For Life, eNewlands East ngoLwesihlanu.
Uthe inkululeko ebaluleke kakhulu ngeyokuthi abantu bakwazi ukuzodla bangathembeli ekutheni bazophiwa ngabanye ukudla.
Uthe uhulumeni unezinhlelo eziningi ozenzayo zokusiza abampofu ukuthi baphume ebubheni bakwazi ukudla.
UNgqongqoshe wezokuThuthukiswa koMphakathi kulesi sifundazwe uNkk Nonhlanhla Khoza, uthe leli khishi livulwe ngesikhathi lapho inqwaba yabantu iphelelwe yimisebenzi ngenxa yeCovid-19.
"Baningi abantu abazithole sebesesimeni sokuthi abazi ukuthi bazodlani.
Leli khishi lizosisiza kakhulu ngokusehlisela umthwalo njengoba lizophakela abantu baKwaMashu nezinye izindawo eziseduze," kusho uNdunankulu.
UMnuz Vivian Reddy usihlalo weSibaya Trust, uthe bahlale bezimisele ukuxhasa izinhlelo ezizoletha ushintsho kubantu.
Wathi uhlelo lweFood For Life lubonakala sengathi luzoletha ushintsho kubantu abampofu, yingakho befake isandla ekutheni kwakhiwe ikhishi okuzophekelwa kulo.
UMnuz Vidhor Mangaroo, obekhulumela umndeni wakwaMangaroo onikele ngomhlaba okwakhiwe kuwo leli khishi, uthe lo mhlaba wawuthengelwe ukuthi uzokwakha ikhaya lo mndeni kodwa kwabuye kwashintsha okuphethe ngokuthi kunikelwe ngawo kwiFood For life.
Umndeni ukholwa ukuthi ikhishi lizokwenza umsebenzi ozoshintsha impilo yabantu okuyinto nabo abakholelwa kakhulu kuyo," kusho uMangaroo.
Banqabe ukunika ochwepheshe ‘amadayimane’ eMnambithi
BATHWALE kanzima ochwepheshe abebejutshwe KwaHlathi, eMnambithi, ukuzohlola "amadayimane" emva kokuthi lo mphakathi uvuke umbhejazane, unqaba ukubanikeza amasampula ngoba unovalo lokuthi kungenzeka angabuyiselwa.
Noma begcine kukhona abakutholile, kusize ubudlelwano benkosi yendawo, uMnuz Sphiwe Kunene nowesilisa wendawo, ovumile ukulinikezela enkosini "idayimane" lakhe ngethemba lokuthi inkosi ngeke imholele ophathe.
Ochwepheshe bathembise umphakathi ukuthi ngeke iphele inyanga bengabuyanga nezimpendulo ukuthi abakumbayo yidayimane noma cha.
Awuzimisele ngokusuka endaweni yawo umphakathi uma kugcina kutholakala ukuthi abakumbayo yidayimane uqobo.
Bafuna uhulumeni abeke bona phambili ezinhlelweni zokuthuthukisa le ndawo.
Laba bantu sebebeke ithemba labo lokuphuma enhluphekweni kwabakumbayo.
Iningi eliqhamuka kude lilala emigodini eliyimbayo abanye balale ezimotweni abafika ngazo.
Izingane, intsha, abesifazane asebekhulile namadoda emizi yawo, babona le nto ebehlele njengenhlanhla yabo evela kuMdali ukuba azophucula isizwe sabo ebubheni obusikhungethe.
Lokhu ukubona ngolaka olubavukayo uma kukhona okubaphazamisayo noma obaphula umoya ngezinsolo zokuthi akulona idayimane abakumbayo.
Sekukhona nasebevule amabhizinisi badayisa ukudla, utshwala neziphuzo ezihlohlozayo zokubuyisa amandla njengoba kumbiwa ubusuku nemini.
Abantu abebehlukene ngamaqoqo ububafica bemba imigodi bebheka "idayimane" abanye ubathole emfuleni bewasha abakutholayo.
Iningi labantu livuka ngesikabhadakazi linikele kule ndawo eyiqele enamatshe nentaba, liyomba.
Bathe abafune kususwa kule ndawo ngenkolelo yokuthi abakumbayo uidayimane elizobakhipha enhluphekweni, endlaleni nasosizini lokungabibikho kwemisebenzi.
NgoLwesibili emini kufike izikhulu ebezivela ezinhlakeni zikhulumeni ezihlukahlukene ziholwa uNgqongqoshe wezokuThuthukiswa koMnotho, ezokuVakasha nokoNgiwa kweMvelo eKZN, uMnuz Ravi Pillay nobuholi bendabuko, bezoxoxa nabambayo.
Bacele abantu abebemba ukuthi babambisana nophenyo lochwepheshe abavela eMnyangweni wezokuMbiwayo nezaMandla.
UMnuz Mondli Mazibuko uthe yintsha egcwele embayo okuyizinkomba zokungabi bikho kwemisebenzi.
Abantu baphila ngemali yempesheni nesibonelelo sikahulumeni.
"Asifuni uhulumeni njengoba esengenelela agcine esesiphuca umhlaba wethu nesesizitholele khona.
Esikutholayo kuzosiza kudale amathuba emisebenzi, kuthuthukiswe intsha," kusho uMazibuko.
UMnuz Bhutiza Msibi uthe izikhulu zikahulumeni ziwathathile amasampula zabakumbayo ukuba ziyokuhlola.
Uthe bafuna ukuhlomula uma kuwukuthi idayimane langempela.
"Isinqumo sokugcina siyophuma enkosini ukuthi kwenziwani.
Kodwa sicela ukubhekelelwa ngemisebenzi uma kuwukuthi kunezinhleo zokuthuhukisa le ndawo," kusho uMsibi.
Inkosi uKunene ikhathazekile ngezinkumbi zabathutheleka kule ndawo abangaqhelelene ngebanga.
UKunene uthe ukhulumile nabantu ebaxwayisa ngobungozi bokuminyana kwabo.
"Kuyangikhathaza nokuthi laba bantu bacekelaphansi imvelo.
Uma bemba bashiya kanjalo.
Kunemigodi eminingi ezothwalisa kanzima imfuyo," kusho uKunene.
U-Pillay uthe okwabo ukunika umkhombandlela ngokumele kwenzeke.
Uthe senzekile isigameko esifuze lesi KwaMachi, eHarding, umphakathi uthi uhlabene ngegolide okwagcina kuvelile ukuthi kakulona.
"Sicela abantu babekezele, babambisane nathi ngesikhathi kusahlolwa amatshe atholiwe.
Sithemba ukuthi akuzothatha isikhathi eside," kusho uPillay.
UMnuz Siyabonga Vezi, imenenja ebambile KwaZulu-Natal eMnyangweni weziMbiwayo nezaMandla, uthe bayalelwe ungqongqoshe (uMnuz Gwede Mantashe) ukuthi baqale uhlelo lokuzohlola le ndawo namasampula.
Uthe bazocwaningisisa bese beyabuya, bezobikela zonke izinhlaka ezithintekayo.
"Kuseva ukuthi kukhona esingakuqagela njengamanje.
Kube khona amalungu omphakathi asinike amatshe athile esizowacubungulisisa bese siyababuyisela wona nombiko ogcwele," kusho uVezi.
Kwehlisa ubuhlongandlebe ukwakhiwa kwesikhungo samabhayisikili
UMPHAKATHI waKwaMashu ubhekene nesihlava somdlalo owaziwa ngesitabane, okungumdlalo wokukotela phezu kwesitimela sihamba, osuholele ekudluleni kwemiphefumulo yabantu abasha abaningi.UMasipala weTheku sewuqhamuke neqhinga lokulwa nalesi sihlava ngokuvula isikhungo esibizwa nge GO!
Durban Academy esizofundisa intsha yaKwaMashu ukushova kwamabhayisikili.
Lesi sikhungo esivulwe ngokusemthethweni ngoMgqibelo, kulindeleke ukuthi lolu hlelo luqeqeshe intsha engu- 400 ngesonto luphinde lunikeze uxhaso kwezemfundo nasekuthuthukisweni kwamakhono.
Lolu hlelo lushaywelwe ihlombe umphakathi nabaholi bomphakathi asebekhathazeke isikhathi eside ngalesi sihlava emphakathini, kodwa bengazi ukuthi yini abangayenza.
Ikhansela lendawo uNkk Lindile Ncayiyana ngesikhathi likhuluma neSolezwe izolo lithe selokhu kwakhiwe lesi sikhungo, usuhlangana nezingane zizidlalela amabhayisikili okuyinto enhle kakhulu.
Ugcizelele ukuthi lokhu kuzonciphisa nezinga lezingane ezikhula zibe yimidlwembe, zingene ophuzweni oludakayo nasezidakamizweni njengoba kumanje sezigxila kakhulu kwezemidlalo," kusho uNkk Ncayiyana.
Uthe okujabulisayo ukuthi indawo esakhiwe kuso, phambilini bekuyindawo abantu abebelahla kuyo imfucuza ngokungemthetho, obekuba nomthelela ongemuhle kwezempilo.
Uthe ziningi izinhlelo aziphathiswe wuMasipala weTheku ezenzelwe ukulekelela intsha ukuze ihlale imatasa abale kuzona ukwakhiwa kwenkundla yekhilikithi engakaqedwa, nendawo evulekile yokuzilolonga okulindeleke ukuthi nayo ivulwe ngokusemthethweni maduze.
Evula ngokusemthethweni lesi sikhungo, uSotswebhu omkhulu kuMasipala waseThekwini uMnuz Sibongiseni Mkhize uthe bazosiza ukuhlanganisa abantu abasha ndawonye babe nephupho elilodwa.
"Sinethemba lokuthi sizolekelela ukugqugquzela usiko lokugitshelwa kwamabhayisikili, lokhu okuyingxenye yezinhlelo zaleli dolobha zokuthuthukisa ezokuthutha, "kusho uMkhize.
Uthe uhlelo lokwakhiwa kwalezi zikhungo luqale ngo-2016 njengoba zikhona nakwamanye amalokishi okuyiNanda, KwaDabeka naseChesterville.
Umasipala uphinde wathola uxhaso lwamabhayisikili awu- 50 okuthiwa azosetshenziswa amalungu omphakathi, okuwuhlelo olusavivinywa, oluzosiza ekugqugquzeleni abantu ukuthi basebenzise lolu hlobo lwezokuthutha.
Isalukazi sikhala ngokuvalelwa endlini
USEFISA ngisho ukuyogcinwa esiteshini samaphoyisa ugogo ongaboni emehlweni waseLindelani, eThekwini, ohlala evalelwe yedwa endlini ubusuku nemini.
Kuthiwa useke wazama ukuzikhunga ngenxa yenhlalo engeyinhle ekhaya.
Lo gogo, owaziwa ngoNkk Ntuli, waseChibini, eLindelani, utholwe ngomakhelwane ehayiza ngaphakathi, ekhala ngomzukulu wakhe ongamphethe kahle njengoba emsola nangokushaqa yonke impesheni yakhe.
Ilungu lomphakathi, elicele ukungadalulwa, lithe uNkk Ntuli uvulelwe ngabantu ebebemuzwa ekhala.
Amalungu omphakathi abe esebiza abaholi bendawo kwafika noNkk Zandile Shezi, oyilungu lekomiti lomphakathi, nofike wahlala naye ugogo wambuza ngesimo sakhe.
UNkk Shezi utshele Isolezwe ukuthi ugogo ukhala kakhulu ngamaphoyisa, ucela abizwe ukuze ezongenelela nasodabeni lwemali yempesheni ayizwa ngendaba.
"Asimficanga umzukulu kodwa ngizamile ukuhlala nogogo ngenzela ukuthi asilandise kahle.
Uyayihola impesheni kodwa uthe imali yonke ithathwa ngumzukulu wakhe bese eyamvalela ahlale yedwa, kube nzima nokuthola ukudla," kusho uNkk Shezi.
Eqhuba uthe isimo sikagogo asisihle neze, bayafisa ukuthi osonhlalakahle basheshe bangenelele ngoba akulula njengoba ehlala edinga ukunakekelwa.
Echaza ngesimo abamfice kuso, uthe ubemapunapuna eduze kwamanzi okugeza abeshiywe wumzukulu ngethemba lokuthi uzozigeza kodwa wehluleka.
"Umzukulu wakhe uthe wumfana nokuyinkinga ngoba kufanele kube khona umuntu ozomgeza ugogo.
Okungizwisa ubuhlungu nokungishayisa ngovalo ukuthi ugogo usitshele ukuthi uke wazama ukuzibulala kabili kodwa wehluleka ukuzikhunga," kusho uNkk Shezi ekhathazekile.
UNobhala wekomiti laku-ward 38, uMnuz Muzi Ntuli, kuthiwa ufikile wasibona isimo sikagogo wazama nokubiza osonhlalakahle kodwa bebengakafiki ukuzobheka isimo.
"Ukhale kakhulu sesihamba, ebalisa ngokuthi siyamlahla noma sesisibonile isimo sakhe.
Siyafisa kushaywe ikhwelo kosonhlalakahle ngokushesha," kusho uNkk Shezi.
Ihhovisi likaNgqongqoshe wezokuThuthukiswa koMphakathi, uNkk Nonhlanhla Khoza, lithembisile ukuthi lolu daba luzosukunyelwa ngokushesha.
Okhulumela umnyango, uMnuz Mhlaba Memela, uthe bakushayela ihlombe ukusukumela phezulu kwamalungu omphakathi.
"Sizothumela osonhlalakahle ngokukhulu ukuphuthuma kulungiswe nodaba lwempesheni kagogo akwazi ukuyothola imali yakhe.
Siyabakhuthaza abantu ukuthi baxhumane namahhovisi osonhlalakahle uma behlala namalungu omndeni ahlulekayo ukuwanakekela.
Kunezinhlelo zamahhala zikahulumeni zokulekelela.
Sizolulandela nodaba lomzukulu sibambisene namaphoyisa, uma kukhona lapho kuphulwe khona umthetho," kusho uMemela.
Leli phephandaba lithole nama-video aqoshiwe ugogo eveza nokuthi umzukulu wamfakela i-sanitizer ethi umuthi wamehlo nokwenza wangabe esabona nhlobo.
Ukhala nangokuthi uhamba isibhedlela kodwa sekunesikhathi eside engahanjiswa.
Udidekile umndeni womfundi obulawe nesoka
NONTUTHUKO NGUBANEUMNDENI ufuna ubulungiswa ngokubulawa komfundi kaGrade 12 nesoka lakhe, kanti izidumbu zabo zitholakale kujantshi wesitimela zinamanxeba okudutshulwa KwaMachibisa, eMgungundlovu.
UMnuz Sbusiso Gumede (22) noNksz Lusanda Dlamini (18), obefunda eNyonithwele High, batholakale bebulewe ngeledlule.
Izidumbu zabo zitholakale zinamanxeba amaningi okudutshulwa, ngakujantshi oseduze kwesikole uMthethomusha.
Ngokuthola kweSolezwe izidumbu zabo zitholwe ngabantu abebedlula base behlaba umkhosi, kwabizwa amaphoyisa.
UNksz Dlamini ubenamanxeba amathathu okudutshulwa ekhanda, isoka lakhe linamanxeba amane okudutshulwa ekhanda.
Ubabekazi kaLusanda, uNkk Neliswa Lukhoza, uthe bafuna abasolwa kuleli cala baboshwe ukuze bazi ukuthi kwakwenzenjani.
"Sizomfihla ngoMgqibelo ozayo uLusanda.
Sidinga ukuthi baboshwe abasolwa abenze lokhu.
Asinalo ulwazi lokuthi kwenzakaleni, sisadidekile nje nathi.
Wayeyovakashela isola lakhe.
Ubefunda umatric eNyonithwele, besisabheke lukhulu kuyena.
Siyalazi isoka lakhe, njengomuntu abebethandana.
Lona belingafundi belizama amatoho.
ULusanda wayeye endlini yesoka ngesikhathi bebulawa.
Asazi nembangela yokubulawa kwabo.
Kumanje sisathukile, sifuna ubulungiswa kulolu daba, asazi ukuthi babebulawa nje kwenzenjani," kusho uNkk Lukhoza.
Ikhansela lendawo uMnuz Xolani Ngongoma, lithe bakhathazekile ngokuhlaselwa kwabantu endaweni engaphansi kwakhe njengoba eyikhansela laseMbali kuze kushaye kwaMachibisa.
"Ayikho into esingathi isitholakele ukuthi kungani bebulewe laba.
Kube yinto ethusayo, eLay Centre kwabulawa abathandanayo, namanje sekuyenzeka futhi.
Umfana obulewe sithole ukuthi owangasoPongolo, asazi nokuthi kuzokwenziwa njani ukuba afihleke njengoba ekhaya kuthiwa kunezingane zodwa.
Kuke kwaba ngconywana ukuhlaselwa kwabantu kodwa manje sekwenzeka lokhu kuyathusa.
Abantu basabulawa kule ndawo nekuyinto ekhathazayo nethusayo kakhulu," kusho uNgongoma.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal uColonel Thembeka Mbele uthe amaphoyisa asePlessislaer aphenya amacala amabili okubulala.
Akekho osaboshiwe.
Abazali bacikeke bavala isikole
KUME ukufunda kwashunqa ithayi lemoto izolo, abazali bebhikisha phambi kwesikole iPhuthini High, eMangweni, eMtshezi.
Kuthiwa abazali bakhala ngesimo esingesihle izingane ezifunda ngaphansi kwaso kulesi sikole.
Kuthiwa izingane zimpitshene emakilasini, amanzi nogesi kakukho.
Okhulumela uMasipala Inkosi Langalibalele, uMnuz Sifiso Mdakane, uthe umphakathi ukhala ngokudonsa izinyawo koMnyango wezeMfundo ekutheni wakhe isikole.
"Kufundelwa ezindlini zesikhashana ezabekwa wuMnyango wezeMfundo.
Umphakathi awanelisekile ngalokhu," kubeka uMdakane.
Ikhansela lakule ndawo, uMnuz Nkosingiphile Mpembe lithe: "Ngo 2010, kwabekwa izindlu zokufundela zesikhashana, abantu banikwa ithemba lokuthi kuzoqhutshekwa kwakhiwe isikole, okungakaze kwenziwe.
Isimo izingane ezifunda ngaphansi kwaso asikho sihle, amanzi amadala ahlala emathangini, awekho esimeni sokuthi aphuzwe ngabafundi.
"Uqhube wathi, emva kombhikisho kufike umhloli othembise ukuthi namhlanje kuzofika ithimba loMnyango wezeMfundo lizokhuluma nabazali, mayelana nalolu daba.
Okhulumela uMnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Muzi Mahlambi, uthe sebexhumene nehhovisi labo lesifunda ukuze lilusingathe lolu daba.
Izithandani zishaywe zafa zisolwa ngokweba
AMAPHOYISA athungatha abasolwa ababulale izithandani ngokuzishaya eShayamoya KwaMpumuza, ngaphandle kwaseMgungundlovu ngoba bezisola ngokweba.
UNksz Londeka Mvelase noMnuz Mxolisi Mchunu, kuthiwa bashaywe ngamalungu omphakathi, baze bafa ngeSonto.
Izithandani bezihlala ndawonye.
Kuthiwa bezisolwa ngokweba imali elinganiselwa kuR2 500 neselula kamakhelwane.
Isolezwe lithole ukuthi laba kwale ngisho sebecela uxolo kabazange bayekwe ukushaywa, bakhandwa nangamatshe.
Kuthiwa bekukhona abesifazane nabesilisa ngesikhathi beshaywa.
Ikhansela lakule ndawo, uNkk Jabu Zondo, lihambele kule ndawo izolo ukuzokhuza ngokwenzekile.
Likhuluma neSolezwe, lithe yize bebesolwa ngokweba kodwa bekungamele babulawe.
"Sengibuya khona emphakathini.
Kukhona ukuthi siyakhala ngobugebengu, buyasihlupha impela kule ndawo, yize kunjalo kodwa akuvumelekile ukuba umphakathi uziphindiselele.
Kumele ubize amaphoyisa kube yiwona abopha abantu abonayo.
Ngolwazi engilutholile, abasolwa bebesolwa ngokuntshontsha endaweni.
Uzinzo lukhona endaweni njengamanje, kunokuthula.
Umfana akuyena owendawo, owesifazane ngowakhona endaweni.
Ngisazofuna umndeni wakhe, bese siyahlangana nawo kusasa (namhlanje) sikhulume ngalolu daba," kusho uNkk Ngubo.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala uthe kuvulwe amacala amabili okubulala, amaphoyisa asathungatha abasolwa.
Imizamo yeSolezwe yokuthola imindeni yababulewe kayizange iphumelele izolo ngoba izinombolo zabo bezingatholakali, kwaze kwashaya isikhathi sokushicilela.
AbakwaGupta babeshushumbisa imali emabhange ahlukene
AFRICAN NEWS AGENCY (ANA) ILINGANISELWA ku-R49 billion imali yombuso eyasetshenziswa ngokungafanele ngokulawulwa koMbuso yidlanzana, ngokusho komqondisi we-Shadow World, uMnuz Paul Edward Holden, ngokophenyo olwenziwe.
Lo mqondisi ukusho lokhu kwikhomishini eholwa nguJaji Raymond Zondo izolo.
Ngokwakhe, bathola ukuthi imali engu-R49 157 323 233.
68 yayilokhu ifakwa emabhange ahlukene.
U-Holden ukusho lokhu efakaza ngemali eyayifakwa iphinde ikhishwe emabhange ahlukene.
Ohola ubufakazi, u-Advocate Matthew Chaskalson, uyena obephonsa imibuzo uHolden.
U-Holden utshele ikhomishini ukuthi ubufakazi bakhe bugxile emibikweni nangendlela imali ebikhokhwa ngayo emabhizinisini akwaGupta.
Uveze ukuthi abakwaGupta bashushumbisa u-R287 million, abawuthola kwi-Estina Dairy Farm Project.
Uhlelo kwakungelokuthuthukisa abalimi baseFree State.
U-Holden uthe abakwaGupta baqala ukushushumbisa imali kusasele unyaka ukuba uhlelo lwase-Estina luqale.
Uhulumeni waseFree State waqala ukukhokhela uhlelo lwase-Estina ngoJuni 2011 kodwa abakwaGupta baqala ukushushumbisa imali abathi bayithola kulolu hlelo ngoMeyi 2011.
"Basebenzisa uhlelo lwase-Estina ukucasha beshushumbisa imali, ngaphambi kokuba lolu hlelo luqale," kusho uHolden.
Ngokobufakazi, kuvele ukuthi uhulumeni wakhokha u-R287 million kulo mndeni wakwaGupta, imali yabe isifakwa kuma-account ahlukene enkampani ukuze kubukeke sengathi wenza inzuzo ka-R880million phakathi kuka-2012 kuya ku-2016.
Ikhomishini iyaqhubeka.
I-video eveza konke ngokufa kukaMyeni
SEKUVELE i-video engahluziwe eveza konke okwenzeka ngosuku okwabulawa ngalo uMnuz Lindani Myeni, eHawaii eMelika.
Kule video uMyeni uvela eyongena emzini thizeni oseHonolulu, egqoke umqhele engena elandela ngemuva kwababili ababemile okuthiwa bayizithandani.
Ubonakala edlule aye ethempelini eliseduze komuzi wabo.
Ufika akhumule izicathulo ethempelini, emuva kwalokho kuvela exolisa kulaba ababili.
Kuthiwa emuva mhlawumbe kwemizuzwana ewu-40, uMyeni ubonakala ephuma kule ndlu ebese esexolisa kulezi zithandani.
Kuthi kusenjalo kuvele owesifazane eshayele u911, ebika ngokugqekezelwa.
Ngenkathi lo wesifazane ebikela amaphoyisa uthi uMyeni ubesendlini yabo egqekeza.
Kuthiwa ngokwemibiko yabanikazi bomuzi bathi akukho okwathathwa emzini wabo.
Abameli bomndeni kaMyeni bathi bakholelwa ekutheni le video ihambisana nokuthi wayebheka ithempeli eliseduze komuzi walezi zithandani.
Ummeli uJim Bickerton, uveze ukuthi inkantolo iphoqe izikhulu ukuthi zikhiphe i-video ingahluziwe.
Amaphoyisa nawo kwathiwa awalethe amarekhodi ezingcingo ze-911 zosuku lwesigameko.
Kwingxoxo uBickerton abe nayo noMnuz William Denselow kwi-eNCA uveze ukuthi ngenkathi uMyeni ehamba kulo muzi wayengacasukile.
"Amazwi akhe okugcina kwaba ukucela uxolo kwaze kwaba uyasithela," kubeka uBickerton.
Kule video eyayikhishwe kuqala kuvela amaphoyisa eya kuMyeni owawabuza ukuthi angobani, wona avele amdubula njengoba ashonela esibhedlela.
Uthe bebengazi ukuthi uMyeni wayexolisa futhi amaphoyisa abenayo le video kodwa abiza isithangami sabezindaba athi ahlaselwa kungekho sidingo.
UBickerton uthe bazoqhubeka bafune iqiniso ukuze kwaziwe ukuthi kwenzakalani.
Kusolwa uqhekeko kwi-IFP kuqhuma inganono eMelmoth
BASOLA amakhansela e-IFP ngokubasasazela ngonogada okuthiwa badubule amalungu omphakathi okulimale kuwo amathathu, emhlanganweni waleli qembu obuseThubalethu, eMthonjaneni (eMelmoth), ngeSonto ntambama.
Kuthiwa kuphoqe ukuthi onogada baqhumise inganono ukuhlakaza isixuku samalungu omphakathi okuthiwa abevuke umbhejazana avala umgwaqo ongenela ehholo obekubanjwe kulo umhlangano.
Enye ingxenye yomphakathi isola ubuholi baleli qembu ngokuzama ukubafaka emanzi emadolweni njengoba befuna kubuyiswe ikhansela lakule ndawo elixoshwe yi-IFP.
Kuthiwa umhlangano bewubizwe wubuholi be-IFP esifundeni saseKing Cetshwayo ukucacisa ngalolu daba oseluhlukanise umphakathi phakathi, njengoba kuthe ngesonto eledlule wabhikisha ufuna kubuyiswe wonke amakhansela axoshiwe kubalwa nobeyimeya uMnuz Bonginkosi Biyela.
Elinye ilungu lomphakathi ebeliyingxenye yombhikisho ngesikhathi kudubuleka laba abathathu elingathandanga ukudalulwa, lisole abaholi be-IFP namakhansela ayekhona ngokutshela onogada ukuthi babadubule ukuze bangakwazi ukuveza ilaka labo.
"Besibhikisha emgwaqweni ngoba sinqatsheliwe ukungena ehholo sekugcwaliswe abantu abebevela kwezinye izindawo.
Inkinga iqale ngesikhathi sivalele elinye ilungu lomphakathi ebelifuna ukudlula ngenkani emgwaqweni obuvaliwe, onogada nabaqaphi bamakhansela abebekhona bathola intuba, badubula," kusho leli lungu.
Umholi we-IFP eMthonjaneni naye ongathandanga ukudalulwa uveze ukuthi amalungu omphakathi kule ndawo ahlukene phakathi.
"Ngesonto eledlule, bekunombhikisho lapho umphakathi ubufuna ukucaciselwa ngokuxoshwa kwekhansela lawo esigcemeni.
Kuhlelwe umhlangano obunawo wonke amakhansela nabaholi be-IFP besifunda ukuze umphakathi unikezwe izimpendulo.
"Inkinga iqale lapho amanye amalungu omphakathi esema izixongololo ngaphandle kwehholo, okuthe uma umhlangano uqala, avala umgwaqo ongena ehholo, ajikijela ngamatshe izimoto zonogada okugcine sekuphoqeka ukuthi badubule ngoba umphakathi obusubahlasela.
Amanye amalungu omphakathi abephethe izibhamu," kusho lo mholi.
Kulo mhlangano kuthiwa bewuhanjelwe yimeya esanda kuqokwa uMnuz Mbangiseni Biyela, yiphini lakhe uMnuz Phumlani Ntombela nawo wonke amakhansela kuMasipala waseMthonjaneni.
Imizamo yokuthola ukuphawula kobuholi besifunda ayiphumelelanga njengoba izingcingo zabo bezikhala zingabanjwa nemiyalezo ingaphendulwa.
Okhulumela lo masipala, uMnuz Thami Shangase, uthe lo mhlangano bewungahleliwe umasipala, wathi udaba lusezandleni zamaphoyisa.
Kuthintwa okhulumela i-IFP kuzwelonke, uMnuz Mkhuleko Hlengwa, uthe leli qembu lizokhipha isitatimende ngalolu daba namuhla.
Uthuthuva luqale ukubonakala kuxoshwa uBiyela (obeyimeya phambilini) namkhansela amane, kwadaleka uqhekeko kumalunga omphakathi ikakhulu angamalungu e-IFP ephethe lo masipala.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uColonel Thembeka Mbele, uthe kuvulwe amacala okuzama ukubulala nelokususa uthuthuva emphakathini aphenywa esiteshini samaphoyisa eMelmoth.
UMbete uchitha ukuthi bayiziba indaba yenkohlakalo
OWAYENGUSOMLOMO wePhalamende, uNksz Baleka Mbethe, ukuchithile ukuthi babeziziba izinto ezithinta inkohlakalo, uthi okunye kwakuvela njengento exoxwayo kodwa engabambeki.
UNksz Mbete ephendula imibuzo kwikhomishini ephenya ngokulawulwa kombuso yidlanzana, ngezinsolo zokuthi amanye amalungu ePhalamende ayethinteka enkohlakalweni, uthe kokunye izinto ezazivela zazingabambeki, okunye kube sengathi kuyahletshwa ngoba abantu ababenolwazi babengenabo ubufakazi.
Uze wenza isibonelo ngodaba lwezikhali oluthinta owayenguMengameli kuleli, uMnuz Jacob Zuma, ukuthi wathola incwadi ebhalwe izinto ezazinzima kodwa akazi yayivela kubani.
"Sihlalo, ngiyazi kade kukhona abantu asebefakazile lapha, nangendlela okusetshenzwa ngayo kwi-ANC.
Ngiyazi nokuthi usomlomo uke weza lana naye washo ukuthi ngeke uvele ukhulume ngento oyizwa ikhulunywa.
"Ngingakhuluma ngecala lezikhali, icala elihlehlisiwe izolo (Msombuluko).
Kukhona incwadi eyafakwa ngaphansi kwesicabha sehhovisi lami.
Leyo ncwadi yayinezinto ezithusayo nezishaqisayo kodwa kwakungasayinwe lutho futhi kungashiwo nokuthi ngubani oyibhalile.
EPhalamende kumatasa, ngangingeke ngikwazi ukuthatha le ncwadi ngingazi nokuthi ibhalwe ubani bese sixoxa ngayo.
Inkinga ukuthi ngubani obhalile, lowo muntu kwakumele eze kumina angiqonde.
Ngizama ukuphendula manje ukuthi ePhalamende sasingeke sikwazi ukuxoxa indaba ehletshwayo," kusho uNksz Mbete.
NgoJuni 2017, ubuzwe ukuthi yena wenzani ngodaba elithinta umndeni wakwaGupta.
"Angisakhumbuli kahle kodwa ngiyazi ukuthi kumayelana nokuputshuka kwezindaba ezithinta abakwaGupta.
Ngiyacabanga ukuthi ngaleso sikhathi kuvela lezo zindaba, sasizobiza labo abazibhalayo.
Sibheke ukuthi lokho abakushoyo okubhekene nezwe lonke kumayelana nani.
Ukuze sithole incazelo bese siyakwazi ukwenza umsebenzi wethu," kusho uNksz Mbethe.
Basola iNSFAS kushona isitshudeni
IZITSHUDENI zigxeka uNSFAS ngokufa komfundi okuthiwa ushone ngemva kokulala izinsuku ezimbili ngaphandle kwesango lesikhungo, iThekwini Tvet College, eCato Manor, ngoMgqibelo.
Kuthiwa umufi, uYonwabo Manyanya (26), obenza iziqu ze-Electrical Infrastructure Construction, uxoshwe wumastende walapho abehlala khona ngenxa yokuthi ukweleta imali yerenti.
Kuthiwa umufi kuphoqeleke ukuthi alale izinsuku ezimbili ngaphandle kwesikhungo ngoba engenayo enye indawo yokufihla ikhanda kulandela ukuxoshwa kwakhe lapho ebehlala khona ngoMsombuluko.
Kubikwa ukuthi ngoLwesithathu kubonakale ukuthi umufi akekho esimeni esikahle ngokwempilo.
Izitshudeni ebezinayo kubikwa ukuthi zimtshele ukuthi kumele athole indawo yokukhosela.
UYonwabo, okuthiwa ubesehamba ehlala, kubikwa ukuthi ugcine ngokuthi ashone ngoMgqibelo efulethini obekuhlala kulo umngani wakhe eDurban North.
Esinye sezitshudeni ebesisondelene nomufi, esicele lingadalulwa igama laso ephepheni, sithe basashaqekile ngokwenzekile, sagxeka uNSFAS ngokuhudula izinyawo ekutheni bathole uxhaso lwezimali.
"Angiphilile kahle emoyeni ngemva kwalesi sigameko ebesingagwemeka.
Ngifisa uNSFAS ungenelele ngoba kubukeka zizokwanda izigameko ezifuze lezi njengoba kungena ubusika," kusho lesi sitshudeni.
Ilungu lomndeni kamufi, esingakwazanga ukuthola igama lalo, lithe abakwazi ukukhuluma nabezindaba mayelana nesehlo.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe alikho icala elibikiwe.
Inkinga yokuntula imali yenabele nasophikweni lwaleli kolishi e-Asherville Campus, eSydenham, njengoba kunezitshudeni ezingaphezu kuka-50 ezibhikishe ngaphandle kwamasango izolo.
Lezi zitshudeni zitshele Isolezwe ukuthi zilale emgwaqweni ngaphandle kwalesi sikhungo ngoba zixoshwe omastende ezindaweni ezihlala kuzona ezingazikhokhele.
Iningi lalezi zitshudeni, ebeliphethe izingubo zokulala, lisuka ezindaweni ezikude okubalwa kuzona iGauteng, Eastern Cape naseMpumalanga.
UMnuz Siyabonga Sambu, wase-Ermelo, eMpumalanga, owenza unyaka wesithathu weziqu zeCommunity Safety, ugxeke isikhungo noNSFAS ngokunqakisana ngabo uma bebuza ngezicelo zabo zemali.
Uthi kusukela ngoFebhuwari abalutholi uxhaso lwezimali, omasitende sebeze bakhomba indlela izitshudeni emiqashweni.
"Akukho nemali yokudla.
Abebefake izicelo zale mali banikwe eyezindleko zokuthutha nakhona ingcosana eyitholile.
Isikhungo asisizi ngalutho kunalokho sisibizela onogada ukuba basixoshe," kusho uSambu.
Lokhu kufakazelwe nguZodwa Mabanga osuka eGoli othi usehlala emgwaqeni ngoba uxoshwe umastende.
Uthi kusukela ngoJanuwari bebenganikwa mali kodwa ngo-Ephreli banikwe uR4 100 akhokhe ngawo izikweletu.
Uthishomkhulu waseThekwini Tvet College, uMnuz Nkosinathi Mchunu, uthe kungamampunge ukuthi umufi ushone ngemva kokuqhinqa ngaphandle kwesikhungo nezinye izitshudeni.
"Zikhona impela izinkinga kuNSFAS kodwa isitshudeni okhuluma ngaso sishone endlini yesoka ebesilivakashele.
U-NSFAS umatasa nokuyilungisa inkinga ekhungethe izitshudeni," kubeka uMchunu.
Ngodaba lwase-Asherville uthe yidlanzana lezitshudeni ebeliqhinqile elinenkinga yoxhaso lwezimali.
Uveze nokuthi kunezitshudeni ezibahlinzeke ngeminingwane eshayisanayo ngenhloso yokuhlomula ngoxhaso lwemali ethe xaxa.
Bethintwa abeNsfas bathembise ukubuya nezimpendulo mayelana nalezi zigameko.
Umnqamulajuqu  kwabaphikisayo embangweni wolweSilo
BASALELWE usuku lwanamhlanje kuphela bonke abaphikisayo ecaleni lombango wencwadi yefa eyashiywa yiSilo uGoodwill Zwelithini kaBhekuzulu, ukuba bafake amaphepha aphikisayo enkantolo.
Kulabo abaphikisayo kubalwa iNgonyama uMisuzulu kaZwelithini kanye nondunankulu waKwaZulu, Inkosi Mangosuthu Buthelezi.
Izolo lize lashona abanye babo bengakawafaki amaphepha.
Umnqamulajuqu wokuba bafake amaphepha bawunikezwa iNkantolo eNkulu eMgungundlovu, ngenyanga eyedlule.
Lo myalelo wakhishwa iJaji Rishi Seegobin, ngesikhathi elalele isicelo sokuba inkantolo ikhiphe isinqumo esivimba ukugcotshwa kweSilo uMisuzulu, kuze kube kuphothulwa icala.
Leli cala lafakwa enkantolo ngaphambi kokuba kuguqe iNdlovukazi Shiyiwe Mantfombi Dlamini Zulu, obeyibambabukhosi.
Icala lihlukene kabili, elokuqala lafakwa nguNdlunkulu waKwaKhethomthandayo, uSibongile Dlamini Zulu, onguNdlunkulu wokuqala kaMdlokombane.
Kuleli cala uNdlunkulu ufuna ukuba athole ingxenye yamafa kaBhejane njengoba ethi umshado wabo uhlanganisa amafa.
Elesibili lafakwa ngabaNtwana baKwaKhethomthandayo, uNtandoyenkosi noNtombizosuthu.
Abantwana bafuna kuchithwe ukuqokwa kweNdlovukazi njengebamba bukhosi ngoba basola ukuthi kukokoteliwe ukusayina kukaMdlokombane, encwadini yefa eyayisho lokhu.
Incwadi yefa eyashiywa yiNdlovukazi, yona yaqokela esihlalweni sobukhosi iSilo uMisuzulu kaZwelithini.
Phakathi kwabeseka leli cala, kubalwa elinye lamazinyane kaMdlokombane uMntwana uNhlanganiso Zulu, wasesigodlweni kaDlamahlahla.
Emaphepheni asenkantolo afungelwe, uMntwana uNhlanganiso wazwakalisa ukuseseka isicelo sokuba kumiswe ukugcotshwa ngokusemthethweni kweSilo kuze kube kuphela icala elisenkantolo.
Imizamo yokuthola ukuphawula komele abaphikisayo, uMnuz Musa Ntsibande, ayizange iphumelele njengoba ucingo lwakhe belukhala lungabanjwa futhi engazange ayiphendule imibuzo ayithunyelelwe.
Umvalelandlini ulambise izitshudeni
UKUVALWA kwezwe thaqa ngemva kokugasela kweCovid-19 kuleli nyakenye, kwenza izitshudeni zabulawa yindlala njengoba ezinye zaziphila ngokuphiwa ukudla.
Lokhu kuvezwe wumbiko weHuman Sciences Research Council, eyenze ucwaningo ngendlela izitshudeni ebeziphila ngayo ngesikhathi kuvalwe izwe nyakenye.
USolwazi Sibusiso Sifunda weHSRC, uthe yintsha ephakathi kuka-18 no-35 ebe yingxenye yalolu cwaningo.
Uthe ucwaningo olwethulwe nguNgqongqoshe wemfundo ePhakeme uDkt Blade Nzimande kuleli sonto, luveza ukuthi u-40% wezitshudeni kwadingeka ukuthi ubuyele emakhaya emuva kokuvalwa kwezwe.
Wathi ucwaningo luveze ukuthi izitshudeni ezingu-53% zazikholelwa ekutheni ngeke zisuleleke ngegciwane kanti u-15% wawusaba ukuthi ungasuleleka.
"U-41% uveze ukuthi wawuhluleka ukuthenga ukudla ngesikhathi kuvalwe izwe, u-10% wawuthembele ekuphiweni ukudla kanti u-15% wawulamba, ungadli kuze kuphele izinsuku.
U-79% uveze ukuthi abazali babekuthenga ukudla ukuze zikwazi lezi zitshudeni ukuthola okuya ngasethunjini.
"UNzimande uthe igciwane libe nomthelela ikakhulu kwizitshudeni ezenza unyaka wokuqala.
"Leli gciwane lishintshe izinto eziningi ikakhulu kwezemfundo Ngikhathazekile ikakhulu ngezitshudeni ezazenza unyaka wokuqala ezazifika zisuka kwa-matric ngoba yizona okwakumele zishintshe impilo ebeziyijwayele yasezikoleni.
Kubalulekile ukuthi uma kunezimo ezifuze lezi, sigxile kubantu abasha ngoba yibona abashayeka kakhulu," kubeka uNzimande.
Lolu cwaningo luveze ukuthi u-65% wezitshudeni waba nokhwantalala ngokomqondo.
Luthole ukuthi ngabesifazane abahlaselwa kakhulu ukhwantalala uma uqhathanisa nabesilisa.
UNzimande unxuse izitshudeni ukuthi ziqhubeke zizivikele egciwaneni ngaso sonke isikhathi.
Uthe njengoba ucwaningo luveza ukuthi u-79% wezitshudeni uzwakalise ukuthi kumele wesekwe ngosizo lwezengqondo, uyalele iHigher Health ukuthi isungule inombolo ezosetshenziswa yizitshudeni zikwazi ukuyishayela yamahhala.
"Nginxusa izitshudeni ukuthi zifune usizo uma zinenkinga yokufunda nokunye.
Kuyangijabulisa ukuthi izikhungo ziyasiza ngokuhlinzeka nge-data nezinye izinhlelo zokufunda njengoba isimo sisenje.
Ngiyazwelana nezitshudeni ngezingqinamba ezibhekene nazo kanjalo nangobunzima ezihlangabezane nabo ngesikhathi kuvalwe izwe ngenxa yeCovid-19."
I-ANC izobhunga ngecala elifakwe nguMagashule
UBUHOLI obuphezulu be-ANC buzohlangana namhlanje, buzobhunga ngecala elifakwe enkantolo nguNobhala jikelele wenhlangano osamisiwe, uMnuz Ace Magashule.
UMagashule ufake amaphepha eNkantolo eNkulu eGoli, lapho ephonsa inselelo ngesinqumo sokumiswa kwakhe njengonobhala jikelele wenhlangano.
Wamiswa emva kokuthi kuphele umnqamulajuqu wezinsuku ezingu-30, ayezinikeziwe kanye nabanye abaholi ababhekene namacala, ukuba bashenxe ezikhundleni.
Ubhekene necala lenkohlakalo ngethenda kaR250 million yokulungiswa kophahla lwezindlu ezifulelwe ngetsheboya, eyakhishwa ngesikhathi esengundunankulu eFree State.
Namhlanje ubuholi obuphezulu benhlangano okungumengameli uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, usekela mengameli uMnuz David Mabuza, usihlalo kazwelonke uMnuz Gwede Mantashe, usekela nobhala jikelele uNkk Jessie Duarte nomgcinimafa uMnuz Paul Mashatile, buzoba nomhlangano lapho buzobhunga ngalolu daba.
Okhulumela i-ANC uMnuz Pule Mabe, ukuqinisekisile ukuthi kuzoba nomhlangano.
"I-ANC iwabonile amaphepha asenkantolo afakwe ngunobhala jikelele osamisiwe, uMnuz Ace Magashule.
I-ANC izokusho ngoMsombuluko (namhlanje) emva komhlangano wezikhulu eziphezulu ukuthi izoya kanjani phambili.
Angifuni ukufaka umbono wami kulokhu.
"UMagashule ufuna inkantolo ichithe ukumiswa kwakhe njengonobhala jikelele wenhlangano.
Emaphepheni asenkantolo, uMagashule uthi umgomo we-ANC wokuthi abaholi ababhekene namacala kufanele bashenxe ezikhundleni, awukho emthethweni.
Ufuna nokuthi inkantolo ichithe umyalelo we-ANC wokuthi kufanele axolise ngokubhala incwadi emisa uRamaphosa emsebenzini.
Ngesonto eledlule isigungu esiphezulu se-ANC samnqumela ugwayi katiki uMagashule, ukuba axolise ngokubhala lencwadi yokumisa uRamaphosa emsebenzini sathi wayengenalo igunya lokuyibhala.
