Ubekade eyalelwe ukuba axolise lungakapheli usuku lwangoLwesithathu ngesonto eledlule, kepha wawushaya indiva umyalelo.
Le ncwadi uMagashule wayibhala emva kokuba kuputshuke incwadi emisa yena emsebenzini.
Ngokwamaphepha asenkantolo, uMagashule ufuna udaba lulalelwe ekuqaleni kukaJuni.
Kula maphepha uthi udaba luyaphuthuma, uxwayisa ngokuthi kungaba nodlame uma lungase lungalalelwa ngokushesha.
Abalandeli bakhe sebeqalile ukubamba imihlangano bebhunga ngokuwuphonsela inselelo lo mthetho wokuthi abaholi ababhekene namacala bashenxe ezikhundleni.
NgoMgqibelo bebehlangene esifundazweni i-Free State, lapho bezwakalise ukungahambisani nomthetho.
Ungqongqoshe nomyalezo obalulekile kwizitshudeni zakuleli
UNGQONGQOSHE weMfundo ePhakeme, ezeSayensi nobuChwepheshe, uDkt Blade Nzimande, uthe ngeke isitshudeni siphucwe uxhaso lweNational Students" Financial Aid Scheme (NSFAS) uma sishintsha iziqu esizenzayo.
UDkt Nzimande uthe ngeke futhi siphucwe uxhaso uma sishintsha isikhungo esifunda kusona.
Uthe uxhaso lwezitshudeni luncike ekutheni lowo olufunayo uyahlangabezana nayo yonke imibandela ebekiwe.
"Kubekwa imibandela ethile ngaphambi kokuba isitshudeni sixhaswe.
Uma isitshudeni siya kwenye inyuvesi, kuzobalwa iminyaka esele ngoba wonke umuntu oxhaswayo ubekelwe isikhathi okumele aphothule ngayo iziqu zakhe," kusho uNzimande.
Uthe yingakho bethi uxhaso ngeke aphucwe lowo noma kungathiwa ushintsha isikhungo.
"Izitshudeni ziphula imigomo uma sezibona ukuthi sezizoshaywa yisikhathi sokuthi ziphothule iziqu zazo njengoba kusuke kubekwe umbandela wokuphothula iziqu.
Zibe seziya kwezinye izikhungo ngaphandle kokusho ukuthi ziyashiya la kade zifunda khona," kusho uDkt Nzimande.
Ukugcizelele ukuthi izitshudeni kumele zisho uma sezishintsha izikhungo, zingamane zivumbuke kwesinye isikhungo.
I-SIU izophenya ngokubhubhudlwa kwemali yomngcele  waseMozambique
I-SPECIAL Investigating Unit (SIU) isezithendeni zabasolwa ngokubhubhudla imali yokwakha izithiyo zikakhonkolo okwakuhloswe ngazo ukunqanda ukushushimbiselwa eMozambique kwezimoto ezebiwe kuleli.
Umengameli uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, usesayine umthetho ogunyaza iSIU ukuba iphenye ngale thenda eyakhishwa uMnyango wezokuThutha KwaZulu-Natal ngo-2018.
Le thenda yakhishwa emva kwezikhalo kubantu abakhele izingxenye ezisenhla nesifundazwe, ikakhulukazi eManguzi, ababekhala ngokwenyuka kwezinga lokwebiwa kwezimoto kule ndawo, ezigcina zishushumbiselwe eMozambique.
Isinqumo sokukhipha ithenda sathathwa emva kokuhambela kowayengumengameli ngalesosikhathi, uMnuz Jacob Zuma, nowayengungqongqoshe wezamaPhoyisa ngalesosikhathi, uMnuz Fikile Mbalula, lapho amalungu omphakathi azikhalela khona ngalesi sihlava sokwebiwa kwezimoto zeqiswe umngcele.
Emva kokungabonakali kwenqubekela phambili yize imali seyasebenza, kuphoqe ukuba kuqalwe uphenyo ngale thenda.
Okhulumela iSIU, UMnuz Kaizer Kganyago, ukuqinisekisile ukuthi le nhlangano izophenya izinsolo zenkohlakalo nokwehliswa ngemilenze kwemali kule thenda.
Le thenda kaR85 million yanikezwa izinkampani ezimbili i-ISF Construction neShula Construction.
Le zinkampani kwakufanele zakhe izithiyo zikakhonkolo ezazizohamba ibanga elingu-8 km emngceleni wakuleli neMozambique.
UKganyago uthe umbiko owathulelwa ikomiti elibhekele ukusebenza komnyango wezeMisebenzi yoMphakathi neNgqalasizinda ePhalamende, wakhombisa ukuthi lezinkampani zakhokhelwa izigidi zamaRandi yize umncane kakhulu umsebenzi ezawenza.
"Umbiko ukhombisa ukuthi lezinkampani zenza umsebenzi oyibanga eliwu-0.
166 km kepha zakhokhelwa isamba sikaR48 million.
Lesamba kwakufanele sikhokhwe uma sekwenziwe umsebenzi ongu-3 km.
"UKganyago uthe uma bethola ukuthi kukhona imali eyehla ngemilenze, bazohlanziswa labo abahlomulayo.
Okhulumela umnyango wezokuThutha KwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Kwanele Ncalane, uthe bayasamukela isinqumo sikamengameli.
"Sizobambisana nazo zonke izinhlaka zomthetho eziphenya lolu daba.
"Yize lolu hlelo lwaqalwa eminyakeni emibili eyedlule, abahlali baseManguzi basaqhubeka nokukhala ngokuntshontshwa kwezimoto eziphelela eMozambique.
Ngenyanga edlule Isolezwe libike ngezikhalo zamalungu omphakathi wakule ndawo, abekhala ngokuthi angenelwa ezindlini adunwe izimoto.
Amalungu omphakathi athi izigila mkhuba ziwashiya ehlathini emva kokuthatha izimoto zawo.
Usathukile umndeni ophunyuke uthunjiwe
NKOSIKHONA CELEASATHUKA izanya amalungu omndeni wakwaGina awu-11, endaweni yaseMange eMkhuze, aphunyuke ethunjwe yizigilamkhuba ebezikade zihlasele kuleli khaya ngezithuba zasentathakusa ngesonto eledlule.
Ngokuthola kweSolezwe NgoMgqibelo, lezi zigilamkhuba zifike kulo muzi zihlome ziyizingovolo zatshela uMnuz Vusi Gina ukuthi azizile ukuzodlala kodwa zizosebenza.
Kuthiwa zingene ngamawindi zashaqa wonke umuntu obesendlini okubalwa nosana olunezinsuku luzelwe.
Uthe babalayishe ezimotweni zalo mndeni, bahamba nabo beboshiwe.
"Asazi ngempela ukuthi ngobani laba abangaze basicabangele into ebuhlungu kanjena.
Namanje sisathukile kakhulu.
Ngiyazibuza ukuthi ngempela yini le engaka esiyonile kubani?""
kubalisa uMnuz Gina.
Uthe bonke balaxazwe endlini emnyama emzini abangawazi, bavalelwa izinsuku ezintathu bengadli futhi bengaphuzi lutho.
Nosana bathi belukhala lukhalile.
Kula malungu omndeni kubalwa unkosikazi wakhe, izingane ezine namanye amalungu.
UGina uthi ngenhlanhla bonke bakwazile ukweqa lapho abebethunjwe khona, uthi babuzile ukuthi yikuphi kule ndawo, batshelwa ukuthi baseHlabazini, eManguzi.
"Kubantu esibuze kubona basitshele ukuthi siseManguzi.
Siyabonga ukuthi sonke sibuye siphephile,"" kusho uGina.
Ubabaza unya lwezigilamkhuba lokungabi nanozwelo lokuthi bathumbe nosana oluncane.
UGina uthe inhliziyo yakhe iyabalisa ngemoto yakhe abayebile, waveza ukuthi lezi zigilamkhuba zintshontshe izimoto ezimbili.
Eyodwa uthi amaphoyisa ayitholile.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa eKwaZulu Natal, uColonel Thembeka Mbele usiqisekisile isigameko.
Uthe leli cala lisaphenywa.
Uthe kusolakala ukuthi kube nezigilamkhuba ezihlasele umndeni wakwaGina.
"Kusolakala ukuthi umndeni waseMange, eMkhuze uhlaselwe ngabantu abebehlomile.
Babathumbile beba nezimoto.
Enye yezimoto igcine itholakala eManguzi,"" kusho uCol Mbele.
Kubhekwe isimemezelo ngesihlalo sobukhosi
WONKE amehlo abheke indlunkulu ukuba imemezele ukuthi kuzokwenzekalani ngesihlalo sobukhosi bakwaZulu ngemva kokutshalwa kwebamba bukhosi, iNdlovukazi Shiyiwe Mantfombi Dlamini Zulu.
Indlovukazi itshalwe entathakusa namhlanje ngokohlelo obeluyimfihlo.
Akucaci ukuthi uzomenyezelwa nini ozongena esihlalweni sobukhosi njengoba undunankulu kaZulu, Inkosi Mangosuthu Buthelezi, esanda kunxusa isizwe ukuthi singayifakeli ingcindezi indlunkulu ukuthi yenze isimemezelo.
Izolo amalungu asendlunkulu abevalelene emhlanganweni okukholakala ukuthi bekubhungwa ngalo lolu daba.
Indlovukazi eguqile ibilokhu ibambile esihlalweni selokhu kwabuza iSilo samabandla onke uGoodwill Zwelithini kaBhekuzulu, owaguqa ngoMashi.
Bekuphithizela esigodlweni kwaKhangelamankengane izolo njengoba bekuqhubeka amalungiselelo okutshalwa kwendlovukazi.
Amabutho nezintombi basine bededelana esigodlweni, beyovalelisa okokugcina kwindlovukazi ngaphambi kokuthi itshalwe ezintathakusa namhlanje.
Kubonakale amaqembu ehlukene amabutho kanye nezintombi ehaya amahubo, ekhuza neziqubulo.
Bekukhona nabavela eSwatini, lapho kuzalwa khona indlovukazi.
Indlovukazi izalwa iNgonyama yamaSwati eseyakhothama, uSobhuza wesibili, kanti ingudadewabo wenkosi ebusayo uMswati wesithathu.
AbaseSwatini bathe baphoxekile ngokuguqa kwendlovukazi abathe bebenethemba lokuthi izokwazi ukucija ozongena esihlalweni esishiywe yiSilo samabandla onke uGoodwill Zwelithini kaBhekuzulu, njengoba indlovukazi ibiyibamba bukhosi.
Ukutshalwa kwendlovukazi kube yimfihlo futhi bekuhanjelwe ngamalungu asendlunkulu, abasebukhosini bamaSwati kanye nabakhethiweyo.
Izolo izintombi zizwakalise ukukhathazeka ngekusasa lomkhosi womhlanga owavuselelwa yindlovukazi, kodwa lathi lizokulwela ukuthi lomkhosi ungafi.
Amalungu eqembu Izinyosi, athe afuna ukuthi leli siko lingashabalali.
Ilungu leqembu uNksz Mningi Zuma, ongumphathi wamatshitshi KwaNongoma, lithe isiko liyasiza ukunqanda ukukhulelwa kwezintombi zisencane.
"Sifuna ukuthi nabalandela emva kwethu balifice leli siko.
"Amalungu eqembu athe indlovukazi azoyikhumbula ngothando ebinalo kwizintombi zomhlanga.
"Ibihlale ikhona lapho kukhona izintombi," kusho uNksz Nokwethemba Nxumalo.
UNksz Nelile Nxumalo, uthe njengendlela yokuhlonipha indlovukazi, bazoqhubeka nokuzigcina.
Ngaphambi kokuthi ifihlwe, kube nenkonzo ebihanjalwe abakhethekile.
Namhlanje kuzokuba nenkonzo yesikhumbuzo esezingeni likahulumeni wesifundazwe.
Undunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal uMnuz Sihle Zikalala kulindeleke ukuthi athule inkulumo yosuku.
Bashiywa ehlathini emva kokuthathelwa izimoto zabo eManguzi
USATHUKILE namanje umndeni waseManguzi eNsukumbili owangenelwa yizigebengu eziyisithupha zihlomile, zifuna ukhiye wemoto.
Bathi loku sekujwayelekile kule ndawo.
Owesilisa (ocele ukuba igama lakhe ligodlwe) uthi imoto yakhe isikhonjwa eMozambique.
Akuyena yedwa ozwa lobu buhlungu.
"Izigilamkhuba zangena ngisathi ngiyadla.
Zabuza ukuthi yini ndaba sibe bahlanu ngoba siyisithupha lapha endlini," kubeka owesilisa.
Uqhube wathi izigilamkhuba zababopha izandla, bathathwa bayohlaliswa egunjini elilodwa.
"Bapequlula endlini bathatha uR2000, bafuna enye imali umama wekhaya wabanika uR300.
Bathatha ukudla, amaselula, ama-laptop, iTV nayo yonke igilosa.
"Uthi wazikhalela wacela ukuba babashiye nokudla okuncane ngoba usuku lomholo lwaluseduze, banqaba.
Uthi okunye okwenza asabe wukuthi bambuza ukuthi iphi enye i-laptop ngoba mabili.
Uthi emva kwalokho izigebengu zathatha izingubo zokulala namajakhethi afudumele, kwathiwa mabangene emotweni yakhe.
Bahamba naye nomndeni wakhe baze bafika endaweni eyihlathi.
"Bafika basibopha izinyawo, mina ngaboshelwa esihlahleni, basimbathisa bathi kabafuni ukuthi sigodole futhi njengoba besishiya la ehlathini akekho umuntu ozosithola nendlela eya ekhaya ngeke siyazi.
""Emva kokuba sebehambile sazama ukuziqaqa kwaze kwalunga, sangena indlela ngoba vele ngangiyazi le ndawo.
Samisa imoto yamaphoyisa eyayidlula, sawachazela ngosekwenzekile.
Abuza ukuthi siyaphi, ngasho ukuthi siya kwamngani wami.
Asithatha amaphoyisa asishiya ngakhona,"Ngenkathi beya esiteshini samaphoyisa bafika batshelwa ukuthi amaphoyisa asemzini wakhe ngoba untshontshelwe imoto, okuyikona athi kwamdida.
Uthi okwamphatha kabi wukungafiki kwamaphoyisa ezothatha amanyela eminwe.
Uthe amaphoyisa amtshela ukuthi akukho angakwenza ngemoto ngoba isiweliswe umngcele.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe kuvulwe icala lokubamba inkunzi esiteshini samaphoyisa esiseManguzi.
Omunye okuthiwa wehlelwa yileli shwa kodwa ongathandanga negama lakhe, uthe uyesaba ukwenzakaliswa, ngeke akwazi ukuphawula ngalolu daba.
Imizamo yokuthola ikhansela lendawo ibhuntshile, belingayiphenduli imiyalezo, nocingo lukhala lungabanjwa.
Zimisiwe ezemidlalo ezikoleni zakuleli
PHILI MJOLIUMNYANGO weMfundo eyisiSekelo izolo umemezele ukuthi zizomiswa ezemidlalo ezikoleni zakuleli, njengoba zinyuka izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19.
UMnuz Elijah Mhlanga okhulumela umnyango, uthe lesi sinqumo sithathwe wumkhandlu wongqongqoshe bezemfundo kuleli emhlanganweni wakamuva.
Uthe isinqumo sithathwe ngemuva kokuthi kube nabafundi abayisikhombisa okubikwe ukuthi bebedlala imidlalo eyenza ukuthi bathintane nabanye, kumbe bathintene nabafundi abenza le midlalo okutholakale ukuthi baneCovid-19.
UMhlanga uthe eminye imidlalo engenzi ukuthi abantu bathintane isazoqhubeka kodwa kumele kuqashelwe ukuthi abafundi abasondelani.
"Kumele kube nesiqiniseko sokuthi kunebanga elidingekayo phakathi kwabadlala leyo midlalo nangesikhathi sokuzilolonga," kusho uMhlanga.
Ngeledlule isishoshovu sezemfundo uMnuz Hendrick Makaneta, saphakamisa ukuthi ezemidlalo zimiswe okwesikhashana njengoba izwe libhekene nesivuvu sesithathu seCovid-19.
UMakaneta wathi izibalo zabahaqwa yigciwane zizokwenyuka njengoba kungena ubusika, ngakho ukuvumela abafundi ukuthi badlale imidlalo eyenza ukuthi bathintane, kungaba ubudedengu.
Imidlalo ethintekayo ibhola lezinyawo, ibhola lombhoxo, umkhalambazo neminye.
Ngesikhathi kuvulwa izikole umnyango wezemfundo washicilela emqingweni kahulumeni imigomo okumele ilandelwe uma izikole zivula ezemidlalo.
"Ngesonto lokugcina lekota yokuqala yokufunda nasekuqaleni kwekota yesibili kube nabafundi okutholakale ukuthi sebehaqekile, eGauteng.
Izibalo bezilokhu zikhula.
Lokhu kusitshela ukuthi ingozi ikhona nakuba kunemigomo ebekiwe elandelwayo yezokuphepha.
Ngokwemibiko esinayo le midlalo inomthelela wokuthi igciwane lisabalale," kusho uMhlanga.
USolwazi Andre De Bruyn wenyuvesi yaseStellenbosch, uthe okubalulekile kulesi sikhathi esibhekene naso, ukuphepha yize ezemidlalo zibalulekile ezikoleni.
"Uma kubonakala ukuthi kunamathuba amaningi okuthi ezemidlalo ezithize zisabalalise iCovid-19 kumele zimiswe," kusho uSolwazi.
Izinhlelo ngentsha ethole iziqu kwezolimo
KUNETHEMBA lokuthi abafundi asebefunde bagogoda emkhakheni wezolimo, bazoziqalela izinkampani zezolimo ukuze kwande abantu abasha kulo mkhakha.
UNgqongqoshe wezoLimo KwaZulu-Natal, uNkk Sithole -Moloi, usho kanje ngoLwesihlanu ngesikhathi ethwesa izitshudeni eziwu-122, eseziphothule iziqu kwezolimo ekolishi lezolimo i-Owen Sithole.
Uthe abalimi abaningi KwaZulu -Natal sebebadala ngakho bayadingeka abantu abasha abazoqhubeka kuwo lo mkhakha.
"Umkhakha unabantu abaningi abaneminyaka engu-55 kuya phezulu ngakho siyabadinga abantu abasha abazokwenza ukuthi lo mkhakha uqhubeke kahle ngoba kuzobe kunabantu abasha abazobe bekhula kuwo," kusho uNgqongqoshe.
Uthe kulaba abaphothule iziqu bayafisa ukuthi babathathe ukuze babasize ohlelweni lomnyango, lokuthuthukisa indlela yokufuya emakhaya, njengoba lo nyaka waziwa njengowokufuya.
"Sifuna ukuthi izitshdeni zisize imiphakathi yasemakhaya ngokuhlola amadiphu ukuthi ngabe asesimeni esidingakalayo, babheke nezifo ezikhona emfuyweni nokuthi zingelashwa kanjani ukuze abantu bakithi bezokwazi ukuba nemfuyo esezingeni eliyilo bakwazi nokuyidayisa ezimakethe," kusho yena.
Uthe olunye uhlelo abanalo olusiza abaphothule kulo mkhakha ngokuthi babatholele amapulazi abazokwenza kuwo uqeqesho ukuze bathole isipiliyoni.
Izitshudeni ezithweswe iziqu uthe abaphothule ngo-2020 nango-2021 bonke bathole ama-diploma emikhakheni ehlukene yezolimo.
"Bakhona abavele besohlelweni lwethu lokuthatha izitshudeni eseziphothulile.
Abanye babo bafake izicelo zokuthola umhlaba ukuze baziqalele izinhlelo zokulima, kuzo bayakwazi ukuqasha abanye kuphinde kwenyuke nesibalo sabakhiqizi bokudla kulesi sifundazwe," kusho yena.
UNksz Sphelele Ngema (23) obenza iDiploma in Crop Production nyakenye ophase ngamalengiso, uthe ubengalindele ukuthi angaphasa adlule zonke izitshudeni kodwa ubazi ukuthi uzophasa kahle ngoba uyazimisela.
Uthe uphase ngamalengiso izifundo eziyisihlanu wase echonywa uphaphe lwegwalagwala."
Ngijabule kakhulu okwamanje angikasebenzi, kulo nyaka bengenza i-Advanced Diploma in Crop Production eMangosuthu University of Technology (MUT)," kusho uNksz Ngema.
Uhleli endlini ewayo umndeni wesishoshovu se-ANC
EMUVA kweminyaka engu-38 kwabulawa isishoshovu se-ANC esasilwela amalungelo abantu, ikakhulukazi abaseLamontville, ayengaphansi kokwakubizwa ngoMkhandlu waseNingizimu, umndeni waso usabhuqabhuqwa yindlala endlini yomxhaso ewayo.
Uma kuthintwa umlando wezombusazwe wakuleli, kalisali ngaphandle igama lesishoshovu esinguMnuz Msizi Harrison Dube esabulawa ngokudutshulwa ngo-Ephreli 25 ngo-1983.
Leli phephandaba selithintwe kaningi ngabantu abahlukene mayelana nesimo somuzi okuhleli kuwona amalungu omndeni wesishoshovu esinguDube, bekhala ngehlazo lesimo indlu eyisona.
Wumuzi onamagumbi amabili, wakhiwe phezu kwesitamukoko.
Abake bangena ngaphakathi bathi endlini encane akukho ngisho umsele odonsa amanzi uma kade begeza, okuphoqeleka ukuthi basebenzise indishi bese bewachitha emnyango amanzi.
Isiqubulo esithi Asinamali okwaze kwenziwa ngaso umdlalo weshashalazi kaMbongeni Ngema, saqanjwa nguDube elwa nohulumeni wobandlululo owawuhlongoza ukunyuswa kwentela emalokishini ayengekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni waKwaZulu omdala.
Indodana kaDube, uMnuz Vusi Dube, okuyiyona ehlala kule ndlu ithembise ukubuyela entathelini kodwa kwashicilelwa ingabuyeli.
Kuthiwa selokhu bafakwa ngo-2005 kule ndlu ngoba bethenjiswe ukuthi basazokwakhelwa kabusha kodwa nonina uze washona besalinde ukususwa endlini.
Ethintwa uMnuz Nhlakanipho Ntombela, okhulumela i-ANC KwaZulu-Natal, uthe uqala ukuluzwa ngentatheli lolu daba.
"Sizocela ukuxhunyaniswa nelungu lomndeni ukuze silulandele ngendlela lolo daba.
Kodwa ngabe nginamanga uma ngithi sake saluzwa phambilini," usho kanje.
Ukubulawa kukaMsizi Dube kwaholela ekuqubukeni kwemibhikisho nasemalokishini ayakhele iLamontville njengoMlaza, Clermont, Chesterville naKwaMashu.
Namhlanje kuleli lokishi, kunomgwaqo oqanjwe ngokuthi uMsizi Dube Road nesikole iMsizi Dube Primary.
Ithala lifuna ukuba yibhange likahulumeni jikelele
ISIKHULU esiphezulu seBhange Ithala, uDkt Thulani Vilakazi, sithi kasikho isidingo sokuthi uhulumeni aqale phansi izinhlelo zokwakha ibhange likahulumeni ngoba Ithala kade laliwenza lowo msebenzi..UVikalazi usho lokhu emuva kokuthi uMnyango wezeziMali uveze ukuthi kawukaziqedi izinhlelo zokusungula ibhange likahulumeni jikelele yize sekuphele iminyaka ewu-10 uzama ukulakha.
"Ithala kade laqala ukusebenza njengebhange likahulumeni, elikudingayo wukwaziwa njengebhange likahulumeni ngokusemthethweni.
Asikho isidingo sokuthi uhulumeni aqalaze kwezinye izindawo ngoba Ithala liyawenza lo msebenzi.
Siyibhange likahulumeni elinelayisensi yokwenza wonke umsebenzi wamabhange ajwayelekile," kusho uVilakazi.
Uveze ukuthi Ithala likulungele ukuba yibhange likahulumeni nokuguqula impilo yabantu baseNingizimu Afrika, ikakhulukazi labo akade bengakwazi ukufinyelela ezinsizeni zezimali, abale kubo abahlala emakhaya.
"Ukusungulwa kwebhange likahulumeni kuzosiza ukuqeda ukungalingani, okwadalwa wubandlululo.
Kuzosiza imiphakathi ebingafinyeleli kwezezimali.
Ithala lisekwa wuhulumeni waKwaZulu-Natal ukuthi libe yibhange likahulumeni.
Lineminyaka ewu-60 likulo mkhakha futhi lingasiza kakhulu ekuqedeni ububha, ukungalingani nokungasebenzi," kusho uVilakazi.
Uphethe ngokuthi ukusiza kwabo imiphakathi yasemakhaya kukhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi bayahambisana nezinhlelo zikahulumeni, zokuthuthukisa umnotho, ngakho uma sebeyibhange likahulumeni akukho okuzobahlula.
Angikaze ngimkhaphele uZuma: Gigaba
SIHLE MAVUSOEMUVA kweminyaka aphefumula kwiCNN owayengungqongqoshe weziMali noMnyango wezaseKhaya, uMnuz Malusi Gigaba, ngodaba lowayengumengameli wezwe uMnuz Jacob Zuma lokuthi makenze okufanele, ugcine ephefumulile izolo ukuthi wayeqondeni.
Enkulumweni ekhethelekile nezintatheli ze-Independent Media, eThekwini ngoLwesibili, uthe ayekusho wabe esekuchazela uZuma eNkandla, emuva kwale nkulumo yakhe, ikakhulukazi njengoba abalandeli bakaZuma basola ukuthi lokhu kukhuluma kwakhe kwakufana nokukhuluma kabi ngomholi, ekubeni wambeka esikhundleni sokuba ngungqongqoshe weziMali phezu kokuba izimakethe zazifuna kuqhubeke uMnuz Pravin Gordhan.
UGigaba wasolwa ngokuthi lokhu wakwenza ezincengela kowayezongena ebe nguMengameli uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, nakuba kwakucaca ukuthi uGigaba uzosuswa esikhundleni uma umbuso kaZuma uphela.
Ngesikhathi kuba nale nkulumo uZuma wayethwele kanzima, ephansi kwengcindezi.
Iqembu lalimfuna ukuba asule kwesokuba ngumengameli.
Le nkulumo kaGigaba yezwakala sengathi uthi uZuma makenze okufanele, ngokuthi asule esikhundleni.
Ababengamuzwa kahle uGigaba ngo-2018, basebenzisa le nkulumo yakhe bemfakela ingcindezi ngoNovemba 2018, ukuthi makasule ekubeni ngungqongqoshe woMnyango wezaseKhaya, enze okufanele.
UGigaba ngokwakhe, uthi kwakungekhona ukukhaphela uZuma njengoba abanye babecabanga kanjalo.
Kule nkulumo noGigaba, osesebenza eLuthuli House njengomunye wabantu abahlela imigomo, ukhulume ngezinto eziningi.
Uthe ukhathazekile ngezinsolo ezenziwe asezohlukanisa naye umshado noNkk Nomachule Mngoma, ukuthi wasebenzisa amandla akhe ukumbophisa koKlebe.
Uthe oKlebe bathinteka kulolu daba ngoba babevele bephenya udaba.
Uthe uNksz Mngoma ngesikhathi elimaza iMercedes-Benz yomngani wakhe, uMnuz Pieterson Siyaya, oKlebe babizwa ngoba kwakuwudaba olubucayi.
UNksz Mngoma uthintiwe ngalolu daba, wathi uzobuye aphawule.
I-Corona inyomfe izinhlelo zabeseka uMagashule
UKUDLANGA kobhubhane iCorona eGauteng, kufake unyawo lwedada ezinhlelweni zabalandeli bakaNobhala Jikelele we-ANC osamisiwe, uMnuz Ace Magashule, zokuyomeseka enkantolo namhlanje nakusasa.
Ukungena kwalesi sifundazwe ngaphansi kwesivuvu sesithathu sobhubhane nokufakwa kwezwe ngaphansi kwesigaba sesithathu somvalelandlini, kubhuntshise izinhlelo zezinkumbi zabalandeli bakaMagashule zokuyomeseka ngaphandle kweNkantolo eNkulu yaseJohannesburg namhlanje.
Leli cala elilalelwa ngamajaji amathathu namhlanje nakusasa, bekulindeleke ukuthi lihehe izinkumbi zabalandeli be-ANC abeseka uMagashule.
Omunye wabalandeli bakaMagashule, uMnuz Nkosentsha Shezi, nofake isicelo sokuba yingxenye yaleli cala lapho ezokube eseka isicelo sikaMagashule, ukuqinisekisile ukubhuntsha kwezinhlelo zabalandeli bakaMagashule.
"Njengoba izwe lisesigabeni sesithathu somvalelandlini, kusiphoqile ukuba sichithe izinhlelo zokuthutha abalandeli.
Besinezinhlelo zokubathutha ngamabhasi, besuka ezindaweni ezahlukene.
Kepha manje silindele abambalwa ikakhulukazi njengoba nenkantolo ivele isimemezele ukuthi icala lizolalelwa kusetshenziswa ezobuchwepheshe.
"UShezi uthe ukungabi khona kwabalandeli abaningi ngaphandle kwenkantolo namhlanje nakusasa kuzokube kungachazi ukuthi sebenciphile abantu abeseka uMagashule.
"Sesekwa yizigidi zabantu abathi bona bakhathele yinkohlakalo eqhutshwa wuhulumeni ophethe njengamanje.
Abasebenzi bakahulumeni ophethe njengamanje bantshontsha ngisho imali yokuthenga izinsiza zokuvikela ubhubhane iCorona.
"UShezi ukuqinisekisile ukuthi uzokuba yingxenye yecala lapho ezokuba eseka isicelo esifakwe uMagashule.
Kulesi sicelo, uMagashule uphonsela inselelo ukumiswa kwakhe wuKhongolose.
UMagashule uphinde enze isicelo sokuba ithathwe njengesemthethweni incwadi yokumiswa kukamengameli wale nhlangano, uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, ayibhala.
UMagashule wanikela enkantolo emva kwesinqumo sokumiswa kwakhe yi-ANC, okwenzeke sekudlule umnqamulajuqu wezinsuku ezingu-30 ayewunikwe yisigungu esiphezulu se-ANC, sokuba yena nabanye abaholi ababhekene namacala bashenxe ezikhundleni.
UMagashule ungaphandle ngebheyili njengoba aboshelwa icala lethenda kaR255 million yokushintshwa kophahla lwezindlu ezifulelwe ngetsheboya eFree State, eyakhishwa ngesikhathi esengundunankulu wakulesiya sifundazwe.
Emaphepheni asenkantolo, uMagashule uthi lo mgomo wabekwa ngoba kuliwa naye.
Wathi lo mgomo unyathela amalungelo akhe, okuthi umsulwa kuze kube inkantolo ikhipha isigwebo ecaleni lenkohlakalo asolwa ngalo.
Encwadini ayibhala neyachithwa yi-ANC, uMagashule wathi umisa uRamaphosa ngenxa yokuthi uyasoleka ezenzweni zenkohlakalo.
UMagashule wathi uRamaphosa usoleka enkohlakalweni yokugwazela izithunywa engqungqutheleni ye-ANC yango-2017, ukuba zimvotele esikhundleni sokuba wumengameli wale nhlangano.
Le ncwadi uMagashule wayibhala emva kokuba kuputshuke incwadi emmisa emsebenzi.
Kwethulwe amabhasi azolekelela abantu abathungatha imisebenzi
UKUBHEDUKA kwegciwane iCovid-19 nokufadabala komnotho kulahlekisele ngomsebenzi owesilisa osenenqola ahamba edayisa ngayo imithi yokubulala amaphela, amagundane nokhula enkabeni yedolobha iNewcastle.
UNjabulo Mntambo (27) wase-Osizweni, uhlangana naye emigwaqweni eqhuba inqola yakhe ememeza ngenhloso yokudonsa amehlo amakhasimende akhe ikhona ezothenga.
UMntambo ungomonye wabantu abangu-32.
6% baseNingizimu Afika abangasebenzi.
Uthi udonsa kanzima njengoba, ethanda engathandi, kumele adayise ukuze azothola imali yokuthenga okuya ethunjini"Sidiliziwe emsebenzini ngonyaka odlule ngenxa yeCovid-19.
Besisebenzela inkampani ebisikela uMasipala waseNewcastle utshani.
Isimo sinzima yingakho ngidayisa le mithi.
Ngithola uR70 ngosuku ngicoshacoshe esizolala sikudlile ekhaya," kusho uMntambo.
UMnuz Philani Khumalo waseDannhauser, uthe akasazihluphi ngokufaka izicelo zomsebenzi okuyinto athe sekuphele iminyaka engu-10 eyenza ngale kwenhlanhla.
Uthi sewakhetha ukuzokwenza umsebenzi wokupakisa izimoto edolobheni kunokuthi ahlale phansi, aphile ngokucela.
"Uma sikhala kubaholi ababhekelele izinhlelo zentsha sicela imisebenzi, kufana nokuthi siyadlala.
Asinakwa nhlobo," kusho uKhumalo.
Lokhu kufakazelwe uMnuz Sipho Masondo othe uselilahlile ithemba lokuthi uyoke aqashwe, asebenze.
"Imisebenzi yesikhashana engamatoho ikhishelwa abangani nezihlobo zabaholi.
Sifike sivolontiye, ekugcineni kuqashwe abantu esingabazi.
Sesikhathele ukwenza amaCV, sifake izicelo zomsebenzi ngemali yokugcina," kusho uMasondo.
Laba abathathu bebemi buqamama ngoLwesibili, bebukela uNgqongqoshe wezokuQasha nezemiSebenzi, uMnuz Thulas Nxesi beneMeya yaseMajuba, uDkt Musa Ngubane, bethula ihhovisi elinezinhlelo abahlose ngazo ukucija intsha ngamakhono futhi ilekelelwe ekuyifuniseni imisebenzi.
Kuphinde kwethulwa amabhasi amabili aphendulwe aba ngamahhovisi angomahamba nendlwana aseMnywangweni weziSebenzi.
Lolu hlelo lamabhasi oluzonabela kuzona zonke izifunda, luzodla uhulumeni uR84 million.
La mabhasi amabili ethulwe izolo, azozulazula emiphakathini eyakhele Amajuba ngezikhathi ezithile nangezinsuku ezizomenyezelwa ngenhloso yokusondeza izinsiza zalo mnyango kubantu.
UNxesi ukhale ngokuntuleka kwamakhono, ukufadabala komnotho okubhebhethekiswe ukubheduka kweCovid-19 njengembangela eholele ekupheleni kwemisebenzi.
Ukhombe ngenjumbane uhlelo lwemfundo ukuthi alubaniki abantu amakhono anele emisebenzi adingekayo esikhathini samanje.
"Umuntu uya enyuvesi kodwa aphume engenalo ikhono lokwenza ugesi, afake amanzi noma enze umsebenzi wezandla.
Uma kufuneka abantu abanamakhono ale misebenzi, kuqhamuka ikhehla elidala lomlungu.
Uma kungumuntu omnyama, kuba ovela ezwenikazi i-Afrika," kusho uNxesi.
UNgubane ubonge wanconcoza kuNxesi nomnyango wakhe ngamabhasi.
Uthe bazokwakha uhlelo lokuthi isigceme ngasinye eNewcastle, eMadlangeni naseDannhauser ifike ibhasi kusona ukuze abantu basizakale eduze.
UCele uxwayisa  amakhansela avula amacala angekho
AZOBOSHWA amakhansela avula amacala okuzama ukubulala angekho emaphoyiseni, athi ahlaselwe ekubeni ezihlasele wona ngoba efuna ukunikwa abaqaphi nguhulumenAmakhansela adonswe ngendlebe nguNgqongqoshe wamaPhoyisa, uMnuz Bheki Cele, obethula umbiko wekomiti eliphenya amacala athinta ukubulawa kosopolitiki KwaZulu-Natal eseThekwini, ngoLwesithathu.
Esithangamini bekukhona uMnuz Zizi Kodwa oyiPhini likaNgqongqoshe wezokuPhepha koMbuso, uKhomishana wamaphoyisa kuzwelonke uGeneral Khehla Sitole nowesifundazwe, uLieutenant General Nhlanhla Mkhwanazi, umphathi woKlebe kuzwelonke uLt General Godfrey Lebeya nabanye.
UCele uthe azohlangana nezimbila zithutha ziholwa ngemhlophe phambili amakhansela nosopilitiki abaqhubeka nokwenza le migilingwane.
Uqhube wathi amanye ala makhansela azama ukuzidubula, amanye akhulume kumaselula awo nabanye abantu, ethi ahlaselwe ukuze athole ukugadwa.
"Sekukhona amakhansela aboshelwe lo mkhuba.
Badlala ngezinsiza nesikhathi samaphoyisa, okumele ngabe enza umsebenzi wawo ngabantu abafuna ukuduma.
Elinye ikhansela lazidubula ehlombe nge-AK47," kusho uCele.
UCele uthe kuzokwengezwa isibalo samaphoyisa, imali nesikhathi azosisebenza esifundazweni njengoba kubhekwe okhethweni.
Uthe njengamanje bahlezi phansi baqhamuka nezindlela ezizosetshenziswa ukuze kungabi bikho ukuchitheka kwegazi njengoba kubhekwe okhethweni lohulumeni basekhaya ngo-Okthoba 27 nonyaka.
Izibalo ezethulwe nguCele izolo, ziveza ukuthi kwehle kakhulu ukubulawa kosopolitiki KwaZulu-Natal kulo nyaka, bane kuphela, kwaboshwa ababili ngakho.
Ngo-2016 kwabulawa osopolitiki abangu-31, ngo-2017 bawu-20, ngo-2018 babangu-12 ngo- 2019, bawu-14, ngo-2020 babengu-14.
Kusukela ngo-2018 kusungulwa leli komiti, kuboshwe abantu abangu-251.
Kulesi sibalo bawu-46 abalahlwe ngamacala okuthe abangu-30 kubona batholwa benamacala okubulala.
Emacaleni awu-34 okubulala, kukhishwe odilikajele abayisishiyagalolunye.
Abasolwa abangu-22 banikwe isigwebo seminyaka ephakathi kuka-10 no-50.
Abanye abasolwa abangu-12 balahlwe ngamacala banikwa iminyaka engaphansi kuka-10.
Kukhona nabanye abasagqigqa ezinkantolo.
Ubalule amacala ayisishiyagalolumbili okusocongwa kosopoitiki aba sematheni.
Uthe lizoqala ngoJulayi 21 nonyaka icala lokubulawa kowayikhansela le-ANC, uMnuz Qashana Mchunu, okuboshwe kulona abasolwa abayisikhombisa.
Elokubulawa kukaMnuz Sandiso Magaqa lingena enkantolo ngo-Jalayi 19, 2021.
Bayisishiyagalombili abasolwa ababoshelwe leli cala.
Amadoda amabili asolwa ngokubulala uMnuz Wandile Ngobeni, avela ngoNovemba 12, 2021 enkantolo.
NgoNovemba 22 nonyaka lingene enkantolo elokubulawa kwelungu le-IFP, uMnuz Sibuyiselo Phineas Dlamini.
Abasolwa ngokubulala owayeyikhansela le-ANC, uMnuz Sibusiso Mphumulo bazovela enkantolo ngoMeyi 2 ngonyaka ozayo, kuthi elokubulawa kowayengumqondisi kuMasipala i-Alfred Duma, uMnuz Oscar Hlatshwayo, liqale ngo-Agasti 16 nonyaka.
UCele uveze nokuthi bashaqe izibhamu ezingaphezu kuka-200 emkhankasweni wabo wokuthungatha izibhamu ezingekho emthethweni njengoba engu-107 asezinkantolo ngakho.
Kushaqeke umndeni kutholwa osizayo entanta emanzini
USHAQEKILE umnikazi womuzi ngokufa kowesifazane obengumsebenzi wasendlini yakhe amfice entanta kwi-swimming pool eMatabetulu, eNanda, ngoMsombuluko ekuseni.
UMnu Sicelo Nzimande usola ukuthi umufi ukhubekile wawela kwi-swimming pool ngoba bamthole egqoke ephelele izingubo namasokisi kodwa ophaqa bentanta naye emanzini.
UNzimande uthi ufike kwakhe ngo-11 ekuseni ezoshiya indodakazi yakhe abeyilande esikoleni iqeda ukubhala wafica uNksz Nobuhle Ndlovu (46) eminzile.
UNzimande ulandise wathi yena nomkakhe nezingane ezimbili ezifundayo bahambe ekhaya ekuseni kwase kufika uNksz Ndlovu eze emsebenzini njengenjwayelo.
Uthe umufi ubesebabenzele unyaka nezinyanga ekhetha izinsuku, eza ngoMsombuluko, uLwesithathu nangoLwesihlanu engena ngo-7:30 ekuseni ephuma u-4:30 ntambama.
Uqhube wathi umufi ubenokhiye wakhe abengena ngawo kulesi sithabathaba somuzi oyisitezi afike asebenze bese eyagoduka ntambama abuyele emndenini wakhe eStop 8, eNanda.
"Kuthe uma ngivula isango lemoto ngisondela, ngabona kunento emnyama emanzini.
Sengiseduze ngibonile ukuthi uNksz Ndlovu, ngathuka, ngavele ngafonela amaphoyisa.
Sibe sesithinta nomndeni kamufi ngaphambi kokuthi akhishwe emanzini khona uzozibonela nawo lesi sehlo esibuhlungu kangaka," kusho uNzimande.
Uthe kungenzeka ukuthi umufi ushelelile waphonseka wase ehluleka ukubhukuda aphume kule swimming pool engu-1.
8 metres ukujula kwayo.
Uthe umufi ubeyedwa kwehla lo mshophi futhi bafike endlini izinto zisenjengoba bezishiye zinjalo ekuseni, ukhiye uNksz Ndlovu angena ngawo ulenga esicabheni.
Indodakazi kamufi, uNksz Tholakele Ndlovu ithe ishayisa amakhala indlela okushona ngayo unina.
Ithe ubegqoke ephelele unina futhi isidumbu sakhe simi phuhle emanzini singavundlile okomuntu ominzile.
Iqhube yathi abazi bazongcwaba ngani ngoba unina kuphela obekade esebenza emndenini.
"Sifike sekukhona amaphoyisa sambona engakakhishwa emanzini kwase kuthiwa asihambe.
Sithe sizohamba uma sekufike imoto yezidumbu nebala efike yamthatha.
Sisola isandla somuntu ekufeni kukamama, ukhona omphushele ku-swimming pool," kusho uNksz Ndlovu.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uColonel Thembeka Mbele, uthe kuvulwe idokodo ngokushona komuntu eliphenywa ngamaphoyisa asesiteshini saseNanda.
I-Pepkor itshale uR1.5 billion KwaZulu-Natal
UNDUNANKULU waKwaZulu-Natal uSihle Zikalala, uthe izofukula umnotho futhi idale nenqwaba yamathuba omsebenzi ezindaweni ezakhele iPinetown intuthuko kaR1.
5 billion elethwa yiPepkor, eHammarsdale.
UZikalala wethule ngokusemthethweni le ntuthuko eseKeystone Business Park ngoLwesibili wathi kuyamjabulisa ukubona kwenzeka into eNtshonalanga yeTheku emuva kokuvalwa kwezimboni eziningi ngeminyaka yawo-1990 nango-2000.
UZikalala uthe intuthuko yemboni yakwaPepkor izodala amathuba omsebenzi awu-2 200, kanti kuyimanje eKeystone Business Park kuqashwe abantu abawu-5 600.
"Kuyasijabulisa ukubona intuthuko iza eNtshonalanga yeTheku emuva kokuvalwa kwezimboni eminyakeni edlule.
Le ntuthuko elethwa yiPepkor izovusa umnotho, idale amathuba omsebenzi igqugquzele nabanye abatshali zimali ukuthi beze ngapha.
Izokwandisa nempahla engena echwebeni laseThekwini ngo-30%.
Iyingxenye yentuthuko yaseCato Ridge," kusho uZikalala.
Uthe uma isiphelele intuthuko yaseKeystone Business Park, izofaka uR6 billion emnothweni waKwaZulu-Natal.
Ubuye waveza nokuthi i-Aquelle izoletha ingxenye yomsebenzi wayo eKeystone Business Park.
UNgqongqoshe wezokuThuthukiswa koMnotho, ezokuVakasha neMvelo KwaZulu-Natal uMnuz Ravi Pillay, uthe le ntuthuko ikhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi isifundazwe sikulungele ukusebenza nosomabhizinisi.
Ubonge osomabhizinisi abathanda izwe labo ngokuqhubeka nokutshala imali emnothweni waKwaZulu-Natal ukuze kusimame umnotho, kuqashwe nabantu.
Ucele iPepkor ukuthi yandise impahla eyithenga ezimbonini zakuleli ukuze kusimame umkhakha wendwangu nempahla.
Isikhulu seRokwil esungule iKeystone Business Park, uMnuz Rod Stanton, sigqugquzele osomabhizinisi ukuthi batshale imali yabo emnothweni waseNingizimu Afrika.
UStanton uthe uhulumeni uzivulile izandla ukusebenzisana nosomabhizinisi nokwakha isimo esenza kube lula ukuqhuba ibhizinisi.
Uthembise ukuthi bazomlandela uZikalala ezinhlelweni zokuthuthukisa umnotho.
Othisha basebenza ukuphipha abafundi
KUMA nse ukufunda nokufundisa esikoleni samabanga aphansi KwaMaphumulo, lapho othisha beshintshana ngokuphipha nokugada izingane ezincane uma ziyozikhulula ngenxa yobungozi bezindlu zangasese.
I-OTimati Primary, okungesinye sezikole ezinabafundi abaningi kule ndawo njengoba bengu-600, kuvela ukuthi sekuphele iminyaka engaphezulu kwewu-10 isebenzisa izindlu zangasese ezingumahamba nendlwane, emuva kokugcwala ngokweqile kwezomgodi ezazakhiwe umphakathi.
Abazali abebedinwe beveva batshele Isolezwe ukuthi ekuqaleni konyaka kufike inkampani yathatha ezinye zezindlu zangasese ikhala ngokuthi umnyango awusakhokhi.
Kube sekusala izindlu eziyisithupha, kwafika enye inkampani izozilanda, banqaba abazali.
Bathe izindlu zangasese zibekwe phezu kwalezi zomgodi ezindala kanti ziphezulu ngokweqile okwenza zibe yingozi kubafundi.
"Kunzima kulesi sikole othisha bathi befundisa bebe beshintshana ngokuyogada ezindlini zangasese ngoba kuyingozi ezinganeni zikaGrade R, zingaphonseka phakathi.
Kade zicelwa izindlu zangasese zangempela umnyango uthembisa kodwa asisizakali bafuna kuze kulimale izingane okuyinto esingafisi yenzeke," kusho omunye wabazali ocele ukungadalulwa.
Okhulumela isigungu sabazali uMnuz Sandile Nxumalo, uvumile ukuthi abazali abaneme futhi udaba okade balufaka emahhovisi omnyango wezemfundo kodwa lutho usizo.
"Abazali badinwe kakhulu ngoba sesiside isikhathi sidlulisa izikhalo ngezindlu zangasese kunalokhu kwalethwa ezinye ezingumahamba nendlwane okuyinto engasadingeki.
Okwenze kwazwela ziphinde zalandwa izindlu zangasese, nenye nkampani yafuna ukuzilanda lezi eziyisithupha ezisele, sanqaba.
Manje azisalungiswasekwandisa izinkinga," kusho uNxumalo.
Leli phephandaba liphinde lathola ukuthi kunezikole ezingomakhelwane, esinye esinabafundi ababalelwa ngaphezulu kuka-200 nesinabafundi abaw-94 kodwa zakhelwe izindlu zangasese.
Abazali bathe ngeke liphele leli sonto bengathathanga izinyathelo ezizoshaqisa nezikhulu zomnyango ukuze zizwe lento eziwa abafundi.
Okhulumela umnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal uMnuz Muzi Mahlambi, uthe bakubeka phambili ukuvikelwa kwesithunzi sabafundi nothisha ngakho bazosisukumela lesi sikhalo.
"Uma ngiqeda ukukhuluma nawe ngizothinta umuntu esizokwazi ukumthumela ayobheka.
Umnyango uyakuqonda ukubaluleka kokuvikelwa kwesithunzi sothisha nezingane okuyingxenye yamalungelo abo.
Yingakho umnyango uhlala uqinisekisa ukuthi uyangenelela uhlinzeke nengqalasizinda lapho kudingeka khona," kusho uMahlambi.
Ethula isabelo sezimali ngeledlule uNgqongqoshe walo mnyango uMnuz Kwazi Mshengu, uthe zingu-410 izindlu zangasese zomgodi asebezakhile kwezingu-1377.
Uthe zingu-526 ezakhiwayo ezizophothulwa kulo nyaka wezimali.
U-DJ ugeqa amagula ngobuhlobo neSilo esisha
U-DJ waseThekwini ongumngani omkhulu weSilo uMisuzulu kaZwelithini, omenyezelwe ukuthi usengena esihlalweni seSilo uZwelithini kaBhekuzulu, ugeqa amagula ngobungani babo.
USiyabonga Zikode, owaziwa ngoDJ Kotin, uveze uhlangothi olusha ngeSilo uMisuzulu kaZwelithini.
Uthi babe ngabangani kusuka ngo-2009 ngesikhathi besahlala eHillcrest.
Uthe kuningi akufundile eSilweni esisha ngamasiko esiZulu nokusetshenziswa kolimi.
Uthe bahlangana eMkhosini waMaganu, esigodlweni sobukhosi bakwaTembe, eMfihlweni ngaseManguzi.
"Ungumuntu onenhlonipho futhi onesizotha.
Ziningi izinto engizifunde kuyena ebengingazazi zesintu.
Mina ngikhule elokishini, okuningi bengingakwazi ngamasiko akwaZulu.
"Ngisho ukusebenzisa amagama esiZulu ngendlela eqondile, ngikufundiswe yisona iSilo uMisuzulu kaZwelithini.
Ubengichazela ngokusetshenziswa kwemvunulo, eveza ukuthi kawuvele nje uvunule noma yinini ngoba iyahlonishwa imvunulo.
Ngisho nginaye endlunkulu wubengifundisa ukuthi kumele ngiziphathe kanjani uma ngikhona nendlela eqondile yokukhuluma uma ngikhona.
Emculweni ukhonze amahubo," kusho uKotin.
Uthe phezu kokuba ebenolwazi ngokuthi iSilo esisha singuMntwana waseNdlunkulu kodwa ubengazitsheli ukuthi nguyena ozongena ezintanjeni ebezibanjwe nguMdlokombane, njengoba luhlale luyimfihlo ulwazi ngozothatha isihlalo.
Naye uthe ubengazi njengoba kuyinto abengakaze akhulume ngayo njengoba kukuningi abebexoxa ngakho kobungani.
UKotin uveze ukuthi bebevakashelana neSilo uMisuzulu, esazi ngisho unina.
Nangesikhathi kushone umfowabo weSilo uMisuzulu, uMntwana uLethukuthula nyakenye, uthe wamthumela umyalezo edlulisa amazwi endunduzo ngokushiywa ngumfowabo.
Uphethe ngokumchaza njengomuntu olungile, onobubele okhathalele amasiko kaZulu.
"Okungichaze kakhulu ngeSilo wukuthi noma sihlale kakhulu eMelika kodwa besingakhohliwe ngamasiko kaZulu kanjalo nolimi,"kubeka uDJ Kotini.
Imizamo yokuzwa uvo lweSilo uMisuzulu kayiphumelelanga.
Kushone ababili nengane kshayisana izimoto
KUSHONE abantu ababili nengane, kwalimala abathathu ngesikhathi kutholana phezulu izimoto ezishayisane emgwaqweni, uN2, eMandeni ngoMgqibelo ekuseni.
Kuthiwa kwenye yalezi zimoto ebinamalungu amathathu omndeni owodwa, kushone owesilisa, owesifazane nengane abebehamba nayo.
Emotweni yesibili kulimale owesifazane nengane ephuthunyiswe esibhedlela.
Okhulumela abezimo eziphuthumayo uMnuz Paul Herbst we-IPSS Medical Rescue, uthe ithimba labo lifike laxilonga abantu abebelimele endaweni yesigameko.
"Ngenxa yendlela esifike isimo sibucayi ngayo, kuphoqeleke ukuthi kuvalwe umgwaqo ukuze sixilonge kahle abantu abebelimele kanzima engozini," kubeka uHerbst.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, usiqinisekisile isigameko sokushayisana kwezimoto ngoMgqibelo.
"Ayikaziwa imbangela yengozi.
Amaphoyisa aseMandeni aphenya icala lokubulala ngokungenhloso," kubeka uCaptain Gwala.
Khonamanjalo kushayisane izimoto ezintathu emgwaqweni uN2 eTinely Manor eduze kwendawo okulungiswa kuyo lo mgwaqo.
Eyodwa yalezi zimoto ishe yangqongqa.
UCaptain Gwala, uthe amaphoyisa asesiteshini saseMhlali athole umbiko ngale ngozi.
Uthe akukho muntu olimale kule ngozi.
Bazoqeqeshwa emapulazini asebegogode kowezolimo
UMLIMI owashiya ubunjiniyela waba ngumfuyi wezinkukhu usiza abantu abasha abaneziqu emkhakheni wezolimo ukuze bathole ukuqeqeshelwa umsebenzi.
UMnuz Sibusiso Phakathi, onepulazi lezinkukhu eDannhauser ngaseNewcastle, uthe cishe yonke indawo kukhalwa ngabantu abasha abangasebenzi yingakho ethe akabheke ukuthi yini angayenza emkhakheni akuwo ukuze alekelele.
Ube esekhetha ukuthi naye abe kubalimi abasiza abantu abasha abangasebenzi, babaqeqeshele umsebenzi emapulazini abo.
"Uma uvula umsakazo noma ufunda emaphepheni kukhalwa ngokungasebenzi kwabantu abasha.
Nami njengomuntu omusha ngithe akube neqhaza engilibambile ngithuthukise abanye abantu abasha," kusho uPhakathi.
Uhlelo luholwa wuMnyango wezeLimo KwaZulu-Natal, lwaziwa nge- Unemployed Agricultural Graduates Programme (UAGP), lwethulwe ngokusemthethweni nguNgqongqoshe woMnyango uNkk Bongi Sithole-Moloi, ngoLwesihlanu.
UNkk Sithole-Moloi uthe inhloso ngohlelo wukuthi izitshudeni esezifunde zagogoda kwezolimo zitholelwe amapulazi ezizosebenza kuwo ngenhloso yokuthi zithole ulwazi ngomsebenzi wasepulazini.
"Kulolu hlelo zingu-400 izitshudeni esezigogodile ezizotholelwa amapulazi ezizozoqeqeshwa kuwo.
Sifisa ukuthi ngokuhamba kwesikhathi sande isibalo sabafundi abazohlomula kulolu hlelo oluxhaswe wuhulumeni ngemali yokugibela enikezwa abenza uqeqesho emsebenzini.
Ngalolu hlelo akuzusizakala kuphela izitshudeni ngokufunda kubalimi kodwa nabo abalimi bazothola abantu abazobalekelela.
Ngaleyo ndlela umkhakha wezolimo uyakhula," kusho ungqongqoshe.
UPhakathi uthe lolu hlelo ulwamukele ngezandla zombili futhi usenazo izitshudeni ezisebenza epulazini lakhe.
UMnuz Sizwe Makhoba osebenza epulazini likaPhakathi, uthe uhlelo lozomsiza ngokuthi athole isipiliyoni esingenye yezinto ezenza ukuthi abantu bangayitholi imisebenzi ngoba basuke bengenaso.
UNkk Sithole-Moloi uthe bangu-109 abalimi abayingxenye yohlelo KwaZulu-Natal okwamanje.
Umzanyana uthuswe ukushona kwengane wadla phansi
KUMTHUSILE ukubona ingane abeyigadile ishona phambi kwakhe wakhetha ukubaleka, ashiye isidumbu sayo embhedeni owesifazane obewumzanyana wale ngane ebinezinyanga ezintathu.
Kuze kwaphela izinsuku ezine umndeni umthungatha, ufuna izimpendulo.
Lesi sigameko, esenzeke eNgwelezane, eMpangeni, ngesonto eledlule, sishiye abaningi beshaqekile, kwathi abanye bahlaba umkhosi wokufunwa komzanyana, kwavulwa necala lokushona kwengane esiteshini samaphoyisa eMpangeni.
Le ncazelo kuthiwa inikezwe umndeni yilo wesifazane emva kokuthi egcine ekwazile ukuxhumana noyise wengane, uMnuz S'bo Mthethwa, ngocingo lwesihlobo, izolo.
USimikahle Mthethwa watholwa ngunina eseshonile lapho bebehlala khona ngesikhathi ephuma emsebenzini ngoLwesithathu olwedlule.
Elandisa Isolezwe, uMthethwa uthe nakuba incwadi yokuhlolwa kwesidumbu, ekhishwe wudokotela, iveza ukuthi ingane yakhe ibulawe ukugula kodwa incazelo yomzanyana (igama lakhe eligodliwe ngoba engatholakanga ukuphawula), ayimgculisanga.
"Kuyiqiniso ukuthi akukho okubi engicabanga ukuthi ukwenzile futhi anginanxa naye.
Ubesigadele kahle ingane izinyanga ezimbili, kungekho okukhalisayo.
Okungiphatha kabi ukuthi wavele wanquma ukubaleka washiya isidumbu sengane, wangasifonela nonina ukusazisa ngosekwenzekile, mhlambe yayikhona imizamo eyayingenziwa," kusho uMthethwa.
Uthe ukushona kwengane kubaphathe kabi kakhulu kangangokuba unina ugcine engeniswe esibhedlela ngenxa yokhwantalala, emva kokuthi ingcatshiwe ngoLwesihlanu.
Uthe abakanqumi ngesinyathelo abazosithatha njengomndeni kuze kube unina wengane yakhe ululama ngokugcwele.
Echaza ngokwenzeka, uthe nakuba engahlali nonina wengane, ngokusho kwakhe, uthi wazithela phezu kwesidumbu sengane yakhe silaliswe embhedeni, umnyango uvuliwe, umzanyana engasabonwa ngalukhalo.
Uchaze umzanyana njengomuntu wesifazane oseqinile futhi obewenza kahle kakhulu umsebenzi wokugada ingane kulezi zinyanga ezimbili bemqashile.
Uthe bebeyazi imvelaphi yakhe kangangoba bebexhumana nomndeni nangesikhathi enyamelele kwazise bayazi nasemzini wakhe KwaDukuza.
Uthe izincomo zokuthi bamqashe bazinikwa ngesinye isihlobo sabo kanti bebeshaqekile ukuthi ukuphi njengoba engazi muntu endaweni"Uthe wakhoseliswa komunye umuzi okhona eNgwelezane, wabakhohlisa wathi ubezohlangana nabathile abebemqashele ukugada ingane kodwa abasafiki ekubeni engenayo imali yokuphindela emuva futhi engazi muntu endaweni," kusho uMthethwa.
Alikho icala abamvulele lona okwamanje.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe kuvulwe idokodo lophenyo ngokufa komuntu esiteshini samaphoyisa eMpangeni.
Umzali ufuna kujeziswe unogada ngelokushaya abafundi
UNINA womfundi owenza uGrade 11, okubikwa ukuthi ulinyazwe ngunogada ngemuva kokumtalabha emsola ngokubuyisana nabafundi abenza uGrade 12 lapho eqashe khona, uthi ufuna ajeziswe ngakwenze enganeni yakhe.
Lo mfundi (16) esiligodlile igama lakhe, oseyekiswe ngunina ukufunda eVelangaye Secondary eNkandla, kuthiwa ubephuma ekilasini lantambama nomngani wakhe ngoMeyi 5, ngesikhathi behlelwa yilesi sehloKubikwa ukuthi unogada wacasulwa ngukuthi labafundi babuya kanye kanye nalabo abenza uGrade 12, wababhaxa bobabili ngenduku esangweni.
Unina womfundi kaGrade 11 ocele ukungavezwa, uthe kuyamxaka okwenziwe ngunogada onqume ukutalabha ingane yakhe nomngani wayo ekubeni bebephuma esikoleni.
"Angiqondi ukuthi kungani unogada enze lesi senzo kulaba bobabili kuphela njengoba bekunezinye izingane ebeziphuma ukuyofunda.
Okungiphatha kabi wukuthi isikole siyaziqhelelanisa nesenzo sakhe.
Othisha basitshela ukuthi ubengasiye umsebenzi wabo unogada njengoba ebevelontiya," kukhala umzali.
Uthe usenqume ukuyikhipha ingane yakhe kulesi sikole njengoba othisha beziqhelelanisa nokushaywa kwengane.
Umzali ufisa kujeziswe unogada futhi bavule icala lokushaya esiteshini samaphoyisa eNkandla.
"Ingane ngiyayibona ukuthi ihlukumezekile ngokomqondo yingakho ngithathe isinqumo sokuthi ngiyifunele esinye isikole.
Uma ngihluleka, ngizozama ukucela abomnyango ukuthi bangilekelele ekufuneni esinye isikole," kubeka umzali.
Kwesinye isigameko sokushaywa komfundi kulesi sikole, kusabalale ivideo ngeledlule okubonakala kuyo kutalajwa umfana ezindlini zemiqasho yabafundi okubikwa ukuthi ubenenebulwa yiqembu lamadoda.
Yize kwivideo kungacaci ukuthi ubeshayelwani lo mfundi, amahlebezi aveza ukuthi utholwe nezinhlamvu zensangu esikhwameni.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe abasolwa abathinteka emacaleni okushaya abafundi bavele eNkantolo yeMantshi eNkandla ngoLwesihlanu.
"Unogada ubingelele imantshi mayelana necala lokushaya.
Abanye abasolwa abathinteka ecaleni lokushaya omunye umfundi waseVelangaye Secondary, nabo bavelile enkantolo," kubeka uCaptain Gwala.
Udutshulwe washona egoloza ukuqhela emotweni yemali
UVELE namuhla eNkantolo yeMantshi yaseNtuzuma unogada wemoto ethwala imali, obhekene necala lokubulala, okuthiwa udubule owesilisa onqabe ukuhlehla eduze kwemoto ethwala imali enxanxatheleni yezitolo eKwaMashu kwa-L, ngoMsombuluko emini.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uColonel Thembeka Mbele, uthe kube nokujikijelana ngamazwi phakathi kukamufi ona-39 nalo msolwa ona-42.
"Kusolwa ukuthi onogada, abebenza umsebenzi wabo kule nxanxathela yezitolo, batshele lo wesilisa ukuthi akaqhele emotweni yemali kodwa wenqaba, kunalokho wabalwisa.
Kuthiwa kungaleso sikhathi unogada ekhiphe isibhamu wadubula umufi esifubeni," kusho uColonel Mbele.
Uthe umgilwa uphuthunyiswe esibhedlela enenxeba lokudutshulwa wafike washonela khona.
Uthe ngesikhathi kusanakwe lesi sigameko abantu besashaqekile, kusolwa ukuthi amanye amalungu omphakathi abekhona agijime angena esitolo azama ukuzitapela impahla.
Kuthiwa onogada bakwazile ukubamba abasolwa ababili abaneminyaka ephakathi kuka-31 no-32 nezimpahla zokwebiwa.
UColonel Mbele uthe kuvulwe icala lokugqekeza esiteshini samaphoyisa esiseNtuzuma, laba basolwa kulindeleke ukuthi bavele enkantolo efanayo namuhla.
Bakhala ngombhishobhi ovale isikole
KUKHALWA ngobudlova kumbhishobhi webandla lamaZayoni okuthiwa uvale isikole Umzokhulayo Primary KwaNyuswa, eNdwedwe, okuthiwa uphoqe abafundi ukuthi babuyele emakhaya, babuye uma sekuxoshwe uthishomkhulu.
U-Bishop Bheki Ngcobo obuye abe wumengameli we- African Freedom Revolution (AFR), kuthiwa ngesonto eledlule ungene wakhipha ngoshova abafundi emakilasini, wavala isikole.
Kuthiwa ubehambisana nedlanzana ebelidlubhe izikibha zeqembu lakhe.
Baqoqe izingane baziyalela ukuthi ziphume esikoleni, zingalubhadi esikoleni zizozwa ngabo uma sekumele zibuye.
Kuvele ukuthi abamfuni uthishomkhulu ngoba kungesiye owendawo futhi ekhokhisa abazali o-R100.
Nayizolo kuthiwa itshe belisome inhlama, abafundi nothisha abazange balubhade esikoleni.
Uthisha olandise Isolezwe owayekhona ngosuku lwesigameko kodwa ongathandanga ukudalulwa, uthe uNgcobo nayehamba nabo kabazange bazihluphe ngokucela imvume kothisha kodwa bathi isikole bayasivala.
"Isikhathi sokuphuma sasingakashayi nomuntu owelisa izingane umgwaqo wayengakafiki.
Izingane zaphoqwa ukuthi ziphume ngababegqoke izikibha ze-AFR, iningi labo okungebona abendawo.
Bathi abamfuni uthishomkhulu nabanye othisha futhi bafuna kusebenze abantu bendawo kuphela," kusho umthombo.
Kuthintwa uNgcobo, uvumile ukuthi baziyalele izingane ukuthi zingalubhadi esikoleni kuze kube umnyango uxosha uthishomkhulu.
"Lokhu sikwenze emva kokuzwa izikhalo zabazali ngodaba lokukhokhiswa kwabo o-R100 okwenziwa uthishomkhulu.
Lokhu uthi ukwenza ngoba edinga ukukhokhela uthisha ongaqashwanga wumnyango," kusho uNgcobo.
Uthe akukhona okokuqala bekhala ngalesi senzo njengoba nangonyaka owedlule babhikisha bemfuna exoshiwe kodwa umnyango wabaziba.
Umzali osesigungwini esilawula isikole ongathandanga ukudalulwa ngoba ethi usaba ukwenzakaliswa wuNgcobo, uthe ukukhokhwa kwale mali ekhokhwa ngonyaka, kwavunyelwana ngakho emhlanganweni wabazali bayemukela ngoba bebona iqhaza likathisha osefundise kulesi sikole evolontiya kusuka ngo-2014 engaqashiwe.
"UNgcobo uyisidlova.
Iningi labazali liyahambisana nokukhokhwa kwale mali futhi akubanga yisinqumo sikathishomkhulu kodwa ngesethu singabazali.
"Iyahlukaniswa le mali, uthisha ayihole nyangazonke ukumsiza athole insipho.
Okubuhlungu wukuthi isikole asivalayo kasikho ngakubo, yena ongowakwenye indawo kodwa uyagxambukela futhi akanazo izingane ezifunda kuso.
Kulahlekelwa izingane zethu," usho kanje.
Okhulumela uMnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Kwazi Mthethwa, usigxekile isenzo sokuvalwa kwesikole.
"Sithanda ukuqwashisa abaholi bamaqembu epolitiki amancane ukuthi badlalele kude nezikole ngoba ziyindawo okubunjwa khona ikusasa lezingane, akusona ezokuzama ukukotela udumo.
Umnyango uzoqinisekisa ukuthi ukufunda nokufundisa akuphazamiseki," kusho uMthethwa.
UZuma uthi usekulungele ukuqulwa kwecala
OWAYENGUMENGAMELI wakuleli, uMnuz Jacob Zuma, uthi usekulungele ukuqulwa kwecala lenkohlakalo abhekene nalo nenkampani yaseFrance, iThales, nakuba leli cala liphinde lahlehliswa ngenxa yesicelo ahlongoza ukusifaka enkantolo.
Bebephume ngobuningi babo abalandeli bakaZuma ukuzomeseka ngesikhathi evela eNkantolo eNkulu, eMgungundlovu, ngoMsombuluko.
Kulokhu bekukhona nobuholi be-ANC eKZN ngempelasonto okuvele izindaba zokuthi bukhethe ukumeseka kuleli cala.
Ngesikhathi kulindeleke ukuthi kubonakale ufakazi wokuqala kuleli cala, uNkk Patricia De Lille, uMshushisi, uBilly Downer, uveze ukuthi abameli abasha bakaZuma sebeveze ukuthi bazofaka isicelo sokuthi ahoxe kuleli cala.
Izizathu zalokhu azibekwanga enkantolo kodwa uJaji Piet Koen ubavumelile ukuthi bafake isicelo sabo enkantolo ngoLwesithathu kuleli sonto bese umbuso uyaphendula, yena uyobe esememezela isinqumo sakhe kulolu daba ngoMeyi 26.
Ekhuluma ngaphandle kwenkantolo kubalandeli bakhe, uMnuz Jacob Zuma ubabongile ngokumeseka, wagqugquzela ubumbano kwi-ANC ekhuza labo abebehhahhameza abaholi be-ANC KwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Sihle Zikalala, noMnuz Mdumiseni Ntuli.
Uthe ngisho naye kunabantu afike aphikisane nabo ngasese kodwa bayakufihla lokho uma sebekhuluma esidlangalaleni ngoba akafuni ukujabulisa izitha.
Nakuba icala lihlehlile, uZuma uthe usekulungele ukuthi kuqale ukuqulwa kwalo kodwa ufuna ukuqinisekisa ukuthi liqulwa ngaphansi kwezimo ezihambisana nomthethosisekelo.
Thola udaba olugcwele kwiSolezwe ngoLwesibili.
I-EFF isabisa ngokuphula imithetho yomvalelandlini
UMHOLI we-EFF, uMnuz Julius Malema, usesabise ngokushaya indiva imithetho ebekelwe ukulwa nokusabalala kobhubhane iCorona.
UMalema usefunge wagomela ukuthi iqembu lakhe angeke lisayilandela imithetho yomvalelandlini kuze kube uhulumeni usheshisa uhlelo lokugomela iCorona aphinde ahlehlise ukhetho lohulumeni basekhaya.
UMalema uthe ayikho into ezoshiwo uMengameli wezwe, uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, abazoyilalela.
"Akukho mthetho womvalelandlini ozosivimba.
Ayikho into azoyisho uRamaphosa esizoyilalela.
Kade siyihlonipha imithetho yeCorona, saze sabanika (uhulumeni) ngisho uR15 million ukuba kuliwe nalolu bhubhane.
"Manje sesikhathele ibona.
Leli lizwe akusilona elikaRamaphosa, angasijwayeli kabi.
Uma kuwukuthi kufanele sife, kulungile.
Uma kufanele siboshwe, kulungile.
"UMalema ubekhuluma emcimbini wale nhlangano wokugubha usuku lwentsha, obubanjwe eGauteng, izolo.
Lo mcimbi ububanjwe ngaphandle kwesikole esizimele i-Uitsig High School, esisematheni kulezi nsuku kulandela ukusabalala kwe-video ekhombisa umfundi webala elimnyama ogqoke umfaniswane wale nhlangano, exhakathiswa ngonogada bebala elimhlophe, bemkhipha emagcekeni alesi sikole.
Ekhuluma nezinkumbi zabalandeli baleli qembu abebehambele lo mcimbi, uMalema uthe uma uRamaphosa efuna leli qembu lihloniphe imithetho yesigaba sesithathu somvalelandlini ayimemezele ngoLwesibili ebusuku, akahlehlise ukhetho lohulumeni basekhaya.
"Angeke ungitshele ukuthi singathi sibheke okhethweni, wena uqinisa imithetho yomvalelandlini.
Sekusele izinyanga siye okhethweni lohulumeni basekhaya, kepha asivumelekile ukukhankasa.
Imithetho yomvalelandlini ayisivumeli ukuba sikhankase.
"Asikwazi nokukhetha abazosimela okhethweni ngenxa yayo le mithetho yomvalelandlini.
Ukuze sikwazi ukukhetha abazosimela, kufanele kube nemihlangano yamagatsha.
Amanye amagatsha ethu anamalungu angaphezulu kuka-300.
Sizoyibamba kanjani imhlangano uma kuwukuthi akuvumelekile ukuhlangana kwabantu abangaphezu kuka-100?
"UMalema uthe okunye okubacasulayo ukuhamba ngonyawo lonwabo kohlelo lokugomela iCorona.
Uthe ukube lolu hlelo luhamba ngesivinini esiphezulu, besingezukuba khona isidingo sokuqiniswa kwemithetho yomvalelandlini ngoba abantu abaningi ngabe sebegomile.
UMalema uthe kabazi ukuthi kungani leli lizwe lingasebenzisi umgomo okhiqizwa eRussia, iSputnik V, nokhiqizwa eChina, iSinovac, ukuze kwandiswe imigomo ezosetshenziswa ukugoma izakhamuzi zakuleli.
UMalema umemezele ukuthi bazobhikisha ngaphandle kwamahhovisi esikhungo esigunyaza ukusetshenziswa kwemithi kuleli, iSA Health Products Regulatory Authority (Sahpra), ngoLwesihlanu lwangesonto elizayo.
"Sifuna ukwazi ukuthi kungani le migomo ingasetshenziswa kuleli.
Sizobanika izinsuku eziyisikhombisa ukuba baphendule.
Uma behluleka ukuphendula sizokuya kolala emzini wesikhulu esiphezulu sale nhlangano."
Mazivalwe izikole ezinsukwini eziyisikhombisa ezizayo: Malema
I-ECONOMIC Freedom Fighters isinqumele uhulumeni ugwayi katiki ngodaba lokuvalwa kwezikole, njengoba ibhebhetheka ngamandla iCovid-19 kuleli.
Ekhuluma nabezindaba ngoLwesine umengameli we-EFF uMnuz Julius Malema, uthe bawunikeza izinsuku eziyisikhombisa uhulumeni wakuleli ukuthi uvale izikole zamabanga aphansi ngoba bakhathazekile ngesibalo sabafundi abatheleleka ngeCovid-19.
"Siwunikeza izinsuku eziyisikhombisa uhulumeni ukuthi uvale izikole.
Kwakubuhlungu sishonelwa abantu abadala ngesivuvu sokuqala nesesibili.
Awucabange-ke manje uma sekumele singcwabe izingane...ngale ndlela esasingcwaba ngayo abantu abakhulile.
Sisesimeni esibi, izikole kumele zivalwe" kusho uMalema.
UMalema uthe into ebalulekile ukuphepha kwabafundi ngoba izingane seziyatheleleka ngeCovid-19.
Izolo isibalo sabantu abahaqwe yileli gciwane sinyuke ngo-8 881, kanti selibulele abawu-57 310 kuleli.
Ngaphandle kwezikole, uMalema unxuse i-IEC ukuthi ihlehlise ukhetho lohulumeni basekhaya ngenxa yokukhula kwesibalo sabahaqwe yiCovid-19, ngokunjalo nemithetho ebanqanda ukuthi babe nezingqungquthela zokuqoka ubuholi ezindaweni abasadinga ukulungisa kuzo.
Uphinde wagxeka isinqumo sikaMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa nohulumeni wakuleli, sokuthenga imigomo yeCovid-19 evela emazweni ase-Europe kuphela, ekubeni ikhona eyaseChina neyaseRussia etholakala ngamanani angcono.
Udlokodle inkomo yentombi ngesikhuni sivutha
NKOSIKHONA CELEASAMANGELE futhi ayathuthumela amalungu omphakathi waseSonyongwe, phambili kwaseMzimkhulu, ngesenzo sowesilisa obhadame intombi yakhe isocansini nomakhwapheni wavele wayigwaza yathula, maqede wabasa umlilo wase eyishutheka isikhuni esithweni sayo sangasese.
Wabasela i-ayina, wayishisa inkomo maqede wayihudula wayoyilahla eweni.
UMnuz Mvelo Makhanya (26) kuthiwa ubeseneminyaka ethandana nomufi uNksz Zimbili Nyibe (21), ogcine embulala ngalesi sihluku.
Kuthiwa uMvelo unengwe wukubhadama intombi yakhe izitika ngocansi nomfana wasendaweni uMnuz Sanele Jaca, okuthiwa uphume wabaleka emapunapuna ngesikhathi behlaselwa nguMakhanya.
Isolezwe NgoMgqibelo lithole ukuthi uMakhanya ubemenza ibhola lakhe uNksz Nyibe ngoba ubemhlukumeza ngokumshaya mihla namalanga.
Kuthiwa kukaningi uuNksz Nyibe evulela isoka lakhe amacala okushaya kodwa uMakhanya axolise nayo intombi imxolele maqede isule amacala nempilo iqhubeke kube sengathi akukaze kwenzeke lutho.
UMakhanya ubhadame intombi yakhe isembhedeni ngemuva kokuba elunywe indlebe ngomunye wasendaweni.
Kuthiwa akazange apholise maseko ube esenikela khona kwaJaca, lapho obekulele khona intombi yakhe.
Ngemuva kwalesi sigameko, kuthiwa uMakhanya usihudule kabuhlungu isidumbu sikaZimbili sinqunu sinjalo, wahamba naso wayosiphonsa endaweni ewumsele naye wangena kuwona.
Amalungu omphakathi abesho ukumudla luhlaza uMakhanya kuthiwa amane adikabala ngemuva kokuba ewatshele ukuthi "awambulale vele ayisekho into ayiphilelayo ngemuva kokugilwa yithemba lakhe ebeliletha ukukhanya empilweni yakhe" esho uZimbili.
UMnuz Mondli Phoswa, oyilungu lomphakathi elibhekelele izinto eziningi kule ndawo, uzwakalise ukukhathazeka kwakhe ngesehlo.
"Sonke sisamangele kakhulu ngale ndaba.
Ukukhuluma iqiniso nje bobabili bebephila ngokuklwebhana mihla namalanga.
Kodwa akekho obebanaka ngoba sonke besazi ukuthi baxabana namhlanje, kusasa baphinde bazwane,"" kusho uPhoswa.
Elinye ilungu lomphakathi nelingusomabhizinisi uMnuz Thimothy Maduna, lithi lesi sigameko sibamangazile kakhulu.
UMaduna uveze ukuthi ngemuva kokuba uMakhanya esenze lesi sigameko ufike kuyena wamazisa ukuthi usebulale umuntu ngephutha.
"Ngesikhathi engitshela lento bengizitshela ukuthi uyadlala kanti uqinisile.
Yimi obize amaphoyisa afika ambopha,"" kuchaza uMaduna.
Umndeni wakwaNyibe awuholakalanga ukuba uphawule ngodaba.
Kodwa Isolezwe NgoMgqibelo lithole ukuthi lo mndeni ugqemeke engeqiwa ntwala ngokudlula emhlabeni kwelungu lawo ngesihluku esinjena nesimo kuwona kuthiwa simuncu kakhulu.
Umufi kuthiwa ubengumuntu obezifela ngobumnandi.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala usiqinisekisile isigameko.
Uveze ukuthi umsolwa zimkhalele ngosuku agile ngalo umkhuba.
Uthi bathole ukuthi umsolwa ugwaze wabulala intombi yakhe.
"Kusolakala ukuthi owesilisa wabulala intombi yakhe ngokuyigwaza kabuhlungu emqaleni.
Yafa ngaleso sikhathi.
Lesi sigameko senzeka emini," kuchaza uCaptain Gwala.
Kushone abathathu iloli ingena endlini
USADIDEKILE uyise wowesilisa oshone ngesikhathi iloli, ephelelwe ngamabhuleki, ingena endlini yabulala abathathu edolobheni iGlencoe, KwaZulu-Natal, ngoLwesibili emini.
Kushone nomshayeli weloli (34) nomsizi wakhe (46) kulesi sehlakalo esinyantisayo.
Kuthiwa iloli beyehla ngomgwaqo uBiggar nokusolakala ukuthi liphelelwe ngamabhuleki langena lasithela kule ndlu esengasekhoneni lomgwaqo.
Umufi, uMnuz Siphakanyiswa Radebe (35), ubesanda kubuya emsebenzini ehlezi nabangani bakhe kuveranda, begundana.
Kuthiwa umufi ubalekele endlini efuna ukuyophuma ngomunye umnyango kanti iloli lizobhodloza udonga, izitini zawela phezu kwakhe washona.
Abangani bakhe basindile kule ngozi njengoba kuthiwa abamlandelanga umufi.
Uyise kamufi, uMnuz Alpheus Radebe, uthe kusemnyama amehlo, udidekile ngoba ubesehlale iminyaka engu-13 kulo muzi awuqashe kwaTransnet.
"Besisebenza ndawonye emsebenzini nomfana wami wangishiya eseshayisile.
Ngifike ekhaya ngazithela phezu kwalo mhlola.
Iloli lingene lonke endlini lacishe layophuma ngale," kusho uRadebe ngosizi.
Uthe badabuka Ekuvukeni, ngaseMnambithi, njengamanje baqutshiswe ehholo nokuyilapho behlinzekwe khona ngokudla nangezimpahla zokulala.
Okhulumela amaphoyisa KwaZulu-Natal, uCaptain Nqobile Gwala, uthe kuphenywa icala lokubulala ngokungenhloso.
Uthe kusolakala ukuthi iloli liphaphalazile layongena kulo muzi.
"Umshayeli nomsizi wakhe bashonele endaweni yesehlakalo.
Umnikazi wendlu ushonele esibhedlela ngemva kokulimala kanzima," kusho uCapt.
Gwala.IMeya yaseMzinyathi, uMnuz Petros Mthandeni Ngubane, ubabaze indlela ebinyantisa ngayo le nhlekelele njengoba eziyele ngokwakhe ukuyokhalisana nomndeni, eyohlola nomonakalo.UNgubane uthe kumphathe kabi akubonile, wathi ubikelwe wumphakathi ukuthi ziyisikhombisa izigameko zokufa kwabantu esezibikiwe kulo mgwaqo.
"Ngicele ukuthi umgwaqo ufakwe isinciphisajubane futhi kwehliswe nejubane ezimpawini zomgwaqo.
Amakhansela awalekelele, angabheki ukuthi umuntu uphuma kuliphi iqembu lezepolitiki.
Awangaze abizwe kodwa awazifikele ngokwawo uma esetholile ngesigameko," kusho uNgubane.
Kuyanda ukuhlaselwa kothisha ezikoleni
KUKHALWA nkalo zonke ngokudlanga kobugebengu bokuhlaselwa, kuphangwe othisha befundisa ezikoleni KwaZulu-Natal.
UMnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal uthi ukhathazekile ngoba kubukeka sengathi izikole seziphenduke umhhume wabaphangi, abagebenga othisha nezikole kungabi ndaba zalutho.
Umnyango uthi muva nje, izigebengu zimane zizingenele esikoleni ziphange othisha ngaphandle kokuphazamiseka.
Okhulumela umnyango, uMnuz Muzi Mahlambi, unxenxe imiphakathi ukuthi ivikele izikole.
UMahlambi uthe uNgqongqoshe wezeMfundo UMnuz Kwazi Mshengu, uxoxisana nozakwabo eMnyangweni wezokuPhepha nokuXhumana koMphakathi esifundazweni, uNkk Peggy Nkonyeni ngenhloso yokuqhamuka namaqhinga nezindlela ezizoletha ukuphepha ezikoleni.
Unobhala wenyunyana yothisha iSouth African Democratic Tearchers Union (Sadtu) KwaZulu-Natal, uNksz Nomarashiya Caluza, uthe iyinkinga indaba yokwanda kwezigameko zokuhlaselwa nokuphangwa kothisha ezikoleni.
Wathi izehlo zilimaza othisha emoyeni nasemqondweni futhi kuthikameza nabafundi abasuke bebukela kwenzeka le migilingwane.
"Luyaphazamiseka uhlelo lokufunda nokufundisa uma kwenzeka izigameko ezinje.
Umnyango kumele unxenxe imiphakathi ukuba ivikele izikole.
Nathi siyiSadtu silwa nodlame nezenzo zobugebengu sisebenzisa umkhankaso wethu onesiqubulo esithi: I Am A School Fan," kusho uNksz Caluza.
UNksz Cyntia Barnes onguNobhala jikelele wenyunyana yothisha, iNational Teachers Union (Natu), uthe ukuze izingane nothisha baphephe umnyango awuqashe onogada abaqeqeshiwe ezikoleni.
UNksz Barnes uthe unogada kumele anikezwe izinsiza kusebenza, achazelwe ngemithetho yesikole nokuthi ngubani okumele avunyelwe ukungena ngaphakathi emagcekeni esikole.
"Kade sasiwutshela umnyango ukuthi isikole ngasinye asibe nonogada oqeqeshiwe khona ezovikela othisha nezingane ezigebengwini.
Uma kuqhubeka kanjena impilo yabo isengcupheni nezingane zingagcina sezinukubezekile," kusho uNksz Barnes.
Ukhuze umnyango wathi awuyeke umkhuba wawo wokuthatha umuntu emgwaqweni umgadise isikole.
"Umnyango awusinaki uma sikhuluma izinto ngoba uthi sifuna kulalelwe thina.
Kwesinye isikhathi uthi efundisa uthisha kube nomuntu odlula ngendlela amchaphe ngenhlamba emehlisa isithunzi.
Sekukubi manje ngoba bangenelwa esikoleni baphangwe nesikole," kusho uNksz Barnes
Bazothuthukisa ezolimo nezokuvakasha eZululand
INTATHELI YESOLEZWEUZOGXILA ekuthuthukiseni amabhizinisi kwezolimo nakwezokuvakasha uMasipala wesiFunda iZululand kulo nyaka wezimali.
Lokhu kuvezwe yiMeya yalo mkhandlu, uMfu Thulasizwe Buthelezi, izolo kade ethula isabelomali sika-R1.
1 billion esabelwe lo masipala.
Lo masipala ungeminye yemikhandlu enenkinga yamanzi nokuyinto umphakathi ohlale ukhala ngayo.
Ethula isabelo salo mkhandlu ezinkundleni zemidlalo zaKwaGqikazi, KwaNongoma, uButhelezi uthe umasipala uzimisele ukuxazulula le nkinga osekuneminyaka ihlupha umphakathi.
Kulesi sabelo uhlelo lokusabalaliswa kwamanzi nokuthuthwa kwendle lunikwe u-R583 million.
"Ngifisa kakhulu ukugxila kule misebenzi yokuphakelwa kwamanzi.
Lapha KwaNongoma sinemiklamo emibili yokuphakelwa kwamanzi, okuyiMandlakazi RWSS Bulk Water Supply Scheme noSuthu RWSSS.
Ngaphansi kwale miklamo kuningi okwenziwe ukusabalalisa amanzi futhi sizimisele ukuqhubeka nokuqinisekisa ukuthi amanzi ayafinyelele kuzo zonke izakhamizi zomkhandlu," kusho uButhelezi.
Uveze nokuthi banezinhlelo zokufaka nokuthuthukisa umphakathi kwezamabhizinisi ezolimo nawezokuvakasha.
"Siyazi sonke ukuthi iCovid-19 ihlasele futhi ishintshe nendlela esiphila ngayo.
Yingakho nathi sishintshe izinhlelo, sasungula nezinye ukulekelela umphakathi wethu.
Sinohlelo esilusungulile olubizwa ngeSethembe Food Programme esibambisene kulo nezitolo zakwaBoxer.
Kulo sinika izinkumbi zabantu bakulo mkhandlu abahlwempu ama-voucher ka-R1000 umndeni umunye.
Sibe sesibuka nokukhahlamezeka kosomabhizinisi, ikakhulukazi abasafufusa, sabe sesithatha isinqumo sokuba kube nendlela nabo abalekeleleka ngayo.
Yingakho namhlanje (izolo) sethula ngokusemthethweni uhlelo lokuxhasa osomabhizinisi abasathuthuka abaxhaswe ngo-R50 000 umfelandawonye ngamunye.
"OPhongolo nje kuhlomule imifelandawonye engaphezu kuka-50.
Le mifelandawonye igxile kwezolimo namabhizinisi ezokuvakasha nokuyinto esifuna ukuqinisa kakhulu kuyo," kusho uButhelezi.
Kulo mcimbi bekukhona noMntwana waKwaPhindangene owethule inkulumo ekhethekile nalapho encome khona izinhlelo zomkhandlu waphinde wagqugquzela nomphakathi ukuthi uzibandakanye nezinhlelo zomkhandlu ukuze uthuthuke.
UMntwana uSimakade uchitha eyokunyonyobela esobukhosi
UMNTWANA uSimakade Jackson Zulu usephumele obala wakuchitha ukuthi uhlela ukuphonsela inselelo isihlalo seSilo uMisuzulu kaZwelithini.
UMntwana uSimakade uveze lokhu ngezwi likaNdunankulu kaZulu, iNkosi uMangosuthu Buthelezi, obefunda isitatimende sakhe ngesikhathi ekhuluma nabezindaba ngezakamuva eNdlunkulu ngoLwesibili ntambama.
Uthe uzwile ukuthi kunamahemuhemu okuthi kukhona abamfisela lesi sikhundla kodwa bafundiswa besakhula eNdlunkulu ukweseka lowo osuke ekhonjiwe.
"Ngijabulile uma ngibona uMntwana ezisholo kumabonakude ngokwakhe ukuthi angikaze ngisho nakuye ukuthi ngiyasifuna lesi sikhundla (sobukhosi).
Nami ngiyakufakazela lokho.
Ngingakuqinisekisa ukuthi angikaze ngisho kumuntu ukuthi ngiyasifisa lesi sikhundla," kusho uMntwana.
"Ngiyakuqinisekisa ukuthi ngeke ngiweqe amagama abantu abadala.
Ngicela uMntwana asale esengicelela ezintathelini ukuthi ziyeke ukungifonela ngalolu daba ngoba akukho okunye engingakusho okudlula lokhu engikushoyo," usho kanje.
UMntwana Simakade uyizinyane elidala likaBhejane, kwasadla anhlamvana, kanti uzalwa yintombi engazange igane iSilo.
Wakhulela esigodlweni KwaKhangelamankengane, kweseNdlovukazi uShiyiwe Mantfombi Dlamini Zulu, okunguye oqoke isilo esisasanda kumenyezelwa.
Umhlangano ngefa lasendlunkulu ngo-5 ntambama
KULINDELEKE ukuthi iNdlunkulu kaZulu ibe nomhlangano wokwabiwa kwefa ophuthumayo, okulindeleke ukuba ube wumhlahlandlela mayelana nozongena esihlalweni sobukhosi njengoba kukhotheme iNdlovukazi ebibambile esihlalweni, uMantfombi Dlamini Zulu.
UMntwana waKwaPhindangene Mangosuthu Buthelezi umemezele enkonzweni yesikhumbuzo namhlanje ukuthi ngezithuba zehora lesihlanu ntambama, indlunkulu izohlangana izwe mayelana nefa elishiywe ngobeyiBambabukhosi.
Emhlanganweni kulindeleke ukuthi kufundwe incwadi yefa, uShenge aveze ukuthi iNdlovukazi ishiye isilabile.
Yize kungakahlanganwa kodwa sekukhona ukuqagula ukuthi ngubani osezohola isizwe samaZulu khona namhlanje.
Inkonzo yesikhumbuzo ibihanjelwe yizikhulu zikahulumeni ezahlukene.

Ziyenyuka izibalo zeCovid-19 ezifundazweni ezine
ZILOKHU zenyukile izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli nababulawa yileli gciwane.
Izibalo zakamuva ezikhishwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli, zikhomba ukuthi emahoreni angu-24 abahaqwe yileli gciwane bangu-1 129, okuholele ekutheni izibalo zabahaqwe yigciwane zenyukele ku-1 597 724.
Izifundazwe ezihamba phambili ngezibalo zabahaqwe yigciwane, yiGauteng enabantu abangu-428 717, Eastern Cape enabangu-196 307, Western Cape ngabangu-288 299 neKwaZulu-Natal enabantu abangu-337 397.
UMnyango wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, ekhasini lawo leFacebook uthe emahoreni angu-24 bangu-64 abahaqwe yigciwane.
Uthe lesi sifundazwe singesesine kwezihamba phambili ngezibalo eseziqale ukwenyuka zabahaqwe yigciwane, iGauteng ihamba phambili ngezibalo ezenyukayo.
Bangu-54 825 ababulelwe yigciwane kuleli.
Abashone esikhathi esingamahora angu-24 bangu-60.
Ukwenyuka kwezibalo zabahaqwa yigciwane kuholele ekutheni abantu babe nengebhe, bazibuze ukuthi ngabe sesingenile yini isiqubu sesithathu sokuhlasela kwaleli gciwane.
Abanye benze isiphakamiso sokuthi kuqiniswe imithetho elawula imingcele namachwepha.
INhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), yenze isiphakamiso sokuthi kulawulwe ukungena kwezivakashi emazweni ehlukene.
Ithe akumele imingcele namachweba kuvalwe ngoba lokho kuzophazamisa ezomnotho.
Kodwa amanye amazwe ayazinqabela izivakashi ezivela emazweni akholwa wukuthi anengozi kakhulu.
Izivakashi eziphuma kuleli kazivumelekile e-USA.
Izivakashi ezisatshwa kakhulu ngeziphuma e-India.
UDkt Zweli Mkhize onguNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uthe kawekho amabhanoyi asuka e-India eza kuleli, izivakashi eziphuma khona ziyaxhuma.
Ngenxa yalokho kubekwe imigomo emisha yokuthi izivakashi kumele zihlolwe.
Uma kutholakala ukuthi zineCovid-19 zigonqe.
Uchitha eyokhwantalala kwindodakazi yakhe uyise wengoduso ka-AKA
UYISE wengoduso yomrepha wakuleli odumile uchitha eyekuthi indodakazi yakhe ibiphethwe wukhwantalala kulandela izinsolo zokuzibulala kwayo.
UMnuz Moses Tembe onguyise wengoduso ka-AKA u-Anele "Nelli" Tembe (22) obengcwatshwa namhlanje, enkonzweni ebibanjelwe e-ICC eThekwini uveze ukuthi indodakazi yakhe beyinenkinga yokusebenzisa izidakamizwa okubalwa kuzo nophuzo oludakayo.
UTembe usho kanje encwadini ebeyibhalile efundwe usomabhizinisi ongumengameli waMaZulu FC uMnuz Sandile Zungu.
Kule ncwadi uTembe uthe uyazithanda zonke izingane zakhe, ziphelelisa impilo yakhe.
U-Anele umchaze njengengane ebinothando emndenini futhi ebikhonze ukwenza izinto ngokuzimela"Bengingekho ngeSonto kwenzeka lomshophi.
Angiqondile ukwakha izinsolo njengoba kusolwa ukuthi ubenokhwantalala kodwa u-Anele ubengeyena umuntu obecabanga ngokuzibulala futhi akazibulalanga .
Alikho ngisho elilodwa ilungu lomndeni elingamhlanganisa nokuzibulala.
Njengoyise ngithi ubengeke azibulale, kumele siqonde izikhathi esizithola sikuzo.
Usathane uhlasela intsha yethu esebenzisa utshwala nezidakamizwa, sinenkinga enkulu yokusetshenziswa kwezidakamizwa," kusho uTembe.
Uthe iphupho elikhulu lika-Anele bekungukuvula indawo ephambili yokudla eNingizimu Afrika nokwenze wafunda wagxila emkhakheni wezokupheka.
UTembe uthe wamyala ngokuthi aqinise ekufundeni nomkhakha wamabhizinisi nokuyinto abephezu kwayo.
Umchaze njengentombazane ebingahluphi ngamasoka kodwa ebizazi ukuthi ifuna ukukhula ishade kwaze kwaba ilotsholwa u-AKA.
Wabayala nangokuthi laba bathole nokwelulekwa ngaphambi kokushada ngoba ebona ukuthi umshado nenjabulo yabo iyasidinga isisekelo.
Ekhuluma kule nkonzo uNgqongqoshe wamaPhoyisa kuleli uMnuz Bheki Cele udlulise amazwi enduduzo emndenini wakwaTembe.
Uthe okunye ngeke akukhulume enkonzweni ngoba amaphoyisa awakuzikhulumi izinto ezisabhekwa.
"Ngoba angifuni ukubizwa ngelinye ilanga ngizofakaza kuthiwe wathi...ngoba izinto ezisabhekwa," usho kanje.
UMkabayi uthi wacishe wasilaxaza Isibaya
UMLINGISI weSibaya oyibambe iminyaka eyisishiyagalombili kulo mdlalo, uThembi Nyandeni, uveze ukuthi wacishe washiya kuwo ngenxa yokuthi babefuna ukuthi abe nesoka.
UThembi, ubelingisa indawo kaMkabayi Zungu, okungowesifazane ongusomatekisi futhi ovikela umndeni wakhe, nobezibambela inganono uma behlaselwa njengoba bebenezitha emkhakheni wamatekisi.
Isolezwe likhulume naye ngebanga aselihambile kulo mdlalo nokuthi kube njani ukuba yingxenye yawo kusuka, uqala kuze kube yimanje.
Uzophela ngo-Ephreli.
"Ebengikuthanda kakhulu kulo mdlalo wukuthi kubalingisi, yimina ebengimdala kunawo wonke umuntu futhi nginobudlelwane obuhle nabo bonke.
Ukulingisa ngenye yezinto engizithandayo kakhulu njengoba ngesikhathi ngifika eGoli, ngisuka eNewcastle nabazali bami, ngabona ukuthi impilo ngizoyakha ngokungena kulo mkhakha.
Ngempela wangiphilisa, buka manje ngikuphi.
Ngangena khona ngoba ngingafuni udumo kodwa ngenxa yokuthi ngifuna ukuphila," kuchaza uThembi.
Uthe okunye azokukhumbula ngomdlalo ukusebenza nentsha abenganqeni ukuthi uma kukhona engakwenzi kahle uma beqopha, amise yonke into ayisize.
"Mina benginganqeni ukuthi ngimise yonke into, ngisho ukuthi lo mlingisi akenzi ngendlela bese ngimbonisa ukuthi kumele kwenziwe njani.
Okunye esake sakuxabanela nophrojusa wukuthi babefuna ngibe nendoda kulo mdlalo.
Leyo nto angiyamukelanga futhi ngendlela engangingayithandi ngayo ngakubeka kwacaca ukuthi ngizoshiya kulo mdlalo, uma bengayishintshi indlela abenza ngayo, ngempela bakuyeka lokho.
Ukunginika kwabo umyeni kwakuzoshintsha indlela okumele uMkabayi anakekele ngayo umndeni wakhe.
Alibale indoda okuyinto eyayingavelanga ngithola le ndawo," kuchaza uThembi.
Ngisho empilweni yakhe yangasese uveze ukuthi akanaye umuntu wesilisa aphilisana naye.
"Ngiyathemba ukuthi indawo kaMkabayi ibafundisile abesifazane bakuleli okuningi abazophila ngakho.
UMkabayi ngisho engekho umfowabo uMpiyakhe, ubesala anakekele amakhosikazi akhe wonke, abheke ibhizinisi nezingane.
Kuyaphileka ngaphandle kwendoda, kumele sikunake lokho singabesifazane," kuchaza le ngqungqulu yomlingisi.
Uveze ukuthi maduze nje, abantu bazobona zanda izinkinga KwaManzini okuzophela belwa nazo njengomndeni.
Kulo mdlalo into athe akayithandanga ngawo, indlela owashintsha ngayo ekuhambeni kwesikhathi, yize kwakuthiwe uzogxila ematekisi.
"Kwakuthiwe uzogxila ematekisini kubonakale izinkinga zakhona kodwa lokho bakwenza kusizini yokuqala bakudedela.
Sila sikhona nje yingoba nami bengike ngibatshele ukuthi akesibuyele lapho umdlalo wawuya khona, siyeke lokhu osuyikhona manje senze nocwaningo.
Kodwa bebengitshela ukuthi angigxile kulokhu enginikwe khona, okunye ngikuyekele kubona.
Ababhali abaqala kulo mdlalo bese bengekho, bahamba, kwafika abanye base beqhamuka nokuhlukile," kuchaza yena.
Kulo nyaka uthe usazophumula njengoba kungekho mdlalo asazongena kuwona, okuzothi ngonyaka ozayo bese ethatha imisebenzi ezoqhamuka.
Ibuya ngonyawo olusha iBlood and Water
ABADIDIYELI befilimu eqoshelwa eKapa, iBlood and Water sebememezele ukuthi le filimu izoqala ukubonakala maphakathi nalo nyaka kwiNetflix.
Le filimu eyaba nesasasa ngonyaka odlule, abadidiyeli bayo ngempelasonto bamemezele izindaba zokuya emaphethelweni okuqoshwa kwayo, lokhu bakwenze bememezela nabalingisi abasha kule filimu iningi labo okuyintsha, esencane nedumile kulo mkhakha wokulingisa.
Baveze ukuthi abalingisi balo mdlalo abadala bonke bayabuya, ngakho ababukeli kumele bangakhathazeki.
Esitatimendeni abasikhiphile baveze ukuthi njengoba ababukeli bale filimu bacela isizini yesibili, sebengaqala bazilungiselele ukubona okuphethwe ile yisizini yesibili.
"Kumanje abalingisi balo mdlalo basebenza ngokuzikhandla ukuqopha le filimu sikhuluma nje.
Siyajabula ke ukwethulela ababukeli bale filimu intsha esanda kufika emkhakheni wokulingisa nezoqhubeka nokudala olunye uthuthuva kule filimu nakubafundi besikole iParkhurst," kuchaza isitatimende.
Baveze ukuthi kubalingisi abasha abajoyina lo mdlalo kukhona uLeroy Siyafa ozolingisa indawo kaSam.
"Uzoba ngomunye wabalingisi abazoba sembangweni kwezithinta uthando nozoshukumisa izinto kubafundi besifazane eParkhurst.
Asingabazi ukuthi lo mlingisi ungomunye wozothandwa ababukeli bale filimu.
Abanye abalingisi kukhona uGreteli Fincham, ozolingisa indawo kaRecee, Katishcka Chanderlal ozoba nguPauline no-Alzavia Abrahams ozoba uZyd," kuveza isitatimende.
Kubalingisi ababuyayo kubalwa uKhosi Ngema, AmaQamata, Natasha Thahane, Gail Mabalane, Cindy Mahlangu, Thabang Molaba, Arno Greeff, Mekaila Mathys noDillon Windvogel.
Abantu bakuleli bazijabulele izindaba zokumenyezelwa ukuthi sekuya ekupheleni ukuqoshwa kwale filimu futhi izophuma maduzane.

INHLANGANO yezokusakaza iSouth African Broadcasting Corporation (SABC), idilize abasebenzi abangu-621, iningi labo eligcina namhlanje.
Le nhlangano yamemezela ukuthi izodiliza abasebenzi ukuzama ukwehlisa izindleko.
I-SABC ithe abasebenzi abangu-346, yize kukhona eminye imisebenzi abebengafaka izicelo zokuyenza, banqume ukuthi bathathe imali yabo bahambe.
"Abanye bebekhathazeke ngomthelela wokwehla kwemali abebezoyihola okudalwe ukubuyekezwa kabusha kwamaholo nempesheni," kusho umkhulumeli wale nhlangano obambile, uMmoni Seapolelo.
Uthe abasebenzi abangu-275 bebenza imisebenzi esivaliwe futhi abanye bazamile ukufaka izicelo zemisebenzi kodwa bangaphumelela.
Kwenzeka lokhu nje, kulindeleke ukuthi kuqale izinhlelo ezintsha emisakazweni yale nhlangano kusasa njengoba kwenziwa izinguquko.

"Sibaningi esithole izincwadi nami ngingomunye wabo.
Akukhona ukuthi isikhundla sami asisekho kodwa sishintsha igama futhi kwehle nomholo njengoba iSABC izama ukonga imali.
Noma ngingazi ukuthi imali ibizokwehla kanjani kodwa ngithathe isinqumo sokuthi ngihambe," kusho uMngadi obesehlale iminyaka engu-15 kuKhozi.
Uthe njengamanje uzogxila emculweni futhi uhlela ukukhipha i-EP yakhe yokuqala aphinde asayinise nabanye abanethalente enkampanini yakhe.
