Ubuye ngesivinini uDJ wodumo kwezobumnandi
UBUYE ngesivinini uDJ wodumo endimeni yezokungcebeleka njengoba esemalungiselweni okukhipha i-EP yakhe maduze.
UDumile Kunene, odume ngelikaDJ Dumile ezindaweni zobumnandi, ubeseqalile ukubonakala enandisa ngezimpelasonto ngaphambi kokuthi izwe libuyele kumvalelandlini wesigaba sesithathu.
Exoxa neSolezwe NgeSonto uveze ukuthi bese kuyisikhathi eside ehlabe ikhefu kwezikaqedisizungu kodwa usebuyile.
"Empelei akukona ukuthi bengihlabe ikhefu kodwa bengimatasa ngizithuthukisa ngokufunda ama-software amasha okukhiqiza izingoma," kusho uDumile.
Uthe uma konke kuhambe kahle uzodedela i-EP ngamaholidi ePhasika, okuyilapho kuzozwakala izingoma zakhe, ezingakaze zizwakale.
Lo mklwebhi wamapuleti usanda kukhipha ingoma ethakaselwa ngabaningi, apike kuyona uMafa no-Amanda ethi Falling For You.
Echaza ngengoma, uthe yiyona emnike ugqozi lokukhipha i-EP ngendlela abantu abayamukele ngayo.
"Bese nginesikhathi ngagcina ukukhipha ingoma kodwa kube sengathi angikaze nginyamalale, ngendlela abantu abangamukele ngezandla ezifudumele ngayo," kusho uDumile.
UDumile useke wasebenzisana nabaculi abadumile kuleli, okubalwa kubona uJoe Nina nabanye abaningi.
Kulokhu wenze okuhlukile ngoba usebenzisana nophrojusa nabaculi abangakadumi, ngenhloso yokuvumbulula ithalente elisha.
"Kuhle ukubona namanye amaciko ephumelela kanti lokhu ngeke kufezeke uma sonke sizofuna ukusebenza nabaculi abadumile kuphela.
Yingakho ngizimisele ukuvundulula ithalente elisha ukuze sonke sizokhuphulana kule ndima," kusho uDumile.
Uthe ezinye zezingoma uzoziqhulula kancane kancane ezinkundleni zokuxhumana njengoba zisavaliwe izindawo abejwayele ukunandisa kuzona.
"Ngizobazwisa kancane ukuthi i-EP izobe iphetheni ukuze kuthi mhla iphuma, kube wukuthi bese bekade bayilangazelela," usho kanje.
Uphethe ngokuthi ubonga akaphezi kubalandeli bakhe abangamdubanga yize eke wanyamalala isikhashana, wathembisa ulozolo lwezingoma njengendlela yokubabonga.
SelukoKlebe 'olokugwazisa' kwabaculi oKhozini
NKOSIKHONA CELE noCHARLES KHUZWAYOKUYABASHUBELA abasakazi abasolwa ngokugwazisa abaculi ukuze kudlalwe izingoma zabo emsakazweni.
Kulaba basakazi kubalwa nabathathu bomsakazo Ukhozi FM.
Ngesonto eledlule ohola amaciko ngaphansi kwalo mkhankaso wokulwa nokugwazelwa kwemisakazo, uMzwakhe "The People's Poet" Mbuli, uthe lolu daba sebelufake koKlebe njengoba benamagama abasakazi nobufakazi ngalo mkhuba.
UMbuli, obecasuke egane unwabu, uthe kuyinto engakholakali ukuthi izingane zabantu eziculayo kumele zikhokhele amakhono azo ukuze zizothola ithuba lokuba kudlalwe umculo wazo emsakazweni.
"Ngeke size sithule sibona kudlalwa ngathi.
Ngeke size silenze iphutha lokuthi sigoqe izandla ekubeni sibona ukuthi kuyonakala.
Sifuna ubulungiswa," kusho uMbuli.
Okhulumela oKlebe kuzwelonke, uKatlego Mogale, ukuqinisekisile ukuthi uphiko lwabo, oluphenya ngenkohlakalo ebucayi, luthintwe yiqeqebana lamaciko akuleli maqede laletha nencwadi  efungelwe emaphoyiseni.
"Izinsolo eziphakathi zizophenywa kodwa ngebhadi ngeke sidalule amagama nezikhundla zabathize njengoba udaba lusaphenywa," kusho uMogale.
Amaciko afuna kuphenywe abadidiyeli bezingoma, abasakazi nophrojusa bezinhlelo zemisakazo engaphansi kweNhlangano yezokuSakaza kuleli (SABC).
Kwabasohlwini kubalwa umsakazi weSidlo Sasekuseni noSigiya Ngengoma oKhozini, uKhathide "Tshatha" Ngobe, abadidiyeli bomculo kulo msakazo okunguKhetha "KSG" Gwala noZanda Mthembu.
UKhetha uthe akaboni kulungile ukuthi angaphawula ngalolu daba olubucayi kangaka.
Uyalele intatheli ukuba ixhumane naloyo okhulumela iSABC.
UZanda, owake wasakaza oKhozini nakwiGagasi, naye igama lakhe elinaphazwe kakhulu, wale waphetha ukuphawula ngalolu daba ekhala ngokuthi ngokwenqubomgomo yomsakazo akagunyaziwe ukuba aphawule kwabezindaba.
UZanda usolwa nangokuba yiqili elizikhotha emhlane njengoba kuthiwa ushintshanisa ama-sim cards mihla namalanga.
Imizamo yokuthola ukuphawula kukaTshatha ayiphumelelanga.
Okhulumela iSABC, uMmoni Seapolelo, uthe sebeyazi ngezinsolo zokugwaziswa kwamaciko kodwa bazothatha izinyathelo ezifanele uma sebethole ubufakazi ngoba iSABC iyinyanya kabi iPayola.
UMbuli uthe baqale ngokubamba umhlangano nezikhulu zakwaSABC, uMadoda Mxakwe oyi-CEO nesikhulu sezemisakazo, uNada Wotshelwa, e-Auckland Park ngoFebhuwari 26.
Basuke lapho bayobhikisha buthule phambi kwamahhovisi futhi banikeza izikhulu uhlu lwezikhalazo ngoMashi 10.
Eqhuba uthe amaciko aphinde ayobonana nosigaxamabhande, uBrigadier Basi, nozakwabo emahhovisi amakhulu oKlebe, ePretoria.
"Umhlangano olandelayo ngePayola ngesizowubamba noMengameli wezwe, uMnuz Cyril Ramaphosa, khona maduze," kuphetha uMbuli.
Ukhala ngesenzo somculi kamaskandi umndeni kaMeyiwa
UMNDENI wowayengunozinti we-Orlando Pirates, udinwe uyaveva ngesenzo somculi kamaskandi, oqambe i-albhamu yakhe ngegama likaSenzo Meyiwa ngaphandle kwemvume yawo.
Lo mculi uGlama omatasa nezinhlelo zale albhamu engakatholakali ezitolo, kubikwa ukuthi akakaze ahlangane nalo mndeni okuthiwa uvutha ungabaselwe ngesenzo sakhe.
USfiso Meyiwa utshele Isolezwe ukuthi bamangele sebethola imibiko yokuthi kunomculi oqambe i-albhamu yakhe ngegama likamfowabo.
Uthe ngemuva kwalo mbiko, baphinde bathola ukuthi uGlama uhlela ukubonana nabo maduze.
"Bekumele aqale asithinte ngaphambi kokuthi anqume ukusebenzisa igama likaSenzo.
Sesiludlulisile lolu daba kubameli bethu.
Sizimisele ngokuthi siyilwe le mpi uma lo mculi (uGlama) engenzi ngendlela efanele," kubeka uMeyiwa.
Ethintwa uGlama, uthe bahlela ukuhlangana nomndeni ukuze balungise lolu daba.
"Iyafana necala into esiyenzile.
Yingakho sihlela ukuyobonana nomndeni ngaphambi kokuthi iqale ukudayisa i-albhamu.
Sizobe sesizwa ngawo ukuthi silulungisa kanjani lolu daba.
Okwamanje angizokwazi ukwanda kakhulu ngoba asikahlangani nomndeni wakwaMeyiwa," kuchaza lo mculi.
Lo mculi uthe uhlela ukuthi i-albhamu yakhe iqale ukutholakala ezitolo ngoJuni.
Uzoshubisa izinto kwiSono uZola Nombona
UMLINGISI wakuleli uZola Nombona, useveze ukuthi esikhathini esinzima lapho umsebenzi ungekho khona ngenxa yeCovid-19, uyalibonga ithuba alitholile lokulingisa emdlalweni Isono.
Kulindeleke ukuthi ishukumise indawo kaZola ayilingisa kulo mdlalo okhonjiswa esiteshini iBET (129), aqale ukubonakala kuyona ngeledlule.
Kulo mdlalo ulingisa indawo kaZoleka Sigcawu, ongowesifazane osebenza kahle, oyinhloko emkhakheni wezethelevishini nowebhola, esiteshini i-UltraSport.
"Ngaphandle nje kokusweleka komsebenzi nginengane encane okumele ngiyinakekele, ngiyabonga impela ngokuthola lesi sibusiso," kuchaza uZola ngamafuphi.
Kulo mdlalo uZola uzolingisa no-Anga Makubalo, olingisa indawo kaMakwande.
"UMakwande kuzoba sengathi kukhona okungahambi kahle ekhanda lakhe uma eqeda ukubona le ntokazi ezothatha amehlo akhe agcine ngokuthi acele ukuchitha isikhathi nayo nalapho ezobuya ejabule ngendlela eyisimanga, kodwa kukho konke kuvela into emshiya emangele engazi ukuthi enze njani njengoba bese ezitshela ukuthi konke kuzohamba kahle phakathi kwabo," kuchaza isitatimende esithunyelelwe abezindaba.
Siveze ukuthi kulo mdlalo kuningi okusazokwenzeka okuzojabulisa ababukeli.
Emasontweni adlule lo mdlalo ubugubha ukuhlanganisa iziqephu ezingu-100 waqala, lapho kwavela khona ukuthi kuningi okuzokwenza uthakaselwe ababukeli.
Baveza ukuthi abalingisi abaningi basazobonakala kuwona njengoba babesanda kwethula abaseNigeria ababekuwona okubalwa kubona u-Anthony Oseyemi, Christine Osifuye noChioma Umeala.
URasta uthi usematasa nomdwebo weSilo
ISILOMO seciko elidume ngokudweba osaziwayo siveza ukuthi leli sonto limatasa kakhulu kodwa abantu abangakholwa noma yini emataniswa naye ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.
ULebani "Rasta" Sirenji uthi ucela abantu behlise umoya bangamtatazelisi ngoba usematasa nomsebenzi wokudweba iSilo samaBandla, uMenzi Ngubane kanjalo noNoxolo Noxee Maqashalala.
Kusukela ngoMsombuluko ziqalile ukusabalala ezinkundleni zokuxhumana izithombe okuthiwa ngezomdwebo kaRasta kuvela iSilo, uMenzi Ngubane noNoxee.
URasta uthe abantu abangakholwa nanoma yini esabalaliswa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngoba imidwebo esafakiwe akuyona eyakhe.
"Ngimatasa nokudweba iSilo noMenzi, ngisahlalelwe nawu mdwebo kaNoxolo.
Ngizowufaka owami umsebenzi uma sengiqedile.
Benginazo izinhlelo zokuyihambisa emndenini (imidwebo) kodwa ngimiswe imigomo yeCovid-19, ngisacabanga indlela engizomisa ngayo ukubheka phambili," kusho uRasta.
Eqhuba uthe abantu bayathanda ukwenza umsindo ngomsebenzi wakhe bagcine sebekholwa namampunge asabalala ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.
Uthe ukusabalala kwezithombe okungezona ezakhe kugcina sekumqhatha nabantu abanye baze bamsabise ngoba kukhona abagangayo.
Ngikhulelwe, ethanda engathandi:Babes
UBHODLA umlilo umculi weGqom" uBabes Wodumo osolwa ngumamezala ngokusenga ezimithiyo ngokuthi uzithwele.
Le ntokazi yaseLamontville eThekwini ogama layo langempela uBongekile Simelane, ithi ngeke ivume ukuhlanjalazwa kanje, ngakho izovulela umamezala icala.
Ekhuluma nephephandaba elinguzakwabo weSolezwe, iDaily News ngoLwesibili, uBabes uthe uyibonile le video enezinsolo ezishaqisayo ngaye kaNksz Zama Gumede, ongunina kaMampintsha.
"Ngikhulelwe, ethanda noma engathandi.
Uma enenkinga nalokho angihlangene.
Ngiphatheke kabi ngalento.
Ngiyazi ukuthi akumele sizinake izinto azikhulumayo uma edakiwe kodwa kulokhu wedlulele.
Ngizomvulela icala.
Ngifuna ageze igama lami," kusho uBabes.
Kule video egcwale ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngoLwesibili unina kaMampintsha uthi uBabes wathi ukhulelwe amawele kodwa nanamhlanje akakawazali.
Uqhube wamsola ngokuthi ufake izipontshi esiswini ngoba efuna kuthiwe uzithwele.
UBabes ukuqinisekisile ukuthi uzithwele futhi ujabule kodwa ngeke asho ukuthi unezinyanga ezingaki.
Umthombo othembekile uthe unezinyanga eziyisithupha ezithwele.
Kuthiwa uNksz Gumede wazama ukuphazamisa umshado ngoMgqibelo kodwa wehluleka.
"Wafika edakiwe emshadweni efuna izinto.
Angazi mina lo mama ukuthi ufunani ngoba akazange amkhulise uMampintsha.
UMampintsha wakhuliswa ugogo wakhe, angazi kungani esengifaka kwipolitiki yakwakhe, bekungewona umsebenzi wami ukumazisa ngomshado.
Ngibuhlungu ngalento (ayikhuluma kwivideo) futhi ngeke ngiyiyeke idlule.
Ngifuna ukumkhombisa ukuthi ngingowaseLamonti, ngizombophisa," kusho uBabes.
Uqhube wathi unina kaMampintsha wayazisiwe ngomshado futhi akukho okuthinta isiko angakwenzanga njengomakoti wakwakhe ngoba ubefuna ukuhlanganisa imindeni yabo ngalo mshado.
UBabes noMampintsha babophe ifindo lika sofa silahlane ngempelasonto.
Umshado wabo wesintu obuseBallito ubuhanjelwe osaziwayo, umndeni kanye nabangani.
Laba culi baveza ngo-Okthoba nyakenye kwivideo eyasabalala ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ukuthi sebethembisene umshado.
U-Elaine ethubeni lonkuqoba indodo yeBET
INTOKAZI yakuleli engene yezwakala endimeni yomculo, u-Elaine, ingelinye lamaciko asemasha endimeni yomculo eliqokwe emcimbini wezindondo wase-USA, amaBET Awards.
U-Elaine, ezwenikazi lase-Afrika, uqokwe emkhakheni weThe Viewer's Choice: Best New International Act nentokazi yaseNigeria, uTems, nokuyibona bobabili abamele i-Afrika kulo mkhakha.
UMonde Twala wakwaViacom uveze ukuthi kuyabajabulisa ukuqhubeka nokuqokwa kwabaculi base-Afrika abakade bafika kulo mkhakha nabasha njengoba kucaca ukuthi umculo wabo unakiwe nakwamanye amazwe.
"Umkhakha weThe Viewer's Choice: Best New International Act wakhelwa ukuhlonipha abaculi abasanda kufika kulo mkhakha nabangene kuwona kwezwakala futhi abenza kahle kuwona.
Okunye ngawo ubheka ukuthi umculo wakho uhambe kangakanani kwamanye amazwe nokuyingakho kubonakala laba baculi kuwona, " kusho uMonde.
Uthe kuyajabulisa nokubona lonke uhlu lwabaculi abazohlonishwa kulo mcimbi njengoba benze kahle kakhulu ezingomeni zabo abaqokwe ngazo kulo mcimbi kanjalo nama-albhamu abo.
U-Elaine ubonge abalandeli bakhe noNkulunkulu ngokuqokwa kulo mcimbi, wathi uyohlale ebathanda ngenxa yento abemenzele yona.
Ukuvotela lo mkhakha kuqale ukuvulwa ngoMsombuluko, kuyoze kuvalwe ngoLwesihlanu ngo- 4 ntambama.
Abanye abaculi abaqokwe kulo mcimbi base-Afrika baqokelwe emkhakheni weBest International Act nguBurna Boy waseNigeria, Diamond Platnumz waseTanzania noWizkid waseNigeria.
Lo mcimbi uzosakazwa bukhoma ngoJuni 28 kuBET Africa (DStv channel 129) ngo-2h00 ezintatha.
Sizogadla nangezinhlelo zakuleli isiteshi esisha kuDStv
SELUMENYEZELWE usuku okuzoqala ngalo isiteshi sethelevishini esisha esizobe sigadla ngezinhlelo ezahlukene zase-Afrika, iHONEY ezotholakala kuDStv (173), kusukela ngoFebhuwari 15.
Kulesi siteshi kuzobonakala izinhlelo ezintathu zakuleli uma siqala okukhona kuzona oluthi Pastors Wives, Shine Shine neThe Buzz.
Ohlelweni iPastors Wives kuzobonakala amakhosikazi abefundisi bamabandla amakhulu kuleli ekhombisa ngempilo yawo yansuku zonke.
Lolu hlelo lusungulwe intokazi engumlingisi uSonia Mbele, owasungula iThe Realhousewives of Joburg.
UYolisa Phahle ongumphathi wakwaMultichoice,uveze ukuthi, izinhlelo abazibophele kulesi siteshi zizogqamisa ithalente izwe i-Afrika elinalo.
"Ohlelweni iPastors Wives sizobona ukuthi abesifazane abayeni babo abangabefundisi bamabandla adumile, bamelana kanjani nokuphatha ibandla nemindeni yabo.
Kulolu hlelo ngeke nje kugqame okuhle kuphela kodwa kuzobonakala nezimpi phakathi kwala makhosikazi.
Okunye ngalo wukuthi ngeke kubonakale amakhosikazi abefundisi bakuleli kuphela kodwa nawakwamanye amazwe ase-Afrika," kusho uYolisa.
Uthe abanye besifazane abazobonakala ezinhlelweni ezihlukene kukhona uPearl Umeh waseNigeria, Patricia Kihoro noFoi Wambui baseKenya, Anele Mdoda, Mbali Nkosi no-Anele Zondo bakuleli.
"UMbali uzokwethula uhlelo oluthi Shine Shine, oluzogxila ekusizeni abantu abafuna ukushintsha indlela ababukeka ngayo.
U-Anele Mdoda uzokwethula uhlelo oluthi The buzz, okuwuhlelo oluyinkulumo ngxoxo, la ezokhuluma khona nabesifazane basemazweni ahlukene ngezinto ezithinta isiko, ezothando, ezempilo abangani nemindeni,"" kuchaza uYolisa.
Uthe kulesi siteshi okubajabulisa kakhulu wukuthi sizoveza izinhlobo ezihlukene zamasiko nendlela okuphilwa ngayo emazweni ase-Afrika.
NjengeDStv uthe bayathemba ukuthi bazoqhubeka nokuletha izinhlelo ezenza baziqhenye ngendlela abaphila ngayo abantu base-Afrika.
Lesi siteshi uthe sizotholakala kuleli eNigeria, eGhana, Kenya, e-Uganda, Namibia, Botswana, Malawi, Zambia, Angola,Mozambique, eTanzania, DRC naseCameroon.
Sona kuDStv uthe, sizotholakala kuCompact, Compact Plus nePremium.
Isayine esitebeleni                   sase-USA iJoyous
ABASUNGULI beqembu lomculo wokholo iJoyous Celebration, sebeveze ukuthi banqume ukusayinisa leli qembu esitebeleni saphesheya kwezilwandle ngenhloso yokusabalalisa umculo walo.
Lokhu kulandela ukuthi kube nesivumelwano phakathi kwesitebele sakuleli i-Universal Music Africa neMotown Gospel, ezinze e-USA.
UDkt Lindelani Mkhize ongomunye wabasunguli baleli qembu, uveze ukuthi lesi isiqalo esisha kubona njengoba belungiselela ukukhipha i-albhamu yabo yesi-25.
"Kule minyaka engu-25 siyingxenye yaleli qembu, kuningi ebesikufunda ngakho ke ukushintsha kwezinto ezenzeka ngayo kulo mkhakha esikuwona sibone kungcono ukuthi sithathe lesi sinqumo.
Umculo weJoyous usuzotholakala e-USA naseCanada okwamanje esithemba ukuthi lesi yisiqalo esisha.
Sizizwa sivuselelekile, sinomdlandla omusha njengoba sishintsha izinto nje siya kwelinye izinga," kuchaza uLindelani.
Uthe uhambo lwabo lube olungelula kuyona yonke le minyaka kodwa kuyabajabulisa ukuba la bekhona manje.
"Ukuhlanganisa iminyaka engu-25 akulula neze, ukuba nobudlelwano nalesi sitebele kuyasijabulisa njengoba kuzovula amanye amathuba emazweni aphesheya kwezilwandle njengoba sidinga ushintsho.
Esifuna ukukusho, i-albhamu entsha isetshenzwe kakhulu futhi abantu abalindele okuhle nokumnandi kodwa kuyona maduzane, njengoba izophuma iPhasika lingakadluli," kusho yena.
U-EJ Gaines ongomunye wabaqondisi besitebele iMotown Gospel, uveze ukuthi bakujabulele ukusebenzisana ne-Universal Music Africa, ebathulela iJoyous Celebration asebebonile ukuthi yiqembu elithandwayo emhlabeni wonke.
USipho Dlamini ophethe i-Universal Music Group kuleli, uveze ukuthi leli thuba kube elijabulisayo njengoba leli qembu liqhubeka likhula.
"Umculo wabo uzofinyelela nakwabanye abalandeli babo.
Siyabemukela futhi siyathemba ukuthi sizosebenzisana kahle ukuze kuqhubeke nokuvuleka kwamanye amathuba.
Sizosebenza nabo kukhona konke abakwenzayo okuthinta nokuqopha umculo wabo nokuhambisa iqembu lonke la liya khona.
Lokhu kufezekise iphupho lethu leminyaka," kuchaza uSipho.
I-albhamu yeJoyous Celebration 25 ezophuma isihloko sayo sithi Still We Rise.

Njengoba umyalezo wawubhekiswe emaphoyiseni ngesikhathi sikahulumeni wobandlululo, ngokuhlukunyezwa kwabantu abamnyama, namanje zisenzeka izigameko zokuhlukunyezwa kwabamnyama ngamaphoyisa.
Isihluku esenzeka eMarikana kubulawa abantu ngamaphoyisa, singesinye sezibonelo zokuthi amaphoyisa asenesihluku asibhekise kubantu abamnyama," kusho uMtwa.
UMtwa uthe bazoqala kusasa ukuzilungiselela lo mdlalo okulindeleke ukuthi uye nakwezinye izifundazwe.
Phambilini umdlalo wavakashela emazweni ahlukene njengoSwaziland, Scotland, England, USA nase-Australia.
ike yahlabana ngezindondo kwiDrama Critic Circle Awards, eyeBest Play, Best Director neBest Actor kwiLos Angeles International Festival ngo-1987.
Ngo-1993 yaphendulwa ifilimu yaseHollywood, eyayiqondiswa wumlingisi wamafilimu waseMelika, uMorgan Freeman.
Kuvulwe eminye imingenelo kumaSaftas
ABEMIKLOMELO yezokulingisa ehlonishwayo eNingizimu Afrika amaSouth African Film and Television Awards (Saftas), banxusa ukuba kuthunyelwe imingenelo yeminxa yokuhlonipha abenze kahle.
AmaSaftas okuzobe kungaka-15 uma esenziwa kulo nyaka ngoMeyi 21 no-22.
INational Film and Video Foundation ebhekele imiklomelo ifuna imingenelo emunxeni weLifetime Achiever Award.
Kulo munxa okwake kwahlonishwa kuwo abalingisi okubalwa uThembi Mtshali-Jones, John Kani, Lillian Dube, Joe Mafela, Cynthia Shange nabanye, kufuneka abantu abanamava abanegalelo elikhulu kwezethelevishini namafilimu eNingizimu Afrika naphesheya.
Omunye umunxa okufuneka imingenelo kuwo ngoweYouth Achiever Award.
Kuwona kufuneka abantu abenza umsebenzi wabo ngokuzimisela abaneminyaka engaphansi kuka-35.
Kowe-Outstanding Person with Disability Contributor Award kufuneka ophila nokukhubazeka ogqame kwezamafilimu nethelevishini, Outstanding Provincial Contributor Award okuzohlonishwa ngawo umuntu, iqembu okanye umkhankaso othuthukisa amafilimu nethelevishini esifundazweni nowe-Emerging Filmmaker Award okuhloswe ngawo ukuklomelisa umuntu osemusha kwezamafilimu nethelevishini.
Yonke imingenelo kumele ithunyelwe kwiNFVF ngaphambi kuka-Ephreli 2.
Ukungenela kweminye iminxa kuvulwe ngoNovemba ngonyaka odlule kwaze kwaba nguJanuwari 22.
Muva nje kusanda kuphuma ithenda lokufuna inkampani ezohlela umcimbi wakulo nyaka ozodonsa izinsuku ezimbili.
Ukulifakela kuvalwa kusasa.
Akudluli kumsakazi woKhozi owaliwa yisoka
UMSAKAZI woKhozi FM othandwa abaningi ngomusa namancoko, uMroza Buthelezi udlulise enduduzo kunontandakubukwa obuye abe ngumethuli wezinhlelo osanda kugilwa yisoka lakhe, uLaSizwe.
UMroza uveze ukuthi isigameko sokugileka kukaLaSizwe simvusele iminjunju yokwaliwa yisoka engalonanga ngalutho.
Lo msakazi uveze lokhu ohlelweni lwantambama iSisonke Drive alwethula noMzokoloko, uthe lo mshophi wamehlela eminyakeni eminingi eyedlule kodwa uma ecabanga ngakho kuvele kuzwele engathi yinto eyenzeke izolo.
Uthe lokhu kwamehlela ngosuku olukhulu lokuhlukanisa unyaka, ngalowo mzuzu wayetetemuka nabanye kumnandi bengcebeleko olwandle kanti isoka lihlela ukumala.
"Awufuni ukudlula lo myalezo Mzo, ngempela ngiyadinga ukwelulekwa ngoba noma sengimdala ngingaka manje kodwa umyalezo wahlala.
Cha, wagadla mfowethu," kusho uMroza ephela insini.
Okumangaza kakhulu ukuthi le nsizwa ayigcinanga ngokucela bahlukane kuphela kodwa yaphinde yavuvuzela usawoti esilondeni"Waze wakugcizelela impela ukuthi uyabona sengathi impilo yami imile.
Ifana nesiqeda ngakho ngeke akwazi ukuthi siqhubeke," kusho uMroza.
UMzokoloko ubelokhu emduduze njalo uzakwabo.
Kuphinde kwavela ukuthi leli soka labuye lazisola ngokuhamba kwesikhathi selibona uMroza esimama kwasho khona ukuthi wawuzwa kahle umyalezo njengoba usankeneneza namanje ezindlebeni.
UMroza ungomunye wabasakazi boKhozi abahlala benconywa ngokuba nobuntu nokuhlonipha umsebenzi nabalaleli nokumenza ahlale ehamba phambili.
Ngaphandle kwalokhu uma kuziwa endimeni yezokusakazi ukhombisile ukuthi alukho uhlelo olungamhlula njengoba ekwazi ukusakaza ngesikhathi ezahlukene kanti nezinhlelo asezenze kulo msakazi seziningi kakhulu.
Ulaxaze ubuthishela olingisa kwi
UKUHLALA etshelwa ukuthi akabukeki kahle futhi nomzimba wakhe awuhehi, akumvimbanga ukuthi afeze amaphupho akhe umlingisi waseBergville.
UNompumelelo Vilakazi (23), olingisa indawo kaSne kwiDiepCity edlala kwiMzansi Magic, uthi ukhulele esigodini saseMagangangozi, nokuyilapho afunda waqeda khona eWinterton, eBergville.
Kumanje uNompumelelo ungomunye wabalingisi abaphambili, kulo mdlalo ongene endaweni yeSibaya.
Engxoxweni neSolezwe le ntokazi idalule ukuthi ngenkathi iqeda umatric yafundela ubuthishela e-UKZN eThekwini, okuyilapho yafunda kabanzi ngomkhakha wokulingisa.
"Ngasekhaya kuneqembu elenza izinto ezihlukene emkhakheni wamaciko engaba yingxenye yalo, futhi lalihambela izindawo ezihlukene eBergville.
Bengihlala ngitshelwa ukuthi angimuhle futhi nginomzimba omkhulu, lokhu kwenza ngizenyeze kakhulu ngangakhululeka ekwenzeni into engizithandayo.
Ngaqeda isikole ngase ngiya kokwenza iziqu zobuthishela e-Edgewood, nokuyilapho ngabuyelwa ukuzethemba ngenxa yezinto engafike ngazithola khona, ezithinta ukulingisa yize ngingakufundelanga kodwa kuningi engakufunda khona," kuchaza uNompumelelo.
Uthi esafunda ngemva kokubuyelwa ukuzethemba kwakhe, wangenela umncintiswano wozime wabantu abondlekile, nokuyinto eyamjabulisa.
"Ngabuyela ekhaya ngo-2019, ngaqala ngazama ukungena emkhakheni wokulingisa.
Bengithumela ama-video ami ngilingisa ezinkampanini ezihlukene kuleli.
UMandla N ngibone ngenkathi efuna abantu abazolingisa ku-Instagram, ngazama kodwa ngangaphumelela ngoba inetwork ibingihlupha emakhaya.
Lelo thuba lagcina lingilahlekele.
Kuthe sengingalindele lutho, uMandla wangibiza eGoli ngizokwenza inhlolokhono yalo mdlalo, okuyilapho ngashiya phansi nokufundisa eNtatakusa Secondary, la kwamina ngafunda khona," kuchaza uNompumelelo.
Uveze ukuthi indawo kaSne njengoba abantu sebeyibonile, izoqhubeka nokukhombisa owesifazane obekezelela ukuhlukunyezwa yisoka lakhe.
"USne ngesikhathi uqala lo mdlalo ubeyisigebengu esikhululekile, kodwa manje usenovalo ngemuva kwesigameko esehlile kwaze kwakhona oboshwayo.
Okunye ngaye wukuthi uhlalele ubudlelwane lapho ahlukunyezwa khona kodwa ngeke aye ndawo ngoba uthola uthando esokeni lakhe, nokuyinto akhule engayazi.
Ubudlelwane bakhe nesoka buzogqama kanti abantu bangalindela nokunye okukhulu kulo mdlalo," kuchaza intokazi yaseBergville.
Lo mlingisi uveze nokuthi ubusisekile empilweni ngokuthola indawo ephambili emdlalweni omkhulu kangaka, ekubeni uyaqala ukulingisa emdlalweni wethelevishini.
'Kusenzima ukukhuluma ngoNgamla'
UVEZA ukuthi bekusenzima ukukhuluma ngokushona kukazwakwabo umlingisi owayedlala indawo ephambili kumdlalo wansuku zonke phakathi nesonto kuSABC 1, iGenerations, uSonia Mbele.
Lo mlingisi owayedlala indawo kaNtombi kwiGenerations nokuyindawo eyayimsondeza kuMenzi Ngubane, owayelingisa ekaSbusiso "Ngamla" Dhlomo, uveza ukuthi ubengathule nje ngoba engezwanga ngezindaba ezibuhlungu zokudlula kukaMenzi kodwa bekusenzima ukuthi aphawule ngakho.
"Bengithule ngisetshisa izindaba zokudlula kwakhe emhlabeni.
Okwethu bekuwuthando olwaluhlanganiswe umdlalo wethelevishini, uyohlala uwubambo lukaNtombi," kusho uSonia.
Abantu abaningi bakhumbule izikhathi ezazimnandi nemdima eyadlalwa yilaba bobabili kwiGenerations eminyakeni edlule.
Le ndawo njengoba esho USonia yabenza basondelana kakhulu nokwenza kwabanzima ukwamukela kubabukeli uma bexoshwa laba balingisi kwiGenerations.
UMenzi uqhubeke nokulingisa kweminye imidlalo emikhulu okubalwa kuyo neSibaya kanjalo namafilimu.
Kuyona yonke imidlalo ebelingisa kuyo ubevelela ngekhono lakhe nobekumenza abenogazi kubabukeli.
Yize ebesewumlingisi onamava kodwa ubengababukeli phansi ozakwabo abasebasha kwezokulingisa ngokushona kwabanye babo okubalwa nomlingisi weHostella uThobani Nzuza.
Ezindaweni zokungcebeleka nasezitolo uMenzi ubevamisile ukubonakala exoxa nabantu ethatha nezithombe ngaphandle kokukhononda.
Uzobonakala kuZalo uMaMkhize
UZOTHI xinti izinsuku ezimbalwa emdlalweni Uzalo usomabhizinisi waseThekwini uShauwn Mkhize.
UShauwn udume kwabaningi ebonakala ohlelweni obelukhombisa ngempilo yakhe oluthi KwaMamkhize, obelukhonjiswa kuMzansi Magic.
NgoMsombuluko ntambama inkampani eqopha Uzalo iStained Glass, iveze izindaba zokuthi uShauwn, uzobonakala kulo mdlalo kusukela ngoLwesine (namhlanje).
Ngokwesitatimende esithunyelwe kwabezindaba uShauwn uzobe elingisa indawo yowesifazane ongusomabhizinisi onemali, ofuna ukuthenga ibandla iKwaMashu Kingdom Church.
Ngokwamazwibela alo mdlalo kuleli sonto, abazalwane sebezwile ukuthi umfundisi wabo ufuna ukudayisa ibandla, okuzothi esiqeshini sangoLwesihlanu bathole ukuthi kukhona oselithengile.
Ekhuluma ngokuba yingxenye yalo mdlalo uShauwn, uthe ube nesikhathi esimnandi eqopha kuwona.
"Ngijabule kakhulu ngokuthola ithuba lokubonakala kulo mdlalo isikhashana, njengoba kungeke kube isikhathi eside.
Ukubona abalingisi balo mdlalo futhi ngibe nesikhathi nabo kube umzuzu ojabulisayo kimina futhi okusekude ukuthi ngiwukhohlwe.
Esengikulindile manje ukuthi wonke umuntu abone uhlangothi lwami lwethalente ebengilifihlile, lingaziwa muntu," kusho uShauwn.
NgoLwesihlanu iyaphela isizini yesithupha yalo mdlalo njengoba kuzoqala eyesikhombisa ngoMsombuluko.
UNomfundo Zondo okhulumela lo mdlalo, uveze ukuthi kuleli sonto bazokhipha isitatimende esizocacisa ngokusha okuzobonakala kusizini entsha, nokuthi obani abadlali abazobonakala kuyo.
Kuleli sonto kuphinde kwavela izindaba zokuthi uJet Novuka, obelingisa indawo kamseshi uMpambani, uyashiya kulo mdlalo.
Abanye abashiyayo kubalwa uSiyabonga Shibe noBaby Cele ogcine ukubonakala kulo mdlalo emasontweni amabili adlule.
Ekupheleni kwaleli sonto ababukeli balo mdlalo bazobe sebazi ukuthi obani abalingisi abasha abazoqala ukutheleka kulo mdlalo ngesonto elizayo.
Kuwona ezinyangeni ezizayo kulindeleke ukuthi abalingisi abadala balo mdlalo babonakale kuwona maduzane.
Kwababuyayo kubalwa uKhaya Dladla, Nokuthula Mabika, Ntokozo Dlamini noNay Maps.
Amacala endoda awahlangene nomkayo: Ongoti
UKUVELA kwesiqephu ohlelweni iReal Housewives of Durban lapho ongunkosikazi wesihlabani sokholo esingasekho emhlabeni, u-Ayanda Ncwane etshelwa ukuthi kumele ayohlawula amacala awashiya kubo kwentombi, simangaze abaningi.
Izakhamizi zaseNingizimu Afrika nababukeli bohlelo lakwiShowmax iThe Real Housewives of Durban oselukhonjiswa kuMzansi Magic, balokhu bephawule njalo ngokuvela kwezindaba zokuthi u-Ayanda Ncwane kumele angenelele azame ukuyohlawula amacala kaSfiso Ncwane owashiya ethembise ukuyohlawula kubo kanina wengane yakhe naye oyingxenye yalolu hlelo.
Kulolu hlelo lokhu kuvele njengento eyingxenye yesiko newubuntu futhi umndeni wakubo kanina wengane obona kungaba yisixazululo esingaqinisa nobuhlobo.
Ongoti bezamasiko bathi noma ikanjani ingane nonina bafanelwe ukuyohlawulwa futhi nabakubo kantombi bafanele ukubasela inhlawulo.
Ungoti wezesintu nesazi samasiko uSolwazi Sihawu Ngubane uthe lokhu kusuke kudinga ngqo umuntu wesilisa ngoba amacala akhe okumele ahlawulwe uyena.
Owesifazane oyingoduso noma oshade naye ephila noma engasekho emhlabeni usuke engangene nakancane.
"Akangene nakancane owesifazane emacaleni enziwe indoda yakhe ngoba noma ngabe bashadile yaphinga, kufanele kube iyona eyohlawula ingane ekhabonina.
Uma kwenzeka indoda ishona ingakahlawuli, unkosikazi akangene lapho.
Angikaze ngizwe ngisho emlandweni ukuthi endulo kukhona okufaka owesifazane emacaleni endoda," kusho uNgubane.
Eqhuba uthe isintu sihambisana nobuntu.
Uma kwenzeka owesifazane enothando lokuqoqa izingane zendoda yakhe, kuhle futhi kuyakhuthazwa kodwa kodwa akukho okomphoqayo.
Uma kuvuka amacala endoda kusuke kufanele abakubo kantombi bayozibika kubo kandoda. "
Inja ibanjelwa umnikazi wayo, uma indoda ishona kade ishiye yone komunye umuzi yaze yathola nomntwana, kumele kuyobikelwa abazali bayo ekhaya.
Yibona okumele bamele lawo macala ngoba uma kuzohlawulwa komunye umuntu, kuthintwa nomsamo kubikelwe idlozi.
Uma unkosikazi enesifiso sokufaka isandla, angapha abazali imali kube yisipho sabo bese bona beyisebenzisa ngendlela yabo,"kusho uNgubane.
Eqhuba uNgubane uthe okuba umqondo omuhle ukuthi owesifazane onengane engaziwa noma etholwe ngaphandle, abakubo bayombika nangalo usuku okuvele ngalo ukuthi indoda ayisekho emhlabeni ukuze uma kunesiko eligcinwayo nelingakhaleleka enganeni isheshe ilithole.
"Isiko elingagcinwa ngaleso sikhathi eliqondene nesifo kodwa uma sekukhaleleka amanye kufanele enziwe ingane seyihlawuliwe abakubo kandoda.
Unkosikazi naye onezingane naleyo ndoda eshonile okumele azikhulise yedwa ngakho ukuhlawula ingane eyodwa kungabe sekusho ukuthi uma kuvela enye ingane nayo kolindeleka ukuthi enze okufanayo,"kusho uNgubane.
Omunye futhi ungoti wesintu nokukhuliswa kwezintombi, uNkk Nomagugu Ngobese ubambe emazwini kaNgubane njengoba ethe ingane ezalelwe ekhaya ngokomthetho wesintu eyasekhabonina ngoba nezinto zesintu zisuke zilindeleke komalume.
"Uma kuyingane yentombazane kuze kulindeleke imicimbi efana nembeleko nomemulo yenzelwe ekhabonina lapho sithi ikomalume khona.
Unkosikazi wendoda eyakutholisa untwana akahlangane nakancane nenhlawulo yengane nokugcinwa kwesiko ngaphandle uma ezenzela yena kusuka othandweni,"kugcizelela uNkk Ngobese.

UMNGANI omkhulu ka-Emmanuel "Mjokes" Matsane, uDJ Mahoota uthe ukhalise okwengane encane ngesikhathi ezwa ngokushona kwakhe.

ITrompies ibunjwe nguMjokes, Spikiri, Mahoota, Donald Duck noJakarumba.

Yilapho sisungule iqembu lomculo khona ngaphambi kokuhlangana noJaros (Jakarumba) wasifaka kuSpikiri noMdu Masilela eqenjini iMM Deluxe.
USpikiri wasifaka njengabadidiyeli nonjiniyela bomsindo.

OwoKhozi ucasule omaskanda eqamba izinja zakhe ngabo
UZITHINTELE owoKhozi FM eqamba izinja zakhe ngamagama omaskanda maqede wawadalula kwiFacebook.
U-Ayanda Melansi, onguphrojusa wohlelo iJabul" Ujule oludlala kuKhozi FM nolushayelwa nguDudu " Lady D" Khoza, ucasule abaculi bakamaskandi, ngenkathi edalula ukuthi izinja zakhe zinamagama afana nawabo.
Ubhale kwiFacebook ezwakalisa ukukhathazeka ngokugula kwezinye zezinja zakhe, athe uthole ukuthi ngesikhathi ziyohlolwa kuvele izinsolo ezithi zidliswe ushevu.
U-Ayanda ubethe ukhathazekile ngokugula kwezinja zakhe, okunguNtencane noNyonemhlophe.
Kuyona iFacebook kukhona obuze ku-Ayanda isizathu sokuqamba izinja zakhe ngamagama omaskandi, waphendula ngokuthi akunasizathu kodwa ngamagama awathandayo.
Udalule nokuthi empeleni bezinhlanu izinja zakhe sezizonke, okunguMfazomnyama, Mgqumeni, Nyonemhlophe, Ntencane noSgwebo Sentambo.
Uthe kodwa uSgwebo Sentambo noMgqumeni sebathengwa, usesele nezinye.
Kuthintwa uSgwebo Sentambo ngalolu daba, uthukuthele wagana unwabu, wathi kumele u-Ayanda asho ukuthi ufunani kuyena usengaze aqambe inja yakhe ngegama lakhe.
"Ngeke ngikwazi ukuthula ngale nto eyenziwe ngu-Ayanda ngoba ngiyabona ukuthi unenkinga nami.
Wake wangitshela emehlweni ukuthi akangithandi.
Manje usezoqamba inja, ngami.
Ngifuna angichazele ukuthi ufunani.
Ngeke ngithule nje enza le nto.
Ngeke futhi ngimncenge ngoba ngisaba ukuthi umculo wami kawuzodlalwa kuKhozi ngoba vele kawudlalwa," kusho uSgwebo Sentambo.
USgwebo Sentambo usho kanje maqede waqopha i-video wayifaka ezinkundleni zokuxhumana echapha u-Ayanda Melansi ngenhlamba.
UNdlemnyama waBafana bakaMgqumeni, uthe okwenziwe ngu-Ayanda kungubukela phansi omaskanda.
"Uma kungukuthi la magama uyawathanda, kungani engaqambanga izingane zakhe ngawo kunokuthi aqambe izinja?
Angimazi ukuthi uhloseni ngale nto," kusho uNdlemnyama.
UNyonemhlophe uthe usamangele ngesenzo sika-Ayanda.
"Kufana nokuthi usithukile ngoba kuyacaca ukuthi usibona siyizinja.
Kuyadumaza ukuthi akhombise ukubukela phansi umculo kamaskandi ngalolu hlobo," kusho uNyonemhlophe.
UNtencane uthe yena akaboni lutho olubi futhi ubengeke u-Ayanda afake negama lakhe uma kungukuthi ubeqonde into embi.
"U-Ayanda ngudadewethu.
Ngiyamhlonipha naye uyangihlonipha.
Ngisho kukhona inkinga enginayo ngiyaxhumana naye, ngifune iseluleko," kusho uNtencane.
Ethintwa u-Ayanda, uthe ngeke esakwazi ukuphawula ngalolu daba.
"Into esingicasula wukuthi uSgwebo wenze ne-video engichapha ngenhlamba.
Akaqhubeke enze ngendlela abona ngayo.
Mina ngisamile ekutheni bengikhuluma ngezinja zami engikhathazekile ngokugula kwazo," kusho u-Ayanda.

UMSAKAZI woKhozi FM ophinde abe nguDJ wasezindaweni zobumnandi, uKing Sfiso, uthi kuqondanile ukuthi ethi esehlele ukukhipha ingoma ehlonipha Isilo samaBandla, sivele sikhothame.

"Ngeke ukholwe ukuthi ingoma eyango-2019.
Sasihlele ukuthi siyikhiphe ngonyaka odlule kodwa ngenxa yomvalelandlini yagcina ingaphumanga," kusho uKing Sfiso.
"Isilo sikhothame sengivele ngiluhlelile usuku ezophuma ngalo.
Isizathu esenza ngingakaze ngikhulume ngayo le ngoma nokuyiphusha ingoba angifuni kube ngathi ngisizakala ngokukhothama kwaso.
Ngike ngakucabanga kodwa ngabona ukuthi abantu bazosho ukuthi "awubuke leli thatha.
"Uthe umqondo wokuhlonipha Ongangezwe Lakhe waqhamuka emuva kokuzwa uBlack Coffee edlala izibongo zakhe uma edijeya.
"Sasifuna ukuthola enye inyosi ukuthi izozisho engomeni kodwa sagcina singayitholanga," kusho yena.
UKing Sfiso owethula uhlelo iBhampa 2 Bhampa neChillas, uthe ubefuna ukukhipha i-albhamu kodwa ucwaningo lwakhe lwaveza ukuthi isikhathi asivumi.
Uthe ngonyaka odlule ukhiphe ingoma ethi Maqondana noDJ Vitoto noSkyewanda, eyenza kahle ngokudlalwa emsakazweni kodwa yasheshe yaphupha.
"Ingoma yenza kahle izinyanga ezimbili bese iyacwila.
Ukuphusheka kahle komculo kuncika ekutheni uyaya yini kubantu.
Uma uthembele emsakazweni nakuthelevishini kuyashesha ukuphela.
Ingoma sasihlola ngayo ukuthi kuyenzeka yini, sabona ukuthi akwenzeki, yingakho ngikhiphe i-EP ukuze ngizokwenza abantu bangangikhohlwa.
"I-EP yakhe itholakala ezitolo zomculo okubalwa kuzo i-iTunes, Traxsource nezinye.
Asibanike ithuba abasakazi ezinhlelweni ezintsha
KUYASUKA ukukhuluma kuleli sonto ngoLwesine njengoba iziteshi zeSABC zizoshintsha izinhlelo abasakazi bafakwe kwezinye.
Minyaka yonke uma sekungu-Ephreli kusuke kuqala unyakazimali omusha emsakazweni okusho nokuqala kwezinkontileka ezintsha.
Silinde uLwesine nje, asevele aqalile amahlebezi oukuthi izinhlelo zizoshintsha kanjani kwezinye iziteshi kodwa sesilinde ukuthi kuqinisekiswe yiziphathimandla.
Lo mkhuba wokushintsha abasakazi yinto endala ejwayelekile kodwa kwesinye isikhathi thina njengabalaleli sibuye senze sengathi kusha sifune izinto zenzeke ngendlela yethu.
Ngiyazi, imisakazo ikhona ngenxa yethu futhi nabaphathi kumele bazibheke nezimfuno zethu kodwa kwesinye isikhathi asibanikezi ithuba abasakazi lokuthi bazinze ezinhlelweni.
Uthi umuntu eqala nje ngakho kodwa sibe sesimgxeka sibona izici.
Hhayi ngoba esuke ebheda kodwa sivala izindlebe singafuni ukuzwa okuhle ngoba nakhu isithandwa sethu singangenanga ohlelweni ebesisuke sisibheke kulo.
Ngiyacela sike sibanikeze ithuba lokuthi bazinze ezinhlelweni bajwayele bese kuyima sibehlulela kahle.
Izibalo zokulalelwa kwemisakazo ezikhishwa yiBroadcast Research Council of South Africa yizo ezihlulela kahle abasakazi ukuthi benza njani ezinhlelweni zabo nokuthi iziteshi ngezinguquko ezizenzile ngabe zishaye emhloleni yini.
Ngike ngibone ezinye ngezinyanga zokuqala zenze izinguquko izibalo zidubule ziye phezulu kodwa uma sekuphuma ezilandelayo bese ziyehla.
Ngokwami sisuke sifuna ukuzwa ukuthi izinguquko zikahle yini kodwa uma sezibheda bese siyashintsha siye kwezinye iziteshi.
Kuye kwenzeke futhi ukuthi uma sixoxa nabangani bethu sivumelane ngokuthi umsakazi othile uyabheda kodwa ngaphakathi esiteshini izibalo zokulalelwa kohlelo lwakhe zilokhu zikhule njalo.
Kumele uma kukhona umsakazi esizwa ukuthi akalwenzi ngendlela uhlelo singanikeli ezinkundleni zokuxhumana siyomgxeke simbeke nezici.
Phela ekugcineni naye ungumuntu ophilayo futhi uyazwela njengabo bonke.
Yingakho abanye beze behluthuke baphendulane kabi nabantu ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.
Kumele sizame ukugxeka ngendlela eyakhayo ukuze nomuntu akhule.
Kodwa uma engenzi ngendlela singamuzwa njengabalaleli futhi nezibalo zimphika, abaphathi kumele basilalele bamfake lapho engenza kangcono khona.
Lubuye nomethuli omusha uhlelo iLove Back
"Uhlelo iLove Back lungolunye lwezinhlelo ezingenza ngikuthande kakhulu ukusebenza emkhakheni wethelevishini, ngani ngoba luhlanganisa abantu futhi lwakha imiphakathi egcwele uthando.
Lwenza isiqiniseko sokuthi siyisizwe esihlangene ngenxa yothando esikhombisana lona futhi siyakwazi ukukhuluma ngokuvuleleka emphakathini ngezinto ezithinta uthando," kuchaza uMzwandile.
Kulolu hlelo uveze ukuthi bazoqhubeka nokusiza abantu abafuna ukwakha uthando nabantu abahlukana nabo, nasebebona kungcono baphinde bazame futhi.
"Izingxoxo ezivulelekile engibe nazo nabantu abazobonakala kulolu hlelo, izona ezingenze ngakuthanda kakhulu ukuba umethuli walo futhi ngagqugquzeleka ukuthi ngiqhubeke nokulwethula.
Ngiyabonga kakhulu ngethuba engilitholile, ngiyethemba abalandeli balolu hlelo bazoluthokozela njengoba nami ngikujabulele ukuba ngumethuli walo," kuchaza uMzwandile.
Le nsizwa isanda kukhuza ibuya kwithelevishini ngemuva kokunyamalala isikhashana.
Muva nje, uMzwandile uke wabonakala elingisa emdlalweni iThe River, elingisa indawo ka-Elvis Baloyi obeyiphela endlebeni kuLindiwe Dikana (Sindi Dlathu), owadubula wabulala indodakazi yakhe uTumi.
U-Elvis ubelazi lonke iqiniso ngokufa kukaTumi, futhi efuna ukushada noLindiwe ngenkani ukuze amgcinele imfihlo yakhe.
UNomsa Philiso wakwaM-Net, uthe bakujabulele ukubuya kwalolu hlelo futhi bayathemba ukuthi abantu bazomjabulela uMzwandile ozobe esiza abake bathandana baphinde bavuselele lokhu ababenakho ekuqaleni.

UZodwa nonyanyavu lwemoto
ABAWUVALI abantu umlomo uZodwa Wabantu eziqhasabula ngemoto yomacaphunakusale.
UZodwa Wabantu usematheni kwabaningi selokhu efake isithombe seLamborghini ezinkundleni zokuxhumana njengoba abantu belokhu bembongele njalo.

Emuva kokuvalwa kwemicimbi ebimngenisela imali wabona ithuba lokuqala ibhizinisi ebelibukeka lilincane futhi lingeke limenzele inzuzo etheni.
UZodwa Wabantu usedume ngokudayisa amaqanda muva nje, lama qanda akakhethi zindawo kodwa uwadayisa kuwona wonke amalokishi namadolobha ngisho basemgwaqweni uqobo.
Abantu balokhu bembongele njalo okubalwa ngisho osaziwayo.

Sicela usinikeze ikheli lakho ukuze ugweme ukuthunyelwa amasamanisi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana," kusho ummeli kaBonang encwadini.
UBongani Fassie nohlelo ngempilo yakhe kuMoja Love
INDODANA kaBrenda Fassie, uBongani, izoveza konke okwenzeka empilweni yayo emuva kokudlula kukanina emhlabeni.
UBongani uzokuveza lokhu ohlelweni, iFinding Bongani Fassie, ezoqala ngMgqibelo, ngo-20h30.
Kulolu hlelo uzoveza ukuthi kwenzekani ezimalini azishiyelwa ngunina nokuthi ibe njani iminyaka engu-17 unina engasekho.
ULindiwe Mbonambi weMoja Love uveze ukuthi kulolu hlelo kuzogqama indlela uBongani akhule ngayo, eqala yaba ngefudumele kodwa yahamba yaba nzima.
"Uzalelwe ekhaya elifudumele kodwa ngemuva kokudlula emhlabeni kukaBrenda, impilo yaba nzima kakhulu.
Abantu bazobona ukuthi impilo ayiphilile ibingelula ngempela futhi ibe namuphi umthelela.
Uzoveza ukuthi webelwa kanjani imizi ayeyishiyelwe nguBrenda kanjalo nezigidi zemali, ezinye zazo agcina engazitholanga, nokuthi ukuzihlanganisa nabantu abangalungile kwamlethela buphi ubungozi empilweni yakhe," kuchaza uLindiwe.
Uqhube wathi uBongani uzochaza kabanzi ukuthi abantu abathembisa ukuthi bazomnakekela bamjikela kanjani ngesikhathi esedinga usizo kubona.
"Kukhona abantu, ngesikhathi kushona uBrenda, abathembisa ukuthi bayowa bevuka noBongani, uzoveza ukuthi lukhona yini usizo aluthola kubona noma cha.
Wuhlelo lolu abantu abazoluthokozela kakhulu njengoba luzoveza okuningi okungenzeka ukuthi abantu bebezibuza ngakho mayelana nalo mfana," kuchaza yena.
Kulolu hlelo kulindeleke ukuthi kubonakale osaziwayo okukhona kubo uMercy Phakela, Kuli Roberts noChicco Twala.
Lolu akulona kuphela uhlelo kulesi siteshi okulindeleke ukuba ludonse amehlo abaningi.
Kuqala isizini yesibili yohlelo, Isencane Lengane, ngoMgqibelo, ngo-20h00.
Kulolu hlelo kuzobonakala abashadikazi abasebancane, uSiyacela noThando, emuva kweminyaka emithathu bashada.
Nohlelo olwethulwa wuJub Jub, Uyajola 9/9, nalo lushaya ibuya ngeSonto, ngo-21h00.
UJub Jub noMoss Makwati bazobambisana ukusiza abantu abafuna ukubhekelwa omaqondaba babo ukuthi basathembekile yini.
Selumenyezelwe usuku lweVodacom Durban July
ISIKHISHIWE indikimba yengqephu yomcimbi wamahhasi waminyaka yonke, iVodacom Durban July yalo nyaka.
I-Durban July yalo nyaka izoba ngoJulayi 3 eHollywoodbets Greyville Racecourse kanti indikimba emenyezeliwe, ithi Birds of a FeatherUStephen Marshall oyimenenja kwezokukhangisa kwaGold Circle, nobhekele ukuqhakanjiswa kwendikimba, uthe sebekulinde ngabomvu ukubona abasiki bengqephu ukuthi yini abazoyihlanganisa ethinta le ndikimba.
""Indikimba ejule kakhulu lena uma uyibheka kahle njengoba ihambisana nesimo esinzima esibhekene naso manje emhlabeni, ngakho nabasiki bengqephu bazojula kakhulu uma besika izingubo ezihlukene ezithinta le ndikimba.
Lona ngomunye wemicimbi esiziqhenya ngawo kakhulu njengoba uhlanganisa abantu bezinhlanga ezihlukene zakuleli futhi udonsa amehlo abaningi ngisho emhlabeni," kuchaza uStephen.
Uthe okunye ngale ndikimba ukuthi isondele kakhulu kulabo abahambela lo mcimbi.
"Izimpaphe zenyoni zisondelene, akulula ukuthi uzifice ziqhelelene, nale ndikimba isho khona okwenzeka kulo mcimbi njengoba uhlanganisa abantu abafike basebenze ngokubambisana ezintweni abasuke bezenza kuwona.
Isho ukuthi noma singabhekana nani uma nje sibambisene singanqoba.
Sesikubheke ngabomvu ukubamba lo mcimbi ngosuku esesilumemezele," kuchaza yena.
Ngonyaka odlule lo mcimbi wawubukwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngenxa yeCovid-19.
Yize sewutholakele umjovo waleli gciwane kodwa abahleli balo mcimbi abakuvezanga ukuthi bazowubamba kanjani lo mcimbi kulo nyaka.

Lihoxisiwe elokushaya ebelibhekene nomlingisi
MBALI KHANYILEUMLUNGISI weMbewu; The Seed uPhindile Gwala obesobishini ngokushaya isitshudeni saseMgungundlovu eCubana ngeledlule, ugcine ethelelene amanzi nale ntokazi ehoxise icala emvulele lona.
Lo mlingisi nale ntokazi uNompilo Mkhize (23), kuthiwa bagcine ngokuthi bawahoxise bobabili amacala abavulelana wona ngobusuku abahilizisana ngabo kule ndawo yobumnandi.
Esitatimendini salo mlingisi ku-Instagram, uveze ukuthi yena noNompilo kanjalo nomndeni walesi sitshudeni, bagcine ngokuthi bathathe isinqumo sokuthi bakhumelane umlotha.
"Ezinsukwini ezedlule abantu bakuleli bazwakalise imizwa yabo ngesigameko esingesihle esimbandakanya mina noNompilo.
Ngalokho ngabe ngenza iphutha uma ngingayibongi imizwa yabo eyakhayo, nangendlela engesekwe ngayo ngesikhathi kwenzeka lesi sehlo.
Ngidlulisa ukubonga nakuNompilo nomndeni wakhe," kubeka lo mlingisi.
Uthe yize kube khona ukuphambana kwemimoya phakathi kwabo, umoya wobumbano nokuzwana, yiwo oholele ekutheni bathelelane amanzi.
"Angizogxila kakhulu odabeni lokuthathelana izinyathelo zomthetho kodwa umoya wokubuyisana yiwo osiholele ekutheni sinqume ukuhoxisa amacala ebesivulelene wona.
Sesivule ikhasi elisha manje empilweni yethu.
Ngiyathemba ukuthi ngokwesekwa ngabantu bakuleli, sizokwazi ukudlula kulesi simo sobabili," kuqhuba yena.
Uthe ufisela uNompilo konke okuhle empilweni nasezifundweni zakhe.
UNompilo ekhasini lakhe kuFacebook, utshele abangani bakhe ukuthi uPhindile uxolisile wabe esethenga nomakhalekhukhwini omusha.
Abanye abantu abebephawula kuleli khasi, bebengayizwisisi eyokuxola kwalesi sitshudeni.
Abanye babo bebekhala ngokubhalwe esitatimendeni, bethi akukhombisi ukuthi uyazisola uPhindile ngakwenzile.
UPhindile obeseCubana nabangani bakhe ngempelasonto, kubikwa ukuthi waqonda ngqo kuNompilo owayematasa eshutha izithombe ngomakhalekhukhwini wakhe owawubheke ngakubona (kuPhindile nabangani).
Lo mlingisi okuthiwa wayediniwe, wafike wahlwitha lesi sitshudeni umakhalekhukhwini waso wawuphahlaza phansi, ngaphambi kokuthi asiklwebhe ebusweni.
UNompilo wavulela uPhindile icala lokumshaya ngenhloso yokumlimaza nelokuphahlaza umakhalekhukhwini wakhe.
Umlingisi ukhuza ibuya kwiMbewu
UMLINGISI okhuza ibuya emdlalweni owuchungechunge Imbewu:The Seed uPortia Ncwane, uthe bekunzima ukubuya ngenxa yokushoda kozakwabo.
UPortia (28) owaba yingxenye yalo mdlalo ngo-2018, udlala indawo kaSli Ngwenya.
"Ngithole ucingo lokuthi indawo yami iyabuya.
Angifuni ukuqamba amanga, bekunzima ukubuyela ngaphandle kuka-Enhle Gambushe (owashona engozini yemoto ngo-2018) ngoba sasisondelene kakhulu.
Bekungathi ngizombona kodwa ke umsebenzi kumele uqhubeke kunzima kunjalo," kusho uPortia oke wadlala kuZalo nasefilimini iLove Lives Here.
Le ntokazi edabuka eNanda kodwa esihlala eNewlands eThekwini, ithe uSli ngumuntu ofuna kuzwakale uma ekhuluma.
"Ufuna inhlonipho, futhi uyazikhulumela.
Njengoba manje esebuyile indawo yakhe isondelene kakhulu noKaMadonsela (Brenda Mhlongo), okuyinto ezovivinya ubudlelwano bakhe nomndeni wakwaBhengu.
USli uhluke kakhulu kunami kodwa sicishe sifane ngokuthi nami ngiyayimela into yami," kuchaza uPortia.
Uthe ukhuza ibuya kulo mdlalo nje, uke wanyamalala eNingizimu Afrika wayohlala e-United States of America, emuva kokuthola umfundaze weMandela Washington Fellowship for Young African Leaders eNyuvesi yaseDelaware eNewark.
"Bengihamba izindawo njengakoNew York ngisebenza nabezobuciko bakhona.
Ngibuye ngonyaka odlule ngenza umdlalo wami ngedwa iThe Journey of Growing Pains ePlayhouse Theatre.
Umdlalo ukhuluma ngezinhlungu zokukhula nokujabulela nje impilo.
"Le ntokazi ephinde ibe ngumdansi futhi eke yahambela amazwe ahlukene, ithe iyazifela ngobuciko nangokufukula umphakathi njengoba yaqala inhlangano engenzi nzuzo iPortia Ncwane Foundation, esiza kakhulu abantu abasha.
UPortia kulindeleke ukuthi aqale ukubonakala namhlanje kwiMbewu ekhonjiswa ku-e.tv ngo-9.30 ebusuku phakathi nesonto.
Ukuzibulala kukanina kumenza asize abanye
UMLINGISI womdlalo wethelevishini ophinde abe ngumkhangisi, usebenzisa ubuhlungu abuzwa ngenkathi unina ezibulala, ukuthi afundisa intsha yabesifazane ngokubaluleka kokubhoboka uma ukhungethwe yizinkinga.
UTebogo Thobejane olingisa kuMuvhango uveza ukuthi ukuzibulala kukanina kwashiya amanxeba angakaze aphole yize kwenzeka eneminyaka ewu-11.
Ngaleso sikhathi unina wayeneminyaka ewu-31 kodwa kuze kube yimanje unembuzo engaphenduleki.
Ukuhlasela kobhubhane iCovid-19 nokusebenza nentsha, nabantu ababhekene nengcindezi ngalesi sikhathi, uthe kumvulele isithombe sokuthi nonina yayinkulu impi ayebhekene nayo yedwa.
"Ngikhetha ukukhuluma ngakho ngoba abantu abaningi bacabanga ukuthi akuyona ingcindezi yangokomphefumulo akuyona into yangempela.
Ikakhulu ngalesi sikhathi abantu besifazane abaningi bephelelwa nayimisebenzi benezingane ezibabhekile.
Abantu besifazane kumele belokhu bekhuthazwa ukuthi bakhulume ngezimo ababhekene nazo kuze kube bayabhoboka ngazo," kusho uTebogo.
Yize enohlelo alwenza nezingane zamantombazane ezikoleni kodwa njengamanje umatasa nezinhlelo zokuvula isikhungo ahlela ukuthi siqale ukusebenza maduze nje lapho ezokwazi ukuhlanganisa izingane nonina.
Inhloso yakhe enkulu ukuthi abesifazabe ikakhulukazi amantombazane, bavule izifuba ngezimo ababhekene nazo ukuze bathole usizo.
Kuzokhumbuleka ukuthi emnyakeni edlule uke wavuleleka kuleli phephandaba eveza ukuthi wakhula ngaphandle kukanina nokwamthwesa ubunzima esethola ingane.
UTebogo waveza ukuthi nebhizinisi lakhe lamaBofa okungamabhande esisu, laqala ngoba kwamthatha iminyaka ukwazi ukuthi owesifazane kumele azinakekele abophe nesisu uma esebelethile.
Uphinde waveza nokuthi noma kuyinto ahamba nayo ubuhlungu bokuzibulala kukanina, kodwa okuhle ukuthi uyakwazi ukusiza abanye abesifazane bangazitholi sebethatha isinqumo esifanayo.
"Ngifisa abesifazane bazi ukuthi ingcindezi yomphefumulo yisifo futhi siyelapheka.
Abangazenyezi ngoba usizo bangaluthola akulona ihlazo," kusho uTebogo.
Ephetha uthe ukulekelela nokusiza omunye umuntu kuwumsebenzi wanoma ngubani obonayo ukuqinisekisa ukuthi azikho izingane eziswela onina njengaye.
Uzalo luvikela abalingisi okuthiwa abagculisi
UKUBUYISWA kwabadlali abake balingisa kuZalo phambilini, okubalwa uKhaya Dladla noNokuthula Mabika, kufakele lo mdlalo isigcwagcwa kubabukeli njengoba bekhala ngokuthi izindawo zabo azigculisi.
UKhaya ubuyele endaweni yakhe yakudala kaGC abeyidlala phambilini kanti uNokuthula ubuyele kwekaThobile.
Ababukeli babhale ezinkundleni zokuxhumana begxeka futhi bekhononda ngokuthi abachazekile ngendlela laba balingisi abadlala ngayo kuZalo.
Ngokusho kwababukeli, izinga lokulingisa kwabo lenza uZalo lwehlelwe yisithunzi futhi bathi abagculisekile ngalaba balingisi selokhu bebuyile kulo mdlalo.
Abanye bakhale ngohleko lwabo uma belingisa, bathi alubachazi.
Kukhona abathe laba balingisi baphendula Uzalo isikeshi kanti abanye bebezwela ababukeli abasaqhubeka nokulubukela, bethi bona bahluleka ukuqhubeka nokulubuka ngenxa yabalingisi abangakhombisi ukuba nekhono.
Okhulumela Uzalo, uNomfundo Zondi uthe ukubakhona kwalaba balingisi kubalulekile kuwona nakubabukeli.
Indlela okuhlelwe ngayo indawo kaGC nekaThobile ibalulekile ukwenza lo mdlalo ubemnandi futhi ujatshulelwe ngababukeli.
Sicela ababukeli boZalo baqhubeke nokulubuka ngoba kuningi okusazobajabulisa ngezindawo zalaba balingisi," kusho uNomfundo.
Kwenzeka lokhu nje, kuke kwanemibiko yokwehla kwesibalo sababukeli kuZalo kukhalwa ngokuthi indlela olubhalwe ngayo ayigculisi.
AboZalo bazivikela ngokuthi ngesikhathi kuphuma izibalo, azizange zigxile kuZalo kuphela kodwa neminye imidlalo yayibhekene nenkinga efanayo.
Isolezwe lijabule nabafundi eMaqaqa
BAGEZEKE ubebebe abathandi bobumnandi abebehambele umcimbi weSolezwe, obuse-Adams eMaqaqa Exclusive Lifestyle ngoMgqibelo.
Kutheleke iningi labantu kanti umcimbi ubugabe ngosaziwayo nabaculi abangaconsi phansi kwezikaqedisizungu.
Abaculi abebebhekwe kakhulu bekunguProffessor obegubha usuku lwakhe lokuzalwa, uDJ Mngadi obethula ingoma entsha noBig Zulu onandise kwachwaza iningi.
Basine bededelana oDJ abashisa izikhotha kulezi zinsuku bejabulisa abantu, phakathi kwabo kubalwa uWonder, Oros, DJ Nzwiri, Menzi The Drum, DJ Phumuza, DJ Tx, DJ Ma CDJS nabanye abaningiUNksz Noluthando Ngubane, wophiko lwezokukhangisa kwiSolezwe, uthe inhloso yomcimbi bekungukuhlanganyela nabafundi bephephandaba kwazise ukuthi sekunesikhathi eside sagcina ukuba ndawonye nabo ngenxa yemibandela yeCovid-19.
"Sihlele ukuthi sihambele izindawo ezihlukene esizaziyo ukuthi zinabafundi bethu.
Lolu bekuwuhambo lwethu lokuqala, kanti ziningi ezinye izindawo esisazozihambela.
Siphathela nabafundi izipho njengendlela yokubabonga ngokuseseka kwabo kulesi sikhathi esinzima esibhekene nezwe," kusho uNksz Ngubane.
Uthe kuzomenyezelwa maduze ukuthi lizolibasa ngakuphi Isolezwe ngokulandelayo, wathembisa ukuthi bazozama ukufinyelela kuzona zonke izindawo.
Baningi abanye osaziwayo abebekhona kulo mcimbi kanti neSelimathunzi ibikhona izoqopha obekwenzeka.
Abezokuphepha benze umsebenzi oncomekayo beqinisekisa ukuthi imigomo yeCovid-19 iyalandelwa nokuvikela abaculi, abantu abebefuna ukuzithintela mathupha kubona.
Zimhambela kahle izinto uLucia Mthiyane
KUBUKEKA zimhambela kahle izinto emkhakheni wokulingisa kulezi zinsuku uLucia Mthiyane njengoba esejoyine umdlalo, iDurban Gen.
U-Lucia, ozobe elingisa indawo ka-Albertina Cele kulo mdlalo, uzoqala ukubonakala namhlanje.
Kulo mdlalo uzofika njengoba kusanda kudlula emhlabeni udadewabo ogane kwaGumede, uMaCele (Monica Thuli Zulu), noshone emuva kokuphatheka kabi kwase kuthinteka inhliziyo ngenxa yezigemegeme ebezenziwa ngumyeni wakhe uBab'Gumede (Sifiso Sibiya).
Ngokwesitatimende esithunyelelwe abezindaba, u-Albertina ungowesifazane ozimele nongekho ntekenteke, oyimelayo into ayenzayo.
"Ungowesifazane wasemakhaya okholelwa ukuthi kukhona isizathu esimenza abe okhethekile futhi kumele aphathwe ngendlela ephezulu noma yikuphi la aya khona.
Ungowesifazane okwazi ukubona abantu ukuthi banjani esanda kuhlangana nabo, engakabazi kahle kodwa avele asho nje ukuthi lo muntu asembonile unjani futhi uphila impilo enjani.

Kulo mdlalo uzofika kwaGumede esezizwa ngenye indlela ngoBab" Gumede futhi ngesikhathi behlangana okokuqala kula kuqala khona ingxabano yabo bobabili.
Kulo mdlalo uMaCele ungomunye wabalingisi abasazonyamalala kuwona.
Kuyimanje ungomunye wabalingisi abasanda kubonakala emdlalweni omusha othi Lingashoni ku-1Magic (103).
Abanye abalingisi abasazonyamalala kulo mdlalo kubalwa uNtando Mncube, Lihle Dhlomo noSifiso Sibiya.
Engxoxweni yakhe neSolezwe muva nje, uLucia uveze ukuthi ukujabulele ukubuya ekulingiseni njengoba eke wavela nakuDiep City isaqala.
U-Enhle Mbali ugeqe amagula 'ngokuhlukunyezwa' wuBlack Coffee
UKUHLALA egcwele ukwesaba novalo ngenxa yobengumyeni wakhe uveza ukuthi yikhona obekumenza afele ngaphakathi umlingisi odalule ukuthi ubeshaywa uDJ obengumyeni wakhe.
U-Enhle Mbali Mlotshwa useshicilele isitatimende wasinameka ezinkundleni zokuxhumana emuva kokuthi uBlack Coffee naye ephumele obala izolo waveza ukuthi uyamsukela ngezinsolo zokumshaya.
U-Enhle uthe akekho vele umuntu ohlukumezanayo owake wazivumela ngokwakhe ukuthi uyahlukumezana.
Selokhu ephumele obala u-Enhle uthi uzizwa ezethemba futhi engenavalo manje.
"Angisesabi manje ngifisa sengathi ngingakwazi nokuzibala izikhawu engishaya, engichapha engishiya ngiphuke umoya ngingeyilutho.
Njengo mshadikazi ngiyakwazi ukuhlukumezeka emoyeni, nokuhlukunyezwa ngamagama, imali, ngazo zonke izindlela.
Ngaphezulu kulowo mshado kuhambisana nokuphinga ngaze ngalala esibhedlela ngelashelwa ukhwantalala," kusho u-Enhle.
Eqhuba uthe leminyaka emihlanu edlule bekunzima kuye nezingane zakhe zihlala zizibonela ngamehlo ehlukunyezwa ekhaya.
Uveze nokuthi ngo-2014 wamshaya ngezikhathi ezihlukene ekamelweni labo.
Ngonyaka olandelayo u-2015 emuva komcimbi wakhe uBlack Coffee iMusic is King, uthe wamjikijela ngesikhwama kulandela ingxabano ababenayo ngaleso sikhathi emzini wabo omusha.
U-Enhle uthi akugcinanga lapho njengoba ebuye wamphinda egubha usuku lokuzalwa.
"Selokhu kwaqala uhlelo lokwehlukanisa ulokhu engisabisa  enginswinya nemali ngoba efuna ukungivala umlomo.
Angisoze ngachithela inkantolo isikhathi ngidlale nangokuhlukunyezwa," kusho u-Enhle.
Ukukhuluma kwakhe uthe ufisa kube yisibonelo nesifundo kumadodana akhe azi ngobubi bodlame olubhekiswe kwabesifazane.
Yize ebengafisi ukukhuluma ngezinkinga zomshado wakhe kodwa uveze ukuthi ubona kuzosiza nabaningi, wabonga nokwesekwa akuthola kwabanye abantu besifazane.
OwaseMsinga emafilimini anzima
KUMHAMBELA kahle umlingisi waseMsinga, uSifundo Dladla, njengoba esengomunye wosaziwayo asebevelele emidlalweni yethelevishini.
Khona maduze uSifundo (25), wasendaweni yaKwaHluphiwe, uzobonakala efilimini emfishane kwiMzansi Magic esihloko sithi Lesiba.
Yize engakabi nesiqiniseko sokuthi lo mdlalo uzokhonjiswa nini kodwa unxuse ababukeli ukuba bahlale begqolozele amathelevishini abo.
USifundo uthe ukhuliswe wugogo wakhe uMaNkabinde KwaZulu-Natal kodwa elokhu evakashela unina eGoli.
"Ukukhulela eKZN bekumnandi kwaze kwaba ngifika eGoli ngoba yilapho ngafike ngathola khona ukuthi impilo ihluke kakhulu khona.
Bengilokhu ngivakasha uma kuvalwe izikole.
Ngithe kodwa sengihlala khona unomphela ngoba bese ngizoqhuba imfundo yami, ngathola ukuthi izingane zaseGoli zinamaphupho amakhulu futhi ayafezeka lapha."
Uthe esakhula emakhaya kwakuhlale kukhulunywa ngokuba wuthisha, udokotela noma iphoyisa.
"Uma ngitshela abantu eKZN ukuthi ngifuna ukuba kwiTV, babevele baphele yinsini.
Bathi ngiyahlanya ngoba babekholelwa ukuthi uma ungowaseMsinga awusoze waba yilutho ngaphandle kokuba yiphoyisa noma uthisha.
"Uthe ukhule kubo kungekho ithelevishini nogesi.
"Ngangibuka iTV kuphela uma ngivakashele umama eGoli.
Yingakho ngagcina senginothando lwayo futhi ngangibona ukuthi uma useGoli ungaba kwithelevishini nanoma yinini.
"Uthe uqale ukungena emkhakheni wezokungcebeleka ngo-2008 ngokuba wuDJ nge-computer ne-sound system ayeyithengelwe wunina.
"Umzala wami, uSbongiseni, wayevamise ukungifundisa ukuthi zenziwa kanjani izinsimbi zengoma.
Ngabe sengiba uDJ futhi igama lami lasesteji nguS-Deez."
Uthe ukulingisa ukuqale ngo-2015 futhi wadlala efilimini ethi Mkhulu kwiMzansi Magic.
Ngonyaka olandelayo, uSifundo ulingise kwenye ethi Fatherless.
"Ngabuye ngabamba iqhaza ohlelweni olusakazwa kwiSABC 1 iNow Or Never iminyaka emithathu.
Ngo-2017, ngalingisa kwiGold Diggers kwi-e.
tv, emdlalweni woKhozi nasefilimini yoMzansi Magic ethi Pastor Bae.
Ngo-2019, ngadlala kwiRhythm City nasemafilimini oMzansi Magic athi Toro neMme Matswale.
Ngidlala izindawo eziqavile."
Ngonyaka odlule, uSifundo ulingise indawo kaNew Guy kwiGomora, okuyindawo ethandwe kakhulu ngababukeli.
Ngaphandle kokulingisa, uSifundo ubuye abambe iqhaza nakwingqephu njengoba enezimpahla zokugqoka ezibizwa ngeTypical Zulu Clothing.
Uhoxile ekwethuleni iRea Tsotella uMakamu
ISITESHI iMoja Love sithi siyakwemukela ukwehla ekwethuleni uhlelo kukaMbhishobhi Israel Makamu.
Lokhu kulandela ukusabalala kwengxoxo yalo mbhishobhi, ekhuluma nowesifazane emcela inkonzo yasekameleni.
Le nkulumo uMakamu uveze ukuthi yaqoshwa eminyakeni emine edlule, osekumumangaza ukuthi ivele manje.
Kuyona kuzwakala uMakamu eqala ebuza owesifazane ukuthi unobani, ngoba kukhona into afuna ukumcela yona.
"Uzonginika angithi?
Ngiyakucela phela, angithi uwedwa lapho.
Ngiyakunxusa, oh uyangichomela?.
"Lona wesifazane uzwakala enqaba ethi ngeke akwenze okucelwa inceku yenkosi.
Esitatimendeni esikhishwe ilesi siteshi uMakamu athula kuso uhlelo oluthi Rea Tsotella, baveze ukuthi basazoba nophenyo lwangaphakathi ngalezi zinsolo.
"Siyakwemukela ukuthi uBishop Makamu uthathe isinqumo sokuma ekwethuleni izinhlelo ngaphansi kwesiteshi iMoja Love.
Lokhu kulandela ukusabalala kwengxoxo phakathi kwakhe nowesifazane ethinta ucansi.
Ngaphambi kokuthi abuye emsebenzini sizophenya ngalesi sigameko.
Ekuxhumaneni nesiteshi uMbhishobhi ukuqinisekisile ukuthi umsulwa njengoba lona wesifazane wayemsebenzela futhi kule nkulumo wayefuna imali kuye," kusho isitatimende.
Siqhube sathi umbhishobhi uveze ukuthi kukhona abazama ukudicilela phansi igama lakhe njengoba lolu daba lwaxazululwa ngo-2017.
"Uveze ukuthi umangele uma lolu daba seluphinde luvela emasontweni amathathu adlule.
Ngakho njengesiteshi siyakholelwa ekutheni sizwe izinhlangothi zombili ezithinta lolu daba.
Esikufunayo ukuthola iqiniso ngalo nezinto ezikhulunywa kulona udaba.
Njengesiteshi le ngxoxo siyithathela phezulu kakhulu, sesiluqalile uphenyo futhi sesixhumene nowesifazane othintekayo kulona," kusho umphathi wesiteshi uBokang Moyo.
Uqhube wathi uhlelo lwabo, oluthi AmaBishop izindaba ezifana nalezi luhlale luzibheka, ngakho bebengeke baze baluzibe lolu daba.

Kubuya abalingisi abaxoshwa kuZalo
KUZOSULEKA izinyembezi kubabukeli bomdlalo Uzalo, njengoba izintandokazi zabalingisi balo mdlalo zikhuza ibuya.
Abalingisi okukhona kubona uKhaya Dladla (GC), Nokuthula Mabika (Thobile), Nay Maps (Mxolisi) noNtokozo Dlamini (Mastermind) kuvela ukuthi bazoqala ukuqopha kulo mdlalo kuleli sonto.
Umthombo weSolezwe ongashayi eceleni, uveze ukuthi ukuvela kwezindaba zokushiya kulo mdlalo kukaThandeka Dawn-King (MaNgcobo), yikhona okwenze abadidiyeli bawo bathatha isinqumo sokubuyisa laba balingisi.
"Kucacele noma ubani ukuthi badinga ukubhukula kulo mdlalo.
Abekho abantu ababacabangile ngesikhathi uThandeka eveza izindaba zokuthi uyahamba, babone kungcono ukuthi babuyise bonke abalingisi ababaxosha, okungangabazisi ukuthi nakanjani bazobuyisa isithunzi salo mdlalo uphinde ujatshulelwe ngabaningi futhi," kuchaza umthombo.
Uveze ukuthi kuleli sonto uKhaya noNokuthula bayaqala ukuqopha njengoba beyobuya ngesonto elilodwa nokuyogcina ngalo ukubonakala kukaMaNgcobo kulo mdlalo.
"UKhaya ngizwe ngandlebenye ukuthi nomdlalo iThe Zwide's oqoshelwa i-e.
tv ozovala isikhala seRhythm City uyafuneka nakuwona, asazi ke ukuthi uzowancelisa kanjani amawele, abanye bona bakhululekile ngenxa yokuthi ayikho imidlalo abagxile kuyona bazoqopha ngokukhululeka kuZalo," kuchaza umthombo.
Omunye umthombo uveze ukuthi uNay Maps ngeke aze ahlale isikhathi eside kulo mdlalo.
Omunye umthombo ngaphakathi uveze ukuthi kuleli sonto ababhali balo mdlalo basazohlangana neSABC ukumemezela lezi zindaba.
"Lezi zindaba zisheshe zaputshuka kwabezindaba njengoba kungakaphothulwa okuningi ngokubuya kwalaba balingisi.
Kusamele kubikelwe iSABC ngomqondo ababhali abanawo bese uma ivuma ngokuthi lo mdlalo uzoyaphi futhi uzothakaselwa yini, bese kuqalwa ke besayiniswa izinkontileka ezintsha," kuchaza umthombo.
UNomfundo Zondi okhulumela inkampani eqopha lo mdlalo iStained Glass, uveze ukuthi ngeke liphele isonto bengasikhiphanga isitatimende esichaza ngezinguquko kulo mdlalo.
"Akukho engizokukhuluma manje ngalaba balingisi kodwa engingakuthembisa ukuthi ngeke leli sonto liphele singacacisanga ngezinguquko ezizokwenzeka kulo mdlalo," kuchaza yena.
Kulo mdlalo kulindeleke ukuthi kuphele ngendawo kaGabisile elingiswa uBaby Cele noQhabanga (Siyabonga Shibe).
Ufaniswe neqhawe umlingisi oshonile
UBEHLUSHWA yisifo sikashukela nesifo senhliziyo umlingisi wakuleli oshone ngokuzuma, uShaleen Surtie Richards (66), okuvele izindaba zokudlula kwakhe emhlabeni izolo.
Le ntokazi yase-Upington, eNorthern Cape, kuvele ukuthi ishone ilele endaweni yezivakashi eseKapa.
Kuvela ukuthi ubekule ndawo nje ngoba ubematasa eqopha omunye wemidlalo, i-Arendsvlei.
U-Shaleen uzakhele igama kwiGenerations lapho ayelingisa khona indawo kaMattie.
Waphinde wabonakala efilimini kaLeon Schuster ethi Mama Jack, nokuthe kuvela izindaba zokudlula kwakhe emhlabeni, abantu bathi bayomkhumbula ngayo kakhulu.
Ngokwesitatimende esithunyelelwe abezindaba, umndeni uveze ukuthi amahlebezi okuthi uzibulele awalona iqiniso.
"Umndeni wakwaSurtie uthanda ukuqinisekisa izindaba zokudlula emhlabeni ngokukhulu ukuzuma komlingisi obethandwa kakhulu kuleli, uShaleen Surtie-Richards.
Abaningi bebazi ukuthi uhlushwa yilezi zifo zombili nesisola ukuthi ukudlula kwakhe emhlabeni kusondelene nazo, sizolinda ukuhlolwa kwesidumbu ukuqinisekisa lokho.
Lokhu osekukhulunywa ngabantu ezinkundleni zokuxhumana asikwazi yingakho sifuna ukuqinisekisa ukuthi akazibulalanga kodwa ubengaphilile," kuchaza isitatimende somndeni.
Ubonge uxhaso oluthole kubantu bakuleli ezinhlakeni ezahlukene njengoba beveze ukuthi bezwa ubuhlungu obukhulu njengoba lokhu okwenzekile bebengakulindele.
Ozakwabo endimeni yokulingisa, amaqembu ezepolitiki nabalandeli bakhe badlulise amazwi enduduzo emndenini nasezihlotsheni zalo mlingisi.
Ngo-2014 lo mlingisi wahlonishwa ngeLifetime Achievement Award emcimbini wamaRoyalty Soapie Awards.

UDJ Bongz neseluleko kumaciko
UMAKADEBONA kaDJ waseThekwini, uDJ Bongz, uthi siphelile isikhathi sokuthi amaciko athembele kuhulumeni noma ekuqashweni kuphela ukwenza imali kodwa kumele athathe umculo asebenze nezinkampani ezinkulu.
UBongz owaduma ngengoma ethi Thina Sobabili, uthe amaciko kumele enze izingoma ezizokwazi ukuthi izinkampani zizithathe zizifake ezikhangisweni.
Ukusho lokhu emuva kokukhipha ingoma entsha ethi Lotto ngoLwesihlanu.
"Kumele senze izingoma ezizokwenza kube lula ukuthi sisebenze nezinkampani ezinkulu.
Uma ubheka angu-99.
9% amathuba okuthi abakwaLotto bayizwe le ngoma bese bayayithatha bayifaka ezikhangisweni zayo," kusho uDJ Bongz.
Uthe ngayo akagqugquzeli abantu ukuthi bagembule budedengu kodwa yingoma enezincazelo eziningi.
"Ayikhulumi nge-lotto njengoba injalo kodwa nayo i-lotto ungayifaka ngoba yinto kahulumeni.
Ikhuluma ngokushintsha kwempilo yomuntu.
Ungathola into eshintsha impilo yakho kufane nokuthi unqobe i-lotto ngoba nayo iyayishintsha impilo yabantu.
Ngishaya izinyoni ezimbili ngetshe elilodwa, yingakho abantu besheshe bayithanda ngoba ikhuluma nabo ngqo ezimeni ezahlukene," kusho uDJ Bongz.
Uthe kubalulekile ukwenza izingoma ezinomyalezo ukuze zingasheshi ukuphupha kepha zihlale isikhathi eside emqondweni wabantu.
Uveze ukuthi upheka i-albhamu yakhe entsha.
"Ngiyaqala ukuthi ngikhiphe ingoma bese ngithola imiyalezo kwamanye amazwe, ethi bayayicela emisakazweni yakhona.
Izinkampani ezinkulu ngisebenza nazo isikhashana bese okunye ngiyazenzela.
I-albhamu yami edlule nje ngiyenze ne-Universal.
Uma befuna enye sizohlala phansi sikhulume, angifuni ukuzibophezela ngezinkontileka ezinde, ngimdala manje emculweni.
Ngisebenza nabo ngaleso sikhathi."

INKAMPANI yokuqopha entsha i-AVAD Media, ka-Ayanda Burotho, Adze Ugah noNobuntu Webster, ivundulule ithalente elisha kwezokulingisa okunguNqobile Khumalo ozobe elingisa indawo ephambili kaNqobile emdlalweni omusha kwiMzansi Magic.

Ekhuluma neSolezwe, uNqobile uthe isifiso sakhe ukuthi wonke umuntu wesifazane abuke lo mdlalo njengoba kukhona isifundo kuwona.
"Abantu bazoqala ukubona uNqobile esesimeni esingesihle njengoba kukhona ilungu lomndeni wakhe elishonile.
Leli lunga ligwiliza emanzini endaweni yokubhukuda eyakhiwe ekhaya.
Kwenzeka konke lokhu nje, ukhona ekhaya kodwa ukwenye indlu akaboni.
Umyeni wakhe uyalwa naye njengoba emsolwa ngalesi sigameko.
Kusukela lapho akaphili impilo ejabulisayo, kodwa kukhona konke uyazama ukuthi asebenze kanzima ukuze aqhubeke nempilo," kusho uNqobile.
Uthe kukhona okuzofundwa ngabesifazane nabesilisa ababhekene nokuhlukunyezwa kwanoma iluphi uhlobo.
"Ekugcineni, ngenxa yokuthi usekhathele ukuhlukunyezwa, uNqobile uyasukuma azimele ukuze aphume kulesi simo abhekene naso.
Engikuthanda ngalo mdlalo ukuthi ubhalwe yinkampani eholwa ngowesifazane ongulingisi u-Ayanda.
Ngiyabonga ithuba abangiphe lona nozakwabo kule nkampani yabo entsha eqale ngalo mdlalo ukukhiqiza," kuchaza yena.

Uvuka ngohlelo oluzosiza abefundisi abafuna omaqondana
Kuneziqephu eziwu-13 ezizoveza abesifazane abayisithupha bezama ukuthatha amehlo alaba befundisi.
Ngeke kugcine ngabo kodwa kuzohlanganisa imindeni nabangani babo.
"Uhlelo luzoveza ukuthi ibandla kanye nemindeni kungena kangakanani ekusizeni umfundisi noma umholi walo ekutholeni umaqondana.
Ngeke kugcine ngokuthi kubonakale abefundisi nalaba besifazane kuphela, kodwa baningi abazongenelela basize ekukhetheni intokazi eyiyona yona.
Ngeke bagcine ngokukhethana uma konke kuhambe kahle, siyohamba nabo baze babophe ifindo lo mshado," kuchaza uBasetsana.
Uthe ibandla nomndeni womfundisi bayoqala bahlangane nabesifazane bambuze imibuzo embalwa uma kucaca ukuthi akakulungele okufuna oyedwa kulaba befundisi, yilapho beyobe sebevumelana ngokuthi akhishwe lowo wesifazane ohlelweni.
"Abesifazane okubahambela kahle bayogcina beya ngisho enkonzweni eholwa yilaba befundisi, bayophinde babe nesikhathi bobabili baye eholidini bazijabulise ukuze bazane kangcono.
Okumele bakwazi ababukeli ukuthi kulaba besifazane abayisithupha, uyedwa ozobe ephuma ohlelweni isonto ngalinye kuze kusale ababili abayokhethwa yilezi zinceku.
Sikholwa ukuthi ngalolu hlelo sixoxa indaba yothando futhi sithemba ukuthi abantu bakuleli bazolujabulela.
Siyazi futhi abantu bazozithanda lezi zintokazi isiqephu ngasinye uma bezibona," kuchaza uBasetsana.
