UKZN : Isicelo sokuba kubhekewe izindaba zethu ngendlela efanele nokuthola umhlahlandlela ngezingxoxo
Kungithusile ukufunda umbhalo kaSolwazi Jonathan Jansen obunesihloko esithi "UKZN: It's terrible seeing a varsity die, especially as it was preventable" engosini yakhe ebishicilelwe yi-TimesLive ngomhla we-6 kuNhlolanja (February) 2020.
Njengomuntu owayeyiSekelashansela, ngicabanga ukuthi lo mbhalo wakhe bekufanele ube nokuqonda okungcono ngesimo, ungabi nehaba futhi uqinise kakhulu ezisombululweni.
Okulandela lapha ngezansi akubhekisiwe kuSolwazi Jansen noma embhalweni wakhe, nakuba ungihlupha, kepha kuyisitatimende esicacisa umbono weNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal (i-UKZN).
Ukuqubuka kwezibhelu okusanda kwenzeka emakhempasini ethu kulula ukuthi kuthatheke ngokuthi izingxoxo phakathi komKhandlu wabaFundi nabaphathi beNyuvesi sezifinyelele kwangqingetshe okusho ukuthi phakathi kwalezi zinhlangothi zombili alukho olufuna ukugoba uphondo noma okusho ukuqinisa ikhanda phakathi kohlangothi olulodwa noma zombili nokuthi ukuphazamiseka kwezinhlelo bekungagwemeka ukuba izinhlangothi zombili zikwazile ukuvumelana.
Iqiniso wukuthi akulula ngaleyo ndlela futhi umthelela mkhulu.
UMkhandlu Wabafundi nabaphathi beNyuvesi babhekene nesimo esinzima kakhulu.
Akugcini nje ngokutholakala kwesisombululo salokhu esibhekene nakho manje kepha kumele futhi siqhamuke nesu lokuhlanganisa izidingo zeNyuvesi zezimali kanye nezidingo ezibalulekile zabafundi esikhathini eside.
Okufanele kushiwo kuqala ilokhu okusobala: udlame nokusabisa kuphambene nenqubo nomqondo wempilo yaseNyuvesi.
Labo abenza lezi zenzo abamele muntu.
Izenzo zokusabisa nezokucekela phansi impahla aziyona ipolitiki yanoma yiluphi uhlobo; empeleni ziphikisana nepolitiki nokusebenzisa umqondo.
Aziyona indlela yokubhikisha kepha ziyizenzo zobugebengu kanti iNyuvesi izophokophela ukuthi izigilamkhuba zishushiswe.
Siselapho asichithe ulimi lwepolitiki olusetshenziswa budedengu kucashunwa ngokungafanele u-Franz Fanon.
E-Afrika yonke ukuqhakambisa udlame kuka-Fanon osekuvamile kuphikisana nezinjongo ezinhle; njengoba udlame luholelele kolunye udlame kanti umphumela walokho yiloku esikubona namuhla.
Abasebenzi abazinikele base-UKZN basebenze ngokuzikhandla ukuqinisekisa ukuthi isimo esihle kubona bonke abafundi bethu, ngakho kuyasikhathaza kakhulu ukubona indlela izinto ezenzeka ngayo ezibuyisela emuva.
Indlela yokwenza izinto ngodlame edlangile kwezombusazwe nesilimaze impilo yabantu abaningi eNingizimu Afrika iyindaba yezwe lonke, hhayi i-UKZN kuphela noma ngivuma ukuthi isilimaza kakhulu ngaphezu kwabanye abantu.
Kepha kufanele iphele njengoba icekela phansi wonke umsebenzi omuhle wabangasekho abanikela ngempilo yabo.
Ayamukeleki futhi isenzela phansi sonke manje nangomuso.
AmaNyuvesi kahulumeni ethu aneqhaza elimqoka ukulungisa umonakalo osukela emlandweni wethu.
Ngokunika imiphakathi eyayicindezelwe ithuba lemfundo yaseNyuvesi, senza umsebenzi wesizwe futhi sakha isisekelo somphakathi onokulingana nonekusasa eliqhakazile.
Kepha ayikho iNyuvesi engathintwa yizimo esebenza ngaphansi kwazo.
Lapha sibala konke kusukela esimweni somnotho sezwe nezinjongongqangi zikahulumeni kuze kufinyelele ezimweni zenhlalo yomphakathi wendawo ezithinta umuntu ngamunye nemindeni yonke.
IsiFundazwe iKwaZulu-Natal (i-KZN) singesinye sezifundazwe ezinezinga eliphezulu lobubha ezweni, njengoba izinga labantu abadala lingaphezulu kwamaphesenti angama-60.
Inselelo yokuntuleka kwemisebenzi, ephezulu ngendlela ethusayo nakubantu abaneziqu, yenza abafundi abaningi baqhubeke bahlale esikoleni ngaphandle kwenhloso etheni, okulandelwa umphumela wokuvalelwa ngaphandle ngenxa yokukweleta noma yokungaphasi okuholela odlameni.
Kanti futhi kuyinto ehlale yenzeka.
Isicelo esikhulu soMkhandlu Wabafundi ukuthi iNyuvesi ivumele izitshudeni emindeni yazo ngaphansi kuka-R350.
000 zibhaliswe zingayikhokhile imali yokubhalisa noma yesikweletu esidala.
Inkinga esibhekene nayo ukuthi lezi zitshudeni zilinganiselwa kumaphesenti angama-78 azo zonke izitshudeni zase-UKZN.
Ngaphezu kwaloko kungasho ukuthi zonke izitshudeni zase-UKZN emakhaya azo okunengena imali engaphansi kuka-R350.
000 zifunda mahhala, okungasho ukuthi uma i-UKZN ingase ikuvume kungadlula inqubomgomo ekhona kahulumeni, kubeke isikhungo esimweni esibi kakhulu kwezezimali.
Isikweletu sabafundi base-UKZN ekupheleni kukaDisemba wangonyaka wezi-2019 besiyi-R1,7 billion.
Noma kunjalo kepha siqhubekile senza izindlela (njengokukugunyaza ukubhaliswa ngokwezimali) okusho ukuthi asikho noyedwa umfundi waseNyuvesi obekufanele akhokhe imali ephelele yesikweletu esidala ngaphambi kokubhalisa.
Empeleni imali enkulu edingeka kumuntu okweletayo imiswe kuR45.
000 kumfundi ngamunye bese kuthi amaphesenti angama-67 abafundi kudingeka bakhokhe imali eyizi-R10.
000 umfundi ngamunye yesikweletu sakhe.
Umbono weNyuvesi kulolu daba uholwa umgomo wokwemukela abafundi kodwa ibe iqinisekisa ukuthi iNyuvesi ihlala isesimweni esihle kwezezimali futhi iyachuma, ikwazi ukuphatha izimali zokusebenza zansuku zonke ngendlela eyeseka ukuhlinzekwa kwezidingo zansuku zonke, ukubhekana nezibopho zayo kwezezimali kubasebenzi, abafundi nezinkampani esebenzisana nazo futhi ikwazi ukulawula indaba yesimo sesikweletu esiphezulu - esiwedlula wonke amaNyuvesi eNingizimu Afrika.
Kuyacaca ukuthi okunye ukuvunyelwa kokubhalisa ngaphandle kwezimali ezidingekayo kungabeka iNyuvesi engcupheni yokugcina ivaliwe, okungalimaza wonke umuntu.
Noma kunjalo siyavuma ukuthi ukuntuleka kwezimali kusabalele kuwona wonke amakhempasi eNyuvesi futhi kungenza ukuthi abafundi abakweletayo bangaphumeleli ezifundweni zabo, okungabenza bavaleleke bangatholi thuba ngaphakathi noma ngaphandle kweNyuvesi.
Kuleli phuzu, isicelo sesibili esikhulu sabaholi babafundi ukuthi kumiswe uhlelo lokunqatshelwa ukubhalisa kubafundi abangaphumelelanga ezifundweni zabo.
Kepha iqiniso lithi abaphathi beNyuvesi banomsebenzi wokuvikela igama leNyuvesi ngokuqapha izinga nesithunzi seziqu zase-UKZN.
INyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natali inentshisekelo enkulu ngomsebenzi wayo kubantu bendawo eyakhele.
Sinerekhodi elihle ekwemukeleni izitshudeni nezinga eliphezulu lokuxegisa amatomu esimweni sezimali.
Izinga liphezulu kakhulu kangangokuthi iKZN inesikweletu esingaphezu kwe-R1 billion.
Kepha iqiniso ukuthi iphakethe leNyuvesi noma likahulumeni aliwona umthombo ongashi.
Eqinisweni akusekho lutho ndawo zombili.
Singawenza kanjani umsebenzi wethu wokuba yiNyuvesi yomphakathi waKwaZulu-Natali, siqhubeke sichume ngasezimalini sibe siqinisekisa ukuthi isibalo esikhulu sabafundi bethi abakhathazeki ngokwezimali nasezifundweni?
Seloku ngiqalile ukuba iSekelashansela ngisebenza ngokuzikhandla ngaso sonke isikhathi nabaphathi nabaholi bezitshudeni sizama ukubheka izidingo zabo nesidingo sokuqinisekisa ukuthi sihle isimo sezimali seNyuvesi.
Esibambelele kukona wukuthi esikushoyo akusiko ukusabisa ezingxoxweni kepha yiqiniso elimsulwa esingeke silibalekele.
Njengoba bonke abantu abaqotho baseNingizimu Afrika befisa ikusasa eliqhakazile futhi bebheka abaphathi bamaNyuvesi kube kufanele kodwa ngeke senze imilingo kanjalo nohulumeni noma izinkampani.
Ithini ke indlela eya phambili?Okokuqala nje, sidinga ipolitiki engcono.
Udlame kufanele luphele, futhi luphele ngokushesha futhi unomphelo.
Kanjalo, umkhuba omdala wokufuna ngenkani nokwehlela ngezansi kufanele uphele.
Yebo, zonke izinhlangothi zifika ezingxoxweni nezinhloso kodwa ngeke sithathe kancane umsebenzi wethu sonke wokusimamisa iNyuvesi negama layo.
Lokhu kufanele kube seqhulwini kithina sonke kanti lokho kudinga izindlela ezintsha zokubambisana nobuholi obuqotho ngempela ngasohlangothini lwabaphathi beNyuvesi nabaholi babafundi.
Okwesibili, ukulungisa lesi simo esikhona kudingeka ukuthi sibe neqiniso ngokuthi yikuphi iNyuvesi engakwazi ukukwenza nalokho engeke ikwazi ukukwenza.
INyuvesi ngeke ikwazi ukubhalisa bonke abafundi abangakwazi ukuthola imali yakwa-NSFAS ekubeni u-NSFAS uqobo ubheka izinto ezithize ngaphambi kokuthi uxhase labo bafundi abadinga usizo.
Kusukela ekuqaleni iNyuvesi izimisele ukusiza abafundi bango-2020 abazothola u-NSFAS.
Sikhulu isidingo sokuthi sithole isisombululo kwizinselelo ezikhona ngaleli qoqo labafundi ngoba basethubeni elingcono lokungabi nesikweletu uma benakekelwa futhi besekelwa ngendlela efanele yiNyuvesi ukuze baqede izifundo ngesikhath.
INyuvesi izibophezele ekubambisaneni Nobuholi Babafundi ngaleli qoqo ukuthola isisombululo.
Okwesithathu, iNyuvesi izimisele ukusebenzisana nabo bonke abafundi abasalelwe yisifundo esisodwa noma ezimbili ukuthi baqede ukufunda.
UMkhandlu weNyuvesi uzocabangisisa ukuthi yisiphi isixazululo esemukelekile sokusiza laba bafundi baqede isikole, kuthi uma kunesidingo kwenziwe ezinye izindlela zokuhlola abantu uma kuwukuthi indlela ekhona yokuhlola iyabakhinyabeza abafundi.
Iphini LeSekelashansela  namaDini EzokuFunda NokuFundisa banikwe umsebenzi wokuqoqa amagama alezi zitshudeni ukuze abhekwe yizinhlaka ezifanele zaseNyuvesi.
NjengoSekelashansela noMPhathi wase-UKZN ngiqinisekisa bonke abantu baseNyuvesi nesizwe sonke ukuthi singabaphathi sizoqhubeka ukwenza izinto ngendlela efanele ngokubeka umgomo nombono phambili.
*Kuloba uSolwazi Nana PokuIsekelashansela NoMphathi wase-UKZN
Umnyango uhlanganisa amasu azosiza ngesikhathi esilahlekile
NJENGOBA izolo bekuwusuku olubalulekile okubuyela ngalo abafundi bakaGrade 11 noGrade 6 esikoleni emuva kwesikhathi eside behleli emakhaya ngenxa yokuqubuka kweCoronavirus, sikuqonda kahle kamhlophe ukuthi mukhulu kangakanani umsebenzi omele uMnyango wezeMfundo KwaZulu-Natal.
Ngaphandle kokwenza konke okusemandleni ukuzama ukuqinisekisa ukuphepha kwabafundi nabasebenzi bethu ezikoleni, sinomunye omthwalo onzima osemahlombe ethu wokuqinisekisa ukuthi sinendlela yokuvala isikhathi esilahleke ngesikhathi kungafundwa.
Kungalesi sizathu ngesonto eledlule besihlangene sicwaninga uhlelo lwethu lokuqinisekisa ukuthi abafundi bacijwa ngendlela efanele, i-Academic Recovery Plan.
Lapha besibheka zonke izindlela ezimqoka nezizoholela ekutheni izingane zethu zithole imfundo esezingeni elifanele nezokwenza kungazweli kakhulu ukuthi sekunesikhathi eside zihleli emakhaya.
Ukucwaningwa kwalolu hlelo bekuhlanganise sonke isigungu esiphezulu sokuphathwa koMnyango i-senior management ukuze kuphunywe nezinqumo kanye nemiphumela edle ngokujiya nezosiza izingane zethu.
Ngingasho nje ngaphandle kokungabaza ukuthi ngasohlangothini lokuqinisekisa ukuthi abafundi bethu ababuyela esikoleni namhlanje nalabo asebevele bebuyele okunguGrade 12 noGrade 7 sibalungiselele kahle kakhulu ukuthi bangasali emuva ngenxa yesikhathi eside sokuvalwa kwezikole okwadalwa wumbhedukazwe wesifo esaqubuka kwelaseChina ngoDisemba nyakenye kodwa esesisabalele umhlaba wonke.
Yize sazi ukuthi ukuvikela ukusabalala kweCoronavirus edume ngeleCovid-19 kuncike kakhulu endleleni yokuziphatha nokunakekela kubantu, nathi njengomnyango senze konke okusemandleni ukuqinisekisa ukuthi njengoba isibalo sabafundi sesizothi ukwanda kancane ezikoleni ngenxa yokubuya kwalaba bamabanga amabili kodwa ezokuphepha zihlala njalo zisezingeni eliphezulu.
Phakathi kwezinto esizenzile nangesikhathi kubuya ithimba lokuqala, kube wukuqinisekisa ukuthi abafundi kabahlali ngokusondelana emagunjini okufundela kodwa bashiyelana ibanga elingaphezu kuka-1.
5 metres ukuze kungathi omunye uma ethimula kumbe ekhwehlela kutheleke omunye.
Siphinde saqinisekisa ukuthi bonke abafundi bethu sibathengela izifonyo okuzothi uma befika esikoleni bazifice bese beyazisebenzisa.
Siphinde futhi senza isiqiniseko sokuthi sihlinzeka ngamathanki amanzi izikole obekunzima ukuthola kuzo amanzi ukuze siqinisekise ukuthi abafundi nothisha bethu bayalithola ithuba lokuhlamba izandla ngaso sonke isikhathi ukuze bahlale njalo benezandla ezihlanzekile nokuyinto inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation eyitusa kakhulu ekuvimbeleni ukusabalala kweCovid-19.
Izibulalimagciwane zokuhlamba izandla nazo zikhona ukuze abafundi behlale njalo behlanza ngazo izandla.
Namagumbi okufunda kuyaqinisekiswa ukuthi zonke izinsuku ahlanzekile.
Siqinisekisile futhi nokuthi uma abafundi befika esikoleni bayabhekwa isimo sabo sokushisa khona uma kungukuthi kukhona oshisa ngokungajwayelekile sithathe izinyathelo ngokushesha ukuze simnike usizo ngokuphazima kweso.
Zonke lezi zinto ezisenzayo sizenza ngoba sikhathalele ukuphepha kwabafundi bethu okumqoka ukuthi bafunde ukuze kuthi uma iCovid-19 isidlulile kodwa bona babe ngabantu abazokwazi ukuba nekusasa eliqhakazile.
Amathemba okuphepha nokuthola imfundo esezingeni aphezulu kakhulu.
Ngakho-ke sithi amaphaphu phansi.
Asiqinise kakhulu ekusebenzisaneni ukuze silinqobe igciwane.
Kuleli qophelo ngiyafisa ukuphawula ngokudideka okuke kwaba khona kwezinye zezikole zethu uma kubikwe ngomuntu osehaqwe yigciwane.
Izikole eziningi bekuthi uma kuke kwabikwa zivele zikhiphe umyalelo wokuthi zizovala okungenani izinsuku eziwu-14.
Siyafisa ukucacisa ukuthi umthetho ohambisana nemigomo yezempilo uthi uma kunesehlo esibikiwe esikoleni, leso sikole kumele sivale amahora awu-24 okuyizinsuku ezimbili kuphela ukuze sihlanzwe kahle kubulawe amagciwane okungenzeka ukuthi akhona.
Mayelana nokuhlolwa kwabantu kuleso sikole okubikwe kuso isehlo, indlela yokusebenza nemigomo yezempilo ithi kumele kuhlolwe kuphela labo abebeseduze nalowo okubikwa ukuthi unegciwane kunokuthi kuhlolwe wonke umuntu esikoleni.
Siyacela ukuthi sibambisane kakhulu kulesi simo.
Ukubambisana yikho okuyosenza sinqobe lesi sifo.
Sengiphetha nje, siyafisa ukucacisa ukuthi sizoqhubeka nokusebenza ngokuzikhandla ukuqinisekisa ukuphepha kwabafundi bethu nokuqinisekisa ukuthi abasali ezifundweni zabo.
Kungokokuqala ukuthi isizukulwane esiphila njengamanje sibhekana nesimo esibhekene naso njengamanje.
Lokho kusho ukuthi izinto eziningi sizozifunda ngendlela.
Kodwa-ke yize kunjalo, ukuphepha kwabafundi kanye nabasebenzi bethu sizolokhu sikubeke njalo eqhulwini.
Masilandele imigomo emenyezelwe nguhulumeni yokuphepha siqinisekise ukuthi siyasinqoba lesi sifo esisihlalise lubhojozi.

MHLELI: Ngithanda ukuvumelana nomfundi welakho obhale ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi: UCele usazenza umkhuzi wamaphoyisa, oshicilelweni lwangoLwesithathu.

UShenge ulimele iqiniso naseNdlunkulu kaZulu
MHLELI: Ngizwakalisa ukudabuka kwenhliziyo yami ngenxa yefu elimnyama elisibekele ubukhosi bakaZulu njengoba kusanda kuhamba ngokulandela eduzane kwabaseNdlunkulu kaZulu.
Ngithi nje umndeni, izihlobo nabangani nesizwe sonke mabalale ngenxeba.
Ngizwakalisa ukubonga kuMntwana waKwaPhindangene onguNdunankulu kaZulu ngokukhalipha kwakhe nokumela iqiniso.
UMntwana akathandi ukuchema nabantu abangahambisani nokuphatheka, abantu abangondlovukayiphikiswa.
Siyabadinga abantu abanohlonze abazomela iqiniso njengoMntwana.
UMntwana selokhu ema eqinisweni ngisho ebandleni lamaNazaretha walimela iqiniso, wabuza ukuthi liphikiselwani izwi leNkosi uThingolwenkosazane eyabhala incwadi iqoka umholi webandla ozolihola uma lona selushintsha ibhantshi (selukhotheme).
Okwenziwa yiNkosi yesizwe saMaqadi ixova ibandla, uMntwana wakuhlaba wakuhlikiliza.
Nanamhlanje akakaze aguquke kulokho okwashiwo nguThingo.
UMntwana waKwaPhindangene wafundisa abantu ukuthi bayithemba into ebhalwe phansi njengoba uThingo lwenza.
UMntwana akazange aphinde azihlanganise nebandla njengoba kusenombango oqhubeka ngaphakathi kweNazareth Baptist Church osasezinkantolo.
UMntwana wakubuka kukubi ukuthi uma abantu bengavumelani ngento ethile, bese ezihlanganisa nabo.
Wabona kuyichilo ukuthi uma yena njengoyise wesizwe azihlanganise nanoma yiluphi uhlangothi, wakhetha ukuma phakathi nendawo.
Wayebuka ukuthi uyoba yini emlandweni engumholi omkhulu kangaka, uma sekuphuma isinqumo sithi "uhlangothi obuwumbimbi nalo lulahlwe yicala ngenxa yamanga."
Wayeyophinda abe yini nje?
Izwe lembethwe yifu elimnyama ngenxa yokuphikiswa kwezwi loThingo.
Kwathi nabantu abakhulu ababekelwa ukubheka ukuthi abantu bangacindezelwa ngamanga nangobuqili, lokhu esibona amanye amakhosi amaningi asephakathi kwabantu abayizigangi.
iNkosi Buthelezi kayizange ibe nendaba nobuningi babantu, kayizange ibe nendaba neminikelo yezinkomo neyezinqama eyayingathengwa ngayo, ukuze ilidele iqiniso inamathele emangeni nasehlazweni.
Ngibuka umbango usungaphakathi endlunkulu lapho abantu sebengenwe wumoya wokuphikisa izwi leMbube, eshiye ikubhalile phansi okumele kwenzeke uma isikhotheme.
Ngokuzwa kwami kuseyiyo iNkosi uShenge ethi izwe lonke nendlunkulu makuhlonishwe izifiso zikaNdabezitha kulokho akushiyile.
Ngiyathanda nami ukusho ukuthi ondlunkulu bonke nabaNtwana basezindlini zonke mabahloniphe izifiso zeSilo.
Mabahlale phansi babonisane ngomoya wokuthula nokwazisana.
Bahlonishwa yizwe lonke naphesheya kwezilwandle.
Ngiyafisa uNdlunkulu waKwaKhethomthandayo naMazinyane eSilo behlele ngezansi, balihloniphe izwi likaMdlokombane.
Bonke abaNtwana basendlunkulu mababambelele ehlombe likaShenge ngoba uyindoda ongayethemba kwezamaqiniso.
Ngiyathanda futhi ukuthi baye kuMntwana uThembi Zulu-Ndlovu ngokuthi angawudungi umsebenzi wasendlunkulu, kwazise yena sewagana.
Makaphawule lapho ephawula khona kepha angafaki umoya wendlakadla phakathi kwezindlu zeSilo.
Uma enze kanjalo uyofike athini koyisemkhulu abalwela lesi sizwe, basibumba saba yilokhu esiyikho namhlanje.
Sonke masikhulumeni ngazwi linye siwuZulu, sihloniphe izwi likaBayede, ukuze naye lapho ekhona alale ngokuthula.
Thina siyisizwe samaZulu sizogcina sibukelwa phansi ngezinye izizwe.
AmaNazaretha aphikisa incwadi ebhalwe phansi yinkosi, iqoka umholi okhethwe emazulwini.
Kwala noma izinkantolo zisho ukuthi akukho mkokotelo encwadini kepha sangavuma ukulalela.
Namhlanje umlando uyaziphinda ngokuthi iSilo siqoke iNgonyama bese abaNtwana nondlunkulu bebanga umsindo ngoqokiwe.
Ngithi nje nina bezulu eliphezulu mayihlale phansi ibambe umthetho!
Masimhloniphe sonke owaqokwa ngamakhosi asendlunkulu alele othulini lomhlaba.OKHATHAZEKILE
Unolimi olunesankahlu uCele kepha uhlulwa umsebenzi
MHLELI: Ukuhloniphana kuyathengana.
Uma ungihlonipha, nami kulula ukuthi ngikuthobele, ngakho ukuhloniphana kukabili.
Uma ungangihloniphi, ungithatha noma yikanjani kulula nakumina ukuba nawe ngikuthathe noma yikanjani.
Uma ukhuluma nami noma yikanjani, uyangiphoqa ukuba nami ngingayihluzi into engizoyisho kuwena.
Uma ungihlonipha, kunento oyithintayo kinima engithobisayo bese ngiba nenhlonipho.
Uma ungikhombisa inhlonipho nento oyishoyo isuke seyizwakala kahle.
Akwenzeki ukuthi ngingaqondi ukuthi uthini ngoba ngididiswa yindelelo yakho.
Angiqondile kufundisa ngenhloniphi, kepha ngithintwe wukuziphatha kukaMnuz Bheki Cele, uNgqongqoshe wamaPhoyisa (osesithombeni).
Lo ngqongqoshe uyimpi nje uma ekhuluma nabantu.
Lokho kwenza kube lula ukufinyelela ekutheni ukukhuluma kwakhe akunayo inhlonipho.
Unesankahlu ongasazi ukuthi sibangwa yini.
Ukhuluma ngendlela engatshali inhlonipho kubantu, kungenzeka ukuthi usuke eqonde ukugcizelela akushoyo kepha kithina kufika isankahlu sodwa.
Kuthina kufika ulaka esingazi ludalwa yini.
Iqiniso wukuthi uCele uhlulwa wumsebenzi wakhe bese egijimela okaKhomishana wamaPhoyisa, eKhehla Sitole.
Akuwona umsebenzi kangqongqoshe ukutshela amaphoyisa ukuthi kufanele abophe uma sekwenzenjani.
Lowo ngumsebenzi kaSitole.
Kubukeka ugqozi lukaCele luhlala obala uma kukhulunywa ngokuvalwa kotshwala.
Lokhu kwenza umuntu azibuze ukuthi ushonaphi lo mfutho uma sekufanele akhulume ngezinto ezibucayi njengokuhlukunyezwa kwabesifazane nezingane.
UCele akanawo umfutho ngezinye izinkinga ezikhungethe leli lizwe ezidinga ubuholi bakhe njengongqongqoshe wamaphoyisa.
Kuyadumaza ukuthi sinenkinga yokushushumbiswa kwabantu kepha ungqongqoshe akasho lutho ngalokho.
Kepha uma isihloko kuwutshwala, maye babo!
Uzomuzwa kahle ngoba ukhuluma aze ashintshe ngisho ebusweni.
Uma kukhulunywa ngokushushumbiswa kotshwala, uzombona kahle ukuthi akabhenywa, kepha uma kushushumbiswa abantu - kucweba iziziba.
Asikwazi ukuba nongqongqoshe unomfutho wokulwa nento eyodwa.
UMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa uthuli uthini ngongqongqoshe onjena?Sekukhanyela wonke umuntu ukuthi uCele uyamehlula umsebenzi wakhe.
Mhlawumbe udidwa wukuthi wake waba ngukhomishana wamaphoyisa manje akasakwazi ukuhlukanisa phakathi kwamandla kangqongqoshe nakakhomishana.

Masilwe nokwebiwa kokudla okuthengelwe abampofu
UBHUBHANE lwesifo iCovid-19, lusikhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi ukungalingani kuyinselelo enkulu kakhulu ebhekene nezwe lakithi.
Sikhuluma nje, elakuleli laziwa kabi wumhlaba wonke njengezwe lapho kunegebe elikhulu phakathi kwabakhomba ngophakathi nabadla imbuya ngothi.
Osekusibangele inkinga, wukuthi imizamo eminingi uhulumeni azama ngayo ukuvala leli gebe, isiphazanyiswe kakhulu yilo mkhuhlane kwazise baningi asebelahlakelwe yimisebenzi.
Lokhu sekuholele ekutheni sande isibalo sabantu ababhuqabhuqwa wububha.
Kungihlaba umxhwele ukubona ukuthi izibalo zokuthuthukisa izinga lempilo yabantu, zikhomba ukuthi izwe lakithi lenza kahle kakulu kusukela ku- 1994.
Ngokombiko wokuthuthukiswa kwabantu we-United Nations Development Programme ka-2019, kumanje nje elakuleli lilele unombolo 113 emazweni angu-193 emhlabeni wonke.
Ukube uhulumeni wethu awukusukumelanga kuhlinzeka abantu ababenganakiwe nguhulumeni wobandlululo ngezidingonqqangi, bekuzoba wumqansa omkhulu kwakuqala izinhlelo zokulwa nalolu bhubhane.
Sobe siyazikhohlisa uma singakugqizi qakala ukuthi esinye sezizathu zokuthi bathole impilo inzima, njengoba kunalo mkhuhlane, yikho belu ukungalingani.
Yingakho ngithe angibonge uhulumeni kazwelonke ngokumemezela uchatha kubo bonke abantu bakithi abahola imali yesibonelelo.
Angisayikhulumi eyemali ebekelwe ukulekelela ngesikhathi esinzima labo abangasebenzi.
Sinethemba lokuthi izoba negalelo elikhulu emzabalazweni wethu wokulwa nobubhane.
Lokhu kufakazela ngokusobala ukuthi uma sithi uhulumeni wethu ungonakekelayo, sisuke singasengi ezimithiyo.
SinguMasipala weTheku, sikubone kufanele ukuthi sibeke eceleni imali enguR66 million ukulekelela labo abadla imbuya ngothi.
Ngike ngavakashela zonke izinqolobane zethu zokudla, ngajabula kakhulu ngokudla okusezingeni eliphezulu esikunika abantu bakithi.
Senze isiqiniseko, sisebenza namakhansela ethu, ukuthi abazohlomula kulolu hlelo, ngabantu ngempela abakufanele lokhu kanti futhi senze umsebenzi omkhulu wokuthi izinkampani esiziqashayo ukusithengela ukudla, zinikwa lo msebenzi emva kokuthi sizinelise ukuthi zizowenza umsebenzi ngokugculisayo, ngoba sifuna ukugwema ukuthi kungabi nezinkampani ezizogxila ekutheni zenze inzuzo enkulu abantu bakithi bebe bengagculisekile.
Senze futhi isiqiniseko sokuthi uhlelo lomnotho lweRET alusaleli emuva ukuze sikwazi ukuvala igebe kwabacebile nabampofuEThekwini bonke labo abazobe besilekelela ekwabeni ukudla, badonswe ngendlebe ukuthi akungakhishwa ukudla ngokuchema kodwa akube nobulungiswa.
Sinama-ward angu-110 kuwo yimizi engu-1 000 ezohlomula ngalesi sikhathi sikathaqa.
Lukhona uhlu olwakhiwe nokuzothi ngaso sonke isikhathi uma bemukela ukudla abantu basayine eduze kwemininingwane yabo.
Nathi futhi sizoqinisekisa ukuthi siyabashayela ucingo ukuthola ukuthi bathola ukudla okubafanele yini.
Izigameko esizibonile kwezinye izingxenye zezwe lapho kube khona abasebuholini abagxekwa ngokweba ukudla okufanele kuye kwabaswele ziyethusa.
Ngithi lezo zenzo kufanele zigxekwe kuthi abenza lokho babhekane nengalo yomthetho.
Siwumphakathi, lapho sibona khona izenzo zenkohlakalo, asingathuli kodwa sibike kwabasemandleni ukuze sibhekane ngqo namasela.
Siyacela futhi nemiphakathi yethu esingakafinyeleli kuyo nalolu hlelo, ukuthi isibekezelele ngoba lesi yisimo esingajwayelekile esisehle ngaphezulu.
Senza konke okusemandleni ukufinyelela kubo bonke abaswele.
Ngakho asiyeke imibhikisho enodlame necekela phansi impahla lapho abantu bekhala ngokuthi asikafiki kubo ngohlelo lokudla.
Asikudingi lokho, sidinga ukubambana ngezandla sibhekane nale nselelo ngoba udlame luyosibangela izinkinga eziningi nezingenza ukuthi luqhubeke ubhubhane.
Njengoba umasipala wethu usuthathwa njengesizinda salokhu kufa, nginicela nonke ukuthi nihlale emakhaya bese nihlonipha yonke imithetho kathaqa.
Asikuqonde ukuthi inhloso ngalokhu wukuphephisa thina nanokulisiphula nezimapande zalo igciwane.
Angithathe leli thuba ngibonge zonke izinhlangano ezingekho ngaphansi kukahulumeni ngokusabela ikhwela lethu lokuthi zelule isandla ngalesi sikhathi esinzima kangaka.

Masingakuvumeli ukusetshenziswa wuSathane bakithi
MHLELI: Kunamazwi eBhayibhelini athi uSathane wumkhohlisi nomdukisi wezwe odukisa abantu.
Impela manje ngibona sengathi uSathane useyazenzela nje la kithina.
Akukona ukuteleka kwabantu lokhu futhi ungathi sebesetshenziswa wuSathane.
Udlame olungaka, ulaka olungaka, ubudlova obungaka.
Hhayi akusekhona ukufuna izidingo phela lokhu kodwa sekuwukuziveza kukaSathane kubantu abangakholwa.
Izidingo zomphakathi sonke siyazifuna kodwa uma sekuliwa kangaka akuseyikho.
Le nto ngike ngayibona kwenye indawo ngidlula eDenny Dalton abantu bebhikisha.
Babeshaya izimoto zabantu ngamatshe bethulula ukudla emalolini.
Abantu babevutha bhe ngisho nezingane zesikole zivuka umbhejazane.
Akekho umuntu ozihloniphayo nohlonipha abantu ongenza into engayibona.

Sike sakubona lokhu nakwezinye izindawo.

Phela uma esesebenza ungena engqondweni kuqala.

EPhalamende ""kunezinhlanya"" zakhona nasemphakathini kukhona ezakhona kusho ukuthi eNingizimu Afrika konakele kakhulu.

Ukwehla kwentela kudalwa yinzuzo eyehlile yezinkampani
Busi MavusoUkwehla kokuqoqwa kwentela okubangwe yisimo esihambelana neCovid-19 kunomthelela ezingqinambeni ezibhekene nesizwe.
Imbangela yokwehla kokuqoqwa kwentela wukuthi izinkampani bezivaliwe, abasebenzi behleli emakhaya nabathengi okudale ukuthi intela engenayo kanye ne-VAT kwehle kakhulu bengekho.
Kwisabelozimali esasiphuthuma, uNgqongqoshe weziMali, uMnuz Tito Mboweni, wabika ukuthi izibalo zikahulumeni zikhomba ukuthi intela ezongena izoba ngaphansi ngoR300 billion (21%) kwisibikezelo sonyaka.
Enkulumweni yeMTBPS ezothulwa kuleli sonto, sizobekwa esithombeni ngezinga lokwehla kwentela eqoqiwe.
Ukwehla kwentela engenayo kukhombisa ngokusobala ukubaluleka komnotho onempilo oneminxa ezimele enenzuzo futhi ekhulayo.
Asikho esinye isibambelo esizokhuphula imali kahulumeni ngaphandle kwalesi.
INingizimu Afrika inezinkampani ezingaphezulu kwezigidi ezimbili ezibhaliselwe ukukhokha intela.
Phakathi kwazo kunezingaphezu kuka-500 000 ezidlulisela kuhulumeni intela ekhokwa yizisebenzi, iPAYE, kuthi ezingaphezu kuka-800.
000 ziqoqela uhulumeni iVAT.
Izinkampani ezinempilo ziyisisekelo somnotho wezwe.
Umonakalo odalwe yiCovid-19 nokwehla kwemali yentela engenayo ngo-21% yizimo ebezingalindelekile futhi zifikele phezu kwesimo somnotho ebesivele singesihle ezweni.
Intela eqoqiwe yehle ngoR42bn kunesibikezelo sango-2019/20 futhi ngonyaka ongaphambili ibingaphansi ngoR13bn.
Inkinga yentela engaphansi kwezibikezelo iyinkomba yokuthi inzuzo yezinkampani namaholo abasebenzi kwehlile ngendlela evelele.
Ukudlangala kwenkinga kubonakala uma siphosa amehlo kwintela ekhokhwa yizinhlangano ezisemthethweni.
Kodwa umthelela omkhulu wukuthi izinkampani bezingayitholi inzuzo efana neyangeminye iminyaka, ikakhulu ngaphambi kwenkinga yemali ka-2008 eyakhungatha umhlaba wonke.
Izinkinga zemali esibhekene nazo ezweni kazikwazi ukuxazululeka ngaphandle kokubhekana nezinkinga zemikhakha ezimele.
Inqubomgomo yezomnotho kufanele ivumele imikhakha ezimele ukuthi ikhule ukuze ikwazi ukwandisa amathuba omsebenzi, ikhuphule amaholo abasebenzi ithole nenzuzo engcono.
Uhulumeni ube yinsika futhi ewugqugquzela yena umnotho kule minyaka engu-10 edlule kodwa manje kuyacaca ukuthi uma kuzophumelela ukusimamisa umnotho, imikhakha ezimele kumele nayo isimame.
Okusho ukuthi izinhlelo zokuguqula isimo sikahulumeni esithikameza ukusebenza komnotho kumele zifeziwe.
Sibona kuyinto enhle ukuthi uMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa agxile ekuxazululeni izinkinga zamandla kagesi emyankeni emibili ezayo ngenxa yokuthi eminyakeni ewu-10 edlule, isimo sikagesi sibe nomthelela omkhulu ekwehleni kwamandla ezinhlangano ezisemthethweni.
Uma uhulumeni engaxegisa izintambo avumele labo abasebenzisa ugesi abanamandla ukuthola izimvumo zokuzikhiqizela ugesi kungalekelela ekuxazululeni inkinga kagesi futhi kuthuthukise ikusasa lezinkampani.
Ngokunjalo, kufanele kuqiniswe izinhlelo zokufinyelela kwizingqalasizinda yokuxhumana, i-broadband ne-spectrum.
Kwakuhlongozwe eminyakeni engu-10 edlule ukuthi kukhululwe i-spectrum ngokuthi ithengiswe.
Kumele izinkampani zikwazi ukuqasha abasebenzi basemazweni angaphandle abanamakhono angatholakali kuleli ukuze ukulahleka kwamakhono ngenkathi belifulathela leli abanamakhono kungakuphazamisi ukusimama komnotho, isikhathi esithathwayo ukukhipha izimvumo zamanzi nezemvelo sehliswe, kuphothulwe iMPRDA ezonikeza imboni yezimayini ithemba ikwazi ukutshala izimali zokuhlola umhlaba, nokuthi kwakhiwe ingqalasizinda ezokhuphula amandla omnotho ukuze kuhambe imphahla ngaphakathi kwezwe futhi ihanjiswe ngemkhumbhi emazweni angaphandle.
Ukwakhiwa kwezinhlelo zengqalasizinda kuseqhulwini lokufukula umnotho kodwa kumele sikhumbule ukuthi ingqalasizinda ekhona kumanje ingasebenza ngendlela engcono kunalokhu okwenzekayo.
Ingqalasizinda yezitimela nezamachweba eTransnet ingasetshenziswa kangcono uma imikhakha ezimele ingathola ithuba lokubambisana nohulumeni itshale imali futhi ithole nokusebenzisa engasebenzi ngokugcwele.
UMboweni ukubeke obala ukuthi inkinga yesimo semali kahulumeni ibucayi.
Kufanele kube nezinhlelo eziqinile ukwehlisa izinga lokusetshenziswa kwemali nguhulumeni, ikakhulukazi imali engena ezinhlelweni ezingakhuthazi ukutshala imali.
Kubalulekile futhi ukuthi imikhakha ezimele ithole ukwesekwa ukuze isimame okuhlanganisa nokukhula kwemali yentela engenayo.
Sonke siyasikhumbula isikhathi ngaphambili kuka-2008, imali yentela eyayingena yayingaphezulu kwemali eyayisetshenziselwa ukufeza izidingo zesizwe ngokuphindaphindiwe, uhulumeni wakwazi nokuba nenzuzo.
Lowo mphumela wawungenxa yokukhula kwemikhakha ezimele nohulumeni enamandla okuqoqa intela efanele.
Inqubomgomo yemali kaMboweni kumele ihambisane nohlelo lokufukula umnotho likaRamaphosa kuqiniswe ukufeza izinhlelo zokuguqula isimo sikahulumeni uma sizophinde sibuyele kulezo zikhathi.
Abantu kumele bafundiseke ngengozi yotshwala
MHLELI: Ngithi angidlulise ukukhathazeka kwami ngokuphuza kwabesifazane.
Indlela asebephuza ngayo utshwala iyethusa.
Sesiphila esikhathini esinzima lapho abesifazane bephuza kakhulu kunabesilisa kangangoba abantu besilisa bagcina sebenakekela izingane.
Kwesinye isikhathi uyaye uthole umuntu wesifazane esexabana nabantu ngenxa yotshwala, abanye bagcina sebelimazene.
Sekukaningi ngizwa kuthiwa kukhona abashonile ngenxa yokulwa bephuzile kodwa lokho akubethusi odadewethu, bayaqhubeka nokuphuza kuze kweqe.
Abagcini ngokuphuza utshwala, sebedla nezinye izidakamizwa eziyingozi.
Odokotela bathi ezinye zalezi zidakamizwa ziqeda inzalo kumuntu wesifazane.
Baye baphuze utshwala ngenxa yokuthi babona ozakwabo bephuza nabo babone kungcono baphuze besaba ukuthi buzophela ubungani.
Kuye kube buhlungu uma sebephuza imali yezingane yesibonelelo sikahulumeni, bangabe besazifeza izidingo zezingane.
Ababoniseki ngobungozi botshwala bavele bacabange ukuthi wena uzibona ungcono kunabo.
Abesifazane nabesilisa kumele bafundiseke ngobungozi botshwala nangokuthi bakhulume uma kunengcindezi ababhekene nayo engabenza bagcine sebecwile otshwaleni.
Uhulumeni wethu angaze avumele utshwala pho?
Mhleli: Kuyiqiniso elingeke liphikwe ukuthi abaholi bethu kubahlule ekugcineni ukulwisana nalolu bhubhane oluhlasele izwe lethu.
Abakwenze ekugcineni ngenkathi bexegisa imithetho kufane nokudlala ngegeja kuziliwe, ngokuthi kuxegiswe eminye yemigomo emayelana notshwala.
Sekungaze kuvulelwe utshwala pho kuzo zonke izinto.
Yini ejahiwe ekuvulweni kotshwala?
Yebo, siyazi kukhona abakhala ngokuthi kuzolahleka imisebenzi kuphinde kuwe komnotho wezwe.
Yebo umnotho ubalulekile kodwa ngeke ubaluleke ukwedlula impilo yabantu.
Kuthe ngesikhathi umengameli ememezela ukuvulwa kotshwala ngavele ngafikelwa yizinyembezi, ngaphinde ngafikelwa yisililo.
Lokhu kwenzeke ngesikhathi ngizwa kukhala imikikizo namahuthi ezimoto.
Ngize ngazibuza ukuthi hlobo luni lobuholi esinabo ezweni?Uyabona, sinobuholi obucabangela izisu zabo nezisu zongxiwankulu.
Ngiyafisa ukuba ubuholi benhlangano ebusayo buvuke emaqandeni manje.
Lobu buholi esinabo akusibona obashiywa ngowayengomengameli wokuqala ngaphansi kwentando yabantu, uMnuz Nelson Mandela.
Ubuholi bukaMandela babucabangela izisu zabantu abahlwempu.
Mina ngifisa ubuholi bukaMengameli Cyril Ramaphosa buyeke ukudonswa ngekhala ngongxiwankulu.
Phela sisemazingeni aphansi siyabuka nje futhi siyakhala ngobuholi bakhe manje.
Kubuhlungu ukubona abaholi benhlanhlatha phambi kwethu.
Eyokuvulwa kotshwala ivele yafana nokugwazwa kwethu ngemuva ngoba ukhuvethe luzozicanasela ezweni lethu.
Ngiyafisa ukuba ubuholi bethu bucabangele impilo yabantu kuqala kunokucabangela inzuzo.

Wafakelwani uDkt Xhakaza kuKhozi FM?
Kwelakho eliphuma zonke izinsuku nelizikhipha zishisa zingakapholi.
Ngivumele ngibeke ilaka lami ngabaphathi boKhozi FM abasaqubeka nenzondo ngebandla lamaNazaretha.
Okungikhathazayo isihloko esiphume kwelakho langeSabatha esithi "Adinwe ayaveva amaKristu ecikwa ngowakwaShembe.
"Okungihlekisayo ukuthi lo muntu abakhuluma ngaye bethi ubakhubile uDkt Xhakaza ovame ukushintshana nDkt Mahaye ekuhlaziyeni izindaba zamaNazaretha.
Kodwa lona wakaXhakaza ungaphansi kweNazareth Church Of God, lolu hlangothi olungasekho nhlobo ezimisweni zenkolo yobuNazaretha kepha sebesezimisweni zomholi wabo uMfundisi MelusiI Mpanza.
Okungenze ngabhala lana ukuthi kunjena nje kungenxa yomphathi-zinhlelo uZandile Tembe ohlulwa wukuba umholi oqotho.
Phambilini inkolo yobuNazaretha ibihlaziywa uDkt Mahaye eyihlaziya ngobukhulu ubunyoninco.
Kuthe kungavuka isilwane savuka sama ngezinyawo kuDkt Xhakaza waputshukiswa esezoshintshana noDkt Mahaye.
Okwasikhathaza wukuthi uDkt Xhakaza ubengasahlaziyi inkolo kodwa bese ehlasela amazwi kaDkt Mahaye.
Mina engikubonile kuDkt Xhakaza wukuthi wahlulwa isilwane wafuna ukuyohlaziya inkolo yobuNazaretha ekubeni bona sebeyinkolo enezimiso zobuKristu.
Angibasoli oMfundisi Vusi Dube ngokumsola ngokuthi ukhuluma okungamfuni, kepha mina ngingasho ngingananazi ukuthi ukhuluma okumfunayo ngoba bayakholelwa enkolweni yobuKristu.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi abasekho ezimisweni zebandla lakwaShembe, phela bona kade bazihlukanisa bazivulela elabo ibandla eliholwa uMpanza hhayi owakaShembe.
Okungikhathazayo kakhulu ukuthi sekuba sengathi uDkt Xhakaza uyilungu lebandla lamaNazaretha kanti akaselona nhlobo.
Ngifisa ukwazi ukuthi abaphathi bomsakazo Ukhozi FM babengenwe yini ngesikhathi benika uDkt Xhakaza ithuba ngoba uDkt Mahaye ubehlaziya inkolo yobuNazaretha ngale kokugxibha inkolo yobuKristu kunalokho ubeqhakambisa ubumbano nokuzalana kwenkolo.
Kwesinye isikhathi siyabadinga abaholi bomsakazo abazoyilalela into abasuke beyifakile, ngoba kunjena nje yingoba abaphathi abayilaleli into abayenzile, lokhu kusitshela ukuthi sifunzwa ngenkani singabalaleli ukuba silalele.
Uyabona umunwe wami ukhomba ubhekisa kuZandile Tembe ongumphathizinhlelo ngokufaka amasobho amaningi ekubeni ukudla bekumnandi ohlelweni iTendelomcimbi olushayelwa uBheka Prince Mchunu ngeSabatha.
Bengifisa ukuba uDkt Xhakaza agxile entweni ayiyele emoyeni bese eyeka ukuhlasela izinkulumo zikaDkt Mahaye nenkolo yobuKristu.
Ngiyaneseka kakhulu Mfundisi Dube ngokuthi akakhishwe ohlelweni uDkt Xhakaza ngoba sifunzwa ukudla ekubeni singakufuni ngenxa yabaphathi boKhozi FM.
Khabzela KB MZIMELA EZWELIBOMVU
Abama-80s abahlukane nokutinyela ama-2000
KUNEMPI engingayazi ukuthi iyolanyulwa wubani phakathi kwabazalwe ngeminyaka ka-2000 nabeka-1980.
Zaze zalufela ubala izingane ezincane ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, zingenzanga lutho.
Ziningi izinto ezingezinhle ezihlala zibhalwa ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngezingane ezizalwe ngeminyaka ka-2000.
Imvamisa le mpi iba phakathi kwezintokazi zama-80"s ezihlala zifaka izithombe zazo ziswenkile, bese zifuna ukuqhathaniswa nezingane zika-2000.
Yilapho obona khona ukuthi inkulu indaba ngalezi zingane, indlela ezigqoka ngayo nemfashini yesimanje yehluke kakhulu kuneyangama-80"s.
 Okumangazayo wukuthi kunabantu beminyaka ka-1990 ongeke ubezwe bethi vu ngabaka-2000 ekubeni yibona abasondele eminyakeni yabo.
Babodwa abakhala ngokuthi abaka-2000 bayashesha ukuqoma nokukhulelwa futhi abalazi ihlazo.
Kumangaze ngoba kunenqwaba yabaka-2000 enabazali baka-1980 abacishe balingane nabanye babo, okukhombisa ngokusobala ukuthi nabo badlulile kulesi sigaba sobungane nokudideka.
Kwamanye amakhasi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, ikakhulu kuFacebook sekwaba yisitayela ukufaka isithombe sakho bese usho iminyaka onaye maqede uzibongele ngokuthi noma umdala usabukeka kangcono kunabaka-2000, okungawenzi umqondo.
Kuyihlazo okwenziwa ngabaka-1980 kulezi zingane ngenxa yokubona namathuba ezibe nawo empilweni.
Kuyacaca ukuthi konke okusuke kushiwo kuhambisana nomona ngoba lezi zingane zigxekwa ngesingisi esikhulu ezisikhulumayo, ukugqoka izimpahla ezibizayo, amathuba ezikhula ekhona nangokukhula ngokushesha.
Alikho nelincane iphutha elibekwa licace ngama-2000 ngaphandle kokuthi konke okubi kudalwa yibona.
Uma izintokazi zama-80"s zingazehlisa kuningi ezingakufunda kulezi zingane ngisho emakhaya.
Iningi lama-2000 likwazi ukwenza imisebenzi yezandla, ukusebenzisa ubuchwepheshe ngobuchule, yizindlela ezilula nokuzenza izitayela zasemakhanda, yizindlela zokugqokela izitayela zemfashini, ukuzenza izinzipho, ukuziphaqula zibuka kwi-internet.
Ngaphandle kwalezi zinto ziningi nezinye izinto abama-80"s abangazifunda yize ukuphendulana nomuntu omdala kungeyona into enhle kodwa ama-2000 ayakwazi ukuqophisana nawe ngenkulumo besebenzisa izibonelo ezisencwadini, uze ulibone nawe iphutha lakho.
Lokhu kuyakhombisa ukuthi abacindezelekile kangakanani ngokomqondo.
Noma ngabe abaka-1980 bangakhalipha kanganani kodwa akukho abazokufundisa ama-2000 kuzwakale kahle ngoba yonke into ayithatha ngolaka nokujaha ukuzigxeka lezi zingane.
Lesi yisikhathi sokwamukela ukuthi impilo ayisafani futhi indlela okhululiswe ngayo ngeke ifane nokukhuliswa ngayo izingane ezincane kunawe.
Kunezinto ama-2000 azazi kangcono kunabazalwe ngo-1980 futhi akulona ihlazo ngenxa yegebe leminyaka elikhona phakathi kwabo.
Le nto yaqalwa wumuntu oyedwa, walandelwa yinqwaba efuna ukubukwa ngokudicilela phansi isithunzi sabanye.
Uma umuntu efisa ukuguqula lesi simo angaqala ngokuveza okuhle okwenziwa yingane yangakubo ka-2000.
Phansi ngokuhlukunyezwa kwama-2000 ezinkundleni zokuxhumana engenacala!
Uyekeni umkhuba uzonehlisa isithunzi ezinganeni.

Akuphele ngokuhlukunyezwa kwabantu besifazane
MHLELI: Njengophiko lwabantu besifazane eqenjini iNkatha (IFPWB) asiqale sisho ukuthi siyakwamukela ukuboshwa kowesilisa osolwa ngokubulala izingane zakhe ezintathu eThekwini.
Njengabesifazane eqenjini sikhathazekile ngezigameko lapho abantu besilisa bekuthola kunzima satshe ukwamukela uma abesifazane abasebudlelwaneni nabo bebatshela ukuthi ucu alusahlangani entanyeni akuhlukwane.
Bebone kungcono ukuthi baziphindiselele ngokuthi baqothe imbokodo nesisekelo ngisho izingane imbala.
Siyazwelana kakhulu nayo yonke imindeni elahlekelwe zihlobo zayo ngenxa yodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane.
Sithi asiphinde futhi sizwakalise ukukhathazeka kwethu okukhulu mayelana nezigameko zokubulawa kwabantu besifazane ngesihluku.
Lokhu sikusho ngemuva kokubulawa kwesitshudeni sasenyuvesi yase-UCT u-Uyinene Mrwetyana kanye nomshayisibhakela wesifazane waseMdantsane uLeighandre Jegels kanye nabanye okungabikiwe ngokubulawa kwabo.
Lezi zigameko zokubulawa kwabantu besifazane zenzeka esikhathini lapho izwe laseNingizimu Afrika lisenkingeni yokubhekana nezinga eliphezulu lokwanda kodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane, lwenziwa ngabantu besilisa.
Abantu besifazane sebephenduke iziboshwa uqobo ezweni labo ngenxa yokwesaba ukwenzakaliswa ngabantu besilisa.
Nathi siyavumelana nalabo abathi udaba lodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane kumele luthathwe njengesibhicongo senhlekelele ezweni okumele kubhekwane naso ngokushesha.
Sinxusa-ke zonke izinhlaka zomthetho kuleli zwe ukuthi nazo zenze konke okusemandleni ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ziyalwa nalesi sihlava sokuhlukunyezwa kuphinde kubulawe abantu besifazane.
Izinhlaka zomthetho kumele zisheshise ukwenza uphenyo kuwo wonke amacala abikwayo nasebikiwe athinta ukuhlukunyezwa kwabantu besifazane.
Simelene nokuthi kuphele iminyaka kungafinyelelwa esiphethweni samacala okuhlukunyezwa kwabantu besifazane.
Isikhathi manje lesi sokuthi uqine umthetho ovikela abesifazane.
Bonke abahlukumezi kumele bajeziswe kanzima uma ngempela leli zwe lizimisele ukuvikela abantu besifazane.
Ngakho-ke kungumsebenzi kahulumeni wakuleli zwe ukuthi avikele abesifazane kubahlukumezi.
Sinxusa umphakathi ukuthi nawo awubambe iqhaza ekulweni nokuhlukunyezwa kwabantu besifazane nezingane.
Ngaphandle kokuthi zonke izinhlaka zibambisane ngeke inqotshwe impi yodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane.
Siyakholelwa kakhulu futhi ekutheni kumele kube nokushintsha komqondo kubantu besilisa babone ukuthi kuyinto embi ukuhlukumeza abantu besifazane.
Siwuphiko lwabesifazane eqenjini iNkatha sithi sekwanele manje ngodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane.
Into esiyidingayo nje kuphela uhulumeni ozimisele ekutheni aqhamuke namasu amasha angumkhombandlela ocacile oqondene nokulwa nodlame olubhekiswe kubantu besifazane.UMntwana Phumzile ButheleziMPL,uSihlalo kazwelonke wophiko lwabesifazane eqenjini iNkatha (IFP Women's Brigade)

Ubekhalaza ngoKhehlamfana basoKledeni, Bhekumthetho, eNcemaneni, eNkonjeni, kwaSodaka naseNkungwini nakwezinye izigodi ezikuwadi 8 KwaNongoma.
Umfundi ukhohlwe ukubala nenkiyankiya ekhungethe uwadi 8 kumasipala waKwaNongoma.
Ukuzilulaza kwamantombazane aleli wadi kufikiselana ngamahloni.
Awaphuzi ayabuhlaba utshwala!
Ahamba ezineka nje.
Vakashela eNcemaneni uzoyidela inkani.
Kuthiwa kuthi kungahlwa nje, bese ziyabuya KwaMadiba nase-Abu Tavern.
Hamba emzini wekhansela eBuxedene, uzokhexa umlomo.
Uzozibonela ubusantusantu bosisi bethu, bezilulaza ngokuzinikela otshwaleni.
Umbhali ushilo ukuthi ukudliwa kwesishimeyana kwaqala kuphi noBhekumthetho kodwa wakhohlwa ukuthi eBuxedene kwaqalaphi.
Bekumele asho ukuthi eBuxedene kwaqala KwaMankehli, KwaShabha naKwaKhwintshi.
Zazibuya bo lapho!
Nami mfoka Manzini, okungenza ngikhathazeke wukuthi angiliboni ikusasa kule ntsha esizinikele otshwaleni.
Ungalindelani enganeni yentombazane evuka ekuseni iyonkunkana notshwala?
Ihamba ingagezile, igqoke amadixa ekade ilele ngawo, ayendlulile nambhede, ayishanelile, izibi izeqa ngaphezulu.
Intombazane engalawuleki ebuya noma ngasiphi isikhathi ekhaya, uma njalo ibuyile.
Angiphathi uma kuyizinsuku zokuholwa kwemali yeqolo.
Izingane zizwa ngendaba ukuthi imali yazo iholiwe.
Umama ubuya ejekiwe noma ethwelwe ngebhala ngenxa yokudakwa.
Aqambe amanga athi izimpahla abezithengile zilahlekile.
Uma kungenjalo athi imali uyikhuthuzwe ngamaphara ehubhuza amanga kaBhejane.
Imali engabe ugcina ngayo izidingo zengane, uyibhubhudla otshwaleniAngiliboni ikusasa lapha.
Akukho muzi ongakhiwa lapha, akukho nkosikazi wekhaya, akukho myeni ongathatha umuntu onjena.
Ngidabukela abafowabo nomakoti babo abazohlushwa umjendevu ongayifuni inqubekela phambili empilweni.
Ngidabukela ogogo abondla izingane abangazazi nezibongo zazo.
Ngidakukela obaba nomama abazala benethemba lekusasa eliqhakazile.
Kanti bashaye phansi kwashunqa.
Lo mphakathi wakwawadi 8 udinga umkhuleko.
Kumele kuhlelwe isiguqo esiphuthumayo.
Sinxenxa wonke amabandla athathe izevatho, izimpulampula nemijiva kukhulekelwe leli wadi.
Kuyoba ngumbono omuhle kuhlanganwe emzini wekhansela, kukhulekelwe iwadi.
Kwazi bami?

Ngikhathazeka kakhulu ngekusasa lalezi zintombi eseziphenduke izibotho.
