Abathwebuli bengqephu esemazingeni omhlaba oThemba Mbuyisa, David Blaq, Shane Burnell nabo bayingxenye yalo mkhankaso wezobuciko ngokubambisana noLeeroy Jason.
Kulindeleke ukuthi izithombe zabo zengqephu zixoxe indaba ngemisiko eyahlukene yezinhlanga ezahlukene nezenza iNingizimu Afrika yehluke kwamanye amazwe.
UJulian Short oxuba iziphuzo ngendlela ewubuciko evamise ukubonakala emcimbini emikhulu yethelevishini naye uqokelwe ukuba yingxenye yalo mkhankaso.
FUNDA: Ucwaningo luveza okuthandwa abesifazane
KUNOMKHUBA wokuhlekisa ngabesifazane, kuthiwe abazazi ukuthi bafunani, kuthiwe bayakwazi ukuzenzisa ngisho into bengayithandi.
Ucwaningo lwakamumva olwenziwe yiMyEcho kwabesifazane abangu-1000 bakuleli, lucacisa kahle ngokufunwa yibona.
Lwenziwe ukubheka kuyo yonke imikhakha yempilo okubalwa umbono wabo kwezempilo, ezobuhle, ezothando nezokuvakasha.
UNksz Bette Midler obengomunye wabagqugquzeli kulolu cwaningo olubizwa ngeWhat Women Want, uthi kuhlaba umxhwele abakutholile.
Phakathi kwalokhu abebebuzwa kona abesifazane ukuthi yiziphi izimonyo abazithandayo nokuthi bazihlelela kanjani ezezimali.
Ohlangothini lwezobuhle abesifazane baveze ukuthi bakhonze kakhulu i-lipstick nokokuziphophotha ebusweni.
Kwezezempilo kuvele ukuthi okubakhathaza kakhulu ukuyobonana nodokotela olapha izinkinga zabesifazane iGynaecologist.
Bathe kuba nzima ukukhetha abazoya kuye.
Ngesikhathi bebuzwa ukuthi yini abayisaba kakhulu ngokwezempilo baveze ukuthi basaba ukukhuluphala, ukuba nokhwantalala nokuba nomdlavuza.
Mayelana nokuthi bafuna ukuhamba udokotela wesilisa noma owesifazane yini oyiGynaecologist, kuhlukane imibono.
Bangu-71% abathe bancamela ukuya kowesifazane.
Bechaza isizathu ukuthi kungcono ngoba owesifazane uyayiqonda kangcono imizimba yabo.
Bathe kuyasabeka ukutshela udokotela wesilisa izinkinga ezithinta imizimba yabo.
Bebuzwa ngezothando bathe ukuxoxisana yikona okwenza izinto zihambe kahle.
Bakhale nangokuthi bafuna ukunikezwa isikhathi esiningi yizithandwa zabo ukuqinisa uthando.
Baveze nokuthi izipho abafisa ukuthengelwa zona ngabathandana nabo, ubucwebe.
AMAJINI asahamba phambili kwabesifazane abaveze ocwaningweni ukuthi bayazifela ngawo Isithombe: INSTYLE.
COMMayelana nezindawo abafisa ukuzivakashela ngamaholide babale iParis neKapa futhi kube nendawo yokuzibhucunga umzimba.
Kwezemfasini abadala bathe bagqoka kakhulu kwaWoolworths bese kuthi abaneminyaka ephakathi kuka-18 no-24 bagqoke kwaMr Price.
"Sithole ukuthi abakujabulela kakhulu ngokuba umuntu wesifazane ukuthola izingane.
Bathe ayikho into ejabulisa njengomuzwa wokuba ngumama.
Bayakujabulela nokugqoka, abathe amajini yiwo abenza bazizwe bebahle kakhulu kuwona," kusho umbiko wocwaningo.
Lolu cwaningo lwenziwe ngokuhlanganyela yiMyEcho Survey Platform neMooiste Clothing Boutique.
Lwenziwe ngokusebenzisa izinkundla zokuxhumana ngeWomen's Day nonyaka, kwaqoqwa izimpendulo ezingu- 1 151 ezweni lonke kwabesifazane abaxube izinhlanga neminyaka.
IMyEcho yasungulwa yiLightstone Consumer okuyinkampani eyenza ucwaningo lwezimakethe, egxile ePort Elizabeth, e-Eastern Cape.
Ubambisene nesithandwa sakhe enkampanini yabo
UKUNGAYITHOLI inkampani ezomqeqesha ukuze athole isitifiketi sakhe kuholele ekutheni agcine esewusomabhizinisi.
UNksz Sabeliwe Gwala ungomunye wabanikazi benkampani iBambelela Steel Works And Alluminium eyenza amafasitela e-alluminium, ama-carports, amasango ensimbi, ama-buglar gaurds.
UNksz Gwala ungene kulo msebenzi ngo-2015.
Ngaleso sikhathi ubenza uN6 kwiHuman Resource, eLangeni College, eseNtuzuma.
"Angiyitholanga inkampani ezongiqeqesha kwiHuman Resource.
Angizange ngidikibale kodwa ngaphuma ngingena ezinkampanini ngenza noma yimuphi umsebenzi engiwutholayo," kusho uNksz Gwala.
Ngo-2015 uthe wahlangana noMnuz Joe Munguembe owayenza lo msebenzi.
"Ngamtshela ukuthi ngifuna umsebenzi, akazange anginake wabona intombi washela.
Ngaleso sikhathi ngangigxile ekutheni kumele ngithole umsebenzi ngamziba ngaqhubeka ngafuna umsebenzi.
Ngenza amatoho ehlukene okubalwa kuwo ukuhlanza izindlu, ukuba uweta neminye.
Ngabuye ngahlangana naye wangitshela ukuthi ibhizinisi lakhe selikhulile kungaba njani ngifike ngizobona ukuthi yini engingayenza," kusho uNksz Gwala.
Wafika ibhizinisi selikhulile kodwa indlela uMunguembe ayeliphethe ngayo yayenza ukuthi lingakhuli ngendlela efanele.
Wabona ithuba lokuthi alikhulise.
Waqala ngokuvula ikhasi lalo ibhizinisi wamsiza ekutheni benze izinhlobo eziningi zamafasitela neminye imisebenzi yensimbi ukuze amakhasimende athole konke akufunayo.
"Ngenxa yokusebenza kwami savumelana ngokuthi kungcono ngingabi ngumsebenzi kodwa nami ngibe ngomunye wabanikazi bebhizinisi.
Njengamanje sinemoto yethu esidiliva ngayo umkhiqizo wethu.
Kancane kancane kuzogcina kuyile nto esiyiphuphayo," kusho uNksz Gwala.
UNksz Gwala noMunguembe sebeyizithandani kanti bathi ukuthandana kwabo akuliphazamisi iphupho labo.
UNksz Gwala umsebenzi wakhe omkhulu ukufuna amakhasimende, ahambe aye emizini yawo ayokala amafasitela, izicabha, amasango nalapho kuzofakwa khona i-carport.
"Ngesinye isikhathi amakhasimende aba nokungingabaza ukuthi ngiyakwazi ukukala kahle.
Bangibuza kaningi ukuthi sengike ngawenza yini lo msebenzi phambilini noma ngiyaqala.
Uma sekuzofakwa bebona ukuthi lokho okufakwayo kungena ngendlela baba nokungethemba baze babuze nezinye izinto kimi.
Ngemuva komsebenzi ngibuye ngibafonele ngibabuze ukuthi benelisekile yini ngomsebenzi wethu.
Lokho kwenza ukuthi kube yibo abasitholela amanye amakhasimende," kusho yena.
Uthe ziningi izinto ezintsha eziqhamukayo kulo mkhakha wabo.
Yena uhlale efunda izinto ezintsha bese etshela isoka lakhe ngazo baqale ukuzikhangisa amakhasimende azibone.
Nakuba ibhizinisi labo ethi likhula kahle uthe kukhona ababona bebancane bangafuni ukubakhokhela ngendlela.
"Sesize safunda ukuthi ingxenye enkulu yemali umuntu ayikhokhe ngaphambi kokuthi senze umsebenzi ngoba besiba nenkinga amakhasimende engasikhokheli kahle.
Sigcina sishodelwa yimali yokwenza imisebenzi yamanye amakhasimende," kusho yena.
Okuhloswe wuSihlalo webhodi  loMgeni Water
Igama elithi Gabsie alisilo isidlaliso ngoba lithathelwa esithakazelweni sakubo esithi Mgabadeli.
Ukuqinisekisa ukuthi abantu bathola amanzi ahlanzekile le ntokazi yaseManyiseni, eyakhulela eShowe ihlela ukwakha amadamu amathathu amanzi kule minyaka ezayo.
"Idamu elilodwa sesiyitholile indawo yokulakha kodwa kusazokwenziwa ucwaningo kuhlolwe imvelo nokunye okuningi okwenzeka ngaphambi kokwakha, sinethemba lokuthi kuzothi kuphela unyaka kube sekunyakazeka.
Elesibili sizoxoxa noMnyango wezeziMali ngoba sizodinga ukuthi siyofuna imali.
elesithathu elizoba seMkhomazi, inhloso yethu wukuqinisekisa ukuthi bonke abantu banamanzi ahlanzekile.
"Uthe iNingizimu Afrika yizwe elingenawo amanzi amaningi washo nokuthi njengoba kuyisebusika KwaZulu-Natal imvula ayibonwa.
Ukulwa nale ngqinamba yokungabikho kwamanzi amaningi eNingizimu Afrika, Umgeni Water uyawagcina amanzi ehlobo uma izulu lina.
Lawo manzi uNksz Mathenjwa uthe asetshenziswa ebusika ngoba benza njengentuthane eqoqa ukudla kwayo ehlobo.
Uveze ukuthi ufuna kube nohlelo lokuxoxa namakhosi nezinduna ngendlela abantu ababekwa ngayo ezindaweni zasemakhaya.
"Uthola ukuthi uma siletha amanzi ezindaweni zasemakhaya, imizi igqagqene kakhulu okusho ukuthi kufanele ufake amapayipi amaningi.
Ngifuna kube nohlelo lokuxoxa nabaholi bendabuko ngalolu daba ukuze kube lula ukuletha amanzi.
"Uveze ukuthi ezindaweni eziningi abaletha kuzo ingqalasizinda yamanzi kufanele bavule umgwaqo ngaphambi kokuletha amanzi ngoba usuke ungekho esimeni esifanele.
Uthe banenkinga nabantu abakha kuma-floodlines okusho ukuthi imizi esendaweni ligcwala amanzi uma line kakhulu.
Udonse abantu ngendlebe wathi bangalokothi bakhe kulezi zindawo ngoba bazibeka engcupheni yokumuka uma kuna imvula enkulu.
UNksz Mathenjwa uneziqu zemfundo ezehlukene okukhona kuzo iBSC yeHydrology ayithola enyuvesi yaseZululand, amaMaster's amabili, kuyimanje umatasa neMaster's yesithathu.
Ugqugquzele abantu ukuthi bafunde ngoba imfundo ivula amathuba okukhula empilweni nasengqondweni.
"Abantu kufanele bafunde ngoba imfundo iyakusiza ukuthi wenze umsebenzi wakho kangcono, ukwazi nokuthola amanye amathuba.
BengiseNew York kwi-Unted Nations ngiyokhuluma ngamanzi, inhlanzeko nabesifazane.
Ngenhlanhla bengenza ucwaningo ngalolu daba," kusho uNksz Mathenjwa.
Uthe iMaster's yakhe yokuqala wayibhalisa ngo-2000 eneminyaka ewu-23, kwathi ngo-2009 wabhalisela eyesibili.
Ucele intsha ukuthi ingasheshi ukulahla ithemba ngoba yena wafaka izicelo zomfundaze ezingaphezu kuka-400 ngesikhathi eyongena enyuvesi.
Izicelo zomsebenzi nazo uthe ziningi ayezifaka kungabuyi mpendulo kodwa elokhu ezifakile.
"Ngaphandle kokuba wuSihlalo weBhodi yoMgeni Water, ngiwusomabhizinisi, nginenhlangano esiza umphakathi ngentuthuko ebuye ifake nezolimo, Insika Foundation.
Ngiyabaqeqesha abantu ukuze babe namakhono azobasiza.
Kubalulekile ukuthi osomabhizinisi nabo bafunde ngisho bengayanga esikhungweni semfundo ephakeme kodwa bafunde izincwadi ezizobasiza,"Wenze isibonelo sokuthi uma uwusomabhizinisi uyadinga ukuqonda imithetho ebhalwe ezinkontilekeni, wazi nokuthi uma unabasebenzi kufanele ubabhalisele i-Unemployment Insurance Fund nezinye izimfanelo.
Uthe kufanele usomabhizinisi abe namakhono okuqasha abantu, awokuphatha imali, nolwazi lomthetho.
Umgeni Water ubalwa nezikhungo ezidume ngokuthola umbiko womncwaningi mabhuku omuhle.
UNksz Mathenjwa uthe imfihlo yabo wukuthi bayamlalela umcwaningi mabhuku jikelele uma ebayalela ukuthi bathuthukise izingxenye ezithile zokusebenza.
"Sinamakomiti ahlukene ebhodini lethu abhekele ezokuphatha, ukusebenza, isimilo, ukuphathwa kwemali nezikhalo ezingenayo.
Sinosihlalo ozimele obhekela izikhalo ezingenayo eMgeni Water.
Lokhu kuyasisiza ukuthi siwenze ngendlela umsebenzi.
"UNksz Mathenjwa unamadodana amabili eyodwa ino-18 enye ineminyaka emibili, uthe abesifazane bangakwenza konke empilweni uma besihlela kahle isikhathi sabo.
Wenze isibonelo sokuthi uma ezohamba unkosikazi kamfowabo nonina baye bambhekele izingane.
"Abesifazane kufanele bakhulume ngemisebenzi yabo nangempilo nemindeni yabo.
Sikhona isikhathi sokufunda uma uzihlela.
Ungaba nosisi osizayo ekhaya ozohlanza indlu, apheke kodwa awukwazi ukuyalela lowo sisi ukuthi achithe isikhathi nezingane zakho noma anakekele umyeni wakho.
Uwena okufanele uchithe isikhathi nezingane nomyeni wakho nabantu basemzini.
"Uphethe ngokugqugquzela abantu ukuthi bafunde kuma-FET bangawabukeli phansi ngoba ayadingeka amakhono ama-artisan neminye imisebenzi.
Uthe Umgeni Water uyabafundisa abantu ngokubanika imifundaze nokunye okuningi.
Uma kukhulunywa ngoMgeni Water uthe abantu abangacabangi amanzi kuphela kodwa babheke amathuba ebhizinisi ngoba le nhlangano iyasebenzisana nosomabhizinisi abahlukene kusukela kwabahlela imicimbi, abaphekayo, ama-artisan nabanye.
Isexwayiso ngokuzenzela okhilimu bobuso
Mbali KhanyileKUNABANTU ababikelwayo uma sekushaye isikhathi sehlobo ngenxa yohlobo lwesikhumba sabo esincikiselayo uma kushisa.
Abanye balaba bantu kabakwazi ukuthenga imikhiqizo yesikhumba ebizayo, bagcina sebezama ezinye zezindlela zokulwa nobubi besikhumba.
Phakathi kwezindlela abagcina sebethembela kuzo kubalwa ibovu, isibabuli, umuthi wokuxubha amazinyo nokunye.
Lezi zindlela abasuke bezisebenzisa bavamise ukuzincoma kakhulu ngokuba nemiphumela emihle.
Kepha ungoti wesikhumba usexwayise ngemikhiqizo yokuzakhela engahloliwe izingabunjalo bayongokuthi ingaba yingozi esikhunjeni somuntu.
UDkt Cebi Sibisi ongungoti wesikhumba, uthe akabeluleki abantu ukuthi basebenzise imikhiqizo abazihlanganisela yona emakhaya ngoba kwesinye isikhathi abantu iyabashisa esikhunjeni.
"Sekukaningi ngibona abantu belinyazwe yimikhiqizo abazihlanganisele bona.
Abanye basuke bebona ama-video ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngoba bethi banqanda inkinga kanti bayayandisa.
Lokho kugcina sekubafaka ezinkingeni zokuthungatha usizo kodokotela besikhumba abebebabalekelela," kuchaza uDkt uSibisi.
Uxwayise ngale mikhiqizo, i-apple cider, ujusi walamula, umuthi wokuxubha amazinyo, athe akuvumelekile.
Amathiphu okunakekela isikhumba ehlobo:* Phuza amanzi kakhulu-Ukuphuza kakhulu amanzi kuyasiza njengoba ukungcola kwesikhumba kukhishwa ngamanzi osuke uwaphuza.
*Hambela kude nelanga- Gqoka uphinde ugcobe imikhiqizo ekuvikela ekushisweni yilanga.
* Vakashela udokotela wesikhumba ozokucebisa ngokuhambisana nesikhumba sakho.
* Uma usiqonda isikhumba sakho, vakashela ikhemisi ongasizakala kulona ngokumele ukugcobe.
* Zijwayeze ukugcoba i-sunscreen njengoba ivikela ebungozini bokusha kwesikhumba.
Ufisa lwande uthando lwesayensi
UFUNA uthando lwesayensi ezinganeni zase-Afrika lwande, uDkt Bongiwe Mshengu ofundisa isayensi ophikweni lweChemistry nePhysics, enyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal.
UDkt Mshengu (35) waseMzumbe ungomunye wabesifazane abasohlelweni lwe-UKZN, lokuhlonipha abesifazane abasemkhakheni wesayensi olubizwa ngeWonder Women in Science.
Le ntokazi eyafunda eBuhlebethu High, ithe yakhula inothando lwesayensi ngakho ifisa ukuludlulisela kwabanye abantu.
"Ngikhule ngithanda ukuba wudokotela kusukela ngimncane.
Ngineminyaka eyisithupha ngaba nepamuza elikhulu onyaweni lwesokunxele elalenza ngingakwazi ukuhamba.
Ngayiswa kumelaphi wesintu owasebenzisa amakhambi ahlukene ukuze angilaphe.
Kwakuyisikhathi esibuhlungu kodwa ngalapheka ngagcina sengikwazi ukuhamba.
Lokhu kwangenza ngawathanda amakhambi ngafuna ukucwaninga ngolwazi lwawo ekulapheni.
Ngakhetha izifundo zesayensi emsebenzini.
Ngikhule ekhaya nasesikoleni othisha bethi ngizoba wudokotela ngoba ngangenza kahle esikoleni," kuchaza uDkt Mshengu.
Emuva kokuphothula * -matric akakwazanga ukufundela iziqu zobudokotela ngoba wayengenawo amaphuzu enele kodwa wagcina esenza iziqu zeDietics.
Ngonyaka wokuqala wenza iPhysics, chemistry, biology ne-mathematics.
"Ngathola ukuthi i-chemistry ilula kanti ngangiyithanda nePhysics, lwavuka uthando lwemithi.
Ngaqala ngafunda ngeminye imikhakha yesayensi ngoba ngifuna ukwandisa ulwazi lwami ngamakhambi asetshenziswa ukwelapha izifo ezihlukene ngokwesintu nangokwaseNtshonalanga.
"Wathola iziqu zeBSC kwiChemistry neBiochemistry wenza neMasters nePhd eyayigxile emakhambini.
Ushadile unezingane ezimbili.
Ufisa lwande uthando lwesayensi ezinganeni ngoba abantu abaningi abayibheki ngeso lokuthi isetshenziswa nsukuzonke.
"Izingane zizitshela ukuthi isayensi ilukhuni ngoba zifunda izincwadi zingabheki ukuthi isayensi iyasebenza ukulapha nsukuzonke.
Ngikholwa wukuthi isayensi imnandi uma nothisha abayifundisayo beyiqonda kahle.
Umsebenzi onikwa izingane kufanele kube yilowo ozokwenza ukuthi zisebenzise izibonelo ezizibona emphakathini wazo.
"Uthe umsebenzi wakhe wokucwaninga ngesayensi awulula ukuwuthola ngoba kuyabiza ukwenza ucwaningo ngakho abantu abakulo mkhakha badinga ukulekelwa.
"Ngasizakala ngokuthi ngithole uDkt Roshila Moodley, naye okholelwayo kwabesifazane abakwisayensi.
Nginethemba lokuthi uma sisebenzisana isayensi izoba mnandi ezinganeni sande nesibalo sososayensi besifazane kugcwale zonke izinhlanga kulo mkhakha," kusho uDkt Mshengu.
Ugqugquzele abafundi ukuthi bawuthande lo mkhakha, bazinike isikhathi sokwenza umsebenzi, bahlale bezivivinya ukwandisa ulwazi lwabo.
Uthi uma usebenzisa isayensi zonke izinsuku ulwazi luyanda ugcine usungumpetha wayo.
Sekuphenduke isitayela ukuphuca
MBALI KHANYILEUKUPHUCA ikhanda bekwaziwa njengento ehambisana nesiko kubantu besifazane abamnyama njengoba bekuyaye kwenziwe uma kushoniwe.
Mumva nje sekushintshile lokhu njengoba sekuphenduke isitayela ukususa izinwele ekhanda ngale kokuhloniza noma ukuzenyeza.
Lesi sitayela singenisile nakosaziwayo bakuleli kanti nozime othwele isicoco sikaMiss South Africa uShudufhadzo Musida, ushaya ngayo imbungculu.
Abanye osaziwayo abaziwa ngalesi sitayela ngoLebo Mashilo, abalingisi oZikhona Sodlaka olingisa kwiHouse Keepers, Bukamina Cebekhulu olingisa kuMuvhango nomrepha wakuleli uNomuzi Moozlie Mabena.
UNksz Siza Chili, ongumcwali wezinwele, uthe lolu hlobo lwesitayela lulungele lonke uhlobo lomuntu wesifazane ozethembayo ngobuhle bakhe.
Uthe yize silungele wonke umuntu lesi sitayela, abafanelwa kakhulu yiso yilabo abanobuso obugcwele futhi obusandilinga.
"Lesi sitayela sigqamisa ingxenye yobuso edalelwe ukuthi igqame kumuntu wesifazane.
Iziqhomo namehlo ngezinye zezinto ezigqamisa ubuhle bomuntu wesifazane yingakho ubuhle bakhe bunezeleleka uma esuse izinwele," kuchaza uNksz Chili.
Eqhuba uthe yinkolelo yakudala ukuthi umuntu wesifazane udinga izinwele ukuze kubonakale ubuhle bakhe.
"Kubalulekile kumuntu wesifazane ogundile ukuthi aziphaqule kancane ukuze ubuhle bakhe bunezezeleke.
Angafaka i-lip gloss, adwebe ishiya bese efaka ne-mascara," kusho uNksz Chili.
Amathiphu okunakekela lesi sitayela:Qinisekisa ukuthi uyaligeza zonke izinsuku ikhanda lakhoQikelela ukuthi usebenzisa i-conditioner yezinwele noma kabili ngesonto.
Lokhu kuzodala ukuthi izinwele zakho zibe nempilo uma sezikhulile.
Faka i-hair food uma unesikhumba esomile.
Uma kuyisikhumba esichichayo, hlala nayo imizuzu emihlanu bese uyayisula ngaphambi kokuba uphume endlini.
Vikela ikhanda lakho elangeni.
Ugqugquzela ukutshala ngaphandle kwamakhemikhali
UNkk Sibongile Mtungwa-Jakatyanawase-Underberg, usemkhakheni wabalimi obizwange-Agro-Ecology.
Kulo mkhakha kutshalwa ngaphandle kokusebenzisa amakhemikhali nomanyolo, okuthiwa kubulala umhlabathi nemifino.
UNkk Mtungwa-Jakatyana osanda kuphothula nokuqeqeshwa kulo mkhakha, uthe ukube kuya ngaye ngabe kubuyelwa kule ndlela yokutshala.
Uthe ocwaningweni kutholakale ukuthi izifo eziningi zidalwa ukudla okufakwa amakhemikhali uma kutshalwa.
"Ngakhula vele ngikuthanda ukulima, ngingayithengi imifino ngoba ngiyazitshalela.
Umqondo wokugxila kulo mkhakha we-Agro-Ecology, waqala ngo-2007 ngibheka ukuthi ngingabafundisa kanjani abanye.
Ngathola ukuthi alukho uhlobo lwemifino olungeke lutshaleke ngaphansi kwalo mkhakha," echaza.
Ngo-2010 wasungula iWomen's Leadership and Training Programme egxile ekufundiseni abesifazane nezingane ngale ndlela yokulima.
Uthe ukhuthaza ukuthi bonke abazali banikeze amadodakazi abo izindawo zokutshala emakhaya.
Okwenze aqeqeshe nomama ukuthi bakwazi ukubheka izingadi uma izingane zisesikoleni.
Ukulima ngale ndlela kudinga ingadi inakekelwe njalo.
Okuyinselelo wukuthi uma kunesomiso, umhlaba uyathikamezeka.
Uthe nokuguquguquka kwesimo sezulu kuyawulimaza lo mkhakha wezolimo.
Nokho kuningi uNkk Mtungwa-Jakatyana athe kungasiza uma kufundiswa ngalo mkhakha wokulima.
"Akudingeki amanzi amaningi ukuchelela izingadi.
Njengoba sinenkinga yokushoda kwamanzi kuleli, kungasiza ukugxila kulo mkhakha.
Nabagulayo siyabakhuthaza ukuthi badle ukudla okutshalwe ngale ndlela ngoba akunawo amakhemikhali," kusho yena.
Yize engenawo umhlaba abatshala kuwo, uthe uke waxhaswa ngemali ngabeLotto nabakwaSeda ukuqeqesha abesifazane nezingane zabo.
Uthe olunye ulwazi waluthola kwamanye amazwe, okubalwa iGermany lapho lusetshenziswa khona.
Ngaphandle kokuzitshalela ukuze badle nemindeni yabo, uthe bonke abaqeqeshayo uyabakhuthaza nokuthi bayidayise imifino.
Ukhuthaza nokuthi baphe abagulayo, abadinga imifino engenawo amakhemikhali.
UNkk Mtungwa-Jakatyana uneziqu zeDevelopment Studies.
Muva nje uphothule ukuqeqeshwa kwi-Atlantic Fellows for Health Equity in SA -Tekano, ngaphansi kwe-Oxford University.
Ungoti nezeluleko ngezangaphansi
Kuba lula ngisho ukuwasha lezi zimpahla zangaphansi ngamanzi umuntu asuke egeza ngawo esebenzisa nanoma iyiphi insipho umuntu asuke egeza ngayo.
Abanye abanqeni ukududla izimpahla zangaphansi nezinye izingubo umuntu asuke eziwasha, esebenzisa noma yiluphi uhlobo lwensipho.
Ungoti wezimpahla zangaphansi eSatin Candy, eWindermere, eThekwini, uNksz Silondiwe Nkabinde, uthi izimpahla zangaphansi akumele nakancane ziwashwe njengezinye izimpahla, nanganoma iyiphi insipho.
Kuningi athi kungenza izimpahla zangaphansi zakhele iphunga noma zisheshe zibe amatwili ngenxa yendlela eziwashwa ngayo.
Uthi lokhu akukhethi bulili, imikhiqizo enamakha ingadala iphunga ezimpahleni zangaphansi ngenxa yokuthi uhlobo lwendwangu okuthungwa ngayo lezi zimpahla imvamisa iyefana.
UNGOTI wezimpahla zangaphansi eSatin Candy uNksz Silondiwe Nkabinde uthi kubalulekile ukuzinakekela ngendlela izimpahla zangaphansi"Kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu anakekele izimpahla zakhe zangaphansi aziwashe ngendlela ehlukile nayisebenzisa uma ewasha izingubo zokugqoka.
"Akumele nakancane usebenzise amanzi ashisayo noma ngabe kubanda kangakanani.
"Kufana nokuziwasha usebenzisa umshini, akulungile kuyazona izimpahla zangaphansi," kusho le ntokazi.
Uthi empeleni izimpahla zangaphansi zinemikhiqizo eyakhelwe kuphela ukuwasha zona.
Ethakwe ngokucabangela ukuthi impahla yangaphansi isondela kakhulu esithweni sangasese.
Izinsipho ezibizwa ngama-lingerie wash uthi akumele zithathwe njengemikhiqizo yabadla izambane likapondo, kodwa wonke umuntu kumele asondele kuyona.
Uthi le mikhiqizo yakhiwe ngezithako eziyimvelo ezikulungele ukuba kulezi zimpahla.
"Okwenza lo mkhiqizo wehluke kulezi zinsipho ezijwayelekile, uthi ukuthi awubi nazo izithako ezinamakhemikhali.
"Insipho yokugeza ejwayelekile noma lezi zokuwasha, akumele kusetshenziswe," kusho uNksz Nkabinde.
Eqhuba uthe uma umuntu zithi zisuka esebenzisa le mikhiqizo efanele, kuyasiza ekutheni izimpahla zakhe zihlale isikhathi eside ikakhulu obhodisi kubantu besifazane.
"Indwangu yezimpahla zangaphansi iyashintsha iqine uma ungayiwashi ngendlela.
"Uma seyiqinile kuba nzima ukuthi iphinde ithambe kahle ngoba usuke umuntu eqhubeka nokuwasha ngendlela engafanele.
"Lokhu kwenza ukuthi zisheshe ziguge izimpahla zabantu abaningi,"kusho uNksz Nkabinde.
Nakhu okunye okubalulekile:Ungangeni emanzini ungazikhumulile izimpahla zangaphansi.
Khumula konke kuqala, kuyima ungena eshaweni noma kubhavu.
Ukungena nezimpahla zangaphansi kuyazinweba.
Qala ngokuwasha impahla yakho yangaphansi ngaphambi kokugeza.
Ngaleyo ndlela uzokwazi ukuyiwasha ngamanzi abandayo kahle, ungayiwashi ngashisayo obukade ugeza ngawo.
'Ungathathi imishwalense eminingi'
ABANTU abamnyama basasaba ukunqaba uma beshelwa yizinkampani zemishwalense ezifuna ukujoyinwa, okungezinye zezinto ezibadalela izikweletu ezingapheli.
Lawa ngamazwi kaNksz Wendy Ndlovu (41), oyiMenenja yakwaMetropolitan KwaZulu-Natal.
UNksz Ndlovu owaqala ukungena kulo mkhakha wemishwalense ngokugcwele ngo-1999, wadonswa ukuthi baningi emndenini wakhe abazithole besenkingeni ngenxa yemishwalense abayijoyinile.
Unina obenguthisha, wajoyina umshwalense wokufundisa yena (uNksz Ndlovu) okuthe sekushaya isikhathi sokuthi ukhokhe kwaba nenkinga.
"Ngathola ukuthi umama wayengijoyinele umshwalense wokufunda, okuthe sekumele ngiwusebenzise wakhokhela imali yokubhalisa kuphela.
Ngithe sengimbuza kahle ngathola ukuthi kuwona lo mshwalense ubebuye avunyelwe ukuthi aboleke, yingakho agcina ethola imali encane.
Baningi nabanye emndenini engathola ukuthi bebenenkinga efanayo.
Ungathathi umshwalense ongawudingi"UNksz Ndlovu wafundela iFashion Design and Technology eNatal Technikon esibizwa ngeDurban University of Technology, wangaqeda ngenxa yokuswela imali.
Uthe kube nzima ukuthola umsebenzi engenazo iziqu, okwenza wabheka noma onjani angawuthola.
Unina wamtshela ukuthi bekufike abantu emsebenzini wakhe, bezofuna abazosebenzela inkampani yomshwalense.
Wangena kanjalo kulo mkhakha ngo-1997 kodwa engaqashiwe ngokugcwele.
Uveze ukuthi ngaleso sikhathi ayikho inkampani eyayifuna ukumqasha ngenxa yokuba mncane ngeminyaka.
Nokho kumsizile ukuqeqeshwa ukuze athole isipiliyoni.
Uthe baningi abamnyama abangenalo ulwazi ngezezimali, okwenza bathathe nemishwalense abangayidingi.
Ugxeka nozakwabo kulo mkhakha athe basuke bebheke kuphela imali, bangamchazeli kahle umuntu.
"Abamnyama basanenkinga yokuthi bavele bajoyine nje umshwalense ngoba nakhu sekuthiwe abawuthathe.
Umuntu agcine ekhokhela imishwalense eminingi angayidingi.
Kuwumsebenzi wethu esisebenza ezinkampanini zemishwalense ukuthi sichazele abantu ngesimo sezimali.
Umuntu kumele umchazele ukuthi yini ayidinga kakhulu, ngokubheka isimo sakhe sezimali.
Nomuntu akumele athathe iomishwalense eminingi angayidingi"Echaza ngomsebenzi wakhe, uthe kumele abheke ukunyusa kwezinga lokudayiswa komshwalense esifundazweni.
Kumele abheke namathuba lapho bengakha khona ubudlelwano kwezamabhizinisi.
Kudingeka aphinde akhuthaze, abe yiso nakubasebenzi abangaphansi kwakhe.
Sekuvuliwe kwabafuna ukungenela uMiss SA
KUZOVALWA ngoJuni 24, ukufaka izicelo ezintokazini ezifuna ukuzama inhlanhla emcimbini walo nyaka kaMiss SA, ozoba ngo-Okthoba.
Isicoco sangonyaka odlule sakhala semuka nentokazi yaseLimpopo, uShudufhadzo Musida.
Kuvulwe izolo ngehora lesihlanu ntambama ukungenela.
Esikhangisweni esikhishwe izolo ntambama ezinkundleni zokuxhumana naseziteshini ezihlukene zethelevishini, kubonakala izintokazi ezake zaba kulo mcimbi, uShudufhadzo Musida, Thato Mosehle noNatasha Joubert, bekhuthaza izintokazi ukuthi zingagajwa wuvalo kodwa mazenze into ezozijabulisa empilweni.
Isikhangisi siyoze sivalwe ngosuku lokugcina lokungenela umncintiswano.
UStephanie Weil, okhulumela inhlangano iMiss South Africa Organisation ehlela umcimbi, uveze ukuthi sebekulindele ngabomvu ukuhlangana nentsha ezongenela umcimbi walo nyaka, bese beyethula kubantu bakuleli.
"Kuyasijabulisa ukuthi umcimbi kaMiss South Africa uyaqhubeka nokusiza intsha efuna ukufeza amaphupho ayo nokuzwakalisa okuhle efuna ukukwenza kuleli, uma idla umhlanganiso kulo mcimbi.
Kulo mcimbi siyaqhubeka nokuqinisekisa ukuthi ukungenela kuba lula kakhulu njengoba kungekho amafomu agcwaliswayo futhi kungasahanjelwa zifundazwe.
Abafuna ukungenela bangangena ku-website yethu ethi:www.misssa.co.za lapho bezophendula khona imibuzo embalwa, bafake nezithombe zabo," kuchaza uStaphanie.
Uveze ukuthi uShudufhadzo, kuzothi ngoDisemba walo nyaka ayomela leli emcimbini kaMiss World, ozoba sePuerto Rico.
UShudufhadzo uveze ukuthi njengoba uhambo lwakhe kulesi sihlalo seluyela emaphethelweni, angakuveza ngalo wukuthi lube ngolufeza amaphupho akhe.
"Lolu hambo kalugcinanga ngokungikhulisanga nje kuphela, kodwa lungenze nami ngakwazi ukusiza abanye.
Ngibonile ukuthi amaphupho ngempela ayafezeka futhi nempilo yami ishintshe kakhulu.
Lokhu ngiyokuxoxela izizukulwane zami ezizayo.
Ngiyabonga kakhulu ngethuba," kuchaza uShudufhadzo.
UPutuma useqome owokholo emuva kokulaxaza i-jazz
UMCULI uPutuma Tiso uselaxaze umculo we-jazz wagxila kowokholo yize ebesethathwa futhi eteketiswa ngelikaMiriam Makeba ngenxa yekhono lakhe kulo mculo.
Ababaningi abaculi abakwazi ukuxebuka kolunye uhlobo lomculo bangene kolunye ngempumelelo.
Asebeke bakwenza lokho futhi bagcina sebehlonishwa eminxeni emisha ngoRebecca Malope owayecula i-bubblegum kodwa osecula owokholo, uLucky Dube owashona esebizwa ngenkosi ye-reggae noSwazi Dlamini owayecula owokholo kodwa osecula i-Afro jazz.
UPutuma wangena emculweni okhokhelwayo nge-jazz njengoba esebizwa ngeGoddess of Gospel.
Le ntokazi engeyokuzalwa ePort Elizabeth izoqopha iDVD yokuqala yomculo wokholo ethi Restored eFather's House, eLimpopo ngenyanga ezayo.
Kwenzeka lokhu nje usanda kuwina kuma-Independent National Gospel Music Awards (Ingoma) kumunxa weBest Female Artist.
Uqale emculweni we-jazz ngesikhathi ejoyina inkampani kaSipho "Malambule" Sithole, iNative Rhythm, lapho aqopha khona iCD eyayithi Pu2ma.
Le albhamu yamenza wangabe esaba yindlala kwiStandard Bank Joy of Jazz eGoli neCape Town International Jazz Festival.
Uthe lo mculo wamethula kwezinye izinkakha okungoSibongile Khumalo noHugh Masekela abazungeza noPutuma ochungechungeni lwamakhonsathi ngisho naphesheya kwezilwandle.
"UBra Hugh waze wathi ngimkhumbuza uMiriam Makeba, cabanga kusho umuntu osezingeni likaBra Hugh.
"Nakuba kwakumnandi kunjalo kodwa umphefumulo wakhe wawunganeme ngenxa yokuthi lo mculo wawungekho emithanjeni yakhe.
"Umphefumulo wami wawungawuzwa kahle."
Uthe wagcina eshiyile unomphela kwi-jazz njengoba esegxila kowokholo.
Obeyisikhulu sakwa-Engen usengumnikazi wegalaji
AKUMELE kube nento abantu besifazane abathi abakwazi ukuyenza ngenxa yobulili babo.
Lokhu kushiwo nguNkk Thandi MaThabethe Ngxongo, ongumnikazi omusha wegalaji likaphethroli lakwaBP, elisemgwaqweni uChe Guervara (Moore Road) eBerea eThekwini.
UNkk Ngxongo uthathe ngokusemthethweni isikhundla sokuba ngumnikazi omusha wegalaji ngesonto eledlule, kanti kuyaqala ukuthi libe nomnikazi omnyama futhi ongowesifazane.
Elandisa Isolezwe uthe abasebenzi bamamukele ngezandla ezifudumele kodwa uyazi ukuthi ekujuleni kwezinhliziyo, bayazibuza ukuthi ngabe uzofika nani ngoba vele ushintsho lunjalo.
Ezinkundleni zokuxhumana bekuchwaza kusukela ngeledlule abantu bemhalalisela ngokuba ngumnikazi omusha wegalaji elidumile.
"Uma umsebenzi kade uphethwe wuhlanga oluthile, kubakhona ukuthi selizowa ngoba thina bantu abamnyama asinawo umlando wokuphatha umsebenzi onjengegalaji likaphethroli.
Kuliqiniso ukuthi ngiyaqala ukuba umnikazi wegalaji kodwa emkhakheni kaphethroli sekunesikhathi ngikhona," kusho uNkk Ngxongo.
Le ntokazi ekhulele eMooi River, ithi iyaziwa ukuthi ingowesifazane ofohlayo uma esezitshelile ukuthi into uyayenza futhi iyaphumelela.
Iqhube yathi uhlelo lokuthenga ibhizinisi limthathe iminyaka emibili ngenxa yemicikilisho elandelwayo uma uthenga igalaji.
"Kunemicikiliso eminingi ngaphezu kwalokho kudingeka ukuthi okungenani ubenoR1 million okuyimali okungelula ukuthi ubenayo uma ungenawo amanye amabhizinisi.
Amabhange amadolonzima ukukuboleka imali ngoba uthathwa njengomuntu oyingozi ngenxa yokuthi awunawo umlando webhizinisi.
Ngasifaka isicelo sokuthenga ngikwazi konke lokho.
Bengigabe ngokuthi umkhakha kaphethroli ngiwazi njengoba ngizazi, bengisesikhundleni esiphezulu kwa-Engen.
"Ushiye kule nkampani ngeledlule eyiHealth Safety Environment Quality Business Partner Manager (HSEQ), ebhekele iNingizimu Afrika nezinye izingxenye ze-Afrika.
Uthe ngesikhathi ekhula eMooi River, babengabaningi abantu ayebukela kubo abenza imisebenzi ehlukile, umkhakha weChemical Engineering wawukhetha ngoba azi ukuthi ngowabantu abahlakaniphile futhi uhola imali eningi uma usuwenza.
"Ngangifundela ukuthi ngiqashwe, ngihole imali eningi.
Ngangingacabangi ukuthi ngizogcina ngiwusomabhizinisi."
Uthe uthando lokungena ebhizinisini ube nalo ngesikhathi enza izifundo zeMasters of Business Administration (MBA) e-UKZN ngo-2017, ayiphothule ngo-2019.
"Ngenza ucwaningo olwalubheka ushintsho emkhakheni kaphethroli nabanikazi bamagalaji kaphethroli.
Kulapho ngabona khona ukuthi empeleni abantu bezifazane bayingcosana.
Ngaba nevuso lokuthi nami ngingene kuwo ngibe yingxenye yokuwushintsha.
Ngiwumuntu ongahlehli esinqumeni uma esesithathile.
Uma unginike umsebenzi ngisebenza ngokuphindiwe.
"Uma ngiphelelwa amandla, ngibheka ukuthi bangaki abantu abakhulele emakhaya njengami ababukela kimi.
Ngizibuze ukuthi bangaki abathola umfutho ngokubona izinto engizenzayo, bese ngizibamba ziqine ngiqhubeke noma kunzima," kusho yena.
Le ntokazi inendawo edayisa ukudla kwesintu iThandi's Kitchen, eMbilo eyivule nyakenye.
Ubhale ibhuku ngomlando wamaqhawe
Mbali KhanyileOWESIFAZANE waseThekwini obhale izincwadi ezikhuluma ngomlando wezingqalabutho okuqanjwe ngazo imigwaqo emisha kuleli dolobha, uthi uhlose ukufundisa abantu ngomlando wala maqhawe omzabalazo.
UNksz Khethiwe Zulu (40), obhale izincwadi ezimbili ezisihloko sithi, A Beginners Guide to the History Behind Street Names nethi A Beginners Guide to the Women in the Liberation Struggle, uthe ukholwa wukuthi izincwadi zakhe zizolekelela kakhulu ekuvuleni imiqondo yabantu abasenokudideka ngomlando wokuqanjwe ngabo imigwaqo.
"Ngalezi zincwadi ngifisa abantu baqonde umlando wabantu esasididekile ngabo sonke ukuthi kungani kuqanjwe imigwaqo ngamagama abo.
Ngiyethemba ukuthi kuzosisiza kakhulu ukwazi ngabo ukuze sizigqaje ngemisebenzi emihle abayenza besaphila," kuchaza uNksz Zulu.
Echaza ngemininingwane ayisebenzise ebhala izincwadi zakhe, uthe ukuhlanganisa ulwazi abeludinga kwamthatha isikhathi njengoba ayebuye athathe ikhefu ngenxa yezinto ezazimphula umoya ayezithola ngesikhathi efunda ngomlando wabantu ababehlukunyezwa ngesikhathi sobandululo.
Uthe ngesikhathi esazihlanganisa izincwadi, wabe eseqhamuka neqhinga lomdlalo ongadlalwa ngabantu ohambisana nazo nofundisa ngomlando.
Lo mdlalo uthe unoqwembe, idayisi nezinkinobho okudlalwa ngazo uma sekugingqwe idayisi.
Uthe kunemibuzo okumele uqale uyiphendule yomlando waseNingizimu Afrika ngaphambi kokuthi uqale ukuwudlala.
"Lo mdlalo ngihlose ukufundisa ngawo abasashoda ngolwazi lo mlando wezigagayi zomzabalazo.
Nezingane zesikole zizozuza kakhulu kuwona," kuqhuba lo mbhali othe uthando lokubhala waba nalo eseneminyaka engu-13.
Phakathi kwezingqinamba abhekane nazo, ubale ukungatholakali kalula kosizo lwabaxhasi.
Uphinde waveza ukuthi umsebenzi wokubhala unakho ukwenza umuntu abe yinkomo edla yodwa isikhathi esiningi ngoba udinga ukuthi umuntu abe yedwa ukuze akwazi ukubhekana nomsebenzi asuke ewenza ngaphandle kokuphazamiseka.
Uthe yize lokho kusiza ekutheni umuntu abalekele ukwenza amaphutha amaningi, umzwangedwa uyabulalana uma ungumbhali.
Ephetha uthe yize kunezingqinamba ezimhaqayo, uyakujabulela ukuba nabasebenzi abane enkampanini yakhe, iCreative Boss, epakisha izincwadi ezithengiwe.
Wakhuthazwa uyise osenepulazi likamoba
UKUSEBENZA noyise kwezolimo kuholele ekutheni naye agcine esengumlimi ovelele otshala umoba.
UNkk Nonhlanhla Gumede-Shabalala ongumnikazi wepulazi likamoba iThandimvelo eliseMtubatuba, oneminyaka eyisishiyagalolunye elima, uthe uyise wathenga ipulazi ngesikhathi efunda u-matric.
Wayesebenza naye emsiza wagcina esenothando lwezolimo.
"Ubaba sekuphele iminyaka engaphezulu kuka-40 engumlimi.
Ngesikhathi ngifunda u-matric wathenga umhlaba ongamahektha angu-90.
Kulapho nami ngaqala khona ukumsiza," kusho yena.
Uthe ngemva kokuphothula u-matric wafundela umkhakha wamabhange wasebenza washiya kuwo ngo-2010 wabuya wazosebenza noyise.
Ngo-2017 uthe wathenga ipulazi elingamahektha angu-170.
Indawo akwazi ukuyilima epulazini ingamahektha angu-112, enye ingxenye iyihlathi.
Umoba otshalwa epulazini uthe uwudayisela abakwaTongaat Hullet.
Ngaphandle komoba ubuye atshale nemifino ayidayisele izitolo aphinde aphakele nezikole ngemikhiqizo yezolimo kanti ufuye neziklabhu.
"Umoba kuthatha izinyanga eziyisishiyagalolunye ngaphambi kokuthi uvunwe.
Ngaleso sikhathi ngisuke ngimatasa neminye iminxa yebhizinisi lezolimo okungukutshala imifino nokufuya iziklabhu.
Angibi naso isikhathi sokuhlala ngilinde ukuthi umoba uvunwe," kusho yena.
Uthe epulazini iThandimvelo uqashe abasebenzi abangu-10 ngokugcwele kanti ngesikhathi sokuvuna uqasha abanye abasebenzi betoho.
"Ngilifunde ngokushesha ibhizinisi lezolimo.
Kwakuphoqa ukuthi ngibe nesu elicacile lokuthi ngizoyenza kanjani imali ngoba phela ibhange beliyifuna imali yalo.
Bekumele ngenze isiqiniseko sokuthi ngiyayikhokhela i-bond njalo.
Kube kusadingeka ngikhokhele omanyolo nabasebenzi.
Ngike ngaba nezingqinamba zokukhokhela abasebenzi kwadingeka ngifunde ngokushesha ngoba bengingafuni ukulahlekelwa wumhlaba ebese ngiwuthengile," kusho yena.
Ngo-2019/2020 abakwaTongaat Hullet's bathatha isinqumo sokuthi bangabe besazilimela umoba kodwa bathenge umoba kubalimi abasathuthuka okwaholela ekutheni uNkk Gumede-Shabala nabanye basungule uZinzo Sugar Farming.
Abangamalungu oZinzo bakwazi ukuthola umhlaba ongamahektha angu-3 900 abawuqashile abalima kuwo umoba.
Ngesikhathi sokuvuna bakhiqiza amathani angu-160 000 kamoba abawudayisela abakwaTongaat Hullet's.
"UZinzo lwenze ukuthi ngikhule ebhizinisini lezolimi futhi ngifunde kozakwethu esisungule nabo le nkampani.
Ngiyilungu lebhodi lale nkampani nomnikazi wamasheya kanjalo nomsebenzi ngakho bekumele ngifunde ngokushesha ukuze ngazi ngemithetho elawula izinkampani ezinjengalezi.
Ngifunde nokuthi uma kunemihlangano nami kumele ngibeke umbono ophusile okhombisa ukuthi ngiyazi ukuthi ngikhuluma ngani.
Ngafunda nokuthi uma ungumholi yini okumele uyenze," kusho yena.
Uthe bekufanele akufunde ngokushesha lokhu ngoba umsebenzi wakhe wukuthi aqhamuke namasu amasha ebhizinisi.
Asize nasekusebenzeni kwebhizinisi okuhlanganisa umsebenzi wasehhovisi.
"Uma ungumuntu wesifazane akhona amathuba kwezolimo.
Kukhona noxhaso lukahulumeni olusiza abesifazane.
Ebhizinisini kumele wazi ukuthi kungenzeka uwine noma ulahlekelwe," kusho yena.
Iqeqesha nezifundiswa inhlangano yomame
EMUVA kweminyaka emibili kwasungulwa inhlangano ehlanganisa omama nezinhlaka ezehlukene zomphakathi eMsinga, sekwakheke inqwaba yamathuba emsebenzi.
IBuhle Zondo Foundation, eyasungulwa ngo-2018 nguDkt Buhle Zondo, ngenhloso yokusiza omama ebabentula amathuba emsebenzi, seyiqashe abantu abangaphezulu kuka-150, okubalwa omama abatshalayo, abafelokazi, intsha namalungu omphakathi angasebenzi.
IBuhle Zondo Foundation ibhekele ukufuywa kwezinkukhu, kubunjwe izitini zokwakha, kukhiqizwe amaqanda, kutshalwe imifino nezithelo ezahlukene kuye kudayiswe imikhiqizo eyahlukene.
USihlalo wayo, uNkk Victoria Ngobese, uthi kwakubangwa imsebenzi yokupheka kwesinye sezikole nakhona kudingeka abesifazane ababili, kwaze kwabhikishwa, kwaze kwangenelela uDkt Zondo.
UNkk  Ngobese, oseneminyaka eyibambile futhi eqinisekisa ukuthi abesifazane babamba iqhaza kakhulu emisebenzini eyenziwayo, uthe kuyamangaza ukuthi umbono womuntu osemncane ukwazi ukukhulisa abesifazane namadoda emizi.
Uveze ukuthi kunabantu abavuse amakhaya, bakha imizi ngemali abayithola ngokudayiswa kwemikhiqizo yabo.
"Abafelokazi kabaseyona inhlekisa emphakathini.
Bayakwazi ukubhekana nemizi nokukhulisa izingane.
Inqwaba yabantu abangasebenzi seyiyavuka ngosizo lomuntu omncane obe nengqondo enkulu kuneyethu sibadala.
Akekho umuntu ongasizakali ngoba noma sekuyisikhathi sesivuno kuyaqashwa abantu abazosiza," kusho uNkk Ngobese.
Le nhlangabo kayigcini nje ngokusiza izakhamizi kodwa ibuye ibhekele nentsha ephuma ezikoleni efisa ukuzithuthukisa ngolwazi emkhakheni wezolimo.
UNksz Zuzile Zondi, waseMsinga obenza iFarming Management eMajuba TVET eDundee, uthe ungomunye wabantu abacotshelelwa ngolwazi kwiBuhle Zondo Foundation.
Uthe yize esabala izinyanga ekule nhlangano kodwa kuningi asekuzuzile.
Izinto azogxila kuzo kule nhlangano wukufunda indlela okubhekelwa ngayo izimali, izindaba zabasebenzi kanjalo nezitshalo.
"Sengithole ulwazi oluningi, ngifunda nendlela okubhekelwa ngayo izitshalo, zikhuliswa kuze kube ziyavunwa.
Kuyangijabulisa kakhulu ukuthola inhlangano engasekhaya enolwazi engiludingayo ukuze ngikwazi ukusungula eyami inhlangano ngelinye ilanga," kusho uNksz Zondi.
Inhlangano njengamanje imatasa nesivuno njengoba kade ikhipha amakinati nobhontshisi.
Manje ilungisela nokuvuna umbila.
Uyazihlupha ngokunakekela ezikhubazekile
UKUTHATHA njengobizo ukunakekela izingane ezikhubazekile owesifazane obenguthisha esikoleni sazo ophinde abe nendodakazi ethatha kancane ngokomqondo.
UNkk Nozipho Thwala (46) waseMlaza, ungumbhali wencwadi ethi Lezi Izimpawu Ezidala Ukuhleleka Komntwana Esikoleni ayikhiphe ngonyaka odlule.
Wayengazi ukuthi ukutshalwa kwakhe esikoleni sabanokukhubazeka kuzomsiza ayiqonde kangcono indodakazi yakhe.
Yize indodakazi yakhe ineminyaka engu-11, uthe ngokomqondo wayo ilingana nengane eneminyaka elishumi.
UNkk Thwala, ofundise esikoleni sabanokukhubazeka eMontclair eThekwini iminyaka eyishumi, usaqhubeka nokufundela ukunakekela lezi zingane.
Uthe kuyamkhathaza ukuthi abazali abafundisekile ngalezi zingane.
Uthe abaningi bacabanga ukuthi ziphazamisekile emqondweni kanti zithatha kancane kuphela.
Ngesikhathi eshiya umsebenzi wokufundisa ngo-2016 bese ezitshelile ukuthi ufuna ukuqala amalungiselelo okusungula isikole sakhe esizogxila ekuqhakambiseni amakhono ezinganeni ezinokukhubazeka.
Kumanje usewathumele amaphepha okufaka isicelo soxhaso lokwakha lesi sikhungo aseyitholile nendawo yaso.
"Kunabazali abanezingane ezithatha kancane ngokomqondo kodwa abangafuni ukwamukela.
Baphaphama ingane isineminyaka engu-17 ngoba ilokhu ingaphasi.
Kule ncwadi ngifundisa ngezimpawu eziyinkomba yokuthi ingane idinga usizo.
Abantu kumele bazi ukuthi akusona isiqalekiso ukuba nengane ethatha kancane emqondweni.
Abanye bavele bacabange ukuthi bathakathiwe, kuphele imali behamba izinyanga kanti inkinga isemqondweni wengane," kuchaza uNkk Thwala.
Uthe kwamsiza naye ukuthi amukele ukuthi ingane yakhe ihlukile.
Yize ithatha kancane esikoleni kodwa uthe inekhono eliyisimanga lokupheka nokucwala izinzipho.
Uveza ukuthi ngokujwayelekile izingane ezinale nkinga ziba nesinye isiphiwo esihambisana nethalente.
Abazali kumele babheke leso siphiwo bese besiza ingane ukuze sigqame.
Ulinganise ngoMnuz Richard Branson ongusomabhizinisi ohlonishwayo emhlabeni, athe wayenenkinga yokubhala, ephambanisa amagama esikoleni.
Uthe lokhu akusho ukuthi ubephazamiseke emqondweni njengoba esengusomabhizinisi ohlonishwayo.
"Okubalulekile wukuthi abazali bagade izimpawu enganeni isencane.
Kuyenzeka ifeyile esikoleni ngoba umqondo uthatha kancane kodwa hhayi ngoba inokukhubazeka.
Kuyasiza ukuthi isukunyelwe ingane ukuze ithole abazoyihlola ukuthi umqondo wayo ukuliphi izinga bayifundise ngokwezinga layo," kusho yena.
UNkk Thwala uqeqeshwe emkhakheni we-Autistic and Dyslexic kodwa wafundela ubuthisha eShowe College of Education.
Uneziqu zeHonours kwiBachelor of Education in Exclusive Education ayithola e-Unisa.
Manje wenza iMasters.
Uke wafundisa eMlazi Com-Tech ngaphambi kokufundisa eSpecial School.
Kwakunzima babekezela manje sebevelele emikhakheni ehlukene
IZIMO ezinzima ababhekana nazo empilweni abazange bazivumele ziphazamise amaphupho abo okuphumelela abesifazane abasemabhizinisini, abenza ezibukwayo kwezemidlalo nakweminye imikhakha abebekhuluma emcimbini weForbes Leading Women ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi: The Spotlight.
UNksz Kgothatso "KG" Montjane, wakuleli ukleliswe kubantu abangu-10 ezweni lonke abenza ezibukwayo kwi-wheelchair tennis.
Waba owokuqala owesifazane omnyama ukuqhudelana nabanye abadlali eWimbledon.
Uthe ukuze afike lapha kwakungelula neze njengoba wayengowesifazane okhulele emakhaya, okhubazekile futhi engazi nokuthi i-tennis idlalwa kanjani.
"Uma owesifazane wasemakhaya ethole umntwana okhubazekile uye amfihle ngoba kuba sengathi ihlazo futhi umntwana wakho engeke abe yilutho ezweni.
Abazali bami benza okuhlukile, bangiyisa esikoleni bazama ukuthi ngibe nempilo.
Kwakungelula nhlobo ezinye izingane zingafuni ukudlala nami ngoba nginokukhubazeka emlenzeni.
Ngelinye ilanga uthisha wami wathi ngizomela isikole emdlalweni we-wheelchair tennis, ngangingazi nokuthi yini leyo ngoba ngangazi umdlalo webhola kuphela.
Ngaya okokuqala ngaqokwa ukuba ngimele elakuleli, kumanje ngiqopha umlando,ngiyaqhubeka ngiyazimisela.
Umdlalo onzima nobizayo lona njengoba kusagcwele abamhlophe bodwa, yize kunjalo ngiyaphumelela kuwo.
Ungalilahli ithemba ngempilo," kusho uNksz Montjane.
UNksz Linda Ikeji usomabhizinisi waseNigeria yena wake waboshwa ngoba ehluleka ukukhokha imali ayeyiboleke ebhange ngoba eqala ibhizinisi lakhe lephephabhuku.
Uthe ukulandwa amadoda ayehlome eyizingovolo kubo ezofuna imali yakhe kwameza wavuka emaqandeni.
"Kumanje nginenhlangano esiza abesifazane abancane abaqala amabhizisini kodwa bengenayo imali.
Kunamantombazane angu-30 engiwaphe imali ukuze aphembe amabhizinisi abo, ngenxa yokubona ukuthi ngaxakeka kakhulu ngiqala.
Ngazithembisa ukuthi akekho omunye owesifazane omncane okumele asokole njengami ngisaqala ibhizinisi.
Engingakusho ukuthi uma unephupho lilelwe lelo phupho, ungayeki, ungapheli amandla.
Yebo kunzima ukulandela iphupho kodwa akukho okungeke kwenzeke uma uzimisele.
Imali engangiboshelwe yona ngihluleka ukuyikhokha manje sengithenga ngayo izicathulo," kusho uNksz Ikeji ehleka egcwele izinyembezi emehlweni.
UNksz Simidele Adeagbo ongumdlali (Olympian) waseNigeria owaqopha umlando ngokuba owesifazane wase-Afrika nomnyama ukumela izwe lakhe emdlalweni wamaSport Skeleton, lapho usuke ushushuluza khona eqhweni elibandayo, uqhudelana nabanye.
Uthe akuzange kube lula kodwa ukubekezela nokuzimesela ngayefuna ukukufeza ikhona okwenza waphumelela.
"Kukhona isikhathi lapho ngingazange ngiqokwe ukuba ngiyomela izwe lami, kwaqoka umngani wami.
Ngangibona umngani wami ephila impilo yami, amaphupho enganginawo, uyena owayewaphila.
Ngizikhumbula ngikhala ngizibuza ukuthi kungani mina ngingakwazi ukwenza ayekwenza, ngafikelwa umcabango wokuthi isikhathi sami siyeza.
Ngasebenza kanzima nami ngagcina ngiqokiwe, amaphupho ami afezeka.
Kudinga ukuba ubekezele noma kunzima uphikelele kulokho osuke ufuna ukukufeza, ungavinjwa yilutho.
Noma abanye bekudlula endleleni wena phikelela ekuqedeni ibanga lakho," kusho uNksz Adeagbo.
Laba besifazane bebeze bekhale izinyembezi uma bekhuluma ngobunzima abadlule kubo ukuze baphumelele.
Ngazwi linye bonke bathe, ekugcineni awuzisoli ngokuphikelela ekufezeni amaphupho akho noma kunjani, noma kuthiwani.
Washiya ubuthisha wangena ematekisini
UKE wawulaxaza phansi umsebenzi wamatekisi owesifazane wokuqala ukuba ngunobhala kusoseshini waseNanda.
UNkk Sibusisiwe Thabede ongene embonini yamatekisi ngo-2005 ngemuva kokushona komyeni wakhe uthe ubunzima balo msebenzi bamenza washiya phansi.
Uthe ngesikhathi engena kuwo ngemuva kokushona komyeni wayengazi lutho ngetekisi, wayegxile emsebenzini wakhe wobuthisha engazikhathazi ngokuthi kwenzekani ematekisi.
Umyeni wakhe washiya amatekisi ayisithupha.
Ngesikhathi sekungene yena uthe imali yayingena kancane ngoba abashayeli babemkhohlisa ngenzinto eziningi ababazi ukuthi akazazi.
"Ngesinye isikhathi umshayeli wayebuya nemali engaphelele athi uthenge insimbi ethile yokukhanda imoto, ngamukele lokho ngoba ngingazi ukuthi leyo nsimbi ibiza malini.
"Kwesinye isikhathi nami ngangenza izinqumo ezithile ezaziholela ekutheni amatekisi angasebenzi ngendlela ayesebenza ngayo kusekhona umyeni wami.
"Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ngagcina sengibonile ukuthi kulo mkhakha ibhizinisi lenziwa kanjani.
"Ngafunda ukuthetha into engingayazi nokugada ukuthi abashayeli basebenza kanjani," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi uthe esejwayele kwaba nezinkinga kusoseshini.
Uthe wehluleka ukubhekana nazo wakhetha ukuwadayisa amatekisi ngo-2013, wabuyela emsebenzini wakhe wokuba uthisha ngo-2014.
"Ngashiya amatekisi amabili kuphela ayengisiza ukuthi ngikwazi ukondla izingane, ngangingasenalo uthando lwaleli bhizinisi.
Ngizibona sengathi ngisemkhakheni onezinselelo engingakwazi ukuzimela," kusho yena.
Wafundisa imiyaka emibili ngo-2016 wabuyela ematekisini.
Uthe ngesikhathi ebuya wayesecabanga ukuthi usezothatha umhlalaphansi engafuni ukuhlala ekhaya.
"Ngacabanga amabhizinisi amaningi ngagcina ngifikelwe ukuthi kungani ngingabuyeli ematekisini ngoba senginalo ulwazi.
Okunye okwakungikhuthaza ukuthi abanye abanikazi bamatekisi babengitshela ukuthi amatekisi awafani nobuthisha okuthi uma eseshonile kube kuphelile, akekho omunye ongasebenzisa iziqu zakhe.
Ematekisini isitifiketi siyadluliseleka esizukulwaneni," kusho yena.
Ngenhlanhla uthi ubuyele sekunoshintsho oluningi ematekisini.
Uthe bese kunezinhlelo eziningi zokuqeqeshwa kosomatekisi kanye nabashayeli ngaleli bhizinisi.
Uthe ukhethwe ukuthi abe ngunobhala walo soseshini nyakenye.
Ngawo futhi lo nyaka uthe uqokwe ukuthi abe ngunobhala weSantaco, emkhandlwini wamatekisi aseNyankatho yeTheku iGreater North Region.
"Ukuba unobhala isikhundla esibalulekile kusoseshini, uwomgogodla.
Uhlale uyingxenye yezinqumo ezithathwa yisigungu esiphezulu salowo soseshini.
Njengamanje kowethu usoseshini sathatha isinquno sokuthi sikhokhe imali ethile ngenyanga yamathayi.
Uma imoto idinga ithayi kuyiwa ehhovisi lifakwe lokho kwenza ukuthi kusetshenziswe amathayi aphephile kudaleke namathuba emisebenzi eyengeziwe.
Uma kunemiyalezo okumele ikhishwe usoseshini unobhala nguye okumele ayibhale.
Kuyo yonke imihlangano ebalulekile kumele abe khona," kusho yena.
Njengoba ekwiSANTACO uthe akagcini ngokubhalana nososeshini wakhe kodwa uba yingxenye yokuthathwa kwezinqumo ngamatekisi ahambela enyakatho eyeTheku.
Uthe osomatekisi besifazane bakhona kodwa bayidlanzana abakwazi ukufinyelela esigabeni akusona.
"Ziningi izizathu zalokhu abanye basemanqikanqika ukungena bathi shi ngenxa yokuthi le mboni inamadoda amaningi.
Kwesinye isikhathi nawo amadoda asangabaza ukufaka abesifazane ezikhundleni ngoba ebona sengathi ngeke bakwazi ukumelana nomsebenzi onzima," kusho yena.
Uthando lokujimisa luphenduke ibhizinisi
UTHANDO lokujimisa abantu lumphoqile ukuthi ashiye umsebenzi abeqashelwe wona ngokugcwele, avule elakhe ibhizinisi ngokusho kukaLethu Thusi (24).
Uthe ukujimisa abantu yinto akhule eyenza kodwa enganakile ukuthi ngelinye ilanga uzogcina esephila ngayo.
Uqale ukukhokhelwa ngawo ngesikhathi esefunda eNyuvesi yaKwaZulu-Natal (KZN).
"Ngiqale ngokujimisa abafundi e-UKZN, kodwa bangiqeda umdlandla ngenxa yokuthi bebephinde badle ukudla okuzobenza bakhuluphale.
"Ngiphoqelekile ukuthi ngishintshele kubantu abasebenzayo.
Ngibajimisela ezindaweni zabo, bangikhokhele.
Ngo-2018 ngiqale ngaba nekhasimende elilodwa ebelingikhokhela kahle ngokulijimisa.
"Lokho kungigqugquzele ukuthi ngibe namaningi kodwa ngingazi ukuthi ngizokwenza kanjani, ukuze ngiwathola.
"Ngigcine sengizimaketha ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, ngawathola amakhasimende."
Ngo-2019 ngiqashwe kwesinye seziqiwi eHowick, okwenze kwaba nzima ukuthi ngiqhubeke nalo msebenzi ngenxa yokuthi bengibuye ngibe matasa nomsebenzi engiwuqashelwe," kuchaza uLethu.
Ngenxa yaleso sizathu uthe uphoqelekile ukuthi aqale amakilasi awenza ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ejimisa abantu.
"Umuntu oyikhasimende lami ngiyambhalela ukuthi kumele enze kanjani ngiphinde ngimtshele nokudla okumele akudle, ukuze kubonakale imiphumela.
Abaningi bayabuya babonge ukuthi iyasebenza le ndlela engibaqeqesha ngayo ngoba nami ngiyalandelela, ukuthi benza okufanele.
Ngigcine sengithola namakhasimende akwamanye amazwe njengeBotswana, Namibia namanye.
Ngenxa yobuningi bamakhasimende ami, ngigcine sengiphoqeleka ukuthi ngiyeke umsebenzi ngigxile kuwo ngoba kumele ngiwanike isikhathi esanele sokuthi ngixhumane nawo ngoba ayangikhokhela," kusho uLethu.
Uthe manje usenza lo msebenzi ngokugcwele futhi amakhasimende akhe usezowathumelela nezinto zokujima ezinegama lenkampani yakhe, iFlexers Fitness.
Kosaziwayo uthe useke wajimisa noDJ Lesoul.

ENYE yezintandokazi yezimoto zakwaVolkswagen iTiguan izoshintsha indlela ebukeka ngayo uma isitheleka eNingizimu Afrika ngasekupheleni konyaka.
Ingaphambili lizobe lishintshile njengoba inobhampa omusha futhi izobe inamaLED headlights kuzona zonke izinhlobo.
Izofika inezinhlobo ezintathu okuyiTiguan, Tiguan Life neTiguan R-Line.
Izinto enazo kodwa kuya ngenhlobo yakho, kubalwa amarimu aphakathi kuka-17 inch no-19 inch (20 uma uthanda), park distance control, Harmon Kardon sound system, adaptive cruise control, lane assist nokunye okuningi.

4TSI enamandla angu-110kW netorque engu-250Nm.
Inogearbox oyi-6 speed DSG.
Eyesibili ngekadizili i-2.
0TDI efuqa 130kW no-380Nm kanti isebenzisa i-7 speed DSG.
Eyokugcina yi-2.0 TSI ekhahlela 162kW no-350Nm.
Nayo isebenzisa ugearbox oyi-7 speed DSG.
Sizokubikela ukusuka nokuhlala ngayo uma isitheleka.
Ucwaningo luveze ezimnandi ngokuvalwa kukagwayi
UKUMISWA kokudayiswa kukagwayi kwehlise isibalo seziguli eziphuthunyiswa ezibhedlela zidinga usizo oluphuthumayo lokwelashelwa izifo zamaphaphu ngo-63%.
Lolu cwaningo lwenziwe uMnyango wezeMpilo eWestern Cape nophiko olubhekele izimo eziphuthumayo nemindeni esibhedlela iGeorge Regional, ngokuqhathanisa isibalo seziguli ezivakashele kulesi sibhedlela zidinga usizo ngo-2019 nango-2020 ngesikhathi kuvaliwe ukudayiswa kukagwayi kuleli.
Omunye wabacwaningi, uNkk Piero Saieva, uthe lolu cwaningo lwenziwe kucutshungulwa imininingwano yeziguli ezivamise ukungena esibhedlela iGeorge Regional zidinga usizo oluphuthumayo lokwelashelwa isifo samaphaphu, i-Emergency Centre attendance for Chronic Obstructive Pulmonary Disease (COPD) phakathi kuka Januwari 2019 kuya ku-Agasti 2020.
Imiphumela yalolu cwaningo ishicilelwe emqingweni wezempilo i-African Journal of Primary Health Care & Family Medicine.
Abacwaningi bebeqhathanisa amakhadi eziguli agcinwe kumakhompyutha, ama- eletronic card, bebheka ukuthi ukuvakashela kweziguli ezibhedlela kuyefana yini.
I-COPD isifo samaphaphu esenza ukuthi umuntu akhwehlele ngendlela engelawuleki.
Uma ubhema ukukhwehlela kuvuka ngamandla ukhwehlele kuze kunciphe umoya ungakwazi ukuphefumula kahle, kudingeke ukuthi uphuthunyiswe esikhungweni sezempilo.
Ngesikhathi kuvalwe ukudayiswa kukagwayi kuleli, abanye abantu bebengawutholi ugwayi okuholele ekutheni kunciphe ukuvakashela kwabo kulesi sibhedlela ngenxa yale nkinga.
INyuvesi yaseCape Town nayo yenze olwayo ucwaningo olusondelene nalolu, yona yathola ukuthi ngesikhathi kuvaliwe ukudayiswa kukagwayi kuleli, ababhemayo bebewuthola ugwayi kodwa ubudayisa ngemali enkulu.
Ngokwalolu cwaningo bekwenzeka ukuthi ibhokisi elinogwayi ongu-20 ebelidayiswa ngemali ephakathi kukaR25 kuya kuR45 ligcine selidayiswa ngoR144.
Ugwayi ngamunye ubudayiswa ngoR5.
69c obekuholela ekutheni abanye babantu ababhemayo behlise ukubhema ngoba imali yokuwuthenga bebengenayo.
Lolu cwaningo lwenziwe kubantu abangu-12 118, u-42% wabo uzame ukuyeka ukubhema ngenxa yokubiza kukagwayi ngalesi sikhathi.
U-39%, uphumelele ukuwuyeka.
UDkt Sharon Nyatsanza weNational weCouncil Against Smoking, uthe lolu cwaningo luveza ngokusobala ukuthi kubalulekile ukulawulwa kokubhenywa kukagwayi ukuze abantu babe nempilo enhle.
Mancane amathuba okuba namahlule kwabagome ngeJ&J
"Ukugoma esigabeni sokuqala kulindeleke ukuthi kuphele ngoMeyi 16.
Sizimisele ukugoma abasebenzi abasele ngobuningi babo, yize kuke kwaba khona ukuphazamiseka.
Sinxusa abasebenzi bezempilo nabelaphi bendabuko abangakabhaliseli ukugoma ukuthi babhalise kwi-website yoMnyango wezeMpilo," kusho uDkt Mkhize.
Ukugoma ngalo ngomo kwamiswa kuleli ngemuva kokuthi kutholakale abesifazane abayisithupha e-United States benesifo esingajwayekile, sokuba namahlule egazini okusolwa umgomo, okubizwa ngeVaccine Induced Thrombotic Thrombocytopenia (VITT).
Manje sebeyisishiyagalombili abesifazane abajove ngawo base beba neVITT.
"Ngesikhathi kumiswa ukugoma ngalo mgomo kwakusanikezwa ososayensi ithuba lokuthi bacwaninge bese bekhipha isinqumo sokuthi lo mgomo ungasetshenziswa kanjani.
Ucwaningo luveze ukuthi amathuba okuthi umuntu abe nalesi sifo ngoyedwa kwabayisigidi.
Abesifazane okungenzeka bangenwe yilesi sifo ngabaneminyaka ephakathi kuka-18 kuya ku-48.
Nakhona kuthiwa amathuba okuthi igazi libe namahlule mancane.
Ososayensi emhlabeni benze isiphakamiso sokuthi kuqhutshekwe nokugoma ngalo mgomo," kusho uDkt Mkhize.
Uthe kuleli uphiko olwenza ucwaningo ngemithi, iSouth African Medical Research Council (SAMRC), wuMnyango wezeMpilo neSahpra nezinye izikhungo zezempilo bazobe bewuqaphile umgomo .
"Bonke ababhalisele ukugoma ngalo mgomo bazonikezwa ifomu eshoyo ukuthi yibuphi ubungozi balo mgomo.
Bazoyisayina ngaphambi kokuthi bagome," kusho uMkhize.
Balinganiselwa ku-8 million ababulewe yiCovid-19 emhlabeni
PHILI MJOLISIPHINDAPHINDEKE kathathu isibalo sabantu ababulewe yiCovid-19 emhlabeni kunaleso esisaziyo.
Lokhu kuvezwe yinhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO) esithangamini nabezindaba sakamuva.
Izibalo ezikhona njengamanje zithi bangu-3.
4 million abantu ababulewe yileli gciwane emhlabeni selokhu sabheduka eChina ekupheleni kuka-2019 kodwa iWHO ithi izibalo eziyizona ziphindaphindeke kathathu kulezi.
UDkt Samira Asma, osophikweni olucubungula ulwazi kwi-WHO, uthe nakuba abanye abantu bengabulawanga yiCovid-19 ngqo kodwa bebengeke bashone ukube belungekho ubhubhane oluholele ekutheni bangakutholi ukwelashelwa isifo abanaso base beyashona.
"Izibalo zabashone ngenxa yaleli gciwane luphindaphindeke kabili noma kathathu kunokubikwe ngokusemthethweni," kusho uDkt Asma.
Uthe ngokombiko owenziwe yile nhlangano ngo-2020, kuvela ukuthi okungenani bangaphezulu kuka-3 million abanye abantu abashonile ukufa kwabo okweyamaniswa neCovid-19 ngqo.
Ngaleso sikhathi izibalo ezisemthethweni zababulewe yigciwane uthe zazikhomba ukuthi bangu- 1.
8 million abashonile.
Ebuzwa ukuthi ngabe izibalo zababulewe wubhubhane uma ehlanganisa nalabo bantu manje zithini, uphendule ngokuthi: "Ngicabanga ukuthi kuphephile ukuthi ngithi isilinganiso esiyiso kungaba ngabantu abaphakathi kuka-6 kuya ku-8 million.
"Uthe iWHO ibisebenzisana namazwe ukuze iqonde izibalo zangempela zabantu ababulewe wubhubhane.
Uthe lokhu bebekwenzela ukuthi bazihlinzekele ezinye izimo eziphuthumayo ezingavela ngesikhathi esizayoUqhube wathi:" Ukungafani kolwazi kudalwe yizinto eziningi phakathi kwazo ukusilela emuva kokushicilelwa kwababulewe yigciwane kwamanye amazwe.
Elinye iqiniso ukuthi abanye abantu abazange bahlolwe ukuthi babulewe yigciwane noma cha, abanye baze bashona bengazange belashelwe lona ngoba abazange bakwazi nokufinyelela ezikhungweni zezempilo ukuze bahlolwe ngenxa yemigomo yomvalelandlini ebikhona.
Abanye babulewe ezinye izifo ngenxa yokuthi abakwazanga ukuthola ukwelashwa ngoba kubhekenwe nobhubhane."
Ezothando: Ngakhipha isisu umyeni wami akasanginiki ukuphumula
UMBUZO: Nginenkinga kababa wabantwana bami engithandane naye kusuka ngo-2015 ongafuni ukondla izingane zakhe.
Uma ngimqonda ngesenzo sakhe ungitshele ukuthi mina angimthandi.
Usengumuntu osephuza kakhulu nosethanda amantombazane okuyinto engikhathazayo ngoba ngisamthanda.
Ngicela usizo.Hlengiwe, KwaDukuzaImpendulo:Yibhekisise kahle le nto ayishoyo yokuthi awumthandi.
Kusobala ukuthi zikhona izimpawu azibonayo kuwe ezingakhombisi uthando.
Bunjani ubudlelwano benu?Yicabangisise kahle le nto ukuze uzitholele izimpendulo ozidingayo.
Kwesinye isikhathi izenzo zethu zikhuluma ukudlula amazwi ethu.
Nalokuphuza kwakhe nokuthanda amantombazane kuyindlela akhala ngayo noma indlela azama ukukhohlwa ngayo ngokwenzekayo phakathi kwenu.
Uma ngabe ungakazitholi izimpendulo ozidingayo namanje akukho okudlula ukuthi umhlalise phansi ubaba wabantwana bakho ukuthola ukuthi yini ngempela emenza acabange ukuthi awumthandi.
Umbuzo:Sineminyaka emibili sishadile nomyeni wami.
Emva kwezinyangana sishadile ngathola ukuthi ngikhulelwe ngasikhipha isisu engazi ngoba ngangingazimisele ukuphinda ngibe nomunye umntwana ngenxa yokuthi sobabili sifike nabantwana kulo mshado.
Angikaze ngikuthole ukuphumula seloku athola ukuthi ngenzani.
Ungikhumbuza njalo ngisho nokuthi ngabe isingakanani ingane ukube angiyikhiphanga.
Ukhala ngokuthi ngamncisha ithuba lokuba ubaba.
Ngenzenjani ngempela ukuze akhohlwe, nomshado wethu ubuyele esimeni?Igama ligodliwe, eMorningsideImpendulo:Isinqumo sokuba nabantwana nokungabi nabantwana akusona osithatha uwedwa emshadweni.
Kwakumele umazise kwasekuqaleni umyeni wakho ukuthi awuzimisele ukuba nabantwana.
Kube yinto enivumelana ngayo.
Ungamsoli kakhulu umyeni wakho ngokuhlale ekukhumbuza ngoba naye yindlela yakhe azama ukudlulisa ngayo ubuhlungu.
Okubalulekile njengamanje ukuthi uzehlise uxolise kumyeni wakho, bese nithola ukwelulekwa.
Ngaphandle kweziluleko kuzonithatha eside isikhathi ukudlula kulesi simo futhi kugcine kuwuqedile ngisho nomshado wenu.
Umbuzo:Ezinyangeni ezimbili ezedlule besinezinkinga nomama wabantwana bami wacela ukuthi ke sithathe ikhefu okwesikhashana ukuzama ukulungisa izinto phakathi kwethu.
Kodwa kunokuthi izinto zibe ngcono ngibona ziya ngokuba zimbi kakhulu.
Useqale ngisho nokuphuza into entsha kanti ngelinye ilanga ngiyobona abantwana bami ngazithela kumuntu wesilisa engangingamlindele.
Ngeke ngikwamukele ukuthi useqhubekele phambili nempilo.
Kanti kuchazani ngempela ukuthatha ikhefu uma ngabe omunye ezoqhubeka nempilo yakhe?Mnguni, eThekwiniImpendulo:Kusobala ukuthi umama wabantwana bakho useziqhubekela nempilo yakhe.
Indaba yokuthatha ikhefu kwakuyindlela yakhe ehloniphekile yokuthi hlukanani.
Ngeke ke umphoqe umuntu ukuthi abe nawe engasathandi.
Sibona kukuhle ukuthi nivumelane kusemanje ngendaba yabantwana nokuthi bazohlala kubani omunye ababone kanjani.
Kubalulekile ukuthi ube nobudlelwano obuhle nabantwana bakho ngisho ungasathandani nomama wabo.
Akumelanga baphazanyiswe okwenzeka phakathi kwenu.
Qhubeka nokuba wubaba oqotho kubona ngisho umama wabo eseziqhubekela neyakhe impilo.
Sikufisela inhlanhla.
