Kuningi okushintshiwe kwiCorolla
I-TOYOTA Corolla yimoto engadingi kwethulwa ngoba abantu abaningi bayayazi futhi isineminyaka yaqala ukusetshenziswa emhlabeni naseNingizimu Afrika.
Le moto yethulwa okokuqala ngo-1966, ingenye yezintandokazi zakuleli futhi ezinesandla ekufukuleni umnotho.
Okuyenza ibe yimoto ebalulelekile yingoba ibikhiqizwa efemini yakwaToyota eProspecton, eThekwini kwaze kwaba wunyaka odlule kodwa ukwakhiwa kweCorolla Quest, esuselwe kwiCorolla endala, khona kusaqhubeka.
IToyota yamemezela ukuthi izotshala ezinye izigidi zamarandi efemini yayo ukulungiselela ukukhiqiza imoto entsha kusukela ngonyaka ozayo.
Le Corolla yesizukulwane sika-12, ifana neCorolla hatch uma uyibuka, ikakhulukazi ngaphambili.
Uma uyibuka ngohlangothi ikhasa phansi kwazise bayehlise ngo-20mm.
Amarimu ayo makhulu angu-18 inch.
Ngemuva bayenze yabukeka kahle ngamalambu amancane nobhampa onombala omnyama.
Ngaphakathi isihlalo somshayeli usihlela ngogesi futhi ivulekile abagibeli abayisweli indawo yokuhlala.
Sikhulu isikhala ebhuthini, uyakwazi nokusandisa ngokulalisa izihlalo zangemuva.
Uyakwazi nokuyivula ungaphakathi ibhuthi.
Ngaphambili alukho uxhaxha lwamabhathini.
Kukhona itouchscreen enkulu eme yagqama okuyilapho ulawula khona umsakazo, ikuvezele indlela edla ngayo uphethroli nekhamera ngemuva uma uhlehla.
Uphinde ukwazi ukuxhuma iselula nge-apple carplay okanye i-Android Auto uma uthanda.
Okumnandi ukuthi kukhona izimbombo ezimbili zokushaja nge-USB.
Okunye enakho yi-aircon, yize kungeyona lena yokuthi oseceleni azikhethele yena awakhe amazinga okushisa nomshayeli naye akhethe athandwa nguye njengakwiCorolla hatch, amawindi kagesi, yisiteringi osisethayo ukuthi sime kanjani, isibuko sokujeqeza emuva esizidimelayo nokunye.
Injini iCorolla XR ehamba ngayo ingu-2.
0 litre ekhona nakwiRAV4 yakwabo.
Ikhipha amandla angu-125kW netorque engu-200Nm.
Isebenzisa ugearbox ozishintshayo oyiCVT.
Kunama-paddle shifters ngemuva kwesiteringi uzishintshele wena igiya uma uthanda.
Kunebhathini lokuyifaka ku-Sport , lapho usheshe uwezwe amandla uma ufaka amafutha futhi ngaleso sikhathi isuke ishintsha nokuduma ibe nomsinjwana.
Emakhoneni iyabambelela lokho okusizwa ukuthi ikhasa phansi futhi inamasondo amakhulu.
Nakwi-suspension yayo bayishintshile nokuyenza ibambelele kangcono emgwaqweni.
Uma uhamba ngayo uzizwa uphephile ngoba kuningi enakho okusiza umshayeli.
Iyakusiza ukuhlala emzileni ngokuthi izijikise yona isiteringi mbijana uma iphuma, iyakwazi ukuhamba ngejubane elilodwa izinciphise ijubane uma kukhona imoto ephambi kwayo, iyasho uma izoshayisa futhi iyasho uma kunemoto eceleni.
Inama-airbag ayisikhombisa, indawo yokufaka isihlalo sengane ne-ABS, EBD, BAS, VSC neHAC.
IToyota ilinyuse kakhulu izinga leCorolla ngenxa yezinto enazo yenyuse nentengo yayo.
Yigama abalethembayo futhi uma ufuna eshibhile, ikhona iCorolla Quest esuselwe kwiCorolla endala.InaniCorolla 2.0 XR CVT - R 433 700Ifika neservice plan yamasevisi ayisithupha noma u-90 000km futhi kumele iseviswe njalo emuva kokuhamba u-15 000km noma izinyanga ezingu-12.
Ine-warranty yeminyaka emithathu noma u-100 000km.
Ngeke kugwemeke 'ukuvalwa' kwezwe: Mkhize
UKWENYUSELWA kwezwe ezigabeni zokuvalwa kwezwe eziphezulu yinto engeke igwemeke.
UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba ethi maningi amathuba okuthi lokhu kwenzeke njengoba zilokhu zikhula izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane kuleli.
Ngeledlule izibalo zabahaqwe yileli gciwane zike zaba ngu-3000 ngosuku.
Uqhube wathi umkhandlu wongqongqoshe ababhekelele iCorona kuleli, iNational Command Council (NCC) eholwa uNgqongqoshe wezekuBusa ngokuBambisana, uDkt Nkosazana Dlamini-Zuma, nezinhlaka ezithintekayo bazoba nomhlangano babonisane ngesinyathelo okumele sithathwe ukuze kunqandwe ukusabalala kweCovid-19.
"Uma izibalo zikhuphuka izigaba zokuvalwa kwezwe zizokwenyuswa, uma zehla kuzoxegiswa," kusho uDkt Mkhize.
Seziqalile neziphakamiso zokuthi uhulumeni ubheke ukuthi ngeke yini kumiswe ukudayiswa kotshwala nogwayi ngoba kunenkolelo yokuthi kunomthelela ekutheni abantu bathelelane ngaleli gciwane.
Imboni yabadayisa utshwala kuleli, iSouth African Liquor Brandowners Association (Salba), ne-Vinpro ithe uma uhulumeni engathatha isinqumo sokumisa ukudayisa utshwala futhi uzobe ebeka engcupheni imisebenzi engu-200 yabasebenza kule mboni.
UMnuz Sibani Mngadi, weSalba, uthe uhulumeni akakaze aziveze izizathu ezibambekayo zokuthi kungani evala ukuthi utshwala budayiswe, ababuthengayo babuphuzele emakhaya ngezimpelasonto.
Ngeledlule ikhabhinethi lelule isikhathi sokuthi leli lizwe lithathwe njengeliyinhlekelele okuzophela ngoJune 15.
UNdunankulu waseGauteng, uMnuz David Makhura, ngeledlule umemezele ukuthi sesingenile isivunguvungu sesithathu kulesi sifundazwe.
I-National Institute for Communicable Diseases (NICD) ngeledlule imemezele ukuthi iFree State ingesinye sezifundazwe isivunguvungu sesithathu esesifikile kuyo nakuba izinombolo zabahaqwa yileli zingakafinyeleli esibalweni esibekiwe esisho lokhu kodwa ukwenyuka kakhulu kwezibalo zakhona sekukhomba khona.
Izibalo zakamuva zabahaqwe yiCovid-19 kuleli, ezikhishwe wuMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli ngoMgqibelo, zikhomba ukuthi bangu-2750 abantu abahaqwe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 okuholele ukuthi isibalo sabahaqwe yileli gciwane senyukele ku-1 611 143.
Ababulelwe yizifo ezisondelele nalesi sifo ngesikhathi esifanayo bangu-59 okuholele ekutheni isibalo sabahaqwe yileli gciwane senyukele ku-55 183, kubo abangu-20 bashone eGauteng, abangu-18 abaseNorthern Cape , abayisishiyagalombili abaKwaZulu-Natal, abayisithupha abaseWestern Cape, abahlanu abaseFree State, eMpumalanga kushone ababili.
Ugwayi oluhlobo                       lwe-e cigaratte  awukuyekisi ukubhema
UGWAYI oxutshwe nokusamanzi okuthiwa usiza abafuna ukuyeka ukubhema obizwa nge-eletronic cigarette (e-cigaratte) kawusizi ekutheni uyeke ugwayi ojwayelekile kanti futhi uyabiza.
I-electronic cigarette kuthiwa iyindlela esetshenziswa ngabakhiqizi ukuze bahehe intsha ukuze ingene ithi shi ekuyisebenziseni.
Ngakho kumele kube nendlela yokulawula ukusetshenziswa kwayo ngokuthi umthetho sivivinyo, iControl of Tobacco and Electronic Delivery System Bill ka-2018, wenziwe ube ngumthetho olawula ukusetshenziswa kwayo.
USolwazi Olalekan Ayo wophiko lwesayensi ethinta ezempilo eNyuvesi iSefako Makgatho, uthe ucwaningo olwenziwe iHealth 24 ngo-2018 olubheka iminxa eminingi nge-e-cigarette, lukhomba ukuthi abantu abasebenzisa lolu hlobo lukagwayi olubhenywa ngokumunca isisi sikagwayi esiphuma sesinephunga lejusi, abayeki ukubhema.
Uma kwenzekile bayeka kuba isikhashana kodwa babuye babuyele ekubhemeni ugwayi ojwayelekile.
"Esikutholile ngesikhathi senza ucwaningo ukuthi ngesikhathi lufika lolu hlobo lukagwayi, abakhiqizi bathi luwumuthi osiza ekutheni abafuna ukuyeka ugwayi bayeke kalula kodwa lokho akulona iqiniso ngoba lokho akwenzeki kwasebeke bawusebenzisa.
Abantu abaningi abake bawusebenzisa uma kwenzekile bayeka ugwayi babuye babuyele kuwo futhi ngemuva kwesikhashana bewuyekile.
Abanye kuvela ukuthi bakusebenzisa kokubili ngesikhathi esisodwa, uma besendaweni engakuvumeli ukuthi babheme ugwayi ojwayelekile babhema i-e cigarette.
Uma besendaweni abakwaziyo ukubhema ugwayi ojwayelekile babheme wona," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi ucwaningo luveza ukuthi abantu ababuye babuyele ekubhemeni ugwayi bangu-60%.
U-17% ukusebenzisa kanye kanye.
"Kubukeka sengathi abakhiqizi balo gwayi bahlose ukuheha abantu abasha ukuze bangene kuwo ngoba wona awulawulwa, ayikho intela abayikhokhayo.
Zingu-240 izitolo ezidayisa ama-e cigarette kuleli.
U-40% wazo uqhele ngamakhilomitha angu-10 ezikhungweni zemfundo ephakeme, u-65% wazo uqhele ezikhungweni ngamakhilomitha angu-20," kusho yena.
USolwazi Israel Agaku ongumcwaningi oke abhale imiqingo yezempilo ngalolu hlobo lukagwayi, uthe abakhiqizi be-e cigarette baye bathi ushibhile uma uqhathaniswa nogwayi ojwayelekile.
"Ucwaningo olwenziwe ngo-2018, luveza ukuthi umuntu obhema zonke izinsuku ongabhemi ngokweqinile ubhema amabhokisi kagwayi angu-219 ngonyaka.
Ngaleso sikhathi ibhokisi likagwayi elilodwa belibiza uR30.
94c, okusho ukuthi ngonyaka usebenzisa uR4 387 kanti i-e cigarette isebenzisa izinto eziningi.
Kuzo kuhlanganisa amalahle (batteries) ashintshwayo, ijusi engu-100 ml kuya ku-200 ml ngesonto, nokunye okwenza ukuthi kuphume okusantuthu nakho okushintshwayo, konke lokho kwenza ithuluzi elilodwa elibhenywayo," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi umuntu obhemayo njengamanje usebenzisa uR6 933 ngonyaka kanti osebenzisa i-e cigarette usebenzisa uR8 781 kuya kuR19 781.
UNkk Zanele Mthembu weSmoking Free Org, uthe ulwazi abaluthole kososayensi luzobasiza ekutheni balwele ukuthi lo gwayi ulawulwe ngoba njengamanje kunabathi bawusebenzisa noma ikanjani ngoba bezitshela ukuthi uyelapha futhi ushibhile.
Ezobuchwepheshe | Sihlaziya iSPARK 5 egadla ngamakhamera amahlanu
ESIKHATHINI sanamhlanje akusekho lula ukukhetha iselula ngenxa yezinga lobuchwepheshe obuqukethwe amaselula amaningi abizwa ngama-smart phone, kusukela kwashibhile kuya kwabizayo.
Eminyakeni edlule kuqaphelekile ukuthi sandile isibalo sabantu abasebenzisa ama-smart phone eNingizimu Afrika kanti lokhu sekuholele ekutheni kunyuke isibalo sezinkampani ezikhiqiza amaselula ezisezingeni eliphezulu kuleli.
NgoMashi ka-2020, ngesikhathi kuqala ukuvalwa kwezwe njengendlela yokunqanda ukusabalala kwe-Covid-19 kuleli, inkampani yaseChina, iTecno, yamemezela ukuthi amaselula ayo asezodayiswa eNingizimu Afrika.
Ngokocwaningo, ukuthengwa kwama-smart phone eNingizimu Afrika, Nigeria nase-Egypt, kunyuswe yizinga lamaselula abiza amanani aphansi kodwa aqukethe cishe yonke into oyifunayo kwiselula.
Ngenyanga edlule ngithole ithuba eliyingqayisivele lokuvivinya enye yamaselula akhiqizwe yiTecno Mobile, iSPARK 5, ephume ngoSepthemba nonyaka.
Into yokuqala engichazile ngale selula yibhokisi layo.
Ngiyazi abantu abaningi abakunaki lokhu, kodwa indlela iselula ethulwa ngayo ebhokisini layo ibalulekile.
Ifika ngebhokisi elikhulu, elingeke likufakele amahloni uma kungathiwa le selula uyithenga njengesipho sohlekisana naye, ingane yakho, noma uzithengela wena nje.
Ngifake isithombe ngezansi ukuze uzibonele ukuthi bekumele ngiphawule ngebhokisi layo (packaging).
Ngaphakathi kuleli bhokisi akuphumi iselula kuphela, ihambisana nama-HiPods H2 earphones, okungama-earphones asebenza nge-bluetooth.
Anomsindo ogcwele ama-HiPods H2 kanti okuhle ngawo ukuthi uyakwazi ukuwasebenzisa uma kungena ucingo futhi uma uwumuntu othanda ukuzivocavoca uyakwazi ukukwenza lokho engaphumi ngoba ayabambelela ezindlebeni.
Ama-earphones aphuma nebhokisi lawo elisebenza njenge power-bank yoku-charger.
Into evame ukubhekwa abantu abaningi uma bethenga iselula namhlanje yizinga lekhamera.
ISPARK 5 igxile kakhulu ekuqhikizeni izithombe namavideo amahle njengoba iqukethe amakhamera amahlanu.
Inamakhamera amane ngemuva, neyodwa yama- "selfie" engaphambili.
Kwamane angemuva iqukethe ehamba phambili ewu-13MP, ewu-2MP yokushutha okuseduzane, iMacro lens ewu-2MP kanye ne-AI (Artificial Intelligence) Camera.
I-AI Camera ifakelwe ukuqinisekisa ukuthi kuphuma izithombe eziveza imibala yosuke ukushutha njengoba injalo.
Ukuvivinya lokhu ngithathe izithombe ezimbalwa ukubheka izinga lale khamera.
Ngaphandle kwekhamera, iSPARK 5 iqukethe i-battery ehlala isikhathi eside ingacishi.
Iphethe amandla awu-5000mAh, okusho ukuthi ingahlala u-16 hours ukhuluma ocingweni ingacishi, noma uchithe u-14 hours ubuka ama-video ingacishi.
Lokhu kuhambisana nosayizi wayo omuhle wokugcina amafayela eselula owu-32GB.
ISPARK 5 sisebenza ngobuchwepheshe be-Android, okuwubuchwepheshe okujwayelekile kubantu abasebenzisa ama-smart phone okubalwa kuwo iSamsung neHauwei.
Le selula iqukethe eyayo injini ngaphezu kwalokho iHelio A22 chipset yeMediaTek.
Sekuhlangane uthola iselula esheshayo uma uyisebenzisa, kumnandi nokuthinta i-screen sayo ngoba silandela kalula okwenzayo futhi sinama-graphics agqame kahle.
Bakwenzela umsebenzi ube lula ngama-App abakufakela wona, ikakhulukazi awakwa-google, kodwa uyakwazi ukuwasusa uma ungawathandi uzifakele awakho.
Le selula uyakwazi ukuyivula (unlock) ngomunwe nangobuso (facial recognition).
ISPARK 5 ungayithola ngoR2999 kulezi zitolo: Chatz Connect, Vodacom 4U, Cellucity, GAME, Hi store, Foschini, Totalsports naseTechX.
Hlola ukuthi ngabe inhliziyo yakho isebenza ngendlela kule Covid-19
Dkt Bongani Nxumalo Umbuzo okumele uhlale sizibuza wona ngukuthi yini ezobangela ukuthi uma usuhlaselwe wubhubhane lomkhuhlane iCovid-19 ugcine usuya kwagoqanyawo?Kuyacaca ukuthi iningi lethu lizohlaselwa yiCovid-19, lokho kumele singakubalekeli.Okusalayo ukuthi uma igciwane selikuhlasele kuzokwenzekani kuwe?
Uzosinda noma uzodlula nawe?Baningi abantu abazama ngazo zonke izindlela ukuphuza, bahlafune izinhlobonhlobo zezingxubevange zezithako okuthiwa zingakusiza ukuqinisa umzimba, bezilungiselela isimo abangasazi.
Okusalayo ngukuthi leli gciwane likuhlasela kuzwele imithambo yegazi, inhliziyo namaphaphu.
Esinye sezizathu esenza kube ngabantu asebekhulile abadlula naleli gciwane ngukuthi abaningi babo:* Banemithambo yegazi entekenteke nenezivimbo ezehlukene.
* Amakhemikhali asegazini labo awasabhalansile njengalokhuya besebasha.
* Amaphaphu abo nawo ayantengantenga.
Babodwa asebahlaselwa yisifo sofuba iTB abanye abazazi ukuthi banayo iTB, abanye banengxenye noma izingxenye zamaphaphu ezingasasebenzi, kuningi okungenzeka emaphashini ongakwazi.
Uma bethi konke kuya enhliziyweni, bakhuluma iqiniso.
Umhlume ugeqa ngokucishe kufane kwabesimame nabesilisa.
Baningi abafika njalo bezobuza umehluko wesifo umhlume kwabesimame nabesilisa.
Impendulo ilele ekukhumbuleni ukuthi abesifazane nabesilisa banomuzwa ofanayo oqala ekupheleni komgogodla bese ukopela emathanjeni esinqe.
Lo muzwa uhlukana kabili, ingxenye ilawula umbhobho wendle bese enye ingxenye yawo iyolawula izakhiwo zobulili.
Umhlume uqala emzimbeni ngokuthi kulimale lo muzwa, empeleni lo muzwa kuhlangene nokungasabalali ngokwanele kwegazi emzimbeni yizona zimbangela zesifo umhlume.
Ake sibuke izimbangela zomhlume kwabesifazane:* Ukuqumbelana, kube nzima ukhanule kakhulu uma uya kozikhulula.
Ukuba nzima uma ubeletha, kwesinye isikhathi umntwana abe mkhulu bese ekhuhla lo muzwa uze uhuzuke, endleleni yengane uma isiyophuma.
* Kwesinye isikhathi ngaphandle kokuba mkhulu komntwana, kuvamile ukuthi ekuteteni kube nobunzima, kuthathe isikhathi eside ngokwedlulele.
Lo muzwa uba ulokhu uthinteka ugcine uhuzuka, yilokhu kuhuzuka okugcina kukuphembela isifo umhlume.
Yingakho uyaye uthole ukuthi emuva kokuteta ungasenandaba nocansi, abanye besifazane bagcina sekuba nzima ukuvukelwa, ubhontshisi unciphe ushintshe ugqunqe, abanye baze bathathe isikhathi eside kakhulu ukufika kuvuthondaba abanye akufikeki mpela mpela.
Yilesi simo esibangela abantu besilisa bahlale besolwa ngokuthi abakwazi ukufikisa abathandiwe babo kuvuthondaba, kube ngathi inkinga ingakubona kanti isiphetho nguye umlingani wakho owalimala wahuzula lo muzwa waze wagcina esenesifo umhlume.
Baningi abesimame esebephila nalesi simo.
Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi baningi abalingani babo besilisa abazibuza ukuthi yini indaba othandiweyo wabo engafiki kuvuthondaba noma kube nzima ukufika khona.
Abanye bazisola ngapha nangapha bezitshela ukuthi yibo abahlulekayo, abahluleka ukwenza umsebenzi ngendlela; baningi lapha abaze bazisole ngokuthi banezinduku ezingenele mhlawumbe ngobude noma ngobubanzi kanti imbangela akusibo, yibona ebesifazane abanenkinga ngenxa yalokhu kugula.
* Ezinye izimpawu yiqolo elibuhlungu, izinyamana eziphuma embhobheni wendle okuthiwa ngama-piles nokuqumbelana okungapheli okuhambisana nokusuza njalo obekungajwayelekile ukwenzeka kuwe.
Umhlume njengoba wenza nakubantu besilisa uyakwazi ukuqhubeka uhlume nakwezinye izindawo, lapha imbangela isikhathi esiningi kusuke sewukungafikeleli ngokwanele kwegazi kulezo zindawo njengasezinyaweni, imilenze, amadolo, amanyonga neqolo.
Kubantu besilisa njengoba sijwayele ukusho imbangela umuzwa lona ebesikhulume ngawo kwabesimame umehluko kuba yinduku ekhophozelayo, ithambe, iwele phakathi, inciphe ngobude nangobubanzi, isheshe ikhafule kokunye ivele ingafuni ukunyakaza mpela mpela.
Ezinye izimpawu iqolo elibuhlungu nokusuza njalo.
Ekwelapheni umhlume kungaba owesilisanoma kwabesimame into iyodwa uyelapheka.
Okumele ukwenze ukuya kudokotela wakho noma kulowo ofisa akwelaphe uzosizakala.
Ngiyafisa ukugcizelela ukuthi kumqoka ukwelapha imbangela noma umsusa wakhona.
Udokotela akakunikezi imbiza eyodwa ezoshaya konke ngesikhathi esisodwa kodwa uma imbangela kungukuhuzuka komuzwa; sikuvuselelela lo muzwa ukuze izinto zibuyele ngononina.
Ukuvuselelwa kwalo muzwa kuthatha isikhashana kuncika eminyakeni yomuntu lowo nasebunjalweni besibindi salowo ohlaselekile.
Noma kunjalo, umehluko uwubona ngalolo suku uqala ngalo ukwelashwa.
Makulawulwe ukuhamba kwabantu: odokotela
PHILI MJOLIINHLANGANO yodokotela iSouth African Medical Association (SAMA), inxusa uhulumeni ukuthi aqinise imithetho yokuhamba kwabantu ukuze kunqandwe ukusabala kweCovid-19, ukuze isigaba sesithathu singeke sisheshe sihlasele.
UDkt Mvuyisi Mzukwa, oyiphini likasihlalo wenhlangano, uthi kumanje kunegciwane lakuleli eselizishintshile, nelitholakale e-India nelinye elitholakale e-United States (US).
Uthi bafisa ukuthi uhulumeni avale ukuhamba kwabantu phakathi kuka-10 ebusuku kuya-5 ekuseni, kuvalwe nemingcele yakuleli kuphinde kuqinisekiswe ukuthi ababaningi abantu abaya ezikhungweni zokugomela iCovid-19.
"Njengamanje uhlelo lokugomela iCovid-19 seluqalile kodwa ukulawulwa kokuhamba kwabantu kusadingeka ngoba umjovo okugonywa ngawo uthatha isikhathi ngaphambi kokuthi wakhe amasosha omzimba azobhekane negciwane uma kwenzeka lingena umuntu," kusho uDkt Mzukwa.
Uthe kuthatha amasonto amathathu kuya kwamane ukuthi umzimba wakhe amasosha azobhekana negciwane.
Kusazothatha isikhathi ukuthi sibone umehluko wokuthi abantu sebegomile.
Okunye okumele umphakathi ukwazi ukuthi umgomo awuvikeli ukuthi igciwane lingene kodwa uvikela ukuthi umuntu agule kakhulu aze adinge ukuya esibhedlela," kuchaza udokotela.
UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli uDkt Zweli Mkhize, phambilini ephawula ngalokhu wathi ukuqiniswa kwemithetho ukuze kunqandwe ukusabalala kweCovid-19, ngeke kugwemeke.
Phakathi kwemithetho engase iqiniswe, ukulawulwa kokudayiswa kotshwala, ukwehliswa kwesibalo sabantu abavumelekile ukuthi bahlangane, kulawulwe isikhathi sokuhamba kwabantu ebusuku.
Imibiko yabezindaba iveze ukuthi umkhandlu wongqongqoshe ababhekele iCorona kuleli, iNational Coronavirus Command Council (NCCC) ube nomhlangano ngoLwesibili, lapho ubudingida ngezindlela ezingalandelwa njengoba kubonakala zikhula izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi isivunguvungu sesithathu sokuhlasela kwegciwane sesifikile.
Ungoti uxwayisa ngokuzila ukudla kwabehlisa isisindo
KUBUKEKA kungenisile ukuzila ukudla kubantu bakuleli, abasuke bezama ukwehlisa isisindo.
Le ndlela yokwehlisa isisindo ebizwa nge-Intermittent fasting, isho ukungadli amahora athile bese udla ngamanye.
Ongoti bathi akuyona inkinga ukuzinciphisa nokukhetha uhlobo lokudla uma uzimisele ngokushintsha indlela ophila ngayo.
UNkk Ella Mthethwa oyiDietician kwa-Ellagence Wellness uthi, i-intermittent fasting iphoqa ukuthi umuntu adle amahora athile bese, ezila ukudla amahora amaningi kanti lokhu kwenza umzimba ungazitholi ngendlela izakhamzimba. "
Ayikho into entsha ngalolu hlobo lokudla nokuzinciphisa kodwa ngokokusebenza komzimba womuntu, akufanele kube khona isidlo sosuku umuntu esimeqayo.
Isidlo sasekuseni yisona esibaluleke kakhulu, uma uzoseqa bese uhlala amahora amaningi ungadlile uze udle sewulala kuyingozi," kusho uNkk Mthethwa.
Eqhuba uthe into ayikhuthazayo kubantu ukuthi baqale babonane nongoti kuqala, futhi umuntu aveze uhlelo azolulandela ngoba ziningi izindlela zokwenza i-intermittent fasting.
Uveze nokuthi akubi wuhlelo lwamahora ayisishagalombili kuphela kodwa kukhona nabakwenza ngokudla lawo mahora bese umuntu ezila ukudla usuku lonke.
UNkk Mthethwa uthe asikho isidingo sokuzifakela ingcindezi kubantu umuntu ajahe imiphumela ngokushesha ngoba ngesikhathi ulungisa indlela obukeka ngayo ngaphandle kuzokonakala ngaphakathi.
"Kuhle ukukhathazeka ngokubukeka kahle kodwa akumele kuphazamise ukusebenza komzimba.
Zonke izinsuku ukudla okunazo zonke izinhlobo zama-vitamin, amaprotein, amafutha namacarbohydrate kuyadingeka noma ngabe uyazinciphisa.
Asikukhuthazi ukuthi umuntu asebenzise uhlobo olulodwa lokudla okuzomthwala usuku lonke njengalaba abadla inyama bese bethembela ekutheni amaprotein namafutha atholakala kuwo yiwona azomgcina umuntu usuku lonke," kusho uNkk Mthethwa.
Ephetha uthe kuhle uma umuntu enza i-intermittent fasting azivocavoce, angaseqi isidlo sasekuseni noma ahlale izinsuku engadli futhi akufuneki ukujaha imiphumela.
Ukuzivocavota nohlelo lokudla oluphasiswe ungoti ngokwesimo somunye umuntu ngeke simsebenzele omunye ngoba imizimba yabantu nezifo akufani ngokusho kwalo ngoti.
Ukugcizelele nokuthi yize le ndlela isematheni futhi abantu kubukeka beyithandile, kodwa kukhona abantu okungamele basondelane nayo.
- Uma ukhulelwe kungaba yingozi kuwena nengane ukuzincisha ukudla ngezikhathi ezithile kwazise umzimba udinga yonke imisoco ongayithola ukuze nengane encelayo ithole imisoco ngendlela efanele.
-Uma unesifo esithile ophila naso, izakhamzimba zibalulekile futhi uzidinga zonke ukulwa nezifo emzimbeni.
-Kubantu abanesisindo somzimba esincane, akubalungele ukuzila ukudla ngale ndlela ngoba vele isisindo sabo singaphansi kwesifanele.
-Uma usanda kuhlinzwa noma usanda kubeletha kusekhona nokwelashwa okuthola kodokotela, ikakhulu kulaba ababeletha ngomthungo, ungasondeli kule ndlela yokuzinciphisa.
-Izifo ezifana noshukela, inhliziyo nezinye eziyingozi azihambisani kahle nalokhu ngoba umzimba ukuze uhlale unempilo udinga ukuthi umuntu adle izinhlobo ezahlukene zokudla ezizomgcina enempilo.
--Izingane ezincane akufanele nakancane zingene kulolu hlelo ngoba kusuke kusenezingxenye zomzimba ezisadinga izakhamzimba usuku lonke ukuze izicubu zakheke kahle.
Siyenyuka isibalo sabaneCovid-19 kuleli
ZIYAQONGA izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli njengoba kuvele ukuthi ngosuku bangu-4 236 abangenwe yileli gciwane.
Uma kuqhathaniswa nangoLwesihlanu babe ngu-3 332, abatholakale benegciwane ngosuku olulodwa.
Lokhu kukhomba ukuthi izibalo ziyenyuka zinsuku zonke kuleli zabatheleleka ngegciwane.
Ngokusho kukaNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli uDkt Zweli Mkhize, bangu-1 635 465 abakuleli abatholakale benegciwane.
Abashonile ngenxa yegciwane ngoMgqibelo kutholakale ukuthi bangu-53, eGauteng babengu-27, Free State 17, babehlanu KwaZulu-Natal, kanti bathathu eWestern Cape 3, bese eba yedwa e-Eastern Cape.
Abekho okubikwe ukuthi bashonile eLimpopo, Mpumalanga, North West nase- Northern Cape.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi abantu asebeshonile kuleli bangu-55 802.
Abasindile bangu:1 539 395, okusho ukuthi bami ku:94.2%.
Abantu asebehloliwe selokhu kwabheduka igciwane bangu: 11 354 930.
Khonamanjalo ucwaningo olwenziwe i-African Covid-19 Critical Care Outcomes Study (Acccos), luveza ukuthi emazweni angu-10 ase-Afrika, okubalwa nelakuleli siphezulu isibalo sabafayo ngenxa yaleli gciwane.
Lolu cwaningo olwenziwe kubantu abadala abangu-3 140, phakathi kukaMeyi noDisemba nyakenye, luveza ukuthi siphezulu isibalo sabafayo uma sebengeniswe emagunjini abagula kakhulu ngenxa yegciwane.
Luthole ukuthi uhhafu weziguli zishona ngaphandle kokunikekwa i-oxygen.
Ucwaningo luthole nokuthi labo abanoshukela mancane kakhulu amathuba okusinda.
AbakwaBMW bazama ukuvusa iGusheshe
INTATHELI YESOLEZWE AKUNGABAZEKI ukuthi iBMW 325is edume ngeleGusheshe, yimoto enomlando futhi eyintandokazi eNingizimu Afrika.
Ngesikhathi yethulwa ngo-1990, i-325is enezicabha ezimbili yayiyinto ehlukile kuleli futhi kwakhiqizwa eziwu-508 kuphela.
Yayitholakala ngezinhlobo ezimbili okuyi-2.
7 litre straight six engine enamandla angu-155kW (ayebabazeka ngaleso sikhathi).
IBMW ivusa umlando ngokwethula ebizwa nge-330is Edition.
Ngokombhalo okwi-website yakwaBMW, lolu hlobo lwemoto luzoqala kuleli maduze futhi abathengi kumele babhalise khona ukuze bathole imininingwane ngayo uma isikhona.
Okwamanje ayiikho imininingwane edaluliwe kodwa kulindeleke ukuthi ifane ne-330i eyakhonjiswa kwiM Festival ngonyaka odlule.
Yayinamarimu angu-20 inch, umbala omnyama kwigrille, okubhampa ngaphambili nakwispoiler ebhuthini ngemuva.
Mancane amathuba okuthi ithole amandla angaphezu kwe-330i enenjini engu-2 litre turbopetrol efuqa 190kW no-400Nm kodwa okungenani kumele ibe nesuspension esporty nezinye izinto ezizoyenza yehluke.
Leli phephandaba lizokubikela ngale moto uma eminye imininingwane ngayo isivelile.
IGusheshe yazakhela udumo kuleli ikakhulukazi emalokishini.
Yagqama kakhulu emdlalweni wethelevishini Ubambo Lwami ihamba uMazwi owayelingiswa nguMenzi Ngubane.
Nanamhlanje iseyintandokazi kulabo abathanda umdlalo wokushaya izidudla abachazwa ukuthi idonsa ngamasondo angemuva.
EZOTHANDO: Ingixina ngemibuzo ingane kamakhelwane engiyifihlile
Umbuzo:KONKE bekuhamba kahle phakathi kwami nonkosikazi wami.
Izinto ziqale ukushintsha mangabe sekuqala ukungahambi kahle emabhizinisini ethu.
Unkosikazi akasangazi nokuthi ngiwubani.
Sihleze sixabana ngemali.
Unokungifuna izinto azikahle kamhlophe ukuthi anginawo amandla azo.
Ngibona sengathi imali isingene phakathi kwethu ngoba sasingaxabani ngale ndlela sisenemali.
Ngenzenjani?Igama ligodliwe.Impendulo:Kubuhlungu ukubona ikhaya ebelihlangene lidungeka ngenxa yemali.
Kodwa isikhathi esiningi izinto zoniwa ukungakhulumi.
Asazi noma unkosikazi wakho uyazi ukuthi nibhekene nayiphi inkinga.
Kodwa kumele asazi isimo njengoba sinjalo.
Akekho unkosikazi ozimisele ngomshado wakhe ongaphikelela efuna izinto esazi isimo sasekhaya.
Umbuzo:Nginenkinga yomngani womyeni engimazelayo okwenza ngingakhululeki ngokuzwana kwakhe nomyeni wami.
Nginobufakazi bokuthi akathembekile kunkosikazi wakhe okwenza ngizibuze ukuthi yini esile azoyikhuluma nomyeni wami.
Ngabe likhona yini iphutha mangingenelela kulobu bungani babo noma ngithembe umyeni wami?Okhathazekile, North CoastImpendulo:Umhlola kumele niwuxoshe usesemnyango.
Yingakho thina sibona ukuthi kufanele ukhulume nomyeni wakho.
Kungakuhle ube nobufakazi bokungathembeki komngani ukuze umyeni wakho angaziboni sekumele akhethe umuntu ekumele amthembe.
Sikholwa ukuthi kubalulekile ukuthi uphila nabantu abanjani.
Kwesinye isikhathi kuhle ukuziqhelelanisa nezinto zisekude noma akhulumisane nomngani wakhe ukuze ashintshe indlela yokwenza.
Umbuzo:Ngiyibhungu elineminyaka ewu-23.
Nginenkinga yokubanovalo mekuza kubantu besifazane.
Ngesaba ukushela noma sekukhona izindlela umuntu wesifazane angikhombisa ngazo ukuthi angishele kodwa ngivele ngiphelelwe amazwi.
Le nto isingenze ngaqhelelana nontanga yami ngoba mebekhuluma ngamantombazane mina angazi ngizothini.
Okhathazekile, KwaNongomaImpendulo:Sibona ukuthi into engakusiza la ukuthi uzame ukumujwayela kuqala lo muntu obona sengathi uyamthanda.
Ungavele umdilike ngezothando zisuka nje ngoba sengathi loko kukushayisa ngovalo.
Usungamazisa umuntu ngendlela ozizwa ngayo mangabe senijwayelene.
Thatha isikhathi sakho uzazi wena futhi ubujabulele ubuwena.
Emva kokuzazi nokungazifaki phansi kwengcindezi kontanga, uzobona sekulula ukuzibika kubantu besifazane.
Umbuzo:Ngisafunda isikole ngakhulelwa ngikhuleliswa umakhelwane oshadile.
Ngafihla ngangasho ekhaya ngoba ngisaba, baze bagcina bengasangibuzi lutho kuze kube manje.
Inkinga manje ingane yami isikhulile isiqala ukungibuza imibuzo ngobaba wayo, angisazi ukuthi ngizoyibalekela kanjani futhi le ndaba.
Okungicasula kakhulu ukuthi ubaba wayo ingane uyangibuka nje, ngikhulisa ingane ngedwa ekhona.
Ngenzenjani?Igama ligodliwe, Port Shepstone.
Impendulo:Kusobala ukuthi lesi nqumo wasithatha usemcane futhi wesaba nehlazo owawuzofaka umndeni wakho kulo.
Wenza owawukubona kulungile ngaleso sikhathi.
Ayikho into ekuvimbayo ukuthi uphumele obala ngowakwenza futhi uxolise nangesenzo sakho.
Emva kokuhlala phansi nomndeni wakho usungadlulela emntwaneni wakho wenze okufanayo.

Kukhuthazwa imbokodo ukuba ihlolwe umdlavuza webele
NGOKWEZIBALO zakamuva zesikhungo esicwaninga uketshezi kuleli iNational Health Laboratory Service, ezindaweni zasemadolobheni izibalo zakhona zikhomba ukuthi oyedwa kwabesifazane abayisishiyagalombili unomdlavuza webele.
Kule nyanga okuyinyanga yokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza webele, iBreast Imaging Society of South Africa (BISSA) inxuse abantu besifazane abaneminyaka ewu-40 kuya phezulu ukuthi bazihlole ukuthi abanawo yini umdlavuza.
USihlalo weBISSA uSolwazi Jackie Smilg, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi umuntu onalo mdlavuza asheshe azazi ukuze aqale uhlelo lokuwulawula.
"Ukusheshe kutholakale ukuthi umuntu unawo yini umdlavuza kusiza ngokunciphisa amathuba okuthi abatholakale benawo bashone, ngoba uhlelo lokuwulawula lusheshe luqalwe," kusho yena.
Uthe umdlavuza webele uhlasela abesifazane abakuzo zonke izigaba akukhathalekile ukuthi baneminyaka emingaki nokuthi baphila impilo esezingeni eliphansi noma eliphezulu.
"Ukuhlale uzihlola ukuthi awunawo yini umdlavuza kuholela ekutheni umdlavuza webele utholakale usesebeleni ungakasabalali kwezinye izingxenye zomzimba okuyinto eyenzeka uma ungasheshanga ukutholakala.
Kunabantu abanezinkolelo zokuthi uhlelo lokuhlola umdlavuza kusetshenziswa umshini obulala ama-cells omdlavuza, yilo olwenza ukuthi abahlolwe ngawo bangenwe yilo mdlavuza.
Alukho ucwaningo olufakazela lokhu," kusho uSolwazi Smilg.
Mayelana nabantu abasengcupheni kakhulu uthe bonke abesifazane basengcupheni yokuthi babe nomdlavuza webele kodwa labo asebekhulile banamathuba amaningi okuthi bahlaselwe yilo mdlavuza uma beqhathaniswa nabaneminyaka ewu-45 kuya phansi.
-Abesifazane abazalwa emindenini enabantu abake baphathwa yilo mdlavuza banamathuba aphindaphindiwe okuthi nabo babe nawo.
-Owesifazane oke waphathwa wumdlavuza ebeleni elilodwa kunamathuba amaningi okuthi nelinye ibele libe nawo umdlavuza ngokuhamba kwesikhathi.
-Abesifazane abahlolwe ibele emshinini wakhombisa ukuthi linezindlala, elingenawo amafutha kunamathuba amaningi okuthi bahlaselwe wumdlavuza ngoba kuba nzima ukuthi usheshe ubonakale.
-Abesifazane abakhuluphele ngokweqile ucwaningo oluke lwenziwa phambilini lukhomba ukuthi ukukhuluphala ngokweqile kwengeza amathuba okuhlaselwa wumdlavuza.
Olunye ucwaningo luveza ukuthi abesifazane abakhuluphele uma beke balashelwa lo mdlavuza maningi amathuba okuthi uphinde ubuye kubona.
Kwaziswa ngomdlavuza eMlaza
UKULAHLEKELWA wunina ngenxa yomdlavuza, kwagqugquzela insizwa yaseMlaza ukuthi izibophezele ekuqwashiseni ngalesi sifo.
UMthokozisi Shabangu, unguMqondisi weSolempilo Organisation ehlela, i-Eye for Cancer Walk, okuwuhlelo lapho ehlanganisa khona umphakathi ngenhloso yokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza nokweseka labo abaphila nawo nalabo abaphila nabantu abanawo.
Elandisa ngalolu hlelo, uthe kuningi abakwenzayo ngalolu suku kanti uhlelo lwabo luhlukene kabili.
Baqala ngohambo olubizwa nge-5km BIG WALK bese kuba khona indawo yokuhlolelwa umdlavuza mahhala, ama-aerobics nokunye okuningi.
"Akekho ongazi ukuthi kukhona isifo okuthiwa yi-cancer kodwa iningi lihlale lisibukela kude.
Umuntu uze akholwe uma sekukhona amaziyo ophethwe yisona," usho kanje.
Uthe naye wambuleka amehlo ngesikhathi kushona unina eselwe nomdlavuza iminyaka engu-11, okuyilapho anquma khona ukushumayela ukubaluleka kokuzivocavoca nokuhlolelwa lesi sifo ukuze uzazi kusenesikhathi ukuthi umiphi.
Uveze ukuthi inhloso yakhe enkulu ngalolu hlelo wukugqugquzela indlu emnyama ngokubaluleka kokushesha uhlonzwe umdlavuza nokukhuthaza impilo engcono.
"Ngokwami ngabe sihambela nezinye izindawo kodwa ngenxa yokwentula izinsiza sigcina ngokuqwashisa abantu baseMlaza kuphela kodwa sinethemba lokuthi kusazokwenzeka nokunye esikufisayo," kusho uMthokozisi.
Sekuwunyaka wesithathu i-Eye for Cancer yenziwa kanti kungenwa mahhala kuyona.
Kulokhu izobe iseKing Zwelithini Outer Fields ngo-Okthoba 31 kusukela ngo-7 ekuseni.
UMthoko uthe abantu abaphume ngobuningi babo bazozihlolela lesi sifo, baphinde bathole ulwazi oluzobahlomisa ekulweni nomdlavuza.
Abasuke bekulo mcimbi bagqoka noma yini enombala o-pink, okuwumbala ohambisana nokuqwashisa ngomdlavuza.
Kulo nyaka uhlelo bazoluvala ngeJerusalem Challenge.
Akuphoqelekile ukwazisa umqashi ngesifo sengqondo
NGABE uphoqelekile ukutshela umqashi ukuthi uhlushwa yisifo esithile sengqondo?Lona ngumbuzo ohlupha abantu abaningi abanokhwantalala nezinye izifo zengqondo.
NgoLwesihlanu iSouth African Depression and Anxiety Group (Sadag), ibinenkundla yokucobelelana ngolwazi kwiFacebook, lapho abantu bebekhululekile bebuza nangezinkinga ababhekana nazo uma benezifo zengqondo emsebenzini.
Izazi zeSadag, ziveze ukuthi yize abantu abaningi benazo izifo zengqondo kodwa bakuthola kunzima ukuziveza obala emsebenzini ngenxa yokusaba ukucwaswa, ngozakwabo abasebenza nabo noma ukubeka itoho labo engcupheni.
UMnuz Peter Strasheim ongumnikazi weDLM Labour, oyisazi ngezifo zengqondo, ukukhubazeka nomthetho othinta ezabasebenzi, uthi kubalulekile ukuthi umsebenzi abheke imithetho ethinta ezempilo emsebenzini, ngaphambi kokudalula isifo esimphethe.
"Uma ukhetha ukuphumela obala ngokuthi unesifo sengqondo akubalulekile ukuthi usisho igama laso kodwa kufanele ucacise ukuthi sikuthikameza kanjani.
Abaqashi abanemithetho emihle yezempilo bayazwelana nawe, bese bekunikeza usizo olufanele.
Kubalulekile ukutshela umqashi ngoba kwesinye isikhathi uzodinga ukuyobonana nodokotela wezifo zengqondo noma ukuhlaba ikhefu kancane emsebenzini," kusho uStrasheim.
Uthe uma kwenzeka umsebenzi exoshwa emuva kokuthi ephumele obala ngesifo sengqondo, kufanele abikele umnyango wezabaSebenzi , ummeli neCCMA.
UDkt Nkateko Ndala-Magoro oyiClinical Psychologist, uthe kubalulekile nokuthi umsebenzi angavele nje aphumele obala ngesifo sengqondo kodwa asiveze uma siphazamisa indlela asebenza ngayo.
Zisha ngamaPyjama party kulezi zinsuku
Ukuvalwa kwezwe kwenze ukuthi abahleli bemicimbi bazame izindlela ezihlukile nezihehayo zokwenza imicimbi, ehlanganisa imindeni.
Enye yalezi zindlela amaphikhinikhi enzelwa emakhaya lapho, kungadingeki ukuthi umuntu aqashe indawo yomphakathi.
UNksz Thokozisiwe "Hleh" Mnyango waseMtubatuba, osezinze eNewlands East, nongumphathi weZisiwe Decor and Catering, uthe lolu hlobo lwemicimbi lusazoqhubeka nokuheha abantu.
Uthi lemicimbi mihle ngoba ayikhethi, umuntu uyakwazi ukuyenzela nasendlini esebenzisa indlela yokuhlobisa, efanele ingaphandle lendlu.
"Into enhle ngephikhinikhi ukuthi umhlobiso (decor) wakhona uqoqana kahle futhi uyakwazi ukusebenzisa izinto ezihlukene ngaphandle kokukhathazeka ngesibalo sabantu.
"Uyakwazi ukuyenzela epaki, engadini, egcekeni ekhaya noma endlini uma kushintsha isimo sezulu liguqubala noma kunetha," kusho uNksz Mnyango.
Uthe isibalo sabantu asiyona inkinga futhi bangabababili, kodwa kubukeke kahle njengomcimbi omkhulu, ohlelelwe iningi.
"Uma kuwumcimbi womndeni kungaba amalungu angu-10 kuye ngesibalo sabantu ngoba kweminye imndeni kuyenzeka bafike naku-25.
Nezithandani ziyaba nephikhinikhi kube yizo kuphela," kusho yena.
Uthe esikhathini samanje abantu abakhonze amaphathi ngabesifazane lokho sekwenze kwaze kwangena nesitayela samaphathi ezingubo zokulala, iPyjama Party nokwezimpahla zangaphansi, okuthiwa iLingerie Party.
UNksz Mnyango uthe iningi labantu liqala ebusuku ngalolu hlobo lomcimbi luwenzele ekamelweni, bese ngakusasa lenza iphikhinikhi.
"Kuya ngabantu, abanye ipyjama party bayenza nasemini ukuthatha kahle izithombe bese beshintsha baswenke kuqale iphikhinikhi.
Le micimbi ayixwayani uma konke kuzokwenzelwa ekhaya kwenza kube lula kakhulu," kusho uNksz Mnyango.
Buka: IToyota GR Yaris entsha igxuma njengonogwaja
UMPETHA wezimoto zomjaho oseneminyaka ekulo mdlalo uGiniel de Villiers uzwe amandla eToyota GR Yaris ezokwethulwa eNingizimu Afrika maduze.
UGiniel, oseke wanqoba izicoco eziningi emjahweni wakuleli neseDarak Rally, ubevivinya iGR Yaris enkundleni yezimoto zomjaho iKillarney International Raceway, eKapa muva nje.
IGR Yaris inenjini engu-1.
6 litre turbocharged eyithree-cylinder kaphethroli.
Ifuqa amandla angu-200kW netorque engu-370Nm.
Idonsa ngawo womane amasondo futhi bathi ikwazi ukusuka ku-0 iye ku-100km/h ngemuzuzwana engu-5.2.NgoJuni 30 izokwethulwa ngokusemthethweni kwabezindaba lapho sizothola khona ithuba lokuyizwa amandla nemininingwane ephelele ngayo bese sikubukela ngayo kuyo le ngosi.
'Kufanele uthuthukiswe umsebenzi wamanesi'
KUQHAKANJISWA ukuthi uthuthukiswe umkhakha wabahlengikazi kuleli ngenxa yokubhekana nezinselelo eziningi emsebenzini abawenzayo.
Namhlanje kugujwa usuku lwamanesi, olugujwa umhlaba wonke ngaphansi kwesihloko esithi Nurses: A voice to lead.
UDkt Champion Nyoni, ongumcwaningi ophinde afundise esikoleni sabahlengikazi esiseNyuvesi yaseFree State, uthe kuningi abahlengikazi ababhekane nakho ngo-2020.
"Kuningi futhi okusazokwenzeka ngomuso.
I-Covid-19 iphonsele umkhakha wezempilo izinselelo ezihlukene, abahlengikazi ababhekana kuqala nalezi zinselelo.
Abahlengikazi bathintekile ngokomqondo, izinga labo lokubekezela nokwenze bakwazi ukusebenzisana kangcono," usho kanje.
"Esikhathini esizayo, idinga ukuthuthukiswa indima yabahlengikazi, ukukhula komsebenzi wobuhlengikazi kubalulekile.
Abahlengikazi bazokwazi ukuqhubeka nomsebenzi wabo uma bezithuthukisa emsebenzini, ekubambisaneni bebodwa kanye nokusebenzisana nabanye abasebenzi bezempilo," usho kanje.
Uthe ikusasa lonesi liqhakazile ngoba kule minyaka ewu-60 eyedlule lo mkhakha utshengisa ukukhula.

Udinga amasu nosiko oliphusile ukuphumelelisa ibhizinisi
IBHIZINISI akukhona nje ukukhiqiza nokuthengisa kodwa kuningi okufanele ukubukisise uma uqhuba ibhizinisi.
Kuvamile-ke ukuzwa abantu bekhuluma nge-business plan uma bezoqala ibhizinisi befuna ukuxhaso lwemali.
Iningi labasuke bengadingi kuboleka mali abayingeni eye-business plan.
Angiyiphathi-ke lapho seliqhubeka ibhizinisi, ayibonwa i-business plan njengoba sekugxilwe ekwenzeni imali.
Lokhu kufana ncamashi nokuhamba uye phambili kodwa ungazi ukuthi uya kuphi.
Yiyona-ke le inkinga yamabhizinisi amaningi.
Ngaphandle kohlelo oluphusile namasu ajulile kuyasinda ukuncintisana namanye amabhizinisi.
Pho aphumelela kanjani?
Asiqale ngokubhekisisa ukuthi luquketheni uhlelo lokuqhuba ibhizinisi futhi yini umehluko phakathi kohlelo namasu.
Uhlelo lokuqhuba ibhizinisi lubeka ngokusobala izinto okufanele uzenze ukuze uphumelele.
Lubeka ngokusobala ukuthi yini oyikhiqizayo, uyikhiqizela bani futhi uzoyithengisela bani.
Akugcini lapho kufanele wazi ukuthi izovelaphi imali yokukhiqiza, uzoqasha bani nokuthi imakethe ozoyidayisela imi kanjani.
Ngakolunye uhlangothi isu lebhizinisi ligxile ekutheni uzohluka kanjani kwabanye oncintisana nabo, kungani amakhasimende kumele akhethe wena kunabanye.
Kuvamile ukuzwa abantu bethi bona bashibhile kunabanye, yingakho kufanele amakhasimende athenge kubona.
Iqiniso wukuthi ukushibha akulona isu eliphusile lebhizinisi.
Isu lebhizinisi kufanele kube yinto enganakekile koncintisana nabo.
Uma unezindlela ezithile zokwehlisa izindleko zokukhiqiza usethubeni lokushibha kunabanye ube wenza inzuzo efanayo.
Lapha akukhona ukushibha okuyisu lebhizinisi kepha yizindlela zokunciphisa izindleko.
Ukuthola umkhiqizo ngemali ephansi kuyasebenza okwesikhashana kodwa abantu oncintisana nabo bazokwazi bakulandele.
Akulula ukunciphisa izindleko njengoba kufanele ubhekisise ukuthi awehlisi izinga lomkhiqizo.
Enye indlela ongahluka ngayo wukwenza amakhasimende awuthande umkhiqizo wakho noma indlela osebenzisana ngayo nawo.
Kufanele usebenzele ukuthi amakhasimende awubone ungcono umkhiqizo wakho noma indlela owaphatha ngayo.
Eqinisweni ukudinga kokubili, umkhiqizo osezingeni eliphezulu emqondweni wekhasimende nesevisi eqhakambisa ikhasimende.
Uma uthengisa imikhiqizo oyithola kwabanye kuyasiza ukuthi ugxile ebudlelwaneni namakhasimende njengoba abanye bethengisa izinto ezifanayo nawe.
Okunye okufanele ukubheke ngamakhono abantu obaqashayo, ubudlelwane nabakufakela izinsiza zebhizinisi, ukusebenzisana okuhle kwezisebenzi nobudlelwane obuhle nemenenja yasebhange.
Okusemqoka wukuthi isu onalo lebhizinisi kufanele liqondwe ngabantu osebenza nabo ukuze basebenzele ukuthi lifezeke.
Yingakho kufanele libhalwe phansi bese wenza izindlela zokuthi lingene emqondweni weqembu obambisene nalo.
Ngaphezu kwalokho udinga usiko lokusenza oluhambisanayo nesu lakho, ngale kwalokho lifana nento engekho isu lakho.
Usiko luyingqalasizinda yokuthi abantu baziphatha kanjani emsebenzini, bahloniphana kanjani futhi bawaphatha kanjani amakhasimende.
Uma usebenza nabantu abantshontshayo noma abaqhubana ngamadolo awukwazi ukwehlisa izindleko zokukhiqiza.
Khumbula ukuthi zimbili izindlela zokwenza imali ebhizinisini; ukunciphisa izindleko nokubiza intengo ethe xaxa kunabanye.
Konke lokhu kudinga usiko olwenza kusebenzeke kalula ngenxa yobudlelwane obuhle phakathi kwawo wonke umuntu.
Usiko olunjalo lwenza kube lula ukusabalalisa amasu ebhizinsi nokuthi wonke umuntu asebenzele impumelelo yebhizinisi.
Alwenzeki ngokwalo usiko.
Kubalulekile ukuthi ucacise umbono webhizinisi kuzo zonke izisebenzi, ukubaluleka kwendima okumele ziyikhathule ngokuba yingxenye yebhizinisi.
Kuningi abantu abangakuzuza emsebenzini ngaphandle kweholo.
Okulandelayo wukuthi ube nendlela yokuklomelisa umsebenzi omuhle.
Lokhu kudinga ulimele iqiniso ungabonakali ukhetha iphela emasini.
Kufanele izisebenzi zazi ngokusobala ukuthi yiziphi izindlela zokuziphatha nokusebenza eziklonyeliswayo.
Uhlelo lwakho lokuklomelisa kumele luqinisekise ukuthi bonke abantu banethuba lokuhlomula.
Awudingi izindodla zemali ukwenza lokhu, umklomelo wamathikithi ebhola noma ikhonsathi kusho lukhulu uma encoma isenzo esihle.
* Sishayele noma uthumele umlayezo ku-083 354 8794.
Bhalisa uthole ulwazi olunohlonze ku-www.ubuntuwealth.co.za .
- Sikhula Ngomnotho

INKAMPANI edayisa izimoto esidlangalaleni iWoodford Bid, isungule inkundla lapho abantu bengazidayisela khona izimoto zabo kwi-website yayo.

Ithe lokhu ikwenza ngoba ukudayisa imoto kungaba wumdanti futhi kunabathengi abazama ukukuncenga ukuthi wehlise imali.
"Okumele ukwenze ukufaka imoto yakho kwi-website bese ubuka abantu abagunyaziwe bebanga imoto yakho masonto wonke, nokuthi ukhona okwazi ukukhokha imali oyikalile bese ukudayisa kuphasa.
Okunye ukuthi ungadayisa ngemali engaphezu kwaleyo oyifunayo uma beqhubeka nokuyibanga imoto.
"IWoodford Bid ithe ungabhalisa ku-www.woodbid.co.za ufake imininingwane, usho imali oyifunayo bese ubuka bebangisana ngayo.
Ukhokha uR50 wokuklelisa imoto bese kuba nochatha owukhokha uma imoto isidayisiwe.

Ishiya lesimanje kwabahlulwa ukulidweba
UKUDWEBA ishiya kwabesifazane kuhamba phambili kulezi zinsuku futhi ngisho nongakwazi ugwegwesa ziya khona.
Yize belidweba nsuku zonke kodwa nanoma yimuphu umuntu wesifazane ovuka ekuseni ahlale esibukweni uzokutshela ukuthi kuhambisana nobunzima obukhulu kangakanani.
Ishiya lesimanje aliyi ngasipiliyoni ngoba noma ngabe sewungumpetha kangakanani kodwa ngelinye ilanga livele ligoloze likuphike sengathi awukakaze ulidwebe.
Ongoti bezokuzicwala sekwenze baqinisa kakhulu nakwishiya elikwazi ukuhlala isikhathi eside i-eyebrow microblading.
Lolu hlobo lweshiya limba eqolo kodwa lihambisana nobuhle besikhathi eside futhi libukeka lingenisa kwabesifazane abaningi.
Osaziwayo nabo bahamba phambili ngokwenza eyebrow microblading kwazise baziphaqula njalo.
Omunye wabo uDj Happygal oseze waqokwa njengenxusa lendawo yokuzicwala ehamba phambili ngokwenza i-eyebrow microblading iNina Lola Studio.
UHappygal uthe naye kwakunzima ukubhala ngokuhlanganisa epatanisa ishiya waze wathola le ndlela elula neyenza impilo ibelula.
"Ngangihluleka ukudweba ishiya ngabona ukuthi angiyizame imicroblading ngoba kuyona itattoo njengoba abantu abaningi beba nokudideka.
Ngaqala ngenza ishiya elihlala iminyaka emithathu.
Manje engilenzile lihlala eminyaka emibili ngilokhu ngivuka lisekhona.
Ngelinye ilanga ngiyakwazi ukuvuka ngihambe ngingazange ngiziphaqule kodwa ngibe muhle,"kusho uHappygal.
Okwenza eyebrow microblading idlise kwabesifazane yize ibiza-Noma ungavuka sewuphuthuma emsebenzini ekuseni alikulibazisi ungalihlikihla nangesandla ungene indlela.
-Uyazikhethela ukuthi ufuna ishiya lakho lihlale isikhathi eside kangakanani kungaba izinyanga noma iminyaka uphinde futhi uliqede uma sewuthanda.
-Alixebuki noma litsheke ishiya lakho ngisho ugeza, ugijima ugcoba, uzesula noma ugqoka.
-Ukulenza kuthatha isikhathi esijwayelekile umuntu asichitha endaweni yokuzicwala.
-Ngisho ungageza kangaki awushintshi noma uphuphe umbala weshiya lakho.
-Kuphephile ukudweba lolu hlobo lweshiya akusilimazi nesikhumba.
Kuyingozi ukushayela eNingizimu Afrika: Ucwaningo
UCWANINGO lwakamuva lweZutobi Drivers Ed luveza ukuthi iNingizimu Afrika iyizwe eliyingozi kunawo wonke ukushayela kulo.
Ucwaningo luncike ezintweni ezahlukene njengesibalo sabafa emgwaqeni, ijubane elikhulu elisemthethweni nesibalo sabafasa amabhande.
IRSP ithe yize kuyinto eyaziwayo ukuthi isibalo sabafa emgwaqeni eNingizimu Afrika siphezulu kodwa imiphumela yocwaningo iyakhathaza.
"Yize isibalo sithi bangu-25.
9 abantu kwabangu-100 000 abafa ezingozini zomgwaqo kodwa ukuthi kuthiwe siyizwe eliyingozi ukushayela kulo kumele izwe lisebenzele ukukushintsha lokho.
Emiphumeleni yocwaningo iNingizimu Afrika ayibanga nesibalo esiphezulu sabafele emgwaqeni.
Isizathu somphumela wezwe yingoba sinesibalo sesibili ngobukhulu sabafa emgwaqeni kubantu abangu-100 000 futhi isibalo esikhulu sezingozi sihlanganisa utshwala.
"Imithetho yaseNingizimu Afrika iyafana neyamazwe okuthiwa kuphephile ukushayela kuwo.
"Ijubane elikhulu liyafana namazwe amahlanu aphephile futhi nesikalo sikatshwala egazini sikhulu noma siyalingana nala mazwe.
"Kuthiwa umehluko omkhulu usekufaseni amabhande.
"Emazweni aphephile u-95% wabagibeli abahleli ngaphambili bayawafasa amabhande kanti eNingizimu Afrika bayingcosana kakhulu.
Yize nesikali sotshwala egazini sifana nasemazweni amaningi kodwa isibalo sezingozi ezibandakanye abashayeli abaphuzile siphezulu nokukhombisa ukungahlonishwa kwemithetho eNingizimu Afrika.
""Lolu cwaningo kumele kugqugquzele abashayeli ukuthi bashintshe indlela abenza ngayo."
Abesifazane abasafisa abantwana abehlise kuphuzo
INHLANGANO i-World Health Organisation (WHO) isinxenxe abesifazane abazithwele kanye nabesifazane abaneminyaka ebavumela ukuba bathole abantwana ukuba bazithibe otshwaleni.
Lokhu kuvela njengoba iphakamisa izincomo ngaphansi kohlelo lwayo lwe-Global Alcohol Action Plan, nokuyilapho ifuna ukulusebenzisa emazweni ahlukene ukuzama ukwehlisa izinga lotshwala.
Kulezi zincomo abasaziphakamisa, kuvele ukuthi utshwala buba nemithelela emibi empilweni yabantu, kube nemithelela engemihle ngokuthola izifo.
Konina bezingane abazithwele, kuthiwa bangasondelani nhlobo notshwala.
Bese kuthi abesifazane abasazimisele ukuba nabantwana banciphise otshwaleni.
Phakathi kwezinye izinto ezivela kulo mqulu we-WHO ukuthi izingane ziqala zisencane ukuphuza, cishe zineminyaka engu-15, nokuyinto abayihlabile.
Kube nemvunge ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngalezi ziphakamiso ezishicilelwe ngoLwesithathu kwi-website ye-WHO, abanye bethi zicwasa abesifazane abasafuna ukuba nezingane kodwa kungashiwo lutho ngabesilisa.
Bhasobha Isifo iThyroid uma ukhathala ube yimvithi
DKT BONGANI NXUMALOKWAKHE kwafika isiguli sesifazane esasineminyaka eyevile ku-33, esasiqala ukuza kwesinye sezikhungo zethu, sikhala ngokukhathala okwakuvithiza umzimba, amalungu omzimba, izicubu nomqondo kucobeke.
Ukuba kwakuya ngaye ungathi wayengaba yinto ehlala izilalele nje, kungavumi lutho.
Ukusukuma wayephoqwa ukuthi umsebenzi wakhe wayewuthanda, futhi kumele enze imisebenzi yasekhaya njengomama wekhaya.
Wayexabana nomyeni wakhe ngento engenamsebenzi, futhi wazithola engasakwazi ukuma aqoqe umqondo engxoxweni, amagama abekwazi ukuwaphimisela engasaphumi kalula, angiphathi uma esengxoxweni esampikiswano; wayezithola esevele asheshe anikezele into ayengayijwayele.
Wayeshaywa wuvalo ayengalujwayele umzimba wakhe wawuqhaqhazela uma ebeka unyawo, nalapho ethi uyabamba into ngesandla, yiso leso uyaqhaqhazela, ajuluke kakhulu azwele ukushisa nomzimba ushise.
Ibhalansi emzimbeni yayingesakho kahle esehamba ekhutshwa wubala nasemzimbeni nje wayezibona encipha.
Engxoxweni esaba nayo sathola ukuthi ukugula kwakunesikhathi esevile onyakeni kumshuka, enenkinga yokuqwasha ebusuku ehlala kuze kube zintatha ekuseni kungalaleki.
Ubelokhu ecabanga ukuthi unengcindezi yomqondo, ebuka nokukhandleka emsebenzini nasekhaya njengembangela yokushintsha kwesimo sempilo.
Abangani ayenabo baya belokhu bencipha ngenxa yokuthi bese enenhliziyo encane.
Ekuhambeni kwesikhathi uthi wazithola engasenandaba nocansi, engasafiki kuvuthondaba, inhliziyo yabe isincane, izinto eziningi ebezibalulekile engasenandaba nazo.
Wayenengane eyodwa ayithola engakashadi nayo isindala, lapha emshadweni kudala bezama beguduza imimango yokuthola umntwana, lutho kungenzeki.
Odokotela ayehamba kubo babelokhu bemi ngokuthi unokhwantalala futhi unesifo sokwethuka okuthiwa yiPanic Disorder, nemishanguzo yomqondo wayeseyiqalile kodwa engawuboni umehluko.
Uma ebuyela kodokotela bakhe babelokhu beshintshana ngaye bemthatha igazi kodwa imiphumela yayilokhu ingaphumi nalutho okanye kuthiwa ilahlekile.
Yimpilo le abese eyiphila saze sahlangana naye.
Lesi sifo esigxile kuso namhlanje asithathi ohlangothini oluthile kwezobulili, noma nje izinombolo zigebela kwabesimame ikakhulu futhi nezincwadi ezinkulu ziyakuvuma lokhu.
Kunomunye umfo ongumuntu wesilisa, oneminyaka eyevile ku-50 owayelokhu ekhala ngovalo, ukungalali ebusuku, naye wayencipha umzimba ukhathala.
Yena kwakuzwakala sengathi ingalo yakhe iyaqanda sakuvithizeka phakathi engalweni.
Uthi kwakungebuhlungu kodwa kwakulokhu kunokuvithizeka kwengalo okwakuzwakala ngaphakathi le kude kuhambisana nomuzwa osabu'tiya."
Uchaza uthi le nto yayifika ngaphambi kokulala, awulali uma ikuphethe uze ulale lapho iphela khona.
Kwesinye isikhathi kuyenzeka kube nento enyuka iyothi ngci esifubeni kungaphefumuleki, kokunye kuze kushe nezwi.
Ekuphandeni sathola ukuthi bese enenhliziyo encane, esenomkhuba wokubeka unkosikazi nezingane isandla, kungasekho ukuthula ekhaya.
Induku yavele yaziwela yangavuma ukuvuka, yawela phakathi, yagcina izinciphela nangokosayizi.
Ukusuza kwathi ngila, into ebingenzeki.
Konke lokhu kwengeza ingcindezi yomqondo, odokotela belokhu bemyalela ukuthi makabonane nosonhlalakahle nodokotela wengqondo.
Lezi zigameko zombili zibangwa ukuvuvukala, nokuphunduleka ukusebenza kwendlala iThyroid.
Le ndlala ilapha ngasegilweni emqaleni, ihlukaniswe kabili.
Umsebenzi wayo ojwayelekile ukuba ngunondweba womzimba, lokhu kuchaza ukuthi okwenzeka emzimbeni kugqugquzelwa yile ndlala, uma ingasasebenzi izinto ziyonakala.
Imbangela yokuphunduleka ukusebenza kubangwa amasosha omzimba avele asuke ahlasele le ndlala, ayidlikidlikize igcine seyenza ukuthanda kwayo emzimbeni.
Emuva kokuthi lezi ziguli sihlangane nazo, kwangicacela ukuthi imbangela yalokhu kugula yile ndlala iThyroid.
Okuhle ukuthi lezi ziguli zabuyela ezimeni zazo zaphila, usisi wagcina emtholile nomtwana.
Ubaba wayeka nesibhaxu ekhaya, induku yabuyela ekusebenzeni kwayo; kwaba mnandi emndenini.
Engicela sikubone lapha ukuthi zonke izifo zinomsuka wazo, umsebenzi wami njengomthunywa wezempilo ukuthi uma isiguli siphambi kwami angenze konke okusemandleni ukuthi ngiyithole imbangela yokugula kwaso.
Kimi njengomuntu okuzofunwa usizo kuyena akungabi lula ukuthi leli gazi nalokhuya akuniki mpendulo, imbangela yokugula kwakho asiyazi, ngakhoke hamba uye kwabezenhlalakahle mhlawumbe kunento abazokusiza ngayo okanye hamba uye kudokotela oweluleka ngokomqondo kungenzeka kunesimo ongasinakile esenza ugule ngale ndlela.
Yebo kungaba yiqiniso lokho kodwa sonke siphila nengcindezi ethile emqondweni, angithi?
Omunye uzothi, phela dokotela abantu abamukeli, izinto azizweli ngokufana emzimbeni womuntu.
Nalokho ngiyakuvuma, kodwa uma ubuka lezi ziguli ezingenhla ukuba asithathanga isinyathelo sokucinga, sisuse izidindi ukuze sithole umthombo wokugula asazi ukuthi isimo sabo ngabe sinjani namhlanje, mhlawumbe namanje nengane ngabe akaze ayithole usisi, isibhaxu ngabe siyaqhubeka ekhaya, induku yenza ukuthanda kwayo kowesilisa.
Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi wena onenkinga yokuthola abantwana, wena oke wakhulelwa kodwa kwavele kwama nse, wangasazi isizathu, bheka ukuthi iziphi ezinye izimpawu ezisemzimbeni ngaphambi kokuthi ulahle ithemba, okanye uthi kwangena isilwane mhlawumbe imimoya yavala isibeletho.
Hamba uye kudokotela noma kumuphi umsizi wakho wezempilo ozokuhlolisisa afune imbangela.
Nathi thina bafowethu nodadewethu ezikhungweni zokusebenza ngezempilo, ake sifunisise imbangela yokugula kwabantu bethu.
Kubuhlungu kumuntu ogulayo okuthi isifo simhlukumeza, thina silokhu sithi ukugula akubonakali, yena engamile ethatha igazi, kushintshane odokotela ngento efanayo kulokhu kuthathwa igazi.
Ekugcineni anqobeke umuntu.
Bese kuba khona lokhu kokuvele sithi imbangela yi-acid noma isifo samathambo njalo nje.
Akekho okuphikisayo uma ngempela kunjalo kodwa ngithi asingakhohlwa ukuzibeka esayidini lesiguli okanye labasondelene nogulayo izikhathi eziningi.Mpilonde!
Isifikile iLand Rover Defender
INTATHELI YESOLEZWE ISIGCINE yethuliwe eNingizimu Afrika iLand Rover Defender okuyimoto osekunesikhathi kubikezelwa ukuthi isendleleni.
I-Defender yaziwa ngokuba yinqokonqoko yemoto eyinsimbi kayigobi ngenxa yokuthi ihamba noma yikuphi ngaphandle kokuxakeka.
Ifike ihlukene ngezinhlobo njengoba eyokuqala kuyiDefender 110 lapho amakhasimende ekhetha phakathi kwelayisha abagibelo abahlanu, abayisithupha noma abayisikhombisa.

Kukhona nenenjini engu-2.
0 litre turbocharged kaphethroli enamandla angu-221kw ne-torque engu-400Nm bese kuba khona ekadizili enamandla angu-177kw ne-torque engu-430Nm.

I-HSE ine-panoramic roof, Driver Assist Pack, izihlalo zesikhumba ezishisa ziphinde zibande namaMatrix LED Headlights.
I-Defender X eyakhelwe phezu kwesisekelo seHSE ifika nokhakhayi olumnyama nobhonethi, i-chrome, ama-brake calipers aphuzi, 700W Meridian Surround Sound System ene-subwoofer, Head-up Display nokunye.

Kuhle ukushintsha ukubukeka kwekhaya
Mbali KhanyileLo mkhuba ojwayele ukwenziwa uma kuzoba nabantu abaningi, usuphenduke into ejwayelekile kubantu okuholela ekutheni bangasiboni isidingo sokunaka ukubukeka kwengaphakathi lomuzi uma kungekho zinhlelo zemicimbi yemindeni.
Yize kunabantu abangasiboni nhlobo isidingo sokuzijwayeza ukuvuselela indlela okumele libukeke ngayo ingaphakathi le ndlu, bakhona abazinika isikhathi sokubheka indlela esesitayeleni eyenza ikhaya libukeke lilihle futhi liheha ngenxa yokuhlotshiswa kwalo.
UNksz Thando Sibisi weYellow Couch Concept okuyinkampani elungisa ingaphakathi lemizi, uthe okumqoka nokumele abantu bangakukhohlwa, wukuthi indlela ebukeka ngayo indlu isuke ichaza ukuthi uzithanda kangakanani umnikazi wayo.
"Kumqoka ukuthi abantu babheke imibala abapenda ngayo ngaphakathi endlini.
Isikhathi esiningi imibala egqamile nezothe ngendlela ehehayo.
Ngaphezulu kokubheka izindonga, nemibala yama-cushion ebekwa kosofa nayo iyakwazi ukwenza indlela elibukeka ngayo igumbi lokuphumula, lihlobe," kuchaza uNksz Sibisi.
Phakathi kwezinye zezimpahla zasendlini ezenza lihlobe ingaphakathi lomuzi ubale izibuko ezinkulu ezinamekwa odongeni athe kuhlotshiswa ngazo ephaseji, egumbini lokugeza, elokulala, elokuphumula nelokudlela.
Ubale nama-rug abekwa embhedeni uma sewendlalwe kahle, namalambu ahlobisayo esayidini lombhede.
Uthe okunye osekungenisile wukunamekwa kwamatshe obumba odongeni, okwenza indlu ibukeke ngendlela egculisayo nehehayo kwabathanda izindlu ezihlobile.
Echaza ngemibala edlisayo kulezi zinsuku, uthe ngumbala osasibhakabhaka othe ukuzotha, ompunga kanjalo negqamile okubalwa kuyo omhlophe, oluhlaza nombala onsundu.
"Okunye okubalulekile nokumele abantu bakwazi wukugwema ukugcwalisa kakhulu indlu ngezimpahla ezingenasidingo.
Indlu kumele iphefumule ukuze ibukeke kahle futhi ihehe amehlo akho noma kuthiwa sewenze ushintsho kuyona," kubeka le ntokazi.
Uthe inhlanzeko ngokunye okumele kube semqoka futhi bakuqaphele ngaso sonke isikhathi abantu noma ngabe umnikazi womuzi unekhono elingakanani lokuhlobisa indlu.
"Abantu kumele bangakubalekeli ukuthatha amaqhinga asetshenziswa emahhotela abalala kuwona uma bezikhiphile noma behambe ngokomsebenzi.
Amanye amaqhinga okuhloba bangawathatha kuwona," kuphetha uNksz Sibisi.

Inyakazisile esigabeni sayo iSeltos
KUNGENZEKA ukuthi iKia Seltos ifike izimbangi sezivele zinesikhashana zikhona kulesi sigaba samaSUV amancane kodwa akungabazeki ukuthi ukuba khona kwayo kuwususile umsindo.
Le moto itheleke eNingizimu Afrika ngoNovemba futhi abantu bayamukela kahle kwazise ngoDisemba kuthengwe ezingu-510.
Le SUV encane ingena ngaphansi kweKia Sportage yona ethe ukuba nkudlwana okuyimoto le nkampani ebisidinga uma ubheka ukuthi ezinye izinkampani sezingenisile kulesi sigaba esikhula mihla namalanga.
ISeltos ubude bayo bungu-4 315mm, u-1 800mm ububanzi bese kuthi ukuphakama kube ngu-1 620mm.
Lokhu kuyenza ivuleke kahle uma usungaphakathi.
Kodwa ngaphambi kokuthi singene ngaphakathi, ake siyibheke ngaphandle.
Indlela abayenze ngayo bayenze yabukeka nge tiger nose grille yayo enkulu ngaphambili.

Uyakwazi futhi ukuxhuma iselula nge-bluetooth bese udlala umculo.
Engingakuthandi kodwa wukuthi izipikha azizwakali kahle ngemuva.

Izihlalo ziyisikhumba futhi abagibeli abahlanu bahlala kahle, isikhala sanele.
Ngaphambili phakathi nendawo kukhona indawo yokuphumuza ingalo futhi nangemuva ikhona uma abagibeli bezoba babili.
Ebhuthini isikhala sikhona sempahla kodwa bengikuthola kunzima ukuyivala ngoba kumele uyishaye mawala.
Uma ingavalekile kahle iyakutshela kwi-instrument cluster.
I-Seltos ihamba ngenjini engu-1.
6 litre 4-cylinder kaphethroli engenayo i-turbo.
Inamandla angu-90kW ne-torque engu-151Nm.
Isebenzisa u-gearbox oyi-6 speed automatic.
Uma uyinyathela kancane ihamba kahle edolobheni futhi amagiya ashintsheka kahle.
Inkinga ibiba khona uma ususemgwaqweni ovulekile ilokhu ishintshashintsha amagiya ibheka ezohamba ngalo nangesikhathi futhi uthi ufaka amafutha mbijana ibange umsindo.
Bengize ngizishintshele mina amagiya ngoba uyakwazi ukwenza lokho uma uthanda.
Ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kodwa iyajwayeleka ugcine usuyazi indlela okumele uyinyathele ngayo ukuze niphathane kahle.
Ngo-100km ibidla amalitha kaphethroli angu-8.
8 litres futhi uma ithangi layo ligcwele, uhamba cishe amakhilomitha angu-600.
Bathi iyeza maduze ekadizili.
Ngakwezokuphepha, le moto ifika nama-airbag ayisithupha, amabhreki e-ABS, Electronic Brake Force Distribution, ama-sensor asiza uma upaka ngemuva nekhamera, Electronic Stability Control neHill-start Assist Control.

Akuxegiswe amalungelo okukhiqiza imigomo: Ramaphosa
UMENGAMELI Cyril Ramaphosa uthe iNingizimu Afrika ihlela ukusheshisa uhlelo lokukhiqiza imigomo yeCovid-19, uma amalungelo obunikazi bempahla (Intellectual property) exegiswa yiziphathimandla zokuhweba zamazwe omhlaba (World Trade Organisation).
Uthe uhulumeni wakhe ufuna ukuthi kuhoxiswe okwesikhashana amalungelo obunikazi bempahla athinta ukukhiqizwa kwemigomo yeCovid-19 (Trade-Related Aspects of Intellectual Property Rights (TRIPS).
Usho lokhu encwadini ayibhalela umphakathi masonto onke, izolo.
Ukumiswa okwesikhashana kwamalungelo uthe kuzosiza amazwe ampofu ukuze azikhiqizele imigomo azoyisabalalisa emazweni awo, njengoba umhlaba wonke ubhekene nenkinga yokuthi izinkampani ezinamalungelo okukhiqiza imigomo imvamisa okungezasemazweni anothile, ziyehluleka ukukhiqiza umthamo ozokwanela wonke amazwe kanti futhi imigomo iyabiza.
"Lesi simo senza ukuthi amazwe anothile aqhubeke nohlelo lwawo lokugoma, antulayo ahlale elinde ukuthenga umgomo kwacebile.
Abantu emazweni antulayo bayafa kusalindiwe ngoba kunohlu olude lwabalinde ukuthenga," kusho uRamaphosa.
Uthe ngenxa yokuthi imigomo idingeka kuwo wonke amazwe kuholela ekutheni abakhokha kakhulu kube ibona abayithola kuqala.
"Imigomo kufanele itholwe yibo bonke abantu hhayi abakhokha kakhulu," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi u-55% wemigomo yeCovid-19 ukhiqizwa eMpumalanga ye-Asia, u-40% ukhiqizwa e-Europe naseNorth America, i- Afrika ne-South America bakhiqiza imigomo engaphansi kuka-5%.
Uthe iNingizimu Afrika ingelinye lamazwe amahlanu e-Afrika akwaziyo ukukhiqiza umgomo weCovid-19.
"Yize iNingizimu Afrika isiyithengile imigomo okuzogonywa ngayo iningi labantu bese kuvikeleka abanye, kodwa sisesikhulu isidingo sokuthi nathi sikhiqize imigomo ukuze sizivikele," kusho yena.
Isiphakamiso sikaRamaphosa sokuthi kumiswe okwesikhashana amalungelo obunikazi bempahla sesekwa nawumengameli wase-America uMnuz Joe Biden nenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO).
Qikelela ngomphako  owulungisela ingane esikoleni
NJENGOBA kuvulwe izikole abanye abazali babhekana nomqansa wokungazi ukuthi wuhlobo luni lomphako abangawulungisela izingane zabo.
Lokhu kudideka ukubona ngabanye babo abenza ukudla okuphambene nalokho okumele bakulungisele izingane, nokudingeka ezikoleni njengoba ezinye zezikole zikubeka kucace ukuthi kumele ingane iphathe ukudla okunempilo.
Imvamisa lezi ezinabazali abangakunaki ukubaluleka kohlobo lokudla okumele bakulingise, uzifica ziphethe ukudla okungenayo impilo nokungenazo nhlobo izakhamzimba.
Izitsha zazo zijwayele ukuba nomphako ogcwele izoso, uswidi omningi, amakhekhe wodwa noma ijusi enoshukela omningi ngokweqile.
Umpheki uChef Nono Mtshali, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi umzali enze ukudla okungeke kubuye ekhaya kungadliwanga nhlobo yingane.
"Abazali kumele benzele izingane zabo ukudla okuhehayo okuzokwenza ukuthi izingane zikuqede.
Ngakho ukwenza uhlobo lomphako owodwa ngoba unqena, kungagcina sekuholela ekutheni ingane yakho ingakuthokozeli nhlobo ukudla umphako wayo esikoleni," kusho uChef NonoUthe uma ingane ibuya nomphako ekhaya kumele umzali azibuze ukuthi kungani ibuye nakho?
Uthe ziningi izindlela ezingasetshenziswa ngabazali ezingenza ukuthi izingane zabo zihlezi zikuthakasela ukuvula izitsha esikoleni uma sezihlangene nezinye izingane.
Phakathi kohlobo lokudla athe abazali bangakufaka, ubale isemishi elithakwe nokudla okufana noshizi, upholoni, lettuce, cucumber, umkhwepha wenkukhu nakho konke okunye okwenza ukuthi isemishi lihehe.
Uthe isidlo ebesidliwa ngobusuku bayizolo esifana nepasta, i-lasagne kungaphathwa yizingane ezikoleni.
Ama-wrap athakwe ngezindlela ezahlukene uthe angafakwa esitsheni somphako wengane.
"Asikho isidingo sokuthi ingane ihlezi yenzelwa amasemishi uma iya esikoleni.
Izingane ziyacikeka wukudla into eyodwa ngaso sonke yisikhathi yingakho kusemqoka ukuthi abazali basebenzise amacebo ahlukile," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi ukudla kwengane kumele kuqikelelwe ukuthi kunezakhamzimba.
Uthe kumqoka nokuthi abazali bajwayeze izingane zabo ukuthi ziphuze kakhulu amanzi kunejusi.
"Ingane ingaqala ukujwayezwa lo mkhuba wokuthanda ukuphuza amanzi ekhaya ukuze ingabi nayo inkinga yokuwaphuza nasesikoleni.
"Omunye umpheki, uNksz Ntokozo Khanyile, uthe ama-sliders afakwe i-mince, utamatisi, u-lettuce nocucumber ngokunye abazali abangakwenzela izingane.
Uthe i-sauce kumele abazali badlalele kude nayo ngoba inomkhuba wokona ukudla kwengane njengoba isikhathi esiningi yenza ukuthi ifike nakho esikoleni sekumanzi futhi kungasanambitheki ngendlela efanele.
"Kunokuthi kube nama-chips eceleni kwesitsha somphako, umzali akafake ukherothi ongaphekiwe noshizi we-cheddar namagrebhisi, ubhanana noma i-aphula.
Ibhodlela elinamanzi lisemqoka kakhulu emphakweni wengane.
I-yoghurt ngezinye zezinto ezinezakhamzimba abazali abangazifaka, " kusho uNksz Khanyile.
Uphethe ngokuthi ama- meat balls nawo ayathakaselwa kakhulu yizingane.
Uthe umzali kumele aqikelele ukuthi ufaka amathathu kuphela njengoba esuke ehambisana ne-wrap kwesinye isikhathi.

Bajimisa abafuna ‘imizimba  yasehlobo’ eMoses Mabhida
Ngenxa yeCovid-19 kulikhuni ukuthi abantu bahlangane ezindaweni zokujima ngoba imithetho isalawula abantu ukuthi bangabi baningi kakhulu endaweni eyodwa, ukugwema ukubhebhetheka kwegciwane.
Lesi sizathu senze uMnqobi Kunene nozakwabo * -Ayanda Mthembu, bathatha isinqumo sokusiza abantu ngokubajimisa besebenzisa iPeoples Park, eMoses Mabhida, eThekwini okuyindawo evulekile.
Lokho bathe bakwenzele ukuthi kube lula kubona bonke abantu ukuthi bazozivocavoca bebaningi endaweni eyodwa ngoba ivulekile ukugwema ukuthelelana ngeCovid-19 uma kukhona onayo.
Sibone kukuhle ukuthi abantu sibalekelele sisebenzisa iPeoples Park ukuze bangasabi ukuza ejimini.
Siba namakilasi asekuseni kusuka ngo-7:30 ekuseni ngoMsombuluko kuya kuLwesihlanu.
Ngenxa yokuthi sikala isikhathi kwabasuke beze ejimini kubakhona namakilasi aba semini nantambama ukuze nabasebenzayo bakwazi ukuza ejimini uma benesifiso.
Ofuna ukujima ufika axhumane nathi khona eMoses Mabhida ngoba sihlala sikhona bese kuba nomnikelo abasinika wona esivumelana ngawo nabo," kusho uMnqobi.
UMnqobi uthe abagcini ngokujimisa abantu abasuke besePeoples Park kodwa bajimisa nabaphesheya kwezilwandle besebenzisa izinkundla zokuxhumana.
Ngaphandle kokujimisa abantu abaningi, bayakwazi nokujimisa umuntu yedwa, uma ebacela.
Baveze ukuthi bayatholakala ezinkundleni zokuxhumana, kanti ofuna ukuthola imininingwane angabheka uMnqobi Kunene kuFacebook, Twitter naku-Instargram.
