Bafuna yenyuke intela yeziphuzo ezinoshukela
INHLANGANO egqugquzela ukuthi abantu ukuthi badle ukudla okunempilo ukuze bagweme izifo, ifuna inyuselwe ku-20% intela kashukela kuleli.
Njengamanje intela kashukela kuleli ingu-11%, iHealthy Living Alliance (HEALA) ithi ushukela otholakala eziphuzweni ezinoshukela ungaphezulu kwalokho okumele ngabe uyikho yingakho kumele izinkampani ezikhiqiza lezo ziphuzo zikhokhe intela.
UMnuz Lawrence Mbalati ohola lo mkhankaso kwi-HEALA, uthe ushukela otholakala kuzo unomthelela wokuthi abantu bakhuluphale ngokweqile, okubenza ukuthi bangenwe isifo sikashukela, babe nezinkinga zenhliziyo neminye imidlavuza.
Uqhube wathi ngo-2016 uhulumeni wafaka umthetho wokulawula usawoti ofakwa ngesikhathi kukhiqizwa ukudla ngenhloso yokuthi abantu bangadli ukudla okunosawoti omningi ngoba usawoti unomthelela omubi empilweni yomuntu nakushukela kumele kwenziwe okufanayo.
"Umuntu kumele adle ushukela ongamathisipuni ayisithupha kuya kwayisishiyagalombili ngosuku.
Abakhiqizi beziphuzo bafaka ushukela omningi ngakho yibo okumele bakhokhe intela, asifuni ukuthi le ntela ikhokhwe umphakathi ngoba uvele uphila ngaphansi kwengcindezi.
Ukwenyuka kwentela kuzokwenza ukuthi abakhiqizi balezi ziphuzo babuyekeze izithako zabo behlise njengoba sibona sekukhona iziphuzo okuthiwa zinoshukela owehlisiwe noma ezingenawo ushukela njengamanje, kodwa emlonyeni ushukela uzwakala ngendlela efanayo," kusho yena.
Uthe ngalo mkhankaso wabo bafisa ukuthi ungqongqoshe wezezimali kuleli le ntela ayifake kwibhajethi yalo nyaka kodwa uyazi ukuthi kungenzeka kungenzeki ngoba kuningi okubhekwayo.
"Ushukela awunayo intela ngoba ngumuntu olawula ukuthi uwufaka kangakanani kodwa abakhiqiza beziphuzo ezinoshukela bona kumele bakhokhe intela ngoba yibo abafaka ushukela omningi umthengi akakwazi ukukulawula lokho.
Njengamanje uhulumeni wenza imithetho elawula ukufakwa kukasawoti emikhiqizweni yakuleli ngenhloso yokwehlisa izifo.
"Le mali iwusizo kuhulumeni isetshenziselwa ukwenza ucwaningo lwezempilo nakwezinye izinto.
Njengoba sibhekene neCovid-19 kudingeka imali eningi, uma le ntela ingenyuka ibe ngu-20%, uhulumeni uzoqoqa imali eningi engasiza nasezinhlelweni zokuthengwa komgomo weCovid-19," kusho yena.
Izinkinga zingakwenzi uzibe ucansi
UKUYA ocansini isikhathi esiningi kuhambisana nenjabulo nokugijima kwegazi emzimbeni nemicabango emihle ejabulisa imizwa yomuntu.
Lokhu uma kungahambisani noma kukhona lapho kushayisana khona, kwenza kube nzima ukuthi umuntu alulangazelele ucansi.
Ukuhlasela kweCovid-19 nokuphila ngaphansi kwesikhathi sikathaqa kuhambisana nezinkinga eziningi kubantu.
Lokhu kwenza abanye abantu bagcine sebegxila kakhulu ekucabangeni ngezinkinga, umqondo ulibalele ngemcabango yocansi nokwenza kube nzima ukuthi izithandani zivukelwe yimizwa yocansi kalula.
Ungoti wezempilo nezobudlelwane uDkt Nomcebo Mthembu uthe yonke imicabango yomuntu ihambisana nokusebenza ngendlela komqondo, lokhu okusho ukuthi uma umqondo ugxile kakhulu ezinkingeni nemizwa yocansi iyacindezeleka ngoba akukho okujabulisa umuntu ngaleso sikhathi.
UDkt Mthembu uthe yingakho behlala bekugcizelela ukuthi abantu bangalushalazeli ucansi uma benezinkinga.
Ukwenza ucansi uthe kungenye yezinto ezelapha umuntu nomqondo uswabuluke kube khona okumjabulisyao phezu kwezinkinga.
"Kunama hormones athintekayo uma wenza ucansi, yingakho umuntu kuba khona ubumnandi abuzwayo nobumjabulisa ezwe nasemzimbeni kumnandi kahle.
Ukungalwenzi ucansi ngoba kusenezinkinga obhekene nazo akukusizi, kunalokho ucansi yilona olungasiza ukwehlisa ingcindezi ngaleso sikhathi,"kusho uDkt Mthembu.
Eqhuba uthe uma abantu behlala ndawonye kuyenzeka abanye bagcine sebengalukhuthaleli ucansi noma omunye angabe esasicabangela isithandwa sakhe athathe ngokuthi sihambisana naye ngokwezinkinga zasendlini nemcabango.
"Ucansi ngesinye isikhathi alusho ukuya embhedeni kuphela.
Ziningi izindlela zokulenza lwehluke, ukushintsha indawo olwenzela kuyo.
Ngesinye isikhathi ningaze nibe sekhaya.
Lungaqala ngaphandle, nihambe niyoshaywa umoya epaki noma emnyango egcekeni nibambane ngezandla nixoxe izindaba zenu.
""Imizwa izokhula ngokubambana ngezandla nokugijima kwegazi, indlela enibukana ngayo izogcina ithinta imizwa nizibone seningena enkonzweni yasekamelweni,"kusho uDkt Mthembu.
Ephetha uthe ucansi aludingi ucatshangwa kakhulu nokuhlelelwa ngoba konke kuqala ngemizwa yabantu nemicabango efanele emqondweni womuntu.
Sehle kakhulu isibalo sezimoto ezidayisiwe
YIZE ukudayiswa kwezimoto eNingizimu Afrika ngenyanga edlule kwehlile uma kuqhathaniswa nesikhathi esifanayo sangonyaka odlule kodwa kungcono kunangoJuni.
Izibalo ezikhishwe yiNational Association of Automobile Association of South Africa (Naamsa) zikhomba ukuthi isibalo sokuthengwa kwezimoto ngoJuni sehle ngo-13 646 noma u-26.
6% uma siqhathaniswa noJulayi wonyaka odlule.
Zibe ngu-32 396 izimoto ezidayisiwe kanti nyakenye zazingu-46 042.
Uma kuqhathaniswa noJuni kungcono ngoba izimoto ezadayiswa zazingu-31 867 nokuyisibalo esehle ngo-30.
7% owadayiswa ngoJuni wonyaka odlule.
INaamsa ithe nesibalo sezimoto ezithunyelwa ngaphandle sehlile njengoba zibe ngu-24 706 kanti ngesikhathi esifanayo ngonyaka odlule zazingu-35 087.
Lesi yisibalo esehle ngo-2 736 noma * -19.
7% uma kuqhathaniswa no-13 859 wangoJulayi ngonyaka odlule.
Isibalo sezimoto ezithunyelwa ngaphandle sehle ngo-10 381 noma u-29.
6% uma kuqhathaniswa no-35 087 wangonyaka odlule.
Kuphinde kwashona abanye abawu315 kuleli
KUSHONE abanye abantu abangamakhulu amathathu neshumi nesihlanu (315) eNingizimu Afrika emuva kokuhaqwa yiCorona, okwenza isibalo sanyukela ku7 812 kuzwelonke.
Lezi zindaba zidalulwe nguNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, ezinkundleni zokuxhumana izolo.
"Njenganamhlanje, isibalo esesiqinisekisiwe sabantu asebehaqwe iCovid-19 sesifinyelele ku482 169, isibalo sasebesishiyile sesifinyelele ku7 812 kanti asebeluleme sebengu309 601," kusho uMkhize kuTwitter.
Kulabantu aba315 abasishiyile emhlabeni kubalwa abawu121 base-Eastern Cape, abawu96 baseGauteng, abawu55 baKwaZulu-Natal, 34 baseWestern Cape nabangu9 baseNorth West.
"Sidlulisa amazwi enduduzo kwabathandiweyo abasishiyile futhi siyabonga kubasebenzi bezempilo ebebelapha abasishiyile," kusho uMkhize.
Sebebonke asebesishiyile emhlabeni bami kanje: Eastern Cape (1 700), Free State (154), Gauteng (1932), KwaZulu-Natal (767), Limpopo (67), Mpumalanga (65), North West (81), Northern Cape (29) naseWestern Cape (3017).
Isibalo sabahaqekile kuzwelonke sona simi kanje: Eastern Cape (77055), Free State (20398), Gauteng (171574), KwaZulu-Natal (73919), Limpopo (8240), Mpumalanga (13280), North West (18811), Northern Cape (4402), Western Cape (94440) no50 wabangaziwa ukuthi abakuphi.
Sebebangaphezu kuka11 000 abantu abahaqekayo kuleli, okwenza lesi sibalo sinyukele ku482 167.
Izimoto zakwa-Opel sezidayiswa yiPeugeot Citroen SA
IZIMOTO zakwa-Opel sezisatshalaliswa yiPeugeot Citroen South Africa (PCSA) eNingizimu Afrika.
Lokhu kuqale ngoJanuwari 1 ngo-2021.
Kwenzeka ngemuva kokuzalwa kwenkampani entsha iStellantis, lezi zinkampani zombili ezingaphansi kwayo.
Phambilini i-Opel bekungeyakwaGeneral Motors (GM) kusuka ngo-1929 kuya ku-2017.
Kusuka ngo-2017 bekungeyakwaGroupe PSA, kuze kuba wuJanuwari 16 lapho ingene khona ngaphansi kweStallantis.
Ukumenyezelwa kwalezi zindaba kuqondene nombiko oqinisekisiwe wokuthi i-Opel Corsa entsha, izoqala ukutholakala kule nyanga.
Ifika nenjini engu-1.
2 litre kaphethiloli eyi-3 cylinder enamandla angu-55kW.
Uma iqhathaniswa nendala, inciphise isisindo ngo-108kg kodwa icishe ilingane nendala yize isikhala sebhuthi sisikhulu kunendala.
Intengo iqala kuR289 900.
Ingcindezi kwabangazitholi izingane
ABESIFAZANE abanomlando wengcindezi yomphefumulo kunamathuba amaningi okuthi babe nenkinga yokukhulelwa.
Ongoti bezempilo bathi imithi yokwelapha ingcindezi yomphefumulo nayo inawo umthelela wokuthi abantu besifazane abayisebenzisayo babe nenkinga yokuthola abantwana okwengeza ingcindezi, igcine ingaselapheki.
Lezi zinkinga ongoti bezempilo bathi zigcina zidale ukuthi kube muncu ekhaya.
USolwazi Renata Schoeman owungoti wokwelulekwa ngokomphefumulo, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi owesifazane onale nkinga ahlale enaye umeluleki wezomphefumulo ngesikhathi eqala indlela yokwelashwa umgudu wenzalo yikhona ezomeluleka uma kwenzeka kuba nesidingo.
"Inkinga yomgudu wenzalo kwabesifazane nakwabesilisa iyefana kodwa abesifazane bezwela kakhulu kuyona ngoba umphakathi uhlale ubheke owesifazane kakhulu ngokuthi athole izingane emndenini.
Uma leso sifiso singasenzeki esikhathini esiningi uzithola ehlukumezeka.
Kule nyanga yabantu besifazane kugcizelelwa ukuthi kube nokulingana kwabesifazane nabesilisa, kubalulekile ukubheka ukuthi kubaluleke kangakanani ukuthi uma kuba nenkinga yongakwazi ukuthola abantwana aphathwe ngendlela elinganayo kungakhathaleki ukuthi ungowesilisa noma ungowesifazane," kusho yena.
Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithi uma owesifazane nowesilisa behluleka ukukhulelisana esikhathini esingangonyaka beya ocansini olungavikelekile, lokho kuchazwa ngokuthi banenkinga yokuthola abantwana.
Sekumele babone odokotela abazobasiza ukuze bazame ukulungisa le nkinga.
I-WHO ithi abathandanayo abanale nkinga bangu-48 million emhlabeni.
ENingizimu Afrika ithi bangu-20% abantu abanenkinga yokuthola izingane, e-Afrika abahlaselwe yile nkinga balinganiselwa ku-30 kuya ku-40% ngenxa yokuthi ezempilo eziqondene nokwelashwa kwale nkinga kuleli zwekazi azikho esimeni esihle.
"Abesifazane abanenkinga kubathatha isikhathi ukuthi bamukele ukuthi banenkinga, kwesinye isikhathi bazisola kube sengathi kunokuthile abakwenzile okuholele ekutheni babe nenkinga, abanye bayacasuka bafise ukuhlala bodwa okuholele ekutheni isikhathi esimnandi sokujabula komndeni singabe sisaba khona ngoba owesifazane uhlale ekhala," kusho uSolwazi Schoeman.
Uthe yize udaba lwenkinga yokukhulelwa kuyinkinga okumele yelashwe ngodokotela abaqondene nalo mkhakha kodwa iba nomthelela ezinkingeni zokuphazamiseka komqondo zona ezidinga udokotela wezengqondo.
Ukubhema kwandisa amathuba okuba nesifo senhliziyo
Inhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithe * -20% wabantu abangu-1.
9 million ababulawa yisifo senhliziyo ngonyaka emhlabeni, lesi sifo sisuke sidalwe wukuthi bayabhema.
Le nhlangano nenhlangano yenhliziyo emhlabeni iWorld Heart Federation, basho lokhu nje namhlanje wusuku lokuxwayisa umphakathi ngalesi sifo iWorld Heart Day.
UDkt Eduarado Bianco ongusihlalo wophiko olubhekele umthelela kagwayi kwabaphethwe yisifo senhliziyo, uthe ukubhema ugwayi noma ukuhogela ugwayi obhenywa ngomunye umuntu kungakubeka engozini yokuhlaselwa yisifo senhliziyo.
"Ukuthatha isinqumo sokuyeka ugwayi kungehlisa amathuba okuthi uthole lesi sifo ngo-50%.
Uma kubhekwa ubufakazi obukhona bokuthi ugwayi uyingozi kangakanani empilweni nokuthi uma uwuyeka ungasizakala kangakanani, kwenza ukuthi kube nesidingo sokuthi abangafuni ukuyeka ugwayi yize benolwazi babizwe ngabantu ababudedengu.
Inhlangano yenhliziyo kumele ibe nemikhankaso efundisa iphinde iqwashise umphakathi ngengozi kagwayi enhliziyweni," kusho yena.
Uthe ucwaningo abalwenzile luveza ukuthi ugwayi ongayenzi intuthu uma ubhenywa unomthelela ekufeni kwabantu abangu-200 000 ngonyaka emhlabeni.
"Ugwayi owaziwa nge-ecigarattes uholela ekutheni umuntu anyukelwe wumfutho wegazi, okungesinye sezizathu eziholela ekutheni abantu baphathwe yisifo senhliziyo," kuxwayisa uBianco.
Ucwaningo lweWHO luveza ukuthi iziguli ezinesifo senhliziyo nezinomfutho wegazi ophezulu kunamathuba amaningi okuthi zibe neCovid-19.
Kulolu cwaningo kuvela ukuthi kubantu ababulawe yiCovid-19 e-Italy, * -67% wabo ubunezinga lomfutho wegazi ophezulu kanti eSpain kuvela ukuthi * -43% wababulawe yilesi sifo ubunesifo senhliziyo.
UDkt Vinayak Prasad wophiko olubhekele umthelela kagwayi ezifeni kwiWHO, uthe kubalulekile ukuthi ohulumeni bamazwe ahlukene babe nezinhlelo zokunqanda izifo ezidalwa wukubhenywa kukagwayi emazweni abo.
"Uma singase sikwazi ukuyekisa abantu ukubhema ugwayi kungehla izibalo zabantu abalaliswa ezibhedlela ikakhulukazi njengoba sibhekene neCovid-19.
Ukwenyusa intela kagwayi nokuvalwa kwezikhangiso zikagwayi kungasiza ekutheni abanye abantu bayeke ukubhema, " kusho uDkt Prasad.
Igabe ngobuchwepheshe iBMW 3 Series
FANELESIBONGE BENGUNJENGOBA zingenisile izimoto eziphakeme amaSport Utility Vehicle emhlabeni jikelele kodwa iBMW 3 Series ilokhu imile ayiyi ndawo.
Ime kufanele ngoba ukuyibuka kude nokungena phakathi kuyo uhambe ngayo kuyakukhanyisela ukuthi yimoto eseqophelweni eliphezulu kangakanani.
Kule minyaka edlule kwaBMW badayise izigidi zama-3 Series nokufakazela ukuthandwa nezinga layo.
Ekhona njengamanje iG20 ayikhiqizwa embonini yale nkampani iPlant Rosslyn ePitoli njengokudlule kodwa itheleka kwelengabadi isiphelele.
Ngaphandle iyabukeka futhi yona ithe ukuba nkudlwana kunendala.
Ngaphambili inamaLED lights kanjalo nama-fog lights angamaLED ngezansi.
Enze omkhulu umsebenzi kunenkungu ekhasa phansi ngikhuphuka eMthonjaneni.
Iziphathimandla kumele zisilungisele olayini abamaka umgwaqo zifake namakati ngoba kuba nzima impela.
Nangemuva kukhona amaLED lights athanda ukuba mpisholo mbijana nayenza ibukeke kahle.
Ngaphakathi akubuzwa ukuthi yimoto yomndeni kwazise ivulekile.
Inezihlalo zesikhumba ezilayisha abagibeli abahlanu kanti ebhuthini isikhala wudedangendlale.
Kuba yinto elula nje ukulalisa izihlalo bese sithi xaxa.
Uma isihamba emgwaqweni iwubukhosi.
Inenjini eyi-2.0 turbo eyi-four cylinder kaphethroli.
Inamandla angu-135kW/300Nm bese isebenzisa u-gearbox ozishintshayo.
Ngo-100km ibidla amalitha kaphethroli angu-7.4.
Iyanamathela emgwaqeni futhi okungichazayo wukuthi intofonotofo futhi ithule.
Amajika iwashaya kalula ngaphandle kwenkinga futhi amandla iwathumela kahle emasondweni ngokushesha.
I-BMW 3 Series inenqwaba yobuchwepheshe besimanje obenza impilo ibe lula.
Kubalwa ukuthi isho uma kukhona imoto eseceleni kwakho, izihambele futhi izijikise yona isiteringi uma iphuma emzileni, izihlehlele uma iphuma lapho ipake khona, Head-Up Display, ikhamera ngemuva nokunye.
Ine-touchscreen lapho udlala khona umsakazo, ufunda izindaba, uxhume iselula nge-Apple CarPlay, ubone imininingwane ngemoto nokunye.
Uphinde ukhulume nayo ngokuthi "Hey BMW" bese uyitshela ofuna ikwenze njengokushintsha amazinga okushisa ngaphakathi.
I-BMW 320i ikahle iphelele kodwa uma ufuna ecishe ibe ngangayo kodwa enamandla futhi eyongayo, i320d iyona umakhonya.InaniIqala kuR693 800
Uqwashisa abazali ngokumele bakwenze njengoba izikole zivuliwe
ABAZALI babhekene nomsebenzi omkhulu wokulungiselela izingane zabo ngokomqondo njengoba sezibuyele esikoleni.
Lokhu kushiwo uNksz Nqobile Kweyama oyi-Educational Psychologist, oluleka abazali ngokumele bakulindelele njengoba izikole zivulwe phansi kwezimo ezingajwayelekile.
Uthe abazali kumele bangazifihleli izingane, bazitshele amaqiniso ukuthi isikole asisafani nakuqala.
Ukugqoka izifonyo yinto ebingenziwa esikoleni, uNksz Kweyama uthe izingane kumele ziqeqeshwe emakhaya.
"Abazali kumele baphendule yonke imibuzo izingane ezinayo ngesimo esibhekene naso.
Bajwayele ukuzifihlela kodwa sekumele zitshelwe amaqiniso.
"Okuqaphelekayo wukuthi abazali yibona abasaba kakhulu ukwedlula izingane ngalolu bhubhane.
Njengoba kuvulwe izikole namanye amabanga esazolandela, besaba ukuthi izingane zabo aziphephile," kuchaza uNksz Kweyama.
Ugcizelele ukuthi lesi yisikhathi sokuthi abazali babambisane nothisha ngokwedlulele.
Uthe kumele izingane zifundiswe ngendlela efanele yokugqoka izifonyo, zijwayele nokugeza izandla ekhaya.
Uveze ukuthi lokhu kuzokwenza ukuthi kube lula nasesikoleni.
"Izingane azifuni ukungakhululeki, abazali kumele baqinisekise ukuthi bazitholela izifonyo ezingeke zizixake ukuze zingazikhumuli," kusho yena.
Mayelana nomsebenzi omningi wesikole ozobhekana nabafundi njengoba bebehleli emakhaya izinyanga ezimbili, uNksz Kweyama uthe nalapho kudingeka izingane zesekwe ngokomqondo.
Ukhuthaze abazali ukuthi baxhumane nabeluleki bezengqondo uma bebona ukuthi isimo singaphezu kwamandla.
Nokho uthe ucwaningo luveza ukuthi izingane ziyakwazi ukusheshe zibambe futhi ziyakwazi nokumelana nanoma yisiphi isimo.
Uthe zidinga ukwesekwa ngayo yonke indlela.
Abafundi baka-matric nabakwaGrade 7 bavule okokuqala ngoMsombuluko kuleli, emuva kokuhlala emakhaya kusukela ngoMashi ngemuva kukuqubuka kweCovid- 19.
Abanye abazali babe manqika ngokubuyisela izingane ezikoleni besabela ukuphepha kwazo.
Kunzima ukudlulisa kwabashonelwa yizingane zisencane
UKUSHONELWA yingane isanda kuzalwa, yinto ehlale yenzeka kwabesifazane abaningi, kodwa bambalwa abathola usizo nokwesekwa okwanele ukuze bakwazi ukuqhubeka kahle nempilo yabo.
Ziningi nezinto ezenziwayo uma owesifazane ezothola umntwana, njengokubikwa kwesisu kubo kayise wengane, ukwenziwa kwebaby shower, ukuyetha amagama, ukuyibheka ubulili kanjalo nokuthengwa kwezimpahla nokulungiselela kabusha igumbi ezolala kulo nonina.
Abantu abasekhaya nabo basuke sebelindele izindaba ezimnandi zokuzwa ukuthi usebelethile esibhedlela unina wengane.
Kodwa kwabanye abantu besifazane kuba yizindaba ezimbi zokuthi  ingane  ishonile esayibeletha noma engakabelethi unina.
Lokhu akukhethi bala,kwenzeka ngendlela efanayo kwizimpunyela, osaziwayo, abantu abasemazingeni aphansi ngisho nakubahlengikazi nodokotela besifazane.
UNtombi Ngcobo ongumculi, umethuli wezinhlelo  zethelevishini nomsakazi ungomunye wosaziwayo abake babhekana nalesi simo.
Emuva kokushonelwa yindodana wezwa ubuhlungu obungapholi kalula kwaze kwaba uthola usizo ekhaya nakongoti.
Uthe yingakho waqala nenhlangano ebizwa ngeMother's of Angel lapho kuhlangana khona abesifazane abashonelwe yizingane bakhulume ngezimo zabo nongoti abahlukene.
Owesifazane owashonelwa ingane  ngo-2001 utshele leli phephandaba ukuthi kwakungelula ukwamukela kwaze kwaba uthola indodana eminyakeni emibili eyedlule.
Yize engakhohliwe yingane  yakhe yokuqala kodwa uthe akusefani, usethanda ukuxola njengoba eseze waba nomunye umntwana.
"Kujwayelekile emakhaya ukuthi umuntu uma eshonelwe ingane  kube yinto edlulayo ngoba nomngcwabo wenziwa ngakusasa.
Into ebhekwa abakusiza ngayo ukuthi bakugeze.
Akekho umuntu ozikhathazayo ngokukubuza ukuthi kuyaba yini ngcono.
Ngibona sekungcono manje ngoba esibhedlela uyabuzwa ukuthi uyalufuna yini usizo bakululeke.
Mina kwakuba buhlungu njalo uma kukhona onengane encane ekhaya noma uma ungibona eyomuntu engangixukuza naye," kusho lo wesifazane.
Ungoti wezempilo kumkhakha weSociology eBoston University, uDeborah Carr, uke waveza kulo nyaka kwiwebsite yeFatherly ukuthi nakobaba kusuke kuzwela benengcindezi ngokomqondo nokhwantalala.
UDeborah uthi  nanoma yimuphi umuntu wesilisa kuyamkhathaza ukushonelwa yingane ngoba emqondweni wakhe usuke ezilungiselele ukuyinakekela ayivikele.
Ukushona kwengane kwenza owesilisa azibeke icala noma azisole ngezinto engabe uzenzile ukushintsha isimo.
Okungakusiza ukudlulisa -Ukubonana nongoti abeluleka imindeni abazokwazi ukukulekelela ukudlula kulesi simo.
-Hlangana nabanye abantu abake babhekana nesimo esifanayo nabazokwazi ukuthi uzizwa kanjani.
-Ungajahi ukuthola omunye umntwana ukuvala isikhala noma ungasondelani nengane yomunye umuntu ukuvala isikhala seyakho.
-Qhubeka wenze izinto ezikujabulisayo nenhliziyo izoya ngokwamukela futhi ukhumbule nobumnandi bempilo.
-Khuluma nophathina wakho ngendlela ozizwa ngayo nithole usizo kuze kube niyahlela ukuthola omunye umntwana.
I-Corona kayiyi ndawo: inhlangano yezeMpilo
SEKUPHELE izinsuku ezinhlanu izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 kuleli ziba ngaphezulu kuka-5 000 ngosuku.
Lokhu kwenyuka kwezibalo zeCovid-19 kutolikwa ngokuthi sesisemome isiqubu sesithathu sokuhlasela kweCovid-19 kuleli.
Kwezinye izifundazwe lesi siqubu sesingenile.
Izibalo zakamuva zikhomba ukuthi bangu-5 074 abahaqwe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 okuholele ekutheni izibalo zabahaqwe yileli gciwane zibe ngu-1 696 564.
Ababulewe yileli gciwane emahoreni angu-24 bangu-56 osekuholele ekutheni babe ngu-56 974 ababulelwe yileli gciwane selokhu langena kuleli.
Kulaba bantu abangu-56 abashonile, abayisithupha ngabaseFree State, abayisikhombisa abaseGauteng, abangu-15 abaseNorthern Cape, oyedwa owaKwaZulu-Natal, abayisithupha abaseWestern Cape.
UMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli esitatimendeni uthe u-93% wabebenaleli gciwane sebeluleme okusho ukuthi abantu abangu-1 578 033 sebeluleme.
UDkt David Nabarro wenhlangano yezempilo emhlabeni i-World Health Organization (WHO), ucashunwe kweminye imithombo yezindaba ethi okwamanje ukuqeda iCovid-19 akuyona into engenzeka.
Uthe igciwane lizoqhubeka nokuziphindaphinda okuzoholela ekutheni imigomo ekhona ingabe isasebenza ngendlela ebilindelekile.
Into okumele yenzeke ukuthi abantu bafunde ukuphila nalo igciwane.
"Ukuphila neCovid-19 yinto okumele sizifundise yona ngoba kuyabonakala ukuthi leli gciwane lisazoba khona isikhathi eside," kusho yena.
Uqhube wathi into okumele abantu bayiqaphele kakhulu ukuthi ukuthelelana kwaleli gciwane kulawuleke, kungabi phezulu kakhulu.
Abama-medical aid bazokhokhela ukugonywa kwamalungu
WONKE ama-medical aid kuleli azokukhokhela ukugonywelwa kweCovid-19 kwamalungu awo.
Umkhandlu wama-medical aid kuleli uthi ukugonyelwa kweCovid-19, sekufakiwe ngaphansi kwezinto ezikhokhelwa yi-medical, iPrescribed Minimum Benefits (PMB).
UNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo kuleli, uDkt Zweli Mkhize, wamukele indlela ahlelwe ngayo ama-PMB kuwo okukhona nokuthi i-medical aid ikhokhele nokwelashwa okuphuthumayo, kuhlanganisa nezifo ezingu-25 ezingamahlalakhona kanye nezinye izifo ezingu-271.
Ukuhlolelwa iCovid-19, ukulawulwa kwayo nokuphefumula ngomshini konke kufakwe ohlwini olusha lwama-PMB, azokhokhelwa ama-medical aid kungakhathalekile ukuthi ilungu likuluphi uhlelo lwe-medical aid.
Uhulumeni wakuleli kulindeleke ukuthi uqale uhlelo lokugonywa kwabasebenzi bezempilo njengoba umgomo ongenela abangu-1 million, okhiqizwe yi-AstraZeneca, usufikile kuleli.
Isikhulu esiphezulu kwaMomentum Health Solutions, uMnuz Damian McHugh, sithe ikhava yeCovid-19 izozimela, ayizuthathwa emalini ebhekelele ukugula kwelungu eyaziwa ngama-savings.
UMnuz Lee Callakopen waKwaBonitas Medical Aid, uthe bazokhokhela nokugoma kwamanye amalungu abhaliswe ngumnikazi we-medical aid ngaphansi kwakhe.
Uthe basohlelweni lokuhlanganisa ulwazi lwamalungu abo ukuze akwazi ukubhalisa esebenzisa i-online ukuze akwazi ukuyogoma.
"Lo mgomo uphindwa kabili, ukubhalisa ngalolu hlelo kuzokwenza ukuthi umuntu azi ukuthi kuzomele abuyele nini futhi ukuyogoma," kusho uCallakopen.
UMkhize uthe amalungu omphakathi angenayo i-medical aid azokhokhelwa uhulumeni.
"Wonke umuntu osengcupheni yokuthola iCovid-19 uzogonywa.
I-medical aid izokhokha, uma usuphumile kuyona uhulumeni uzokukhokhela," kusho yena
Liphezulu izinga leCitroën C3
IMOTO: CITROËN C3INTANDOKAZI yemoto yakwaCitroën okuyiyo edayisa kakhulu, iC3 ithuthukisiwe ngenhloso yokuqhubeka nokudoba abathengi.
Isesigabeni sama-hatchback amancane lapho ibanga khona abathengi nezimoto, okukhona kuzo iVW Polo, Hyundai i20, Kia Rio nezinye.
I-C3 okungeyesizukulwane sesithathu ekhona emakethe, yethulwa ngasekupheleni kuka-2016.
Uma iqhamuka uzoqaphela ingaphambili elishintshiwe, bese kuba namaLED headlights, LED daytime running lights, ama-fog lights kwiShine futhi nangemuva inamalambu angamaLED.
Ifika nemibala emisha eyisithupha, okwazi ukuthola kuyo nokhakhayi oluhlukile umbala.
Ngaphakathi izihlalo zintofontofo futhi kwaCitroen bathi bathuthukise nendlela onciphe ngayo umsindo ongenayo.
Isikhala ebhuthini singu-300 litres.
Inezinto eziningi njengamarimu aphakathi kuka-15 inch no-16 inch, ama-wiper azishayayo uma lina, ama-sensor asiza uma upaka ngemuva, 7 inch touchscreen okwazi ukuxhuma iselula nge-Apple CarPlay noma i-Android Auto.
Iyasho uma umshayeli engasanakile, ine-cruise control nokunye.
Konke kuya ngenhlobo yakho njengoba zihlukene kabili, kuyiShine neFeel.
Izinjini zihlukene kabili.
Kukhona i-1.2 PureTech enamandla angu-60kW ne-torque engu-118Nm futhi engenayo i-turbo.
Uyithola kwiFeel kuphela futhi isebenzisa i-gearbox eyi-5 speed eshintshwayo.
Itorque yayo ingu-205Nm futhi usebenzisa i-gearbox ezishintshayo eyi-6 speed.
Ngo-100km bathi idla amalitha kaphethroli angu-6.
Ngesikhathi yethulwa sithole ithuba lokushayela iShine.
Ihamba kamnandi intofontofo futhi amandla ezwakala ekwazi ukuyithwala bese iyathula ngaphakathi, uwuzwe kancane umsindo wenjini engu-3 cylinder.
Ngakwezokuphepha izinto enazo ngamabhreki e-ABS, EBA, EBD, TCS ne-ESP.
Kugqugquzelwa omama ukuthi bazincelise ubisi lwebele izingane
Mbali Khanyile UGQUGQUZELE omama ngokubaluleka kokuncelisa izingane zabo ubisi lwebele uNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, uNkk Nomagugu Simelane-Zulu ngesikhathi kwethulwa izibalo zabantwana abazalwe ngosuku lokuqala ku2021.
Ungqongqoshe ohalalisele yonke imindeni yezingane ezizalwe ngalolu suku, uthe umnyango uyakholelwa kakhulu ekutheni uzihluphe ngesimo sempilo yezingane.
Uthe kusemqoka ukuthi wonke umzali ancelise ingane yakhe ubisi lwebele ngoba lubalulekile emzimbeni wayo."
Siyazi ukuthi akusiyo into ehlale ilula ukuncelisa ingane ubisi lwebele kodwa sithi abazame omama njengoba ludlala indima enkulu ekwakheni izakhamzimba enganeni.
Lolu hlobo lokuncelisa alugcini nje kuphela ngokwakha izakhamzimba kodwa luphinde luqinise ubudlelwano obuhle phakathi kwengane nonina wayo," kusho uNgqongqoshe.
Eqhuba uthe kumele omama balihloniphe ishadi elibafundisa ngokukhuliswa nokunakekelwa kwezingane ukuze zihlale ziyimiqemane ngaso sonk iikhathi.
Zingu-140 sezizonke izingane ezizalwe ngosuku lokuqala ku-2021 ngokwembiko yomnyango wezempilo esifundazweni.
Zingu-77 izingane zabafana ezizalwe ngalolu suku.
Angu-63 amantombazane esewonke.
UNksz Slindile Mkhize (35) waseNhlungwane, KwaSiqobelo otete amawele esibhedlela, iNkonjeni eMahlabathini, ubonge abasebenzi balesi sibhedlela ngokumlekelela ekuteteni izingane zakhe ngale kokuhlangabezana nenkinga.
Ngibonga indlela abangeseke ngayo onompilo baseNkonjeni ngesikhathi bengitetisa.
Bekunzima kodwa ngikwazile ukunqoba ngenxa yendlela abebengisingethe ngayo," kubonga uNksz Mkhize, umama wamawele.
Abangaboni bafuna ukugomela              iCovid-19 kuqala
ABANGABONI KwaZulu-Natal bafuna ukuthi uhulumeni ababhekelele, babe ngabanye babantu abazogoma kuqala njengengoba kuqala isigaba sesibili sokugomela iCovid-19 namhlanje.
NgoLwesihlanu, inhlangano ebhekelela abakhubazekile, iGezephi Foundation, ibe nesigcawu sokubonisana sabangaboni ebesiseThekwini lapho beveze khona izinkinga ezibenza babe sengcupheni yokuthola iCovid-19.
UNksz Slindile Makhaye, weBlind Youth Organisation, uthe bayafisa ukuthi uhulumeni nabo ababeke eqhulwini ngoba basengcupheni yokutheleleka ngaleli gciwane.
"Njengoba singaboni nje, sibambelela endololwaneni yomuntu ukuze sikwazi ukuzwa umzimba wakhe ukuthi wenzenjani.
Indololwane njengoba kuneCovid-19 kuthiwa abantu abakhwehlelele kuyo, okwenza ukuthi thina sibe sengcupheni ngoba sibambelela kuyo singazi ukuthi kuke kwakhwehlelelwa kuyo.
Njengamanje sibambelela esandleni kodwa lokho akuphephile ngoba awawuzwa umzimba womuntu," kuchaza uNksz MakhayeUqhube wathi ngaphandle kwalokho, njengoba bengaboni basebenzisa izandla zabo bathinte ukuze bezwe ukuthi abukho yini ubungozi.
"Sibona ukuthi kwasekuqaleni ngesikhathi uhulumeni ebheka izindlela zokunqanda ukusabalala kwaleli gciwane, akazange amcabangele umuntu ongaboni.
Sifisa ukuthi lokho akulungise ngokuthi sibe ngabanye abantu abazogoma kulesi sigaba sesibili," kusho yena.
Usihlalo weGezephi Foundation, uMnuz Siya Zondi, uthe lesi siphakamiso basidlulisele kubaphathi bophiko lwabakhubazekile ehhovisi likaNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal naseMnyangweni wezeMpilo kulesi sifundazwe banethemba lokuthi sizofinyelela kuNgqongqoshe wezeMpilo, uDkt Zweli Mkhize.
UMnyango wezeMpilo kuleli uthunyelelwe imibuzo mayelana nokuthi abangaboni ngabe bayingxenye yini yabazogonywa kulesi sigaba.
Kuze kwashaya isikhathi sokushicilela ungakaphenduli.

Abakuleli bayafuna ukugomela iCovid-19
U-71% wabantu bakuleli uzimisele ngokugomela iCovid-19 ukuze uphephe kulesi sifo.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi abayisikhombisa kwabawu-10 abanankinga nokugoma.
Lezi zindaba zivezwe wucwaningo lwakamuva olubizwa ngeNational Income Dynamics Study (Nids) Coronavirus Rapid Mobile Survey (Cram) olwethulwe ngokusemthethweni kwi-webinar yayizolo.
UMnuz Nic Spaul ongumcwaningi ozinze eNyuvesi yaseStellenbosch uveze ukuthi bawu-29% abantu abangathandi ukugomela iCovid-19 kanti basaba ukuthi umgomo uzobadalela ezinye izifo.
Uthe iningi lalabo abasaba ukugoma lifunda kakhulu izindaba ezingaqinisekisiwe ezinkundleni zokuxhumana.
Ucwaningo luveze ukuthi abantu abasha abaneminyaka ewu-18 kuya ku-25 abathandi ukugoma uma kuqhathaniswa nabadala abaneminyaka engaphezu kuka-25.
U-73% wabadala abaneminyaka ewu-35 kuya ku-59 bazwakalise ukuthi bazimisele ngokugoma.
"Sithole ukuthi abantu abanezifo ezingalapheki bazimisele ngokugoma kanjalo nabadala.
Ucwaningo lwethu luveze ukuthi abakhuluma isibhunu (42%) bayasaba ukugomela iCovid-19.
U-25% kuphela wabantu abasaba ukugoma abakhuluma isiZulu, isiXhosa, isiPedi nezinye izilimi.
Abantu abangasabi ukugoma yilabo abakhuluma iTshiVenda njengoba sithole ukuthi wu-18% kuphela omanqika," kusho uSpaul.
UMnuz Reza Daniels ongumcwaningi eNyuvesi yaseCape Town, uveze ukuthi ukuqubuka kweCovid-19 kushintshe indlela yokufunda ezikoleni.
Abafundi bamabanga aphansi ezikoleni okungakhokhwa kuzo balahlekelwe wu-75% wezifundo zabo.
Uthe izingane ezifunda kulezi zikole aziyi njalo esikoleni futhi azikwazi ukwenza umsebenzi emakhaya uma kuqhathaniswa nalezo ezifunda ezikoleni ezikhokhayo, ezinezinsiza zobuchwepheshe besimanje.
Uveze nokuthi izingane bezingakutholi ukudla kahle njengoba bezisemakhaya kanti namanje u-43% kuphela okwazi ukuphakelwa ezikoleni.
"Sithole ukuthi isibalo sezingane ezilala zingadlile sehlile njengoba izikole zivuliwe sasuka ku-16% saya ku-14% ngoFebhuwari noMashi walo nyaka uma siliqhathanisa noNovemba noDisemba wonyaka odlule.
U-67% wabantu esikhulume nabo uveze ukuthi awunayo imali yokuthenga ukudla yingakho izingane zilala zingadlile.
Uhlelo lokutshalwa kwemithi yokwelapha ngokwesintu
KWETHULWE uhlelo lokutshalwa kwemithi yokwelapha ngokwesintu eMadlangeni, eNewcastle, ngeledlule ukuqhakambisa amakhambi esintu ase-Afrika.
USomlomo kuMasipala waseMajuba, uNksz Phumzile Mgcina, uthe bebephendula nenhlabamkhosi kaNdunankulu waKwaZulu-Natal, uMnuz Sihle Zikalala, yokuthi bangashiywa ngaphandle abelaphi bendabuko ngesikhathi ethula uhlelo lwezolimo.
Emikhandlwini ewu-11 yaKwaZulu-Natal, iMajuba - esanda kuthola indawo okuzotshalwa kuyo - iyona kuphela esinohlelo olucacile lokutshalwa kwemithi yesintu.
"Inkosi yesizwe uSphamandla Khumalo, usisikele endaweni yakhe lapho kuzotshalwa khona imithi.
Sithole indawo ewu-15 hectares ezosiza abelaphi bendabuko ukutshala imithi engasatholakali kwezinye izindawo.
Kuyo kuzotshalwa izihlahla ezidingekayo futhi izolawulwa ngabelaphi bendabuko okuyibona abayaziyo imithi edingekayo nabezemvelo abavikela ukucekelwa phansi kwezihlahla.
Ngokwezinhlelo esinazo imithi ezotshalwa khona izosetshenziswa ukuthi kuthakwe imithi ezohlolwa ngokusezingeni lezempilo ukuze ingagulisi abantu uma belashwa ngayo.
Sifuna nokuthi imithi yabo ikwazi ukusebenziseka ezingeni lomhlaba.
Lolu hlelo aluzogcina ngokusiza abelaphi bendabuko kodwa luzovula namathuba omsebenzi," kusho uNksz Mgcina.
Uhlelo lwenganyelwe ngokubambisana phakathi kukamasipala, noMnyango wezeMvelo, uMnyango wezeMpilo KwaZulu-Natal, owezokuThuthukiswa koMnotho, owezoLimo, i-University of KwaZulu-Natal (UKZN) ebimelwe nguSolwazi Nceba Gqaleni nesigungu sabelaphi bendabuko.
USihlalo wesigungu sabelaphi bendabuko eMajuba, uDkt David Shabalala, uthe uhlelo luzobasiza ukuthi umsebenzi wokwelapha ungabukeleki phansi.
"Sifuna ukuthi abantu bangabi namahloni okusebenzisa imithi yesintu.
Indlela ezobukeka ngayo uma isithakiwe izokwenza uhlonipheke umsebenzi wabelaphi bendabuko.
Sifuna nokuqinisekisa abantu ukuthi izicubu zabantu azingeni emithini yokwelapha kodwa umuntu osebenzisa izicubu zomuntu, akayona inyanga ungumthakathi," kusho uDkt Shabalala.
Uthe bafuna ishintshe indlela imithi yesintu ebukwa ngayo e-Afrika.
IMajuba kuseyiyo kuphela egxile enohlelo olwaphasiswa wuhulumeni eminyakeni edlule.
Uvalo lukhulu ngokugadla okwesibili kweCovid-19
INHLANGANO yezempilo emhlabeni iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), ithi izinyanga ezizayo zisazoba nzima njengoba amazwe amaningi eseqalile ukubona izibalo zabahaqwa yiCovid-19 zenyuka.
UMqondisi-jikelele we-WHO, uDkt Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus, uthe amazwe okubukeka sengathi azoba senkingeni kakhulu yilawo okunezinkomba zokuthi asengcupheni yokuthi ahlaselwe yisivunguvungu sesibili seCovid-19 njengamanje.
Uthe maningi kakhulu amazwe aseqalile ukubona izinkomba zokuthi kungenzeka ahlaselwe yisivunguvungu sesibili seCovid-19.
"Izinyanga ezizayo zizoba nzima kanti amanye amazwe sekubonakele ukuthi azothwala kanzima kakhulu kunamanye.
Maningi kakhulu amazwe kumanje anezibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane ezenyukayo.
Iziguli eziningi kuwo sezilaliswe ezibhedlela emagunjini abadinga ukunakekelwa okuthe xaxa.
"Kwamanye amazwe lezi zibalo ziba wuhhafu wezibalo ebezikhona ngamahora angu-24.
Lokhu kuyakhathaza impela.
Imibhede ebekelwe ukulalisa iziguli ezidinga ukunakekelwa okuthe xaxa, uma ukuhaqeka kwabantu kwenyuka ngendlela efanayo emasontweni ambalwa imibhede izobe isiphelile," kusho uDkt Van Kerkhove.
Amazwe okubikwa ukuthi asenezinkomba zokuthi angase ahlaselwe yisivunguvungu sesibili ngokushesha kubalwa iSpain, Hong Kong neMexico.
KwaZulu-Natal uNdunankulu uMnuz Sihle Zikalala uzwakalise ukukhathazeka ngokuthi ziyanyuka izibalo zabahaqwa yileli gciwane.
Liphezulu izinga leRanger XL Sport futhi iphephile
IFORD Ranger ingenye yezimoto ezidayisa kakhulu eNingizimu Afrika.
Yize kunjalo kodwa iFord Motor Company of Southern Africa, ayisongile izandla kunalokho iyaqhubeka nokwenza izindlela zokuyithuthukisa ukuze ihehe kubathengi futhi iqhubeke nokuba yintandokazi.
Bathathe iRanger XL bayifaka isport pack esishintsha indlela ebukeka ngayo baphinde bengeza ngokuningi kuyo.
Ukuyenza ihluke kuneXL ejwayelekile, ifika negrille emnyama engathi iyacwebezela, amarimu angu-17 inch amnyama, tubular sports bar ngemuva nobhampa omnyama.
IFORD Ranger ingenye yezimoto ezidayisa kakhulu eNingizimu Afrika.
Yize kunjalo kodwa iFord Motor Company of Southern Africa, ayisongile izandla kunalokho iyaqhubeka nokwenza izindlela zokuyithuthukisa ukuze ihehe kubathengi futhi iqhubeke nokuba yintandokazi.
Bathathe iRanger XL bayifaka isport pack esishintsha indlela ebukeka ngayo baphinde bengeza ngokuningi kuyo.
Ukuyenza ihluke kuneXL ejwayelekile, ifika negrille emnyama engathi iyacwebezela, amarimu angu-17 inch amnyama, tubular sports bar ngemuva nobhampa omnyama.
Ebesihamba ngayo ibinesitebhisi sokugibela eceleni osifaka uma uthanda nesenza kube lula ukugibela ngoba iphakeme, yabe isifakwa nopende wokuvikela isikhenke.
Ngaphakathi uyakwazi ukususa iSYNC1 esikhaleni sayo ufake i-infotainment system engu-8 inch touchscreen.
Ukwazi ukuxhuma iselula nge-Apple CarPlay noma i-Android Auto.
Inamawindi kagesi ngaphakathi, aircon, nesikhala esikahle sabagibeli.
Ukungabikhona kolayini abaqeda inkungu ewindini langemuva namasensor asiza uma upaka kuyakukhumbuza ukuthi iXL Sport yiveni elifana neXLT, Wildtrak, Thunder neRaptor.
Emgwaqweni ihamba ngenjini engu-2.
2 litre enamandla angu-118kW netorque engu-385Nm.
Ihamba ngogearbox oyi-6 speed ozishintshayo.
Ihamba kamnandi emgwaqeni futhi intofontofo nokuyinto amaveni akwaFord agabe ngayo.
Noma uyifaka obhuqwini ayinankinga kwazise yi-4x4 futhi asikho nesidingo sokuma uma uyishintsha ku-2H uyifaka ku-4H.
Iphinde ibe no-4L nediff lock.
IToyota Hilux idayise okuzedlula zonke ngoFebhuwari
KUQHUBEKILE ukwehla kokuthengwa kwezimoto njengoba izibalo zangoFebhuwari zikhomba ukuthi zincane uma kuqhathaniswa noFebhuwari wonyaka odlule.
INaamsa ithe kwenzeke obekulindelekile njengoba izibalo ziqhathaniswa nezangaphambi kokubhebhetheka kweCovid-19 ngonyaka odlule.
Ngenyanga edlule kudayiswe izimoto ezingu-37 521 nokuyisibalo esehle ngo-5 775 noma u-13.
3% uma kuqhathaniswa no-43 296 owadayiswa ngoFebhuwari wonyaka odlule.
Isibalo sezimoto ezidayiswe ngaphandle naso sehlile njengoba zibe ngu-29 582.
Qaphela ungangeni enkingeni
NJENGOBA kuza amaholidi kaDisemba baningi abafuna ukuvela emakhaya ngezimoto ezintsha, abanye bafuna ukuqeda unyaka ngegiya eliphezulu ngoba benethemba lokuthi uma benza njalo unyaka omusha uzobaphatha kahle.
Abanye bagcina belutheka ngoba bejahe ukuba nemoto entsha.
Izazi zithi isimo semali siphazamisekile kwabaningi ngenxa yeCovid-19 okwenze abantu babhedelwa amarekhodi abo kwaCredit Bureau okugcina kwenza abantu babe sohlwini lwabangakhokhi kahle.
Lokhu kuyamphazamisa umuntu ofuna ukuthenga imoto kaDisemba ngoba amabhange awakwazi ukumnika imali yokuthenga.
"Kube sekuqala ukuhalela izinto ezingafanele ezifana nabantu abathembisa ukukudayisela imoto ngisho usohlwini olubi.
Umuntu ubona esebishile enkingeni ukuthi bekungamele alwenze lolu hlelo.
"Muva nje kuthiwa kunomthengi ofake idiphozithi kaR100 000 ngoba efuna iSUV ephambili watshelwa ukuthi akhokhe uR15 000 ngenyanga egaraji.
"Into yokuqala nje ekhombisa ukuthi kukhona okunuka santungwana eyokuthi uma uthenga ebhange elisemthethweni, imali oyikhokha nyanga zonke bayazithathela bona abasebhange kwi-akhawunti yomthengi noma bakunike i-akhawunti yalo ibhange, hhayi eyegaraji.
"Kuthiwa ngemva kweminyaka emibili ekhokha umthengi wathuka woma sekufika isikhonzi senkantolo sizolanda imoto.
Umthengi kuthe uma eya kwabomthetho ngalolu daba bamtshela lokhu:- Akukho mthetho omvunayo ngoba ukudayiselana akwenza kuphula umthetho weNational Credit Act othi: Awukwazi ukuthenga ngesikweletu uma unegama elibi, awukwazi ukuthenga imoto ngesikweletu ungenaso isivumelwano nokunika isikweletu osemthethweni.
Imali yakhe yediphozithi ngeke ayithole ngoba ukusebenzisana kwakhe nomthengi omqolile akukho emthethweni kukonke nje.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi umthengi ulahlekelwe nguR100 000 nemali elinganiselwa kuR360 000 aseyikhokhe kule minyaka emibili.
Okubalulekile okumele ukwazi njengomthengi osebenzisa isikweletu ukuthenga imoto noma njengomuntu ofuna ukuthenga imoto yilokhu:- Uma ususayine isivumelwano nebhange othenge ngalo imoto, awukwazi ukuvele ushintshe umqondo.
Kumele wenze ngendlela yesivumelwano ngisho usuhluleka ukukhokhela imoto.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi awuniki noma yimuphi umuntu ukuthi akaqhubeke nesitolimende sakho semoto.
Thinta ibhange kuqala nixoxe ngohlelo oluhlosile uma usenkingeni.
- Akukho semthethweni webhange nababolekisa imali ukudlulisela inkontileka yakho yokukhokhela imoto komunye umuntu esivumelwaneni sokuthenga imoto ngesikweletu.
Kumele uxhumane nebhange lakho ulazise ngomuntu ofuna ukukhokhela imoto.
Ibhange lizokuchazela ngemigudu yalo okumele uyilandele ukuze nivumelane.
- Yize kunguwena othenge imoto ngesikweletu, akusiyona eyakho uze uqede ukukhokhela isikweletu ngokugcwele.
Imoto kusengeyebhange futhi uma ungahambisani nemithetho enavumelana ngayo uthenga, bayakwazi ukuyifuna ibuyele kubona imoto, bamise inkontileka bese befuna isinxephezelo semali sokuphula umthetho kuwena mthengi.
- Imoto engakaqedi ukukhokha isikweletu ngokugcwele, ayikwazi ukudayiselwa omunye umuntu ngoba ibhuku elikhombisa ubunikazi lisukelisebhange.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi nakumthengi ofuna imoto kodwa ingenayo i-log book, akathengi ngokusemthethweni uma ingekho futhi ingakashintshi imininingwane yomnini wemoto kulona leli bhuku.
- Uma kukhona umuntu othi yena umele ibhange othenge kulo imoto futhi ufuna ukuyithatha, thinta ibhange kuqala ngaphambi kokuthi nize nixoxe.
Khumbula ukuthi uma ibhange lizothatha imoto engakhokheliwe, lifika nesikhonzi senkantolo.
Isikhonzi kumele sikukhombise amaphepha avezaukuthi ngempela sisemthethweni.
Isikhonzi sisebenza phakathi kuka-8 ekuseni no-5 ntambama phakathi nesonto.
Izikhathi ezingaphandle kwalezo, akuzona ezomsebenzi wabo ngokusemthethweni.
- Uma kugcina ithathwa imoto ngokusemthethweni, landelela nebhange lakho ukuthi kugcine kwenzekeni mayelana nokudayiswa kwayo nohlelo lwenkontileka yakho nalo njengoba imoto ingasekho.
Ungadembeseli ushiye kanjalo ngoba uthi imoto yakho ayisekho ngoba kungenzeka ithathwe abadayisi mbumbulu bayinike omunye umuntu wena usale nesikweletu.
Izinselelo zokuqhubeka nesikweletu somunye emotweni
KULESI SIKHATHI esinzima sezomnotho abathengi bakuthola kunzima ukuthenga ngenxa yokuthi amaphepha abo okuphathwa kwezimali awamile kahle.
Lokhu kubizwa ngokuthi baBlacklisted (abavumelekile ukunikezwa izikweletu yibhange).
Lesi simo siphoqa abanye ukuthi bancamele ukuqhubeka nesitolimende semoto yomunye umuntu, ohlulekayo ukuyikhokhela.
Kubonakala kuwumqondo ophusile ngoba lowo osuke esehluleka ukukhokhela imoto, uyasizakala ukuze igama lakhe lingancoliswa ukungakhokhi kanti lowo onegama elimbi, yena uthola imoto azoyisebenzisa.
Uma usubhekisisa kahle izingqinamaba abantu abaningi ababhekana nazo uma benza lesi sinqumo kuyaqala kubonakala ukungabi muhle kwawo.
Ake sibuke izimo ezingenzeka:Uma nivumelana ngalesi senzo nomthengi wemoto, wena mnini wemoto kumele ukhumbule ukuthi uma kukhona okwenzekayo kuleyo moto, nguwena obhekelela zonke izidingo zokukhokha nomshwalense.
Abanye babhala inkontileka yokudayiselana kodwa lokhu akusizi muntu uma kukhona ingxabano ngoba ukhumbule ukuthi imoto idayiswe ngokomthetho webhange lapho umnini wayo wayisayinela ngenkathi eyithenga.
Uma kunengxabano phakathi kwalowo ofuna ukwenza "iTake Over," ibhange alisiboni isivumelwano sabo njengesisemthethweni.
- Leli phuzu elingenhla liqala ukwenza umqondo uma kushintsha isimo sokudayiselana, othatha imoto engasakwazi ukufeza isivumelwano engasayikhokheli.
Ibhange libopha umnini wemoto futhi lingcolisa igama lakhe ngokumfakela i-"Judgement" enkantolo nasemabhukwini okuphathwa kwezimali (Credit Bureau).
Khumbula ukuthi lo muntu omnika imoto nge "Take Over," usesimeni akusona nje ngokungakhokheli izikweletu zakhe ezibhekene naye.
Uma isikweletu singasabhekene naye, ngeke azinike ugqozi oluphezulu uma isimo sakhe sezimali sesibheke phansi.
- Uma umthathi we "Take Over" engawukhokheli umshwalense wemoto bese iba sengozini, wena mnini wemoto ubhekana nenkinga wedwa.
Inkontileka esayinwa umnini wemoto nebhange ngesikhathi eyithenga imoto, ibeka kucace ukuthi umnini wemoto kumele abhekele izidingo zomshwalense zemoto ngokugcwele.
Uma lokhu kungenzeki bese ilimala imoto, ibhangi linelungelo lokuyifuna yonke imali yemoto ngisho isilimele.
- Impatho yemoto ibaluleke kakhulu uma ubheka ukudayisa imoto.
Kulezi zimo ze-take over, kujwayelekile ukuthi umuntu oyithathayo imoto angayinaki ngoba azi ukuthi akuyona eyakhe.
Lokhu kudala ingxabano uma imoto ifa izinsimbi bese idinga ukulungiswa.
Uma kubiza ukuyilungisa egaraji, umthengi uvele abaleke aye kofuna enye imoto azoyiqola ngayo "take over " bese umnini wemoto esala nenkinga yokuyilungisa nokuyigayisa.
- Njengoba isivumelwano se-take over singekho ngaphezulu kwenkontileka yomnini wemoto nebhange, wena oyithenga ngayo, uma umnini wemoto eseyifuna akukho ongabambelela kukhona ngokomthetho ngoba imoto isuke kungeyakhe.
Lokhu kujwayele ukwenzeka uma umnini wemoto esesimeni esihle ngokwezimali bese eyifuna imoto yakhe.
Kokunye umnini wemoto ubona sekusondele isikhathi sokukhokhelwa ngokugcwele ebhange bese ethi useyayifuna imoto yakhe.
Lokhu ukwenza ukuze ayidayise enze inzuzo ngayo.

Isangoma sodumo sixwayisa abantu
SILOKHU sizakhele udumo isangoma esithandwa abaningi ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ngokukhuluma amaqiniso aphathelene nobungoma.
UTumi Gogo Skhotheni Dlamini Shange muva nje udalule imfihlo ephathelene nokubethela okwenziwa izangoma emzini yabantu.
Ugogo Skhotheni uqophe ivideo ezinsukwini ezedlule wayifaka ekhasini lakhe lakuFacebook elinabalandeli abawu-196, 171, lapho edalula ukuthi ukubethela kuyinto ejwayelekile futhi efanelwe ukwenziwa emzini yabantu kodwa imithi embiwa izangoma emagcekeni yabantu akulona iqiniso.
Udalule ukuthi lokhu kuwumkhuba owenziwa ezinye zezangoma ezifika nayo lemithi bese ziyimbela ngandlela thile abantu bakulowo mndeni bengaboni.
Naye uqobo uthe uyazi kwenziwa njani lokhu futhi akakhathalele kuthenjwa ngalokhu akudalulayo.
"Umuntu uma ezophuma nomuthi esitsheni ethi uwugubhe phansi kini nimubuka, uyazi bawufaka kanjani, ngiyazi nami ngike ngakhona kwenziwa futhi ngiyazisola.
Kodwa manje angisazisoli ngoba ngathola isifundo sokuthi amanga.
Ngibulaleni uma nithanda anginandaba," kusho uGogo Skhotheni kule video.
"Lalelani umuntu uyafakwa egcekeni kodwa njengesichelo, isangoma sizofika sichele umuzi ngoba uyaqiniswa.
Kodwa le yokuthi uzokhipha umuthi egcekeni amanga," kusho ugogo Skhotheni.
Eqhuba uthe abantu abake bacabangisise ukuthi ngabe umuthi obufakwe nini ngoba basuke bekhona.
Yize abantu beludinga usizo kubalaphi bendabuko kodwa uthe abavule amehlo bangabi izisulu zezangoma.
Akakhohlwanga ukukhuluma nangezilwane abantu abahlala besatshiswa ngazo kuthiwa kumele zilashwe noma zisuswe kubantu.
Konke lokhu uthe kunezindlela ezahlukene zokuphambanisela abantu iqiniso ngoba izangoma zifuna ukwenza imali.
Abantu bamshayele ihlombe ngokuqunga isibindi abavule amehlo.
Le video seyibukwe abantu abangaphezulu kuka-19 000, kwaphawula abangaphezulu kuka-6 100.
Baningi abafisa abenohlelo lwakhe kwithelevishini namathwasa akhe.

Akukakabi yisikhathi sokuvala imingcele: usosayensi
UKUSABALALA ngokushesha kwegciwane leCorona elitholakale kamuva e-India kuzoba nomthelela ohlelweni lokuusatshalaliswa kwemigomo yeCovid-19 emazweni ase-Afrika.
UMqondisi Jikelele weNhlangano yezeMpilo eMhlabeni, iWorld Health Organisation (WHO), uDkt Tedros Ghebreyesus uthe ukusabalala ngendlela engalawuleki kwegciwane elitholakale e-India, kuyayithinta i-Afrika njengoba kuzomele yonke imigomo eyikhiqizayo, iyikhiqizele izwe layo ngaphambi kokuthi kudayiselwe amanye amazwe.
"Maningi amazwe ase-Afrika anesivumelwano sokuthenga imigomo yeCovid-19 e-India, okumanje alinde imigomo yawo.
Ukubhebhetheka ngokwedlulele kweCorona kuleliya lizwe kuzofaka ingcindezi kubakhiqizi bemigomo, okuzodingeka ukuthi bakhiqizele ekhaya ngaphambi kokuthi bacabange ngokudayisa.
Zikhona izinhlelo esezenziwe zokuthi imigomo ithengwe kwamanye amazwe ngenxa yokuthi i-India nayo ibhekene negcindezi yayo.
Lokho kuzosho ukuthi lawo mazwe asezoba sekugcineni ohlelweni lwabazokhiqizelwa imigomo kulezo zinkampani ngoba nazo bezivele zinohla lwazo, lwamazwe ebezihlele ukuwakhiqizela," kusho uGhebreyesus.
UGhebreyesus wubekhuluma nabaholi bezempilo e-Afrika emhlanganweni wabo muva nje.
Uthe e-Afrika bangu-2% abantu abagonyelwe iCovid-19 uma beqhathaniswa nasebegome emhlabeni wonke.
Usho kanjena nje kuleli kutholakale ukuthi bane abantu abanegciwane elitholakale e-India, okudale uvalo olukhulu kubantu.
Abanye bagxeka uhulumeni ngokuthi akazange ayivale imingcele namachweba, ukuze leli gciwane lingafinyeleli kuleli.
USolwazi Barry Schoub, osekomitini eleluleka ongqongqoshe ababhekele iCovid-19 kuleli, iMinisterial Advisory Committee (MAC), uthe ukuvala imingcele namachweba bekungaba yisona sisombululo, ebesingasebenza kodwa ngenxa yesimo somnotho esintengayo kuleli ukwenza lokho kakusona isisombululo okwamanje.
"Okwamanje akusona isinqumo okumele sithathwe wuhulumeni uma sibheka isimo somnotho kuleli.
Mhlawumbe uma isimo siya ngokuya siqina lokho kungacatshangwa," kusho uSchoub.
Indoda idinga ukuhlonishwa ngisho ngabe kayinalutho esandleni
KULELI sonto sigxile ekutheni indoda iyadinga ukuhlonishwa inikezwe indawo yayo kodwa kube yindoda nayo ekukhombisayo ukuthi kuyifanele lokho, kuloba uDISTANCE GUMEDEKwesinye isikhathi kuyenzeka wena ungumuntu wesifazane, uthandane nendoda obonayo ukuthi awuyisabi futhi ungayigingqa ngenqindi kodwa ngokwesiZulu nangendlela esikhuliswe ngayo emakhaya, sazi ukuthi indoda iyahlonishwa futhi ayibekwa isandla noma ngabe ayilutho kangakanani.
Ngisho noma ngabe ayinalutho kanjani kodwa indoda kuyohlezi kuyindoda.
Kwesinye isikhathi thina bantu besifazane sike senze izinto ezikhombisa ubuwula nokungabi nangqondo ngenxa yokwehlulwa wuthando.
Ngikhuluma nje kunabantu besifazane abazithola beboshiwe ngenxa yokuthi bahlulekile ukulawula izinhliziyo zabo nesikhwele abanaso.
Ngikhuluma nje kunabantu besifazane abaliwe ngenxa yokuthi bahlulekile ukuzibamba nokulawula imizwa yabo.
Ngikhuluma nje kunabantu besifazane abafika ezindlini zamadoda bacekele phansi yonke into babulale ngisho amawindi ngenxa yokuhlulwa yisikhwele nokucabanga ukuthi uphathina wakhe akathembekile.
Namhlanje ngifisa thina bantu besifazane, asizifundise ukuhlonipha nokuthobela amadoda esithi siyawathanda.
Ngisho ngabe indoda kayinalutho kodwa ukuyihlonipha kulungile.
Uma Indoda ihlonishwa nguwena kuqala othandana nayo, lokho kudala ukuthi nabantu abasemaceleni bayihloniphe, ibe nesithunzi futhi emphakathini.
Abanye abantu baye basebenzise ukuthi bafunde kakhulu ukudlula amadoda ebese besebenzisa lawo mandla kanti abanye baye basebenzise ukuthi banokuningi ukudlula amadoda kanti bazomosha izinto benganakile.
Mina ngikhule emndenini ongenalutho, ubaba engasebenzi kodwa umama ubengakhohlwa ukuthi wubani inhloko yomuzi phakathi kwakhe nobaba yingakho ngifisa sizifundise ukuhlonipha amadoda thina bantu besifazane.
Angisho ukuthi siwathandaze kodwa ngithi asiwathobele njengabantu besifazaneIndoda enikwa uthando nehlonishwayo ngisho ingenalutho, kukancane uyithole inehliziyo encane ngoba iyazi ukuthi yebo angisebenzi kodwa unkosikazi wami uyazi ukuthi yimina inhloko yalo muzi.
Yebo, ngiyazi ukuthi anginamali kodwa akusho ukuthi unkosikazi wami akahambe ema ngegama lami komakhelwane.
Inhloso lapha wukwakha umuzi nokujabhisa izitha nokwenza umuntu wakho wesilisa into ebalulekile noma ngabe akanalutho kanjani.
Into ebuhlungu kakhulu wukuthi kuthi sesikwenzile konke lokhu, thina bantu besifazane, indoda ebese izozibonakalisa ubunjalo bayo, iphinde ibonge ngepuleti lendle.
Uyenzele yonke into indoda ekugcineni bese izoshada nomuntu wayo wamaphupho.
Yileyo nto-ke eyenza thina bantu besifazane simelwe yingqondo nenhliziyo.
Indoda enjalo ayidingi kuhlonishwa.- Isolezwe NgoMgqibelo (Ungaphuthelwa yingosi kaMaGumede kule mpelasonto kwiSolezwe ngoMgqubelo!)
Siphezulu isibalo sabesilisa abazibulalayo eNingizimu Afrika - ucwaningo
UKUCINDEZELEKA komuntu wesilisa kunzima ngoba njengabantu besilisa sikhuliswa sitshelwa ukuthi indoda ifela ngaphakathi, kungagqugquzelwa ukukhuluma ngezinkinga.
Le ndlela yokucabanga igcina isinomthelela ngisho umuntu esehleli ngokuhlukumezeka, ehlukunyezwa ekhaya noma ehlukunyezwa umuntu athandana naye.
Ngokwezibalo zabantu abashonayo minyaka yonke kuleli, kuvela ukuthi u-17% wabo basuke bezibulele.
Ngokocwaningo lweWorld Health Organization (WHO) olushicilelwe ngo-2018 olusihloko sithi Preventing Suicide: A Resource For Pesticide Registrars and Regulators, kuvela ukuthi bangaphezulu kuka-800 000 abantu abazibulalayo ngonyaka.
Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi ukuzibulala kwabantu kudlula izifo okubalwa kuzo umalaleveva nomdlavuza webele ngonyaka emhlabeni.
Lolu cwaningo nokho luqhuba lushiye isithombe esikhathazayo ngabantu besilisa baseNingizimu Afrika njengoba kuvela ukuthi kubantu abawu-6 476 abazibulala kuleli ngo-2016, abawu-5 138 kubo kwakungabesilsa.
Lezi zinombolo azisho ukuthi wonke umuntu wesilisa ohlukunyezwayo uyazibulala, kodwa zikubeka kucace ukuthi zikhona izinkinga nengcindezi ebhekene nabantu besilisa abadinga ukukhuluma ngazo.
Bephawula ngalolu daba abesilisa baveze ukuthi kunzima ukuphumela obala ngokuhlukunyezwa.
Abesilisa abasibhalelile bacele ukungadalulwa.
"Nami ngingomunye wabahlukunyezwayo kodwa angikaze ngiye emaphoyiseni, usizo alukho lapho bafika bathi hamba uyolungisa izinkinga zakho nomdeni wakho," kusho lo wesilisa othe amaphoyisa kumele alusukumele ngendlela efanayo udaba lokuhlukunyezwa kowesilisa nolowesifazane.
Omunye okhulume neSolezwe uthe ubonga uNkulunkulu ngokuthi akazibulalanga.
"Ubengihlukumeza lo sisi engihlala naye ngimlobolile kwaphela umsebenzi nginaye wavele wangihlukumeza kakhulu ngaze ngacela ukumshiya.
Manje usengihlukumeza ngengane noma ngimcela ukuthi ingane ayingangeni ezindabeni zethu.
"Njengoba kuvalwe izwe, uthathe imali yesondlo wanginika ingane ethi uzosheshe ayithathe yahlala kimi ingane emsebenzini sancishiselwa isikhathi sokusebenza nemali engiyiholayo yancipha.
Ithe ingena imali zabamba izikweletu ngasala nemali encane bese ngiyicela imali kuyena ngimtshela ukuthi ngiyasindelwa.
"Uvele wangithuka wathi kungani ngifune imali kuye ekubeni ingane inami.
Mangichaza ukuthi angiholanga imali ephelele wathi akahlangane nalokho," kuchaza lo wesilisa.
Omunye uthe: "Ayi khona ngempela abantu besifazane bayawahlukumeza amadoda, uthando imali manje.
Uma ungenayo umuntu uyaphinga athi ngizokwenzani ungenalutho, ayilungile leyo nto.
"Engxoxweni noMonwabisi Grootboom wohlelo olukhuluma ngempilo yabashadile kuMzansi Magic, uthe inkulu inkinga yokuhlukunyezwa kwabantu besilisa kodwa abaningi bayesaba ukukhuluma ngayo ngoba besaba ukuthi bangazidonsela amanzi ngomsele kubantu abafuna ukugxila kuphela odabeni lokuhlukunyezwa kwabesifazane.
Uthe ucwaningo lweWHO alushayi eceleni ngoba siphezulu isibalo sabantu besilisa abashadile abazibulalayo kulelo.
"Okwenza abantu besilisa bangakhulumi ngokuhlukumezeka kwabo yingoba isikhathi esiningi kusuke kungathinti ukubekwa isandla kodwa bahlukunyezwa ngokomphefumulo lapho othola khona sebebizwa ngamagama bedelelwa.
Ngakolunye uhlangothi kunabesilisa abahlukunyezwa onina bezingane zabo, abangathandani nabo kodwa othola esehlukumezeka ngoba akakwazi ukukhokha imali yesondlo ekubeni engasebenzi naye.
"Abantu besilisa kuningi ukuhlukumezeka komphefumulo abadlula kukho," kusho uGrootboom.
UMONWABISI Grootboom owathathwa enomkakhe uPhindile, uthi yinqwaba yabesilisa abahlukumezekile nasemishadweni kodwa abakhatha ukufela ngaphakathiUthe lokhu kuhlukumezeka yikho okudala ukuthi abanye babo bagcine izinto ngaphakathi.
"Ngiyaye ngibagqugquzele abesilisa ukuthi kungcono ukuthi uzikhiphe kulobo budlelwano uma uhlukunyezwa.
Uma kuyingxabano yangaleso sikhathi ozithola usuhlukunyezwa ngamagama kuyo, kungcono uyinqamule kwehle imimoya."
Kukhuzwa umkhuba kasawoti novinegar omnyama
KUSUKELA ngempelasonto kuyachwaza ezinkundleni zokuxhumana ikakhulukazi kuFacebook, abantu bekhuluma ngamandla kasawoti novinegar okuthiwa wenza abantu baboniswe izitha zabo.
Kuvele ukuthi abantu bafaka usawoti novinegar omnyama bese bekufaka phansi kombhede ukuze baphuphe sakuboniswa phakathi namabili.
Lokhu kuqubule omkhulu umsindo emakhasini ahlukene akuFcebook kanjalo nakuTwitter.
Babodwa abathi babona abanakwabo, abathakathi, izilwane nokungacaci ukuthi kuyiqiniso kangakanani.
Ongoti bamakhambi esintu bathi lona umkhuba ongajwayelekile kodwa futhi engeke baphikisana nawo kubantu abawaziyo.
UMnuz V V O MKhize uthe akakaze ezwe ngalo mkhuba kodwa angaqwashisa abantu ngobungozi bokusebenzisa into abangakaze bezwe nabo ngayo.
UMkhize uthe ngokujwayelekile uma umuntu eba nesibonakaliso sikhuluma ngaye kuqala nento eqondene nayo nekumele ayilungise.
Lokhu okunye kwabathakathi nezilwane kuba yinto engalandela kamuva uma kwenzile kwavela.
"Kumele kuqale kumbuleleke wena kuqala, akumele isithupha sikhombe omunye umuntu singabhekisi ngakuwe.
Iphutha elenzekayo esikhathini abantu benezinkinga babona sengathi zidalwa abanye abantu kugcine sekulula ukuthi umuntu uyathakatha," kusho uMkhize.
Eqhuba uthe abantu basebenza ngezindlela ezingafani nezindawo zinenqubo engafani nokwenza lo mkhuba abantu abaningi bangawazi.
"Kuningi abantu okumele bakuqaphele, into eyenziwa bese ihambisana nokusebenza komqondo womuntu ingadala nezinkinga.
Yingakho kungcono umuntu aqale athole ulwazi olwanele ngento angenzi into ngoba yenziwa iningi," kusho uMkhize.
Amavideo nezithombe sekusabalele izinkundla zokuxhumana kukhulunywa ngalo mkhuba.
Babodwa abakhala ngamalungu omzimba asale etubekile emuva kokuthi benze lo mkhuba.
I-Ranger Raptor idle ngobukhulu namandla engeziwe
IMOTO: FORD RANGER RAPTORNGENA emgwaqweni bese uyaqalaza ubuke ukuthi mangakanani amaveni ozowabona nokuzosidweba sicace isithombe sokuthi abantu baseNingizimu Afrika bayazifela ngalezi zimoto.
Kule minyaka edlule silokhu sikhula isibalo sabantu abathenga izimoto eziphakeme amaSUV futhi namaveni ayinyama kubathengi.
Okumnandi ngeveni ukuthi wenza izinto eziningi ngalo, ikakhulukazi eliyi double cab.
Lilayisha abagibeli bese kuba nesikhala esikhulu sokulayisha impahla esikhenkeni.
Isikhenke usenza lokhu okufunwa nguwe, kuye ngezidingo zakho.
Kuthe ngonyaka odlule kwaFord bethula iRanger Raptor edle ngobukhulu namandla engeziwe, ikakhulukazi obhuqwini.

Isebenzisa ugearbox oyi-10 speed manual.

Uthi uma uyifaka kuSport uyizwe ishintsha ukuduma isheshe ingene nasejubaneni uma uyipha amafutha.
Angithi inama-driving modes ayisithupha (Normal, Sport, Grass/Gravel/Snow, Rock, Mud/Sand noBaja) Akukho lapho obhajwa khona.
UBaja ungathi uSport wasobhuqwini.
Ikunikeza ukuzethemba uzibone uyizelamani zakwaWoolridge uLance noGareth ezishayela izimoto zomjaho kwiSouth African Cross Country Series.
Amathayi amaBF Goodrich 285/70 R17 all-terrain tyres namashocks eFox ayayivumela ukuthi obhuqwini ihambe ngokukhululeka.
Ezinsukwini eziyisikhombisa esizichithe nayo ibilokhu idla amalitha kadizili angu-10 ngo-100km.
Injalo nje iphephile njengoba ineTraction Control, iyasho uma iphuma emzileni noma kukhona ezokushayisa ngaphambili nokunye.

Yiba neso elibukhali enganeni ngalesi sikhathi sikathaqa
ISIKHATHI sikathaqa sifike nezinguquko eziningi ezithinta ngisho inhlalo yezingane emakhaya njengoba kuvalwe izikole.
Ukuhlala isikhathi eside izingane zisemakhaya kusho ukuthi kudingeka neso lomzali elibukhali.
Njengoba kuyisonto lokukhuthaza ukuvikelwa kwezingane, kukhunjuzwa abazali ngokubaluleka kokugada ngendlela izingane emakhaya.
Ungoti ekukhulisweni kwezingane, uNkk Jackie Branfild weBobbi Bear eManzimtoti, uthe ukuba semakhaya kwezingane akusho ukuthi abazali banethezeke baziyeke zitshakadule noma kanjani.
Uthe izikhathi zimbi, kumele abazali bavule amahle kwazise izingane zihehwa ubala kumuntu futhi akulula ukuthi zibone uma umuntu omdala eseqala ukuzigangela.
UNkk Branfiled uthe izingane imvamisa yezingane ezitholwa zihlukumezeka ngokushaywa, ukuthethiswa nokudlwengulwa noma ngokuntshontshwa, labo bantu abenza lokhu kusuke kungabantu abasondelene kakhulu nemindeni yazo labo abazigilayo.
Yingakho ekhuthaza ukuthi umzali aqale ekhaya abheke uhlobo lomndeni ozosondelana nengane.
"Ngalesi sikhathi impilo ixakazise izinto eziningi ngalesi sikhathi kumele nakanjani umzali avikele inganekw iCovid-19, kodwa angakhohlwa ezinye izinto ezinobungozi.
Ukudlwengulwa kwezingane, ukuntshontshwa nokushaywa kwenzeka ngokuphazima kweso futhi kwenziwa umuntu osondelene kakhulu nengane nesuke imazi."
"Imvamisa yabantu abondlayo emakhaya bayaba nobungozi ezinganeni.
Akuvamile ukuthi kwenziwe umuntu wangaphandle nosuka kude," kusho uNkk Branfild.
Eqhuba uthe kunephutha elenziwa abazali lokushiya ingane ekhaya nomuntu wesilisa ngoba ethi uyise, umalume noma umfowabo.
"Amalungu omndeni ayazithanda izingane kodwa umuntu wesilisa ngokwemvelo angeke akwazi ukumelana nezidingo zengane usuku lonke.
Yize bekhona abakwazi ukugada izingane kodwa ngokwemvelo ngeke bakwazi ukubona noma sekunenkinga ," kusho uNkk Branfild.
Okunye akuvezile ukuthi abantu besilisa kuyenzeka abukeke esenothando kakhulu ngokweqile enganeni kanti useyayigila.
"Uma umuntu wesilisa esekhombisa uthando oluningi ngengane kusuke sekudinga ukubhekisiswa ngoba kungenzeka ukuthi sekukhona okushaya amanzi.
Yingakho ngihlala ngikhuthaza ukuthi umuntu angayigadisi umuntu wesilisa ingane, akukhethile noma eyomfana noma intombazane," kusho uNkk Branfild.
Izinto okumele uzenze njengomzali-Khuluma nengane noma ngabe ubuya ebusuku emsebenzini, yibuze usuku luyiphathe kanjani ukuze kube lula ukuthi ikutshele uma seyinenkinga.
-Lalela ingane yakho uma iqala ikhononda ngomuntu ebihleli naye noma ingafuni ukusondelana noma kungaba owesilisa noma owesifazane.
-Ungayiceleli ingane komakhelwane ongenawo kahle umlando wempilo abayiphila, noma ungazazi izihlobo ezifika khona.
-Fundisa ingane yakho ngezingxenye zomzimba okumele iziqaphele ingathintwa kuzo abantu.
-Uma ingane seyiqala ibuza imibuzo, phendula ulandelele ngoba kusuke sekukhona okwenzekayo engakuqondi efisa ukukuzwa ngawe ukuthi kufanele yini kwenzeke.
-Hlala nayo phansi uyibuze ngabantu basekhaya nokuthi ithanda ukuhlala nobani nezizathu zalokho.
-Yakha ubudlelwano bokuthi ingane yakhe ikwazi ukukuthemba ukuze izokutshela sakuba yimfihlo uma kukhona noyisabisa ngokuyibulala uma imceba ngokuyinukubeza.
